
-----title
许昌 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='dbc3e207ab4440bdbdb07f136da46728_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dbc3e207ab4440bdbdb07f136da46728");'><span id='dbc3e207ab4440bdbdb07f136da46728_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1126')">1118-1126年</a>，1-9岁</div><div id='dbc3e207ab4440bdbdb07f136da46728' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年5月12日</a>　出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　祖父瑨通判颍昌府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1120')">1119-1120年</a>　居颍昌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　是年其祖父瑨请祠，提举洞宵宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　居颍昌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年3月3日</a>　上巳日，叶梦得（少蕴）怀颍昌风物，有词寄其祖父韩瑨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　是春，其祖父瑨以疾致仕，有诗感怀，寄陈州王襄等人，晁说之得诗，有和作。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年闰5月</a>　其祖父瑨卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年闰11月</a>　其父冕卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　居颍昌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年1月</a>　葬其祖父瑨、父冕于灵井祖茔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1126')">1123-1126年</a>　居颍昌。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
苏州
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　从学尹焞。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a2c8f657c73142b388f612e07d93234f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a2c8f657c73142b388f612e07d93234f");'><span id='a2c8f657c73142b388f612e07d93234f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>，35岁</div><div id='a2c8f657c73142b388f612e07d93234f' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏，翁蒙之（子功）护其兄柩归建康安葬，元吉与之相偕至平江而别，作序以赠。作品：《同翁子功之平江午憩涵江净慈寺》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span>《送翁子功序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_242995' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242995' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242995?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同翁子功之平江午憩涵山净慈寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_242995")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242995_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242995'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242995'>蘋花吹尽藕花香，日落风生水面凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242995_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242995'>净洗扁舟载明月，共君长啸饮湖光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242995_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242995'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242995_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1254458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送翁子功序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254458")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254458'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254458'>朝廷往岁复孝廉之举，尝怪远近未有应诏，又其选止于在野之士而不及在官者，故郡县得以藉口而罔敢轻议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254458_comment'></div>盖举一孝谓己必有愧于孝之名，举一廉谓己必有愧于廉之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254458_comment'></div>而真孝悌廉洁者，又以为兹吾道之常，惟惧其有所表见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254458_comment'></div>上下相疑，贤不肖相嫉，而顽戾贪黠者往往得志，此其所以犹愧于两汉者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254458_comment'></div>嗟乎，若吾子功，其可以副兹选乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254458_comment'></div>子功居家孝而慈，在官廉以有立，以孤童侍老母，游宦于四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254458_comment'></div>不幸丧其兄，而兄之子且幼，子功外经营家事，内奉其亲之颜色，俾不至极其兄之思，下抚其幼，俾如其父之存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254458_comment'></div>暇则讲学问，择然后交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254458_comment'></div>其崎岖酸辛，皆人之所难，而子功独无难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254458_comment'></div>吾闻之，良农必躬稼，然后望其有秋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254458_comment'></div>君子必躬行，然后望其有显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254458_comment'></div>士以记问剽窃，希声利而遗行义久矣，子功其知所本哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254458_comment'></div>子功将葬其兄于秣陵，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254458_comment'></div>予感其事而惜其远也，故以序赠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1254458_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至平江，投诗谒平江知府徐琛求荐。作品：《投赠徐平江三十韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投赠徐平江三十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243440")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_243440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243440'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243440'>上圣恢方域，吴门翊帝京。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243440'>千秋季子国，百雉阖闾城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243440'>屏翰资良牧，文昌辍贰卿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243440'>龙墀虚紫橐，虎节驻红旌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243440'>河润功初洽，棠阴政已成。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243440'>农桑归恺悌，弦管乐升平。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243440'>世仰韦公誉，人高白傅名。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243440'>云楼凌月府，花岛烂蓬瀛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243440'>香雾凝春昼，桥虹卧晓晴。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243440'>清规三不惑，盛事二难并。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243440'>旧俗宁论化，重临倍有声。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243440'>向来宣使指，曾是格刑清。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243440'>自觌铜鱼拜，欣闻竹马迎。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243440'>五湖歌吹满，两郡吏民争<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243440'>严助书频赐，萧卿治欲更。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243440'>还应对宣室，俱议直承明。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243440'>鼎席犹虚位，戎亭正息兵。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243440'>安危均注意，中外等持衡。<div id='poem_sentence_17_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_243440'>补衮才猷壮，康时智略宏。<div id='poem_sentence_18_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_243440'>天津飞骥足，云路逸鹏程。<div id='poem_sentence_19_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_243440'>畴昔参宾从，顽疏荷鉴评。<div id='poem_sentence_20_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_243440'>驰驱奉刀笔，谈笑接簪缨。<div id='poem_sentence_21_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_243440'>梦结闽陬远，心惊涨潦横。<div id='poem_sentence_22_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_243440'>寄身侔困鲋，尽室逭长鲸。<div id='poem_sentence_23_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_243440'>官牒沾微禄，恩波拯再生。<div id='poem_sentence_24_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_243440'>膺门怜旧契，祢荐及难兄。<div id='poem_sentence_25_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_243440'>未释盐车驾，徒怀瓦釜鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_26_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_243440'>几年良自哂，一饱定谁营。<div id='poem_sentence_27_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_243440'>洛下裘空敝，新丰酒独倾。<div id='poem_sentence_28_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_243440'>知公行入辅，故吏敢言情。<div id='poem_sentence_29_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_243440'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_243440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_243440'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_243440_0'>⑴ 自注：公尝按刑浙右，而自明移苏。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_243440_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
建瓯
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4725bc5b8f0d4285abb8b3bdb9f59e43_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4725bc5b8f0d4285abb8b3bdb9f59e43");'><span id='4725bc5b8f0d4285abb8b3bdb9f59e43_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是春，迁居建安。作品：《南剑道中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243261' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243261' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243261?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南剑道中<span class='inlineComment2'>（甲子年作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243261")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243261_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243261'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243261'>唤渡春潭侧，堤弯踏晓晴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243261'>回舟动山影，映日见鱼行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243261'>墅远孤烟出，江深白鹭明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243261'>尘劳消底计，对此觉身轻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243261'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243261_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏大水，举家荡覆，福建提举常平茶事杜圯（受言）募人救援，幸免于难。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游福建路转运判官徐琛（献之）幕中。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9fad8eec1b9e478dbe902c89cf8d9587_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9fad8eec1b9e478dbe902c89cf8d9587");'><span id='9fad8eec1b9e478dbe902c89cf8d9587_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1160')">1158-1160年</a>，41-43岁</div><div id='9fad8eec1b9e478dbe902c89cf8d9587' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　赴知建安县任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年2月</a>　作启贺建康留守张焘除端明殿学士。作品：《贺张留守除端明启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张留守除端明启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254439")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254439'>伏审报政陪都，弁华秘殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254439_comment'></div>除音所暨，嘉物望之逾归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254439_comment'></div>诏旨甚明，知上意之攸在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254439_comment'></div>恭惟某官行高当代，道合古人，敏识洞于蓍龟，宏材屹如柱石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254439_comment'></div>长策远虑，耻为近世之规模；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254439_comment'></div>谠论忠言，凛有诤臣之风采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254439_comment'></div>一去文昌之座，屡分连帅之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254439_comment'></div>岂此居留，可淹钜用！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254439_comment'></div>果觌恩荣之异，备闻柬注之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254439_comment'></div>表里江淮，顾久烦于卧护；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254439_comment'></div>扶持宗社，将伫庆于遄归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254439_comment'></div>庶几慰斯民之瞻，岂但为今日之贺！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254439_comment'></div>某顷叨殊遇，逖远崇墉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254439_comment'></div>俛仰一官，敢叹众人之待己？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254439_comment'></div>经纶四海，尚观君子之得时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254439_comment'></div>抃蹈之情，倍越伦等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1254439_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　与客游南涧，有诗。作品：《以“秋气集南涧”为韵自赋五首》（朱墨日过眼）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span>《寒岩分韵得水字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243475' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243475' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243475?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南涧<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243475")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243475_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243475'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243475'>朱墨日过眼，溪山谁复游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243475_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243475'>夜闻西风喧，起看天地秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243475_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243475'>王事有休沐，驾言指林丘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243475_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243475'>新晴鸟乌乐，路入南涧幽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243475_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243475'>高峰左右列，野水纵横流。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243475_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243475'>问舍苦不早，求田亦良谋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243475_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243475'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_243475_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243534?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寒岩分韵得水字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243534")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243534_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243534'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243534'>青山如幽人，不肯住城市。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243534'>客从城市来，一见消吝鄙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243534'>平时与周旋，况复非俗士。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243534'>我初见南山，秀色纷可喜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243534'>谓言官尘埃，洗涤端在此。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243534'>经时未一至，引望若千里。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243534'>昨朝得休暇，佳兴难自已。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243534'>秋原丽新晴，景物为清美。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243534'>独游已不恶，更约二三子。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243534'>初从涧壑危，稍入岩石倚。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243534'>白云随杖藜，苍烟生屐齿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243534'>主翁亦好事，结茆脩竹底。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243534'>庭空百无有，屈曲但流水。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243534'>客来了不问，花草自红紫。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243534'>岂无一樽酒，欲饮还遽止。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243534'>归鞍不可速，吾亦聊洗耳。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243534'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_243534_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　白云山崇梵寺建罗汉堂，为作记。作品：《建安白云崇梵禅寺罗汉堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建安白云山崇梵禅寺罗汉堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254548")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254548'>闽之为郡八，一水之分，上下有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254548_comment'></div>下州之民习王氏，故俗奉佛惟谨，至上州，虽佛之徒未知有佛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254548_comment'></div>建炎初盗起，上州民四斗乱，四郡之境，荡为炎埃，而下州独帖然无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254548_comment'></div>因相与訾病，以为是不奉佛之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254548_comment'></div>自兵火事息，上州之民鲜不畏祸，而佛之徒颇知用其说以警惧动化其俗，凡所以奉佛者，相视出力，惟恐其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254548_comment'></div>无几何，用事者敛佛寺之馀以佐县官，由是佛之徒复睨其居如传舍然，蔑有兴事赴功之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254548_comment'></div>白云在建为望刹，异时以禅学著见号为宗师者阅数世，久敝不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254548_comment'></div>绍兴二十六年，僧惠琳主之，乃叹曰：「闽于天下，僧籍最富，今哀死殆尽，吾将制五百大士之像，使是州之民知虽无僧而有贤圣者存，岂不助吾教哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254548_comment'></div>盖左文林郎叶荐、宋颖实为之劝，二年而告备，又为尊者十八附其旁，佛之像峙其中，费金钱百万馀，辟堂而居焉，求予文为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254548_comment'></div>予笑曰：宋颖盖儒者也，儒之道不语怪以惑民，不取人以自利，今是像之设，不惑民而自利耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254548_comment'></div>宋颖曰：不然，凡吾州之民乐为之者，以其有迁善之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254548_comment'></div>琳之志所以有为者，耻其徒之安于陋而不振也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254548_comment'></div>天下之事，能不安于陋而振以有为，俾民迁善而乐为之，是岂特佛之徒也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254548_comment'></div>予于是愧其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254548_comment'></div>然予尝游天台，至石桥，爱其山林之幽深，泉石之峻洁，以求望见所谓方广寺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254548_comment'></div>而神光钟磬之异，好事者往往能道之，则五百大士之神，其庇荫于世有不可诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254548_comment'></div>宋颖今为台州从事，盍一造其地，以吾言招之，于此方之民，宜有以慰其意者矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1254548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　秋晚，范端臣（元卿）过建安，有诗赠之。作品：《戏赠范元卿》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戏赠范元卿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243423")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243423'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243423'>忆昔苕溪醉中语，屈指凄凉十寒暑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243423'>纷纭世事去如云，两鬓苍苍各如许。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243423'>春风学省数会面，抗袂吁嗟走尘土。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243423'>我惭屡战不能奇，袖手归来仆旗鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243423'>喜君射策有新功，双鹄联翩仍一举。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243423'>胡为不上金马门，簿领卑栖犹哙伍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243423'>风前未厌鹔鹴敝，笔下悬玄凤凰吐。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243423'>闽山千里要佳句，应吊双龙一怀古。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243423'>元戎好士见此客，定肃弓刀按歌舞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243423'>素英丹荔虽已过，海珍正可罗樽俎。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243423'>鹧鸪勾舟木叶堕，秋晚上寒更风雨。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243423'>请君彊饭趣归程，莫为梅花思羁旅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243423'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_243423_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年3月3日</a>　在知建安县任上。上巳日，与王仲宗、赵德温、赵仲缜、赵彥堪（任卿）宴集试诗。作品：《上巳日王仲宗、赵德温见过………》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上巳日王仲宗赵德温见过因招赵仲缜任卿小集以流水放杯行分韵得行字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年3月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243401")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243401'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243401'>春事倏已晚，飞花送啼莺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243401'>长安三月三，水边尽倾城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243401'>缅怀杜陵老，感之见歌行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243401'>青鸟忽飞去，素鳞盘水精。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243401'>往事谁复识，梦绕白玉京。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243401'>朅来官闽陬，江湖渺馀情。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243401'>嘉节闭门卧，客愁随日生。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243401'>风光入樽酒，使我嗟独倾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243401'>良友慰寂寞，惠然成会并。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243401'>金枝三隽才，千里未可程。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243401'>王郎乌衣旧，高论玉麈横。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243401'>相逢寄觞咏，乐此天气清。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243401'>不知山阴会，绝唱畴能赓。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243401'>庭隅有幽花，粲若万玉缨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243401'>好风亦知人，微月相与明。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243401'>萧萧城东路，颇复歌吹声。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243401'>景物正自佳，天涯意难平。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243401'>不须恨陈迹，且用催诗成。<div id='poem_sentence_17_243401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_243401'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_243401_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　其友任古（信孺）进殿中侍御史，致书论“台谏之风不振”作品：《与任信孺书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷13。）</span><div id='poem_1254409' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254409' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254409?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与任信孺书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254409")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254409_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254409'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254409'>比窥报命，伏承执法殿中，不任忻快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254409_comment'></div>久欲具一书为贺，效世俗作笺牍，则惧涉不情，辄以幅纸，又似太简，迟回至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254409_comment'></div>已而思之，不若以意之所欲言者，荐区区于左右，或遂少助，则其胜于寻常之礼万万也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254409_comment'></div>盖台谏之风，不振久矣，至谓中书奉行台谏风旨，十数年来，遂为宰相私人，朋奸报怨，固无足论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254409_comment'></div>自主上赫然更化，士皆亲擢，其间姓名著于中外者，亦不为鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254409_comment'></div>而某独以为不振者，诚见祖宗之时，台谏论事者为多，而弹击者为少，近世台谏弹击者为多，而论事者不特为少，乃近于绝无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254409_comment'></div>夫论事者，将以裨时政之阙失也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254409_comment'></div>弹击者，将以去朝廷之奸邪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254409_comment'></div>今于时政之阙，漫不之省，而于奸邪亦不能大有所去，姑取其失势易逐者，虚张痛诋，以买直欺世，未见其为能振也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254409_comment'></div>盖时政之阙，皆君相已行之事，言之常有拂意忤旨之患，不若弹击臣下可以掎摭细故，下及小吏，藉口而塞责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254409_comment'></div>然使人君以为时政真无阙，而朝廷真无大奸大佞，故台谏之论止于如此，则其为患可胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254409_comment'></div>且人臣论谏，而惟患拂意忤旨云者，此吾之志不坚，理之不胜尔，非必激讦斗怒然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254409_comment'></div>唐之善论谏无如魏郑公，次则陆宣公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254409_comment'></div>以郑公之遇太宗，宜其谏行言听，而德宗之猜忌，犹于宣公无不从者，盖二公之论皆委曲至当，合于人情而切于义理，人君虽欲拒之，无得而拒之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254409_comment'></div>以是观之，人臣不知论谏之道，而特以畏避为事，此孟子所谓贼其君者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254409_comment'></div>包孝肃公在仁祖朝，最为劲正敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254409_comment'></div>尝取其奏议读之，明白简易，一无虚词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254409_comment'></div>其论事则曰伏见某日指挥某事，有不可行而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254409_comment'></div>其弹奏则曰伏见某人授某官，不堪此职而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254409_comment'></div>如人家立语于父兄之前，雍容閒暇，不为缘饰，真可为后世台谏之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254409_comment'></div>下此又有一弊，以为论事失之苛细，欲俟其大者而后发，如阳道州之为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254409_comment'></div>是殆不然，前辈讥道州任谏官七年，都无所论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254409_comment'></div>幸而及裴延龄之事而去，向使止五六年而遂迁，则是终无一言，此犹责道州之浅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254409_comment'></div>夫台谏之为职，要当朝夕纳诲，以格君心之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254409_comment'></div>俾德宗预知延龄为不可相，不待于既相而欲毁其麻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254409_comment'></div>既相而欲毁其麻，则是言无所益，故决去就以为身名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254409_comment'></div>不知七年之间，所陈于人君之前者何事，所以开道启迪者何说，说之不合则宜去久矣，岂必在于相延龄一事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254409_comment'></div>凡此者，某之所欲言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254409_comment'></div>至于条具缕析，又非某所可言矣，不识执事以为然乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254409_comment'></div>窃闻主上之擢执事，得于向时登对之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254409_comment'></div>而执事近为里行，复首论水灾以广上德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254409_comment'></div>自觌除目，舆望实为惬然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254409_comment'></div>恭以素学深厚，必有所处，敢幸志其远者大者，而勿蹈近世之规，使如仆辈不复能有所言，则台谏之风指，其自执事振矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1254409_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　是春，与沈信臣游建安北苑龙焙，有次韵诗。作品：《次韵沈信臣游龙焙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243430' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243430' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243430?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵沈信臣游龙焙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243430")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243430_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243430'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243430'>武夷仙人厌尘埃，金鞭白马飞崔嵬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243430'>丹砂已就不可识，尚有瑶草分灵栽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243430'>千花剪巧缀密露，秀色不待春风催。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243430'>东溪路入三千<span id='poem_sentence_4_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243430'>苍虬绕圭龙护璧，面为铁石口琼瑰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243430'>烹煎斗水出好事，珠璎玉字相萦回。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243430'>已嗟双井甘退步，况复日注真难侪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243430'>我来窃食端为此，把玩一日三徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243430'>手𣂏清泉吊陆子，底用浊酒穷欢咍。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243430'>头风快愈春睡散，老眼尚为群书开。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243430'>知君此游更不恶，坐有纤纤时捧杯<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年8月</a>　以贺允中、樊光远荐，诏令任满赴行在。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　作凌风亭，有诗。作品：《凌风亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span>《晚登凌风亭戏作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>凌风亭<span id='poem_sentence_1_243511'>逶迤雉堞出，一水相萦带。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243511'>诛茅发颓垣，偶与嘉景会。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243511'>天风无边来，云日为破碎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243511'>谁能了蘋末，直欲跨鹏背。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243511'>飘然压尘土，九壤真一块。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243511'>王乔幸齐驱，御寇亦同载。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243511'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_243511_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243372")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_sentence_1_243372'>清谈安得如夷甫，佳句无劳发恺之。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243372'>山色倚江秋更好，烟光连市晚偏宜。<div id='poem_note_243372_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　晤友人赵彥端（德庄），有词记之。作品：《江神子》（十年此地看花时）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243577?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243577'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243577'>十年此地看花时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243090'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243090'>漫仕虽同官事殊，故人来往未全疏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243089'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243089'>吾谋不用可无人，小技文章亦有神。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243089'>一第区区儿戏耳，请君折取桂为薪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243089'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243089_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　子淲生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　春，与赵彥堪（任卿）游北苑，有次韵诗。作品：《次韵赵任卿至北苑二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243210?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵赵任卿至北苑二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243210")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243210_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243210'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243210'>行乐须春事，微官日自忙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243210'>轻云弄天色，细雨出风光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243210'>筠甲连山破，林髯夹道苍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243210'>拟寻花岛去，更待茗芽香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243210'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243210_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243209' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243209' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243209?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243209_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243209'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243209'>好雨惊连夜，疏钟喜报晨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243209'>池心春涨绿，花面晓妆匀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243209'>野渡经年别，官茶几焙新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243209'>风光为传语，何事曲江滨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243209'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243209_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='efb01b9dab9942a5b44e091e974a146c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("efb01b9dab9942a5b44e091e974a146c");'><span id='efb01b9dab9942a5b44e091e974a146c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>，43岁</div><div id='efb01b9dab9942a5b44e091e974a146c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　为仙游朱元飞（彥实）归乐堂题诗。作品：《归乐堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>归乐堂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243415")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243415_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_243415_0'>① 原按：《朱子文集》载《归乐堂记》云：予尝为吏于泉之同安，而与仙游朱彦侯实同僚。即此堂也。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243415'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243415'>百岁自逆旅，微官更周流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243415'>应知归来乐，不减万户侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243415'>渊明一县尹，折腰憎督邮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243415'>松菊绕东篱，田园事西畴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243415'>素琴酌樽酒，稚子相献酬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243415'>朱侯青云士，颇复有此不。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243415'>方为功名驱，乃与贤达侔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243415'>筑堂寄閒暇，笑谈指林丘。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243415'>蕉黄间荔丹，蚝山荐新篘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243415'>嗟我实何人，市朝亦淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243415'>因君动佳兴，拟作汗漫游。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243415'>安得二顷田，可卧百尺楼。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243415'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_243415_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　送赵彥堪（任卿）之芜湖丞任，有诗。作品：《送赵任卿芜湖丞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送赵任卿芜湖丞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243506")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243506'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243506'>青山照濡须，江驶不可渡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243506'>当年黄须儿，跨马识其处。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243506'>奸雄有遗迹，草木尚西顾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243506'>孤城千家邑，政尔横故戍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243506'>翩翩佳公子，儒雅称风度。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243506'>金门向蓬莱，曾未试阔步。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243506'>畴令一官卑，仅乃高尉簿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243506'>得非多言穷，定坐能诗故。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243506'>相从十年间，了不见喜怒。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243506'>千金第深韫，至宝可轻付。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243506'>江山落君手，判断得佳句。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243506'>谁欤招得仙，我欲起谢傅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243506'>似闻王师出，鼙鼓近营驻。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243506'>老生固常谈，愚者亦千虑。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243506'>一樽别时酒，且用慰迟暮。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243506'>去去无久留，功名有夷路。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243506'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_243506_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　四、五月间，上书参知政事贺允中，论朝廷当“亟为自治以俟恢复之机”，并献自治三策。作品：《上贺参政书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷13。）</span><div id='poem_1254407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上贺参政书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254407")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254407'>某愚不佞，荷知遇为甚异，属者弟兄皆辱论荐，内顾何人，可当厚意！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254407_comment'></div>窃闻使事之还，既已累月，不敢以寒暄无益之问上勤省览，诚不知阁下所使何事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254407_comment'></div>然自故岁天下藉口，颇以敌人为虑，朝廷施设，较之往日亦似稍为之备者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254407_comment'></div>疏逖小官，不当预闻庙堂之论，独念既齿一命，以从宦于州县，且又世受国恩，宜与社稷共休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254407_comment'></div>方时安平，固未享富贵之利，而患难或生，则亦均受其害者，私忧过计，怀不自已，辄极愚意，以陈于左右，或者所以报盛德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254407_comment'></div>盖国家越在东南垂四十年矣，自讲和之议兴，敌之结好又二十年矣，其果以和好为万世策耶，抑亦计不获已，姑欲自治而款之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254407_comment'></div>以为万世策，则自古无倚外敌而可以立国者，如欲自治而款之，则二十年之间不为不久，何尚未有发也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254407_comment'></div>昔越尝屈己而事吴矣，故曰越十年生聚，十年教训，二十年之外，吴其为沼，已而勾践之报吴，果不出二十年之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254407_comment'></div>越小国也，其壤地直今会稽数郡，故生聚、教训，必待于二十年而后可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254407_comment'></div>以我之大，二十年之久，曾不知所以报敌者，得不愧于越欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254407_comment'></div>议者徒知归咎秦桧，今桧死遂五年矣，国势之强弱视前日为几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254407_comment'></div>夫讲和之议未大失也，敌虽吾雠，然一旦许我以还母后、复梓宫、休甲兵而谓之和，亦何说以拒之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254407_comment'></div>其所失者，岁入之币始不当甚厚，以坐困吾民尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254407_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254407_comment'></div>祖宗以全盛之时，幅𢄙之大，其馈敌者未如今日之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254407_comment'></div>且前不与我和而后与我和者，是亦畏我之盛，将以图己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254407_comment'></div>彼既有畏我之心矣，盍亦少忍以持其事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254407_comment'></div>虽薄其币，和议安有不成哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254407_comment'></div>然事已往矣，天下之事有未往者，不识朝廷何以待之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254407_comment'></div>如闻敌人遇吾使命之至，必耀其兵甲，陈其车骑，以自示其强盛，且大治东都宫室，浚汴渠，力役并兴，未知信否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254407_comment'></div>夫冒顿之遇汉，惟匿其精兵，见其羸弱，使中国无所畏忌，故高帝有白登之败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254407_comment'></div>今敌乃自示其强盛，盖亦无能为者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254407_comment'></div>阿房之工未休，闾左之戍继起，足以致胜、广之盗而秦遂以亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254407_comment'></div>敌之大治宫室，力役并兴，盖已不胜其扰，天意人事，于此极矣，得无乘隙而奋者，是特迟速之间尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254407_comment'></div>虽可为朝廷贺，亦可以为忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254407_comment'></div>可为贺者，敌于此有败亡之渐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254407_comment'></div>可为忧者，大盗崛起于中原，则有倍费驱除者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254407_comment'></div>闻诸道路，去岁使人之来，其礼稍有不至，夫亦何恃而敢然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254407_comment'></div>其所需乞，又非外廷所可知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254407_comment'></div>使其果遂都汴，自汴而下，顺流鼓楫，不数日可抵四口，则淮南其可不虑耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254407_comment'></div>又汴京四通五达，本非定都之地，祖宗时，徒以东南之粟便于转漕，岁运八百万斛，然后汴京可得而都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254407_comment'></div>今其来也，势亦无所得食，万一欲以岁币少易东南之粟，不识朝廷又何以待之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254407_comment'></div>夫天下有大势有定理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254407_comment'></div>所谓定理者，曲直顺逆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254407_comment'></div>所谓大势者，当自其时而论之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254407_comment'></div>今天下之定理，我为甚直，亦为甚顺，固不必深议，至于大势，窃尝借三国为喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254407_comment'></div>三国之时，吴、蜀皆欲取魏，然魏卒不可取者，以蜀不能有吴，吴不能有蜀尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254407_comment'></div>后吴、蜀交通，而魏以为病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254407_comment'></div>今敌据有中原，势犹魏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254407_comment'></div>北尽江淮，南尽岭海，西控三巴而接汉、沔，则吴、蜀之势吾既兼之矣，反不能以取魏，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254407_comment'></div>关羽下襄阳，魏人几欲移都，今襄阳盖吾有也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254407_comment'></div>刘备得汉中，曹操始不能与之抗，其后由之出师而关辅至于响震，今汉中盖吾有也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254407_comment'></div>荆州之地，魏得之足以制吴、蜀，吴、蜀得之足以抗魏，今荆州盖吾有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254407_comment'></div>夫理与势吾皆有之，则亦何惧于彼而甘为之下！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254407_comment'></div>所未可为者，当谨俟其机尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1254407_comment'></div>曩者敌与我三京陕右，而遽以败盟，此一机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1254407_comment'></div>顺昌之捷，合诸将之力可以取汴，遽复退师，关中之大，随得而随失，不能据有一县犹之可也，厥后敌复弑立其一二官长，狼顾麇骇，未有归附，中原之民，引领南望，此又一机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1254407_comment'></div>是时兴十万师，下一纸诏，势必瓦解风靡，虽未能长驱幽、蓟，近可以得京洛，下不失削其岁币，俟其请命，而与之正君臣之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1254407_comment'></div>然大臣方以养疴而罢谋，宿将方以怙贵而苟安，返以遗敌人之资，得不为之附膺顿足流涕而太息哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1254407_comment'></div>故愿朝廷亟为自治，以俟其机，非欲无机而妄动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1254407_comment'></div>自治不过三策，一曰人，二曰兵，三曰财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1254407_comment'></div>某请先论人之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1254407_comment'></div>夫济大事必以人为本，古今不易之论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1254407_comment'></div>在上则得其财而用之，在下则得其心而用之，皆人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1254407_comment'></div>数年以来，招置人材不为不广，布之中外不为不多矣，而庶事未至振举，风俗未以大变，士风犹为阘然者，此岂无说然也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1254407_comment'></div>昔姚崇叙次郎吏而明皇不答，德宗亲择畿令而柳浑不贺，盖人君所择者辅相，辅相所择者百执事之人，此各有其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1254407_comment'></div>今也人人而荐之主上，使必亲见而后用，此殆诸公惩前日权臣专恣之过，远嫌疑之为也，欲以尽人材而惧其未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1254407_comment'></div>人君之必自用者，惟将与相耳，否则有将相之才而未试者尔，当亲见而识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1254407_comment'></div>至于一介之士，寘之列位，岂必人君之尽识欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1254407_comment'></div>且文臣以是可矣，近者所任武臣，有遂转一官、迁一职者，俟其终更而审察者，此复何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1254407_comment'></div>苟以为军帅多非其人，是不待一日而易之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1254407_comment'></div>如皆其人矣，姑欲收遗材以备缓急，则籍于密院，以次任之足矣，安有未见其功而予之官职乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1254407_comment'></div>予之官职而置于閒地乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1254407_comment'></div>徒为是虚名美观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1254407_comment'></div>至于人心，则尤不可不收者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1254407_comment'></div>急于财则民怨，吝于财则军怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1254407_comment'></div>军怨者祸速而易见，民怨者祸远而难知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1254407_comment'></div>事虽不可概举，然人心之所悦者公，所服者平，所慕者信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1254407_comment'></div>推是三者而行之，则人心得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1254407_comment'></div>其次请论兵之利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1254407_comment'></div>夫师克在和不在众，用兵斗智不斗力，非必援引古今而后见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1254407_comment'></div>国家俪于汉、唐，实以养兵为大蠹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1254407_comment'></div>自渡江以来，西北之兵萃于东南，则其蠹尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1254407_comment'></div>今西北之兵既已老矣，近所召募无非东南之人与西北士卒之子弟，而犹用西北军额以填之，是务多不务精也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1254407_comment'></div>昔者尝怪谢幼度之破苻坚，是时江左为晋已五十馀年，实用东南之兵以却大敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1254407_comment'></div>陈庆之送元颢，是时下晋又已百有馀岁，以兵七千转战魏地，破其四十万众无与抗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1254407_comment'></div>岂东南之兵果不可用耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1254407_comment'></div>顾将之何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1254407_comment'></div>且又有甚弊焉，西北军额皆系于殿前，衣粮之外，日有食钱，诸路将兵则衣粮而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1254407_comment'></div>以诸路言之，江西非无禁兵也，而驻殿前一军于章贡，福建非无禁兵也，而驻一军于漳泉，二广非无禁兵也，而驻一军于潮海，皆以弹压盗贼为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1254407_comment'></div>是逐路禁兵为不足用矣，则逐路禁兵虽阙之可也，犹复促募不已，而外复有弹压之军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1254407_comment'></div>向者禁兵与厢军为二，今又为三焉，县官安得不匮哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1254407_comment'></div>殿前之军给以经总制、上供等钱，逐路禁兵给以州县之常赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1254407_comment'></div>然殿前军所募人，与逐路禁兵何异而所给过倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1254407_comment'></div>为之计者，莫若遇殿前军有阙，选于诸州禁兵而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1254407_comment'></div>循祖宗出军旧制，更番迭戍，于弹压之所，加其粮给，用以激劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1254407_comment'></div>而以逐路弹压之军，理为逐路禁兵所缺之额，取其费以充，则经制、上供之财亦可省矣，此养兵之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1254407_comment'></div>西北之士虽老，近稍汰而出之，方州小者百许人，大者几二百人，彼虽稍释军伍之劳，而反有道路流离之苦，州郡骤添使臣数十百人，夫亦何用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1254407_comment'></div>且俸给有不可以时办者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1254407_comment'></div>此辈诚筋力不逮，然亦习熟戎事，经历艰险，岂无可用之才？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1254407_comment'></div>今近自江东淮甸，远自荆湖襄汉，皆有旷土，与其募民力田，曷若用所汰之士，给其粮具牛种而耕之，一岁之外，使得食其所入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1254407_comment'></div>积聚其众，略仿陕西城寨之法，阅习控御，以为屯田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1254407_comment'></div>因择其强干有劳者用为巡检，而命帅司州将督之，不犹愈于不釐务指使之科而坐食哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1254407_comment'></div>此汰兵之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1254407_comment'></div>朝廷往岁尝以兵权付于一二大将，收之御前，号为都统制，固远虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1254407_comment'></div>然御前都统制者，其名也，其自为一军，犹自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1254407_comment'></div>尝观祖宗所任边帅之效矣，河翔关陕十数大镇，无非宿兵之地，帅则皆用大臣，下亦两制，其将兵之官不过于副总管与钤辖、都监、正副将而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1254407_comment'></div>其后庆历、熙宁用兵，亦命文臣为宣抚，故二百年间，将帅无握兵之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1254407_comment'></div>今诸路帅司所将者州兵，而大兵所驻，则惟都统制驭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1254407_comment'></div>陪都之重莫如建康，留守之臣而都统制盖与之分庭抗礼，他州在所不论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1254407_comment'></div>近日沿淮上下，间用武臣，得为安抚，虽欲潜师为备，庙堂得不深思耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1254407_comment'></div>至于蜀道之远，与夫辇毂之近，又有久任而不易者，则非某所敢议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1254407_comment'></div>下此有财之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1254407_comment'></div>天下莫不以财为急，而某独以为后者，夫财之在民与在国，实无以异，后世掊尅之论兴，始以归之公上为富国之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1254407_comment'></div>今朝廷用度亦窘矣，诚使百姓充实，一旦有大费，虽细民瓶罂囊褚之物，歛而用之，其谁敢不从？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1254407_comment'></div>然不知大费之后，足以奠枕耶，民亦愿输而不惮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1254407_comment'></div>如其未也，安可穷民而自利哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1254407_comment'></div>且财货之目，异于承平时，固已不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1254407_comment'></div>常赋之外有总制，总制之外有经制，经制之外有和籴、有折帛、有月桩、算丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1254407_comment'></div>于僧道鬻爵，于富民贸田，于州县所未卖者度牒，未收者职租而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1254407_comment'></div>觔革羽毛、银铜盐铁，名为不得科歛，而使州县自任其谤以应上之须者，事亦不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1254407_comment'></div>虽欲复取，其又何加？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1254407_comment'></div>朝廷既知以节财为务矣，乘舆之服御，宰执之赐予，官吏之廪稍，朘损盖未已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1254407_comment'></div>然不知诸军之伪券，其果皆去耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1254407_comment'></div>置官总领，实未能覈其数，役使于道路，假借于亲旧者，日纷如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1254407_comment'></div>三衙之军，当有定额，天子之都，白昼掠人于市，刺以为军，特欲充其数耳，缓急何所用之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1254407_comment'></div>此宜密院自招刺于承旨厅，以消其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1254407_comment'></div>且诸军之粮给，皆系于总领，而所谓回易者独不隶之，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1254407_comment'></div>前日盖尝罢之矣，未几而又复之，今其言曰吾军衣粮之外，装饰泛用，皆资于回易，故人人以为不可罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1254407_comment'></div>然主将假之以为妄费者，户知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1254407_comment'></div>罢之诚未尽善，盍亦隶于总领官而权其出纳，殿司则专命版曹一官掌之，其弊将不劳而自去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1254407_comment'></div>僧道日益就少，则寺观为可并，胜于取其宽剩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1254407_comment'></div>官吏日益就少，则祠禄为可减，胜于断其权摄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1254407_comment'></div>馀则仪卫礼文，百司技艺，伶官走马之费，又有宜省而不必尽备者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1254407_comment'></div>昔周宣王不藉千亩，汉光武未尝具大驾，皆不失为中兴之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1254407_comment'></div>此盖因时损益，享实利而不为虚文者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1254407_comment'></div>朝廷今日患在好为虚文而不求实利，谓宜置官<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_126_1254407", 1254407, "Clauses/470/Comments/0")'>讲议</span>而以次更革，不待一人之言，然后改一事、罢一条也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1254407_comment'></div>窃尝深叹朝廷政令或出，不为四方之所尊信，未几果亦变易，正坐轻用人言，未尝深加<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_127_1254407", 1254407, "Clauses/477/Comments/0")'>讲议</span>故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1254407_comment'></div>试以一二明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1254407_comment'></div>递铺既已统于州县，提举于监司、巡辖于使臣矣，而逐州复以指使轮月掌之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1254407_comment'></div>弓手既已职于县尉矣，又以州兵官兼其将领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1254407_comment'></div>不知皆有益耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1254407_comment'></div>如以尉为文臣不可倚仗，参用武臣可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1254407_comment'></div>巡铺使臣为不足用，择道里远处增置其员可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1254407_comment'></div>何在一官之外，又使一官也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1254407_comment'></div>闽中近籍海船，且立赏格，俾土豪募及水手千人，则以承信郎命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1254407_comment'></div>是粮食当自备也，私家虽富，无能日赡千人之理，不知朝廷将以此警海道耶，抑以御大敌也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1254407_comment'></div>传闻敌亦渐治舟船于山东，其意叵测，沿海之备，信不可缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1254407_comment'></div>然海路从横，惟藉风势，一夕千里，若以兵斗于舟楫之上，万无决胜之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1254407_comment'></div>或值风涛，安可会合？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1254407_comment'></div>惟当聚兵要害，控扼其港口，轻舟往来，以为巡逻，严其斥堠，坚其城壁，使敌至不敢越，既越不可归，乃谋之善者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1254407_comment'></div>某以为此非土豪所募水手能办也，所募之人以御小寇或可，御大敌诚非计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1254407_comment'></div>且敌万一用师海道，盖亦掩我不备，直捣州县，以张声势，必不争利于舟楫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1254407_comment'></div>水手但知争利于舟楫，遇其冲突州县，安能舍舟楫而与之战，徒有驾舟而遁尔，不知州县孰为守哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1254407_comment'></div>凡此之类，皆望朝廷更议之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1254407_comment'></div>虽然，阁下今者位实参预，必以为上有二辅，次有右府，任不我专，故有不可尽言与不可尽为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1254407_comment'></div>然前辈如寇莱公、范文正公，皆以参预而行大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1254407_comment'></div>当是之时，人主不疑，同列不忌，终于共济国事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1254407_comment'></div>其后王安石、吕惠卿之为参预，始以制置三司而侵宰相之权，惠卿复欲攘安石之位，故近者多以是为嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1254407_comment'></div>夫如安石、惠卿之为参预则不可，如莱公、文正之为参预则亦何所不可哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1254407_comment'></div>侧闻圣上恭己，委任大臣，实无有间，而诸公同寅协恭之效，道侔志合，非有前日专制忌克之风，阁下于此而云不可为与不可言，非某所喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1254407_comment'></div>今日之事，如救焚拯溺然，一日不图则贻患日深，阁下幸而言之与幸而为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1254407_comment'></div>而果不可也，则当引去山林，以全往年挂冠之美，无为久孤贤士大夫之望而不决也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1254407_comment'></div>昔鲁使乐正克为政，而孟子以为好善优于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1254407_comment'></div>卫之诸臣好善，故贤者乐告以善道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1254407_comment'></div>某之庸陋，不敢自附于贤者，而明公之好善实过于乐正，是以仰恃深眷，喋喋于兹，恭惟恕其狂妄，少加听察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1254407_comment'></div>如有可取一二，冀施行之，非某之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1254407_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_157_1254407_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年8月</a>　贺允中致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年9月</a>　九月己丑，范如圭（伯达）卒，有挽词。作品：《范泉州挽词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>范泉州挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243255")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243255'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243255'>淡墨标名早，飞腾仅石渠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243255'>学传外家蕴，论合古人馀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243255'>议本枫宸疏，评和相第书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243255'>忠言与危行，青史未应虚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243255'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243255_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243254' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243254' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243254?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243254_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243254'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243254'>玉节江南道，铜符海上州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243254'>登车人自化，截镫士争留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243254'>不作田园计，长怀世事忧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243254'>秋风闭黄壤，谁为子孙谋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243254'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243254_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年12月</a>　建安县丞厅修葺竣工，为作题名记。作品：《建安县丞厅题名记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建安县丞厅题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254569")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254569'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254569'>古者辅相之任曰丞，百司九列之贰或曰丞，而郡县之副其长者亦曰丞，盖丞之名将以翊其上而丞之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254569_comment'></div>郡丞秩稍高，下统掾曹，体亦有间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254569_comment'></div>至县，则事无大细，悉关丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254569_comment'></div>然长或能，率其权不以予丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254569_comment'></div>丞或才，复擅其权不以事长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254569_comment'></div>苟异是，则必退避畏缩，而举听于丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254569_comment'></div>远嫌绝疑，漫不助其长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254569_comment'></div>之二者均失矣，岂设官共治之意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254569_comment'></div>莆阳林智可之丞于建安也，而某滥为之长，凡邑之事，智可不遗馀力以助吾，盖更听迭议，必至于济而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254569_comment'></div>由是相与欢甚，脱去畦畛，无区区世俗之病，故建安虽号剧，以某之懦而无讥焉者，智可之赖为多焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254569_comment'></div>智可以其暇日，整治其庭庑，筑室于南端新城扉之楼，以为临观燕息之所，既又集建炎以来丞之名氏于壁，属某为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254569_comment'></div>故为道丞之设、吾二人相与之好，以愧夫世俗之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254569_comment'></div>智可尝为德化令，治有声矣，屈为丞，盖不卑其官如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254569_comment'></div>吾是以等而上之，其知所以共治者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254569_comment'></div>绍兴三年十二月旦，颍川韩某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1254569_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　丞廨作一堂，以“真清”命之，赋诗其上。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e6109ec0685645be9ea1ece8c2c96a1d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e6109ec0685645be9ea1ece8c2c96a1d");'><span id='e6109ec0685645be9ea1ece8c2c96a1d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1176')">1175-1176年</a>，58-59岁</div><div id='e6109ec0685645be9ea1ece8c2c96a1d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年1月</a>　年初，起程赴建宁府任。过武夷山，有诗记之。作品：《过武夷》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243227' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243227' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243227?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过武夷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243227")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243227_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243227'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243227'>不到仙山二十年，道人双鬓亦皤然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243227'>却看翠岭千寻石，又汎清溪九曲船。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243227'>目极已高聊自喜，身轻欲上可无缘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243227'>只应猿鹤遥相认，笑我归耕未有田。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243227'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243227_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　至郡，上到任表。作品：《知建宁府到任表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254309' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254309' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254309?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知建宁府到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254309")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254309_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254309'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254309'>沥恳吁天，莫遂请閒之愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254309_comment'></div>疏恩易地，仍叨共理之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254309_comment'></div>优假至深，凌兢罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254309_comment'></div>伏念臣奋身疏远，遭世盛明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254309_comment'></div>入参侍从之华，每蒙异眷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254309_comment'></div>出领藩宣之寄，曾乏微庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254309_comment'></div>况岁月之仅周，积过愆而靡逭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254309_comment'></div>孤踪易毁，宁分近甸之忧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254309_comment'></div>全度兼容，特畀潜藩之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254309_comment'></div>眷兹建水，实控闽陬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254309_comment'></div>代籍初基，觉溪山之改观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254309_comment'></div>宦游寖老，慨民社之常临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254309_comment'></div>虽驰驱颇愧于壮年，然委付有光于前日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254309_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下惠绥群献，明烛高微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254309_comment'></div>器使人才，举绝重轻之弊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254309_comment'></div>衡持天下，悉无内外之殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254309_comment'></div>不遗管蒯之微，尚费乾坤之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254309_comment'></div>轸其迂钝，锡以便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254309_comment'></div>臣敢不仰体曲成，益思尽瘁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254309_comment'></div>土风末俗，犹粗识其二三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254309_comment'></div>利泽深仁，或布宣于万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254309_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1254309_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　春耕伊始，即行劝农。作品：《建宁府劝农文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建宁府劝农文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254390")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254390'>建宁之境，地狭而民贫，民之力农盖有不待劝者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254390_comment'></div>然太守昔忝邑令于此，去之十五年矣，圣天子以为知此邦风俗之旧，复以千里付之，其出郊而见父老，不敢但循故事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254390_comment'></div>盖闻往岁旱荒，七邑之民，甚阙于食，至掘草木之根以度朝夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254390_comment'></div>游手末作，颇不务本，往往冒法禁，贩茶盐，十百为群，以自取罪犯而负逐利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254390_comment'></div>又多费良田，以种瓜植蔗，其可耕之地，类皆崎岖崖谷间，岁有所收，不偿所费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254390_comment'></div>一至饥馑，则强梁啸聚，迫胁上户以收籴禾米，类皆弗靖，足为乡闾之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254390_comment'></div>父老其为太守戒训后生，后生务遵农业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254390_comment'></div>今造茶夫云集，逮其将散，富家大室，亦宜招集房客，假之种粮，以多耕荒废之壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254390_comment'></div>高者种粟，低者种豆，有水源者艺稻，无水源者播麦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254390_comment'></div>但使五谷四时有收，则可足食而无凶年之患，以少变此邦之俗，实太守所望于父老，亦圣天子委付于太守之意也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1254390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年5月12日</a>　生日，赋词感怀。作品：《醉落魄·乙未自寿》（红蕖漾月）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋词》页1403。）</span><div id='poem_243629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_1_243629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243629'>一年风月今宵别。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243629'>隐隐笙鸾，何处有炎热。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243629_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243629'>凤凰山下榴花发。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243629'>幔亭有路通瑶阙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243629'>知我丹成，容我醉时节。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254594'>凤之阳，鹤之麓，有岏而伏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254594_comment'></div>堂之坳，圃之腹，斯瀵而沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254594_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年8月</a>　八月壬午，跋范端臣（元卿）所藏欧阳修帖。作品：《跋范元卿所藏欧阳公帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254483?labeling=true'
