"poem_title_1254483")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254483'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254483'>文忠公手墨，世固多有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254483_comment'></div>二帖盖与原甫、君谟，皆平日至厚，周致委曲，情如家人，足以见前辈交友之谊为可宝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254483_comment'></div>称谢原甫，戒其用快，而颇讥其豪饮不可当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254483_comment'></div>劝君谟以疮愈当治内，犹寇贼后修武备，所以御后来之患，而自谓各有少病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254483_comment'></div>其为药石之言，互相启发，又可宝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254483_comment'></div>淳熙二年八月壬午，颍川韩某敬观。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1254483_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年8月</a>　应诏与漕臣傅自得（安道）等荐举崇安知县王齐舆、建阳知县黄中立。作品：《荐崇安、建阳两知县状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254347' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254347' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254347?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荐崇安建阳两知县状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254347")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254347_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254347'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254347'>具位检准淳熙元年八月二十三日敕，臣僚上言，命监司郡守精察所部县令留意民事，政有实迹，公共论荐，三省同奉圣旨依奏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254347_comment'></div>右，臣等照对本府诸县内，崇安、建阳最为冲要，民顽吏猾，前后知县持身不谨，驭下无术，少有终任不致诉讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254347_comment'></div>其间留意民事，政有实迹，应得前项指挥者，臣等不敢隐默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254347_comment'></div>臣伏见承事郎、知崇安县事王齐舆，遇事明敏，律己廉恪，断决讼牒，无不中理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254347_comment'></div>本路州县皆重盐纲，以为岁计，齐舆自到任，搬运盐纲，措置出卖，深村穷乡，皆卖官盐，而劝谕有方，略无科扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254347_comment'></div>发纳本府窠名及诸司钱物，悉皆了办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254347_comment'></div>募到上户兴修水利，开成星王陂堰，灌溉民田四千馀亩，皆是众户乐然，雇夫不曾费用分文官钱及强有敷歛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254347_comment'></div>又伏见奉议郎、知建阳事黄中立，临政宽和而事皆无阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254347_comment'></div>禁制盗贼，摧抑健讼，了纳前官欠负，桩办逐岁支费，计置钱本，搬运盐纲，小大并举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254347_comment'></div>本路诸州军今年起发禁军、土兵无不经由本县，中立去替有日，而能预备钱粮，批请券食，日有支费，百色应办，悉无科扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254347_comment'></div>其王齐舆、黄中立二人委有上件政绩，在任满替，并无绾系不了事件。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254347_comment'></div>臣某谬叨郡寄，稽考并皆诣实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254347_comment'></div>臣自得，系前知建宁府事，今来复领漕计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254347_comment'></div>臣俦，系在本府置司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254347_comment'></div>公共审究，备见不诬，敢具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254347_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，特赐旌擢，以为能吏之劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254347_comment'></div>如逐人后犯入己赃，臣等并甘同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254347_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1254347_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　赵蕃（昌父）有诗寄来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年7月4日</a>　其友赵彥（德庄）卒，为文祭之，并志其墓。作品：《祭赵德庄文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭赵德庄文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年7月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254656")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254656'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254656'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254656_comment'></div>德庄为时俊人，吾之迂疏，固无得而友也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254656_comment'></div>惟其平生博取而汎爱，然臭味之同，宜莫如吾之久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254656_comment'></div>忆相遇于建水之滨，岁行甲子与乙丑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254656_comment'></div>相与评文论诗，极当世之妍丑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254656_comment'></div>间掀髯而一笑，餐锦绣与琼玖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254656_comment'></div>我将官于龙渊，君奉檄于传舍，闭关而饮，曾不计其升斗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254656_comment'></div>时各年少而气壮，谓功名可以立取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254656_comment'></div>其后为别数年，辄又一见，慨相顾已白首也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254656_comment'></div>并游建礼之门，分处中台之掾，方群惊而四驰，誓各固其所守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254656_comment'></div>众狺狺而共嫉，几悉堕于虎口也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254656_comment'></div>既皆避而引去，去而复归，其何所怨而奚归咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254656_comment'></div>独出处之幸同，周旋一世，视富贵于何有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254656_comment'></div>方君列于奉常，谓当在文字之职，继常、扬而袭韩、柳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254656_comment'></div>迄有蕴而未尽，况可几于大受也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254656_comment'></div>嗟君去之既遽，而我用之亦偶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254656_comment'></div>少我数年，谓宜寿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254656_comment'></div>岂期奄忽而遽逝，曩时之约铭墓之文，果出于吾手也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254656_comment'></div>二妾茕然，一子甚弱，君意之不如，信八九也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254656_comment'></div>于越之人，思君之爱未忘，今遂葬焉，是亦为其不朽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254656_comment'></div>平时交游，在亡者半，或相视而莫顾，岂必较其薄厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254656_comment'></div>葬不得临其穴，病不得问其牖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254656_comment'></div>死生见于交情，吾于此而则否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254656_comment'></div>孰知吾哀，荐一觞而致三韭也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254656_comment'></div>呜呼德庄，其尚饮此酒也！</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1254656_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年7月4日</a>　其友赵彥端卒，为文祭之，并志其墓。作品：《直宝文阁赵公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷21。）</span><div id='poem_1254622' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254622' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254622?labeling=true' target='_blank'>直宝文阁赵公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年7月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254622")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254622_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254622'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254622'>吾友赵德庄将葬于饶州馀干县某山之原，其婿方友陵以状来曰：盍为之铭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254622_comment'></div>始与德庄游，盖三十年，在朝廷同曹，在外同事，犹兄弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254622_comment'></div>一日道前辈相约志墓事，德庄忽曰：某死，幸子铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254622_comment'></div>呜呼，德庄竟先往矣，予何辞焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254622_comment'></div>予为建宁，后德庄才数年，方治郡圃一堂，德庄诺为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254622_comment'></div>闻其已病，将治书问之，则讣已及门矣，其尚忍铭！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254622_comment'></div>盖德庄，吾宋之贤宗室也，在士大夫亦曰贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254622_comment'></div>力学能文，风度洒落，词辩纚纚不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254622_comment'></div>遇樽酒谈笑，掀髯抵掌，一坐尽倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254622_comment'></div>然持身严甚，非其交不往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254622_comment'></div>当议论是非曲直之际，嶷嶷不可屈，虽坑阱在前弗顾，钟鼎探手可得，不能诱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254622_comment'></div>既受知圣主，亦且用矣，邅如于外，不得尽其才而没，岂命也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254622_comment'></div>德庄讳彦端，德庄其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254622_comment'></div>于宣祖皇帝为八世孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254622_comment'></div>曾祖讳叔邯，赠广德军节度使，封淮阳侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254622_comment'></div>祖讳泽之，赠右朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254622_comment'></div>考讳公旦，终左朝奉郎、知建昌军南城县，赠左中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254622_comment'></div>妣某氏，赠令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254622_comment'></div>德庄年十七应进士举，南城亦锁其厅试进士，父子俱为国子监第一，遂同登绍兴八年礼部第，主临安府钱塘县簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254622_comment'></div>公卿贵人争识之，声名籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254622_comment'></div>为建州观察推官，丁外艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254622_comment'></div>释服，得军事判官于秀州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254622_comment'></div>守不任事，德庄率为之区处，不自以能称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254622_comment'></div>用荐者改左宣教郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254622_comment'></div>有以德庄之文达宰相父子，欲用为中都官者，德庄惧而归，其人果败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254622_comment'></div>从吏部选，知饶州馀干县，为政简易而办治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254622_comment'></div>故德庄谋居邑中，而邑人至今称之，曰吾旧宰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254622_comment'></div>充福建路提点刑狱司干办公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254622_comment'></div>近臣荐所知宗室，隆兴改元，召对，上迎谓曰：「闻卿俊才久矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254622_comment'></div>时王师北伐还，德庄则曰：「臣宗室也，与国家尤共休戚，言敢不尽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254622_comment'></div>前日议者恶人异己，故近臣有不得尽其谋，远臣有不敢进其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254622_comment'></div>如无近者一战之悔，则将赞陛下以群言为可废矣，愿深为他日戒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254622_comment'></div>除国子监丞，迁吏部员外郎，言：「元丰初节度至观察使才八员，今乃四十员；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254622_comment'></div>防御至刺史才二十员，今乃二百员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254622_comment'></div>乞重名器，抑侥倖」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254622_comment'></div>又言：「本朝以兵为国，宜汰厢军以益禁兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254622_comment'></div>宗室孤遗女恩所不及无肯娶者，请听其夫得就转运司试以优之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254622_comment'></div>权枢密院检详诸房文字，会参知政事叶公去位，有阴谓为党者，德庄曰：「吾何党哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254622_comment'></div>党于是而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254622_comment'></div>即请外除，知江州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254622_comment'></div>不数月，召为检详文字，迁右司员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254622_comment'></div>而叶公既相，德庄为言人材巨细，可用不可用，大抵称人之善，以助朝廷之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254622_comment'></div>始德庄父子甚贫，客四方，祖妣与其昆弟及妻子丧，皆藁葬未厝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254622_comment'></div>德庄曰：「吾得去毕此幸矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254622_comment'></div>既诸公留之不可，除直显谟阁，为江南东路计度转运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1254622_comment'></div>即冒大雪走馀干，毕葬而后还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1254622_comment'></div>朝廷增修边备，与予同论江淮事宜及所俘去留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1254622_comment'></div>上批纸尾，俾与大将议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1254622_comment'></div>饶、信州大饥，民强籴为暴，官廪不继，德庄行部，请留二州上供米各三万斛赈粜，自是岁以为常，民以不病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1254622_comment'></div>移福建路计度转运副使，过阙，请久任淮南郡守，休兴筑以安边民，乞放池州被水人户夏税，故徽州折帛钱俾输本色，皆极一路利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1254622_comment'></div>上遣中贵人谕旨，留为左司郎中，假户部尚书馆伴大金贺正使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1254622_comment'></div>前是宗室无出疆为伴使者，自德庄始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1254622_comment'></div>迁太常少卿，复丐外，除直宝文阁、知建宁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1254622_comment'></div>德庄旧悉其俗，民以便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1254622_comment'></div>岁馀治仓廪，亭馆一新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1254622_comment'></div>因严不举子令，且曰：「毋俾民畏，当有以利之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1254622_comment'></div>乃乞下户生子给米一斛，与钱千，及蠲其身丁，凡万四千缗，而以府用之钱偿县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1254622_comment'></div>宰相见其奏，叹曰：赵君平日不吾同，此议何可遏也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1254622_comment'></div>遂著为一路法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1254622_comment'></div>改提点浙东路刑狱，坐衢州账历稽期削两秩，德庄恬弗辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1254622_comment'></div>以小疾，得主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1254622_comment'></div>馀干号佳山水，所居最胜，日与宾客觞咏自怡，好事者以为有旷达之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1254622_comment'></div>德庄在朝时，每欲用为文字之职，讫不得用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1254622_comment'></div>闻其诗词一出，人嗜之往往如啖美味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1254622_comment'></div>然宗戚贵游欲以图画纳禁廷，祈为题赋者，率谢不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1254622_comment'></div>其掾宰府，尽言无所逊避，以是多忤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1254622_comment'></div>与人交坦然，不事畦畛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1254622_comment'></div>其为县务宽其民，其为郡务假其属邑，其为部使者则郡之细故亦不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1254622_comment'></div>喜为义事，重然诺，遇所施与，不顾家有无，亲故客之经年不厌，其田园屋宅之计如不闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1254622_comment'></div>官至朝奉大夫，享五十有五岁，卒以淳熙二年七月四日，葬以是年某月某甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1254622_comment'></div>先娶曾氏，继室李氏，赠封皆宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1254622_comment'></div>一男子，良夫，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1254622_comment'></div>二女，一嫁同年进士秘书省正字方翥之子，即友陵也，一尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1254622_comment'></div>其所为文，类之为十卷，自号《介庵居士集》云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1254622_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_1254622'>汉诸王裔，鲜克蹈义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1254622_comment'></div>惟向与歆，父子同著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1254622_comment'></div>于赫宋宗，仕于四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1254622_comment'></div>有才有良，文艺益彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1254622_comment'></div>德庄父子，声誉则伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1254622_comment'></div>南城弗施，盖在其嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1254622_comment'></div>主实遇圣，知其隽名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1254622_comment'></div>正色委蛇，首于列卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1254622_comment'></div>人则爱之，其用弗究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1254622_comment'></div>天胡啬之，而弗俾寿！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1254622_comment'></div>于越之滨，德庄所安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1254622_comment'></div>没又葬焉，宜千万年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_85_1254622_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　周必大（子充）来书，相商救助亡友赵彥端（德庄）之家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　与客登丹青阁，赋诗。作品：《丹青阁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丹青阁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243406")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243406'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243406'>杰阁跨虚壑，危栏转层峰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243406'>城郭丽朝晖，山水涵秋容。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243406'>幽寻适暇日，况有佳客从。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243406'>微官厌趋走，野性便疏慵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243406'>少摅泉石愿，一洗尘埃胸。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243406'>却上陆羽亭，褰裳踏风松。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243406'>东轩俯乔木，高花烂芙蓉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243406'>感此节物换，愧尔樵渔踪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243406'>清谈且萧散，酌饮亦时供。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243406'>兴阑勿遽叹，胜游当复重。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243406'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_243406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　刻《许昌唱和集》，作跋。作品：《书〈许昌唱和集〉后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书许昌唱和集后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254496")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254496'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254496'>叶公为许昌时，先大父贰府事，相得欢甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254496_comment'></div>大父以绍圣改元登第，对策廷中，有「宜虑未形之祸」之言，由是连蹇不得用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254496_comment'></div>建中靖国初，几用复已，凡四为郡倅，秩满辄丐宫祠，遂自许昌得请洞霄，以就休致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254496_comment'></div>平生喜赋诗，一时士大夫之所推重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254496_comment'></div>故晁景迂公以谓远则似谢康乐，近则似韦苏州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254496_comment'></div>中更乱离，家藏无复有者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254496_comment'></div>绍兴甲子岁，某见叶公于福唐，首问诗集在亡，抵掌慨叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254496_comment'></div>且曰昔与许昌诸公唱酬甚多，许人类以成编，他日当授子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254496_comment'></div>其后见公石林，得之以归，又三十馀年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254496_comment'></div>今年某叨守建安，苏岘叔子为市舶使者，会于郡斋，相与道乡闾人物之伟，因出此集披玩，始议刻之，盖叔子父祖诸诗亦多在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254496_comment'></div>箕颍隔绝，故家沦落殆尽，典型未远，其交好之美，文采风流之盛，犹可概见于此云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254496_comment'></div>淳熙二年九月，具位韩某<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1254496", 1254496, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>谨书</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1254496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年闰9月9日</a>　闰九月九日，赋词感怀。作品：《西江月·闰重阳》（一度难逢佳节）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西江月<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>闰重阳</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年闰9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243578")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243578'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243578'>一度难逢佳节，今年两度重阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243578'>菊花犹折御衣黄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243578'>莫惜危亭更上。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243578_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243578'>况有飞觞滟玉，从教醉帽吹香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243578'>兴来相与共清狂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243578'>频把新词细唱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_243578_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年闰9月</a>　手校《大戴礼记》，闰九月付刻，自为跋。作品：《大戴礼记跋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》拾遗。）</span><div id='poem_1254506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大戴礼记跋<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙二年闰九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年闰9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254506")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254506'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254506'>右《大戴礼》十三卷，总四十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254506_comment'></div>《隋志》所载亦十三卷，而《夏小正》别为卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254506_comment'></div>《唐志》但云十三卷，而无《夏小正》之别矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254506_comment'></div>《崇文总目》则十卷，而云三十五篇，无诸本可正定也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254506_comment'></div>盖自汉兴，得先儒所记礼书凡二百四篇，戴德删之为八十五篇，谓之《大戴礼》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254506_comment'></div>戴圣又删德之书为四十九篇，谓之《小戴礼》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254506_comment'></div>今立之学官者，小戴书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254506_comment'></div>然《大戴》篇始三十九，终八十一，当为四十三篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254506_comment'></div>中间缺者四篇，而重出者一篇<span class='inlineComment2'>（两篇七十三。）</span>，其上不见者犹三十八篇，复不能合于八十五篇之数，岂但当为八十一耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254506_comment'></div>其缺者或既逸，其不见者抑圣所取者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254506_comment'></div>然《哀公问》、《投壶》三篇，与小戴书无甚异，《礼察》篇与《经解》亦同，《曾子大孝》篇与《祭义》相似，则圣已取之篇，岂其文无所删者也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254506_comment'></div>《劝学》、《礼三本》见于荀卿子，至取舍之说及保傅则见于贾谊疏，间与经子同者，尚多有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254506_comment'></div>按《儒林传》，德事孝宣，尝为信都太傅，圣则为九江太守，今德书乃题九江太守，未知何所据也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254506_comment'></div>大抵汉儒所传，皆出于七十子之徒，后之学者仅习《小戴记》，不知大戴书多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254506_comment'></div>其探索阴阳，穷析物理，推本性命，杂言礼乐之辨、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1254506", 1254506, "Clauses/50/Comments/1")'>器数</span>之详，必有自来，以是知圣门之学无不备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254506_comment'></div>予家旧传此书，尝得范太史家一本校之，篇卷悉同，其讹缺谬误则不敢改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254506_comment'></div>益惧其寖久而传又加舛也，乃刊置建安郡斋，庶可考焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254506_comment'></div>淳熙乙未岁后九月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1254506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1254506'><span class='label'>按：</span>《大戴礼》卷末，明刊本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1254506_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年闰9月28日</a>　是年，两浙、福建、江东起发禁军士兵教阅，以人数多寡“参酌推赏”。闰九月二十八日，诏予元吉特转一官。元吉以“津置起发，守臣职也”，滥加赏赐，则启守臣“希觊之心”，辞之。作品：《辞起军转官状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254337' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254337' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254337?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞起军转官状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年闰9月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254337")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254337_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254337'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254337'>臣伏睹进奏院报，闰九月二十八日，枢密院奏两浙、福建、江东路诸州军起发禁军士兵，赴逐处教阅，守臣以人数多寡参酌推赏，数内臣系奉圣旨特转一官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254337_comment'></div>臣钦奉恩命，惊惧无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254337_comment'></div>窃惟国朝军制之密，凡曰禁兵，虽募于方州而皆籍于右府，故守臣号为知其军事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254337_comment'></div>是州郡之兵，实环卫之旅寓粮者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254337_comment'></div>圣神御宇，属意武事，近年以来，又命选择，日加练阅，纪律明备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254337_comment'></div>虎符既下，津置起发，守臣职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254337_comment'></div>道途无虞，部押之官，盖受赏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254337_comment'></div>圣恩优厚，并及臣等，顾臣何功之有，遽此侥冒！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254337_comment'></div>况昨降指挥，止俟春暖，类当发还，若一二年间再或戍役，则为守者动有希觊之心，臣恐自尔赏过乎与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254337_comment'></div>方陛下综覈名实，大明黜陟之秋，如臣守州，叨备侍从，义当体国，内省无庸，岂敢虚受？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254337_comment'></div>兼臣昨因降秩，岁月未满，骤有迁转，尤不遑安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254337_comment'></div>欲望圣慈，留此以励军中效命之士，推此以待天下立功之人，则臣区区愚忠，受赐一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254337_comment'></div>所有臣特转一官恩命，乞不施行，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254337_comment'></div>干冒宸严，臣无任瞻天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254337_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1254337_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年12月</a>　年底，以疾乞宫观。作品：《建宁府乞宫观札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254367' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254367' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254367?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建宁府乞宫观劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254367")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254367_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254367'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254367'>臣辄沥愚悃，仰干天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254367_comment'></div>伏念臣赋才短拙，禀性疏直，蒙陛下特达之知，擢寘从班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254367_comment'></div>既乏丝毫之补，祗荷厚恩，二年之间，叨守两部，自婺易建，曲示保全，天地父母之施益隆，臣罄竭驽钝，未知报塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254367_comment'></div>缘臣忧患之馀，目力顿昏，素苦怔忪之疾，心力不逮，潜藩重地，非所久安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254367_comment'></div>幸今郡境年谷丰登，奸盗警戢，汰军散吏，俸给以时，上供钱物，不曾亏滞，非有规避之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254367_comment'></div>欲望圣慈矜怜病瘁，除在外宫观一次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254367_comment'></div>俾臣少就閒秩，休养筋骸，庶几他日尚可复被使令之末，臣不胜万幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254367_comment'></div>冒渎宸严，无任恐惧战慄之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254367_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1254367_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　周必大（子充）来书，告以乞宫祠不允，并商及刊刻叶梦得文集事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年1月16日</a>　携家人登凌风亭。作品：《凌风亭题字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254579?labeling=true' target='_blank'>凌风亭题字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年1月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254579")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254579'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254579'>予昨以绍兴戊寅岁来宰建安，逮兹假守，今年上元后一日，始得携家登凌风亭，作此以示知县赵伟文，盖恍然辽鹤之游也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254579_comment'></div>淳熙丙申，颍川韩元吉题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1254579_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年2月</a>　汪应辰（圣锡）卒，有挽词。作品：《故端明尚书汪公挽词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故端明尚书汪公挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243278")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243278_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243278'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243278'>未冠登华选，高文动汉廷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243278'>持身严矩席，虑世炳丹青。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243278'>庶府咨沿革，诸儒见典型。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243278'>空嗟廊庙略，不上鼎彝铭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243278'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243278_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243277' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243277' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243277?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243277_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243277'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243277'>献纳高门地，君王识履声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243277_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243277'>闽山歌惠政，蜀道憺威名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243277_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243277'>逝矣嗟天命，谁欤总国成。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243277_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243277'>弟兄无六十，殄瘁亦堪惊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243277_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243277'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243277_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　有旨召赴行在，上辞状。作品：《辞召赴行在状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254336' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254336?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞召赴行在状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254336")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254336'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254336'>右，臣今月十一日准尚书省劄子，正月十七日三省同奉圣旨，臣某召赴行在者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254336_comment'></div>臣钦闻严命，悚惧无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254336_comment'></div>伏念臣资性疏直，学识浅陋，荷陛下拔于众人之中，躐寘从班，曾不能效尺寸之功，图报圣恩于万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254336_comment'></div>昨者出守辅郡，继移闽峤，二年之间，罔有善政，惟知奉行法令，未至旷瘝而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254336_comment'></div>然臣齿发寖衰，心志不逮，比常冒贡危衷，祈就閒散，天听高远，尚閟俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254336_comment'></div>方欲少俟两月，再伸诚恳，敢意遽蒙收召，俾觐阙廷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254336_comment'></div>仰惟圣神念旧，未忍弃捐，在于愚分，实深惊愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254336_comment'></div>伏愿皇帝陛下察臣癯瘁，戒在贪荣，怜臣朴忠，非有避事，敷求名德之彦，使造内朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254336_comment'></div>检会臣前来奏请，畀臣在外宫祠一次，下以全微臣易退之私义，上以副睿主难才之公心，臣则万幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254336_comment'></div>臣除已将建宁府事交割以与次官，一面起发前去信衢州以来听候指挥外，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1254336_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　行前，应父老之请，再为文劝农。作品：《又劝农文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　有诗留别傅自得。作品：《留别傅安道》二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留别傅安道<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243351")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243351'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243351'>华发相看四十年，饱谙世事欲忘言。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243351'>一春离别当寒食，再岁追随作上元。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243351'>湖外溪山明小槛，雨馀花柳暗西园。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243351'>极知老大交朋少，相与论文更一樽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243351'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243351_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243350?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243350'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243350'>场屋俱为拜赐师，烟霄独喜凤毛飞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243350'>壮心似铁何曾老，健笔如椽合一挥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243350'>北渚青山劳我梦，西垣红药待君归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243350'>诏环不作经时隔，沙路薰风卷绣衣<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《南涧甲乙稿》卷四）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243350'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243350_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: -----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0d6c817304394600b000c2be99f54693_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0d6c817304394600b000c2be99f54693");'><span id='0d6c817304394600b000c2be99f54693_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>，27岁</div><div id='0d6c817304394600b000c2be99f54693' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>谒福建安抚使兼知福州叶梦得（少蕴），作《万象亭赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_1254272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254272?labeling=true' target='_blank'>万象亭赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254272")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254272'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254272'>绍兴十有三年，石林先生自建康留钥移帅长乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254272_comment'></div>惟公以文章道学伯天下，推其绪馀，见于政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254272_comment'></div>时闽人岁饥，馀盗且扰，曾未易岁，既怀且威，仓廪羡赢，野无燧烟，民饱而歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254272_comment'></div>乃辟府治燕寝后，筑台建亭，尽揽四山之胜，字曰「万象」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254272_comment'></div>公时以宴閒临之，命宾客觞酒赋诗，以纪一时之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254272_comment'></div>某适以旧契之末，获拜公于庭，知邦人之德公而公之能与共乐也，退而为之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254272_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1254272'>石林先生治闽之初，邦人咏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254272_comment'></div>延览登眺，临城之阿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254272_comment'></div>面长江之回旋，俯重峤之嵯峨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254272_comment'></div>剪凡草于荆杞，发层台之新基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254272_comment'></div>收揽宇宙，以万象而目之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254272_comment'></div>先生曰天地之内，所谓景与物者，不可以既也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254272_comment'></div>方其交于吾前，而其象无穷，触于吾心，而其意无穷，惟达者可以道会而不可以知通矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254272_comment'></div>斯亭也，处于户庭重复之末，而出于阛阓胶扰之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254272_comment'></div>危梯直上，十寻倚空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254272_comment'></div>窥井邑之鳞次，张九衢之飞尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254272_comment'></div>嚣声四起，人烟缤纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254272_comment'></div>励丝竹之馀响，郁椒兰之清芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254272_comment'></div>当其连山如环，秀色四出，林峦郁其映带，烟云度而髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254272_comment'></div>阴晴变态，所获非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254272_comment'></div>极东南而凝睇，莽游目于穷发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254272_comment'></div>海波荡漾，蛟龙惊獝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254272_comment'></div>粲朝日之初升，数山川于异域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254272_comment'></div>飓风角于天际，卷千帆之飘忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254272_comment'></div>或一瞬而千里，或穷年于咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254272_comment'></div>瞻云鹏之独运，哀斥鴳之短翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254272_comment'></div>天池倏其九万，羌决起于蒿藾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254272_comment'></div>白鸥去而西飞，澹长烟之远没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254272_comment'></div>田畴俯见，禾黍如绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254272_comment'></div>耕夫耦而长谣，牛羊散于砂碛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254272_comment'></div>馀霞被于林杪，明月皎其东壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254272_comment'></div>挂北斗于栏楯，泻银汉于雉堞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254272_comment'></div>披风露之冷爽，想飞仙之来接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254272_comment'></div>听鸡犬于云中，奏笙簧之激越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254272_comment'></div>叹佳赏之奚尽，虽妙意其莫述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254272_comment'></div>惟吾兴之所寓，与彼物而所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254272_comment'></div>故可以追阆风之游，而谢华胥之国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254272_comment'></div>客有闻而叹曰，嗟嗟先生，百代之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254272_comment'></div>玉堂金马，载蜚厥声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254272_comment'></div>厌帝所之钧天，歛光芒于一藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254272_comment'></div>而馀风所被，犹足以息潢池之盗而庆高廪之丰年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254272_comment'></div>今夫此邦之形势，最于八州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254272_comment'></div>缭周垣其百里，渺澄澜而为沟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254272_comment'></div>三峰峙而鼎足，盖有类夫蓬莱与瀛洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254272_comment'></div>自无诸迄今，千有馀载，中更王氏，穷侈自泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1254272_comment'></div>异时离宫别馆，乘山瞰海，而今之所存，大则浮屠老氏之室，小则公卿大夫之庐，鸣钟相闻，择胜以居，飞栏危榭，往往而在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1254272_comment'></div>倚岩壑之幽清，翳松桧其晻蔼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1254272_comment'></div>虽一斑之或见，曾未若斯亭之宏大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1254272_comment'></div>碧油画戟，来藩此府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1254272_comment'></div>往贤近臣，盖已百数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1254272_comment'></div>慨登临之遗迹，咸褊陋而无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1254272_comment'></div>独先生至而有之，舞山光于帘幕，冯地势之襟带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1254272_comment'></div>杂支离之万种，烂锦幄其旆旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1254272_comment'></div>荐醽醁于樽俎，剥珍错之螺贝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1254272_comment'></div>发角徵之清唱，挽行云于天外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1254272_comment'></div>使邦人聚观，白首惊拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1254272_comment'></div>岂吾先生浩然之气，六合为隘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1254272_comment'></div>蟠万象于胸中，耿星辰而不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1254272_comment'></div>遇至美而一发，借佳名以自快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1254272_comment'></div>而景物之来，适际其会，彼千古而莫识，信一时之有待者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1254272_comment'></div>于是先生闻之，冁然而笑，众宾避席，迭起为寿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1254272_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>始与赵彥端（德庄）游。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0344c7e3fcdb4625926a08152dee6453_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0344c7e3fcdb4625926a08152dee6453");'><span id='0344c7e3fcdb4625926a08152dee6453_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>，43岁</div><div id='0344c7e3fcdb4625926a08152dee6453' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年4月</a>　知福州、福建安抚使辛次膺离任，至福州送行。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4e2310cef4764250bc9e482ff177ce7b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4e2310cef4764250bc9e482ff177ce7b");'><span id='4e2310cef4764250bc9e482ff177ce7b_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　春至临安，应礼部试，落第。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b20d4256eacf458d955ebda2680e61c9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b20d4256eacf458d955ebda2680e61c9");'><span id='b20d4256eacf458d955ebda2680e61c9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>，31岁</div><div id='b20d4256eacf458d955ebda2680e61c9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年1月</a>　月初，至临安应礼部试，再落第，还谒叶梦得，得《许昌唱和集》以归。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='023ad28467dd470c8bca1be74561038e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("023ad28467dd470c8bca1be74561038e");'><span id='023ad28467dd470c8bca1be74561038e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>，40岁</div><div id='023ad28467dd470c8bca1be74561038e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　年初，至临安，以文谒权礼部侍郎辛次膺（起李），应词科试落选，得知建安县。作品：《上辛中丞书（次膺）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254398?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上辛中丞书<span class='inlineComment2'>（次膺）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254398")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254398_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254398'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254398'>某之得见于门下三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254398_comment'></div>始则阁下之在春官，某以妄应科目，贽其业而见焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254398_comment'></div>中则阁下帅闽而归，某为县于建安，以属部之吏而见焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254398_comment'></div>今也阁下召还于朝，居中执法之任，某亦滥预于百执事之列而复见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254398_comment'></div>踽踽而趋，寒暄而词，意阁下曾未省其面目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254398_comment'></div>阁下之名满天之下，某之愚仰慕盛德，固将卜其遇否，七年之间乃三见而不得致其言焉，亦异于古人一面而谈当世之事者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254398_comment'></div>今当世之事，非某所得谈也，虽然，不敢废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254398_comment'></div>盖天下可忧者一，可虑者二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254398_comment'></div>夫天下有所谓大计，有所谓先务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254398_comment'></div>先务审矣，馀则可以序而推之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254398_comment'></div>今国家不议其大计与其先务，而乃姑试为之，战则姑试而战也，和则姑试而和也，守则姑试而守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254398_comment'></div>朝夕自治者，徒欲百废具举，一旦缓急，计将若何，岂非可忧者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254398_comment'></div>主上之求治亦云切矣，然前日在藩邸，一二小臣使令于前，故得与议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254398_comment'></div>今有天下之大，则天下之才皆我用也，外廷之士曾未尽获进见，而左右近习日有闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254398_comment'></div>宰执侍从之贵，台谏一议则逐之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254398_comment'></div>内侍而典戎器，武臣而治榷酤，章四五上而几不可逐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254398_comment'></div>后有甚者，台谏之言何自入哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254398_comment'></div>此可虑之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254398_comment'></div>诸葛孔明有言：「亲贤臣，远小人，先汉所以兴隆也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254398_comment'></div>亲小人，远贤臣，后汉所以倾颓也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254398_comment'></div>人君之患，莫大于以近习为腹心而朝士为外人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254398_comment'></div>汉元帝有萧望之、刘向，不与之共政而乃任恭、显；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254398_comment'></div>唐文宗有裴度、李德裕，不与之谋事而乃委训、注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254398_comment'></div>后世观之，则固颠倒错谬，当时为之，未之觉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254398_comment'></div>盖小人得用之始，莫不言财利，其终则足以盗威权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254398_comment'></div>不言财利则人君无以谓其能，不盗威权则无以引奸邪而自助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254398_comment'></div>今主上励精庶政，每事欲亲而未得其要，涉于丛脞，则其间易入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254398_comment'></div>以酒坊一事言之，小人骎骎其倡财利之端矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254398_comment'></div>既已荐用人材，士大夫间岂得无刘、柳辈，傥复寖盛，安能保其不从哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254398_comment'></div>此可虑之二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254398_comment'></div>夫事固未至此，要将有以折其萌而削其根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254398_comment'></div>且以德寿宫官属观之，不选大臣从官为使，而独任宦者提举，宜其无所裨益，致私酤之谤闻于天下，而土木花石之运未已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254398_comment'></div>向使儒士参于其间，当必有规正者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254398_comment'></div>故某窃愿主上亦求儒士，以与谋事于宫中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254398_comment'></div>然士风不振已久，以为不肖而无过之可指，以为贤而无善之可议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254398_comment'></div>要之其才为无所用，徒欲偷懦苟容以侥倖于富贵者甚众，不大有以区别之，亦无补于国家之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254398_comment'></div>夫天下大计不定，人君之侧犹有小人间之，而士大夫风俗如此，阁下宜所深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254398_comment'></div>孟子曰：「惟大人为能格君心之非」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254398_comment'></div>夫格之者，渐之以言而后可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254398_comment'></div>以阁下操履之正，名节之伟，主上不即登之政路，而尚以屈耳目之寄，是盖欲朝夕闻阁下之言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254398_comment'></div>他人徒能言之，而阁下之言则能信于主上，安有不格者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254398_comment'></div>皇祐中，仁宗患台谏之任轻，王安简公以前执政命为中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254398_comment'></div>安简受而不辞，乃慨然论事，至留班以争张尧佐四使之除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254398_comment'></div>又言河朔根本之地，将帅之非其人者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254398_comment'></div>又言唐质肃之贬为过，而致言路不通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1254398_comment'></div>狄武襄不当任枢筦之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1254398_comment'></div>意气凛凛，廷臣为之耸动，仁宗谓其得风宪体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1254398_comment'></div>盖风宪之地，非老成重臣，无以振举大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1254398_comment'></div>而搏击琐细之论，世不乏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1254398_comment'></div>主上之待阁下，有符于仁祖矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1254398_comment'></div>阁下之自任，其无愧于安简！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1254398_comment'></div>意者造膝之言，有不得闻于外也，而某也北方之鄙人，守家世之训，不忍自同于流俗，犹复哓哓于阁下之门，多见其不知量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1254398_comment'></div>然就有道而正焉，斯学者之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1254398_comment'></div>故不敢自以为是，并以前者所上封事之副为献，惟阁下不鄙其愚而教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1254398_comment'></div>或谓其可取，因其言而陈之，则某之幸也，非敢望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1254398_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1254398_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a1e7e058f96c4a5daf507e12b24f7d0d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a1e7e058f96c4a5daf507e12b24f7d0d");'><span id='a1e7e058f96c4a5daf507e12b24f7d0d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>，40岁</div><div id='a1e7e058f96c4a5daf507e12b24f7d0d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　返临安候替。其友庞谦孺（祐甫）来访，有序送别。作品：《送庞祐甫序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254466?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送庞祐甫序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254466")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254466'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254466'>庞子将归矣，而告于韩子曰：子盍为我言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254466_comment'></div>吾穷于世久矣，意天下之穷者莫我若也，而吾有幸焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254466_comment'></div>夫世之人类多蠢蠢然也，今吾之生而口能道言辞，手能作字画，知古今，别治乱，识士之贤不肖而亲疏之，兹非幸欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254466_comment'></div>然而齿滋众而食益贫，年加长而仕不进，故吾之志率寓于吾文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254466_comment'></div>而吾之为文也，亦庶几于古而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254466_comment'></div>酒酣而歌，上彻云汉，放意而行，不知所之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254466_comment'></div>世虽不吾求，而吾亦未尝即之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254466_comment'></div>虽然，用舍君子之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254466_comment'></div>人之生也有涯，其将若是而已乎，抑亦不若是也，子以为如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254466_comment'></div>韩子曰：子穷于世而不即者也，吾尝即之焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254466_comment'></div>仕者，人之甚慕也，吾为吏者十年矣，而无知焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254466_comment'></div>名者，人之甚趋也，吾从事于有司者三返矣，而无获焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254466_comment'></div>吾闻之，山之穷者益高，水之穷者益清，人之穷也，其行益峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254466_comment'></div>故吾方将效子之为以自慰，是何子言之悲也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254466_comment'></div>凡人之生也，心志不通，耳目蒙昧，若是者名为天穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254466_comment'></div>衣食不足于身，爵禄不副其材，若是者名为人穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254466_comment'></div>天穷者不得于天，人穷者不必用于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254466_comment'></div>今人之所谓不用者，无过于失夫富贵之期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254466_comment'></div>王公大人身存而名灭，山林之士已死而言立者，亦众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254466_comment'></div>名灭者天绝之，言立者人不得而绝之，其为用也不亦远乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254466_comment'></div>今吾与子也，其皆穷于人者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254466_comment'></div>苟其不用于彼，犹有用于此也，而子何患焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254466_comment'></div>于是相与抵掌而笑，击缶而歌曰：山木兮依依，涧草兮萋萋，猿禽咿嚘兮虎豹往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254466_comment'></div>耕田兮何所，山有夔兮不我肯处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254466_comment'></div>江海倒流兮颓波汤汤，子舟既具兮何病沾裳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254466_comment'></div>遵其涂兮遇潦则止，我车无伤兮从子万里。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1254466_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　有诗寄知滁州徐度（敦立）作品：《寄徐滁州敦立》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243367' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243367' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243367?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄徐滁州埻立</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243367")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243367_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243367'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243367'>青琐金鸾迹未容，寘公犹在昔贤中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243367'>著书定已追迂叟<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：闻编《通鉴后事》甚备。）</span>，得郡何妨号醉翁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243367'>丰乐桥边鱼动镜，清流关下马嘶风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243367'>独怜湛辈犹奔走，不得登临一笑同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243367'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243367_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年9月</a>　为范如圭（伯达）除江西提举常平茶盐公事代作谢表。作品：《代江南提举范直阁谢到任表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254326?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代江南提举范直阁谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254326")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254326'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254326'>千里造朝，方蒙于收召；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254326_comment'></div>十城命使，遽玷于光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254326_comment'></div>已届部封，恭宣诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254326_comment'></div>伏念臣起家寒远，涉世迂疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254326_comment'></div>一昨簉迹于书林，屡尝赐对于便坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254326_comment'></div>身逢圣主，每怀造膝之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254326_comment'></div>意忤权臣，几致反唇之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254326_comment'></div>三祈閒馆，两佐遐州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254326_comment'></div>幸公道之复开，获清光之再睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254326_comment'></div>愚忠自励，虽知仅免于悔尤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254326_comment'></div>旧学寖荒，岂有发明于议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254326_comment'></div>敢期齿奖，曲赐眷怜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254326_comment'></div>宠之内阁之名，付以外台之寄，人微恩厚，感极涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254326_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下懋建大中，敷求至治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254326_comment'></div>乾纲独运，节万务以鼎新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254326_comment'></div>离照无私，萃群材而器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254326_comment'></div>致兹庸琐，亦误选抡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254326_comment'></div>臣敢不深究货源，持平廪政？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254326_comment'></div>虽激浊扬清之事，职所愿为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254326_comment'></div>若奉公守正之心，义当无替。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1254326_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　知静江府施钜荐于朝。作品：《谢施资政启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254431' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254431' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254431?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢施资政荐举启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254431")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254431_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254431'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254431'>十年知遇，久自信于生平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254431_comment'></div>千里荐延，迄遂偿其素志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254431_comment'></div>奇穷已甚，眷顾有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254431_comment'></div>伏念某赋性迂疏，降材谫陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254431_comment'></div>学无所用，敢希当世之荣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254431_comment'></div>愚不自知，每志古人之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254431_comment'></div>游士夫之门者既罕，识公卿之面则又疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254431_comment'></div>一官姑切于为贫，三仕实忘于幸进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254431_comment'></div>昨从吏役，早玷品题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254431_comment'></div>屡棨戟之遽还，偶囊封之未上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254431_comment'></div>周流岁月，仲卿未免于牛衣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254431_comment'></div>赫奕功名，君房已至于鼎足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254431_comment'></div>岂意迍邅之迹，竟纡藻鉴之收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254431_comment'></div>诺有重于百金，古闻其语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254431_comment'></div>书或贤于十部，今庆其蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254431_comment'></div>提撕之意愈加，褒假之词甚宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254431_comment'></div>姬姜在列，独惭憔悴之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254431_comment'></div>糠秕何知，乃费簸扬之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254431_comment'></div>此盖伏遇判府经略参政大资先生道追前哲，德重本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254431_comment'></div>机务均劳，暂出分于阃寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254431_comment'></div>贤愚罔间，思尽寘于门阑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254431_comment'></div>敢云故旧之不遗，是亦典型之尚有！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254431_comment'></div>致兹洪造，远施贱微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254431_comment'></div>某敢不佩弦而韦，循规以矩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254431_comment'></div>慕荆鸡之化，秖荷于生成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254431_comment'></div>怀尺蠖之伸，亦期于报塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254431_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1254431_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c02aa5c523fe42e986e0de156767e371_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c02aa5c523fe42e986e0de156767e371");'><span id='c02aa5c523fe42e986e0de156767e371_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，44岁</div><div id='c02aa5c523fe42e986e0de156767e371' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　至临安，观潮钱塘江，赋诗感怀。作品：《浙江观潮》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_243108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浙江观潮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243108")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243108'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243108'>江翻海涌势难平，鳌掷鹏鶱自不停。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243108'>端为君王洗兵马，参旗井钺万雷霆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243108'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243108_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='74af0951fbb747e4ae6baf2a435022a1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("74af0951fbb747e4ae6baf2a435022a1");'><span id='74af0951fbb747e4ae6baf2a435022a1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1162')">1161-1162年</a>，44-45岁</div><div id='74af0951fbb747e4ae6baf2a435022a1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年9月</a>　九月辛巳，以右通直郎入为司农寺主簿。作品：《谢司农簿启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢司农簿启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254429")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254429'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254429'>百里之才，曷胜选用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254429_comment'></div>一介之贱，误入招徕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254429_comment'></div>俾厕王官，殆踰己望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254429_comment'></div>窃以人之所慕者富贵，盖富贵有时而不可求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254429_comment'></div>士之所志者功名，故功名无往而不可立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254429_comment'></div>然狃于富贵，则见利不知有义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254429_comment'></div>急于功名，则遇事或至失身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254429_comment'></div>此圣贤以为行藏之几，而古今以为治乱之要，在我而已，其谁念之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254429_comment'></div>惟国家取士，既小异于汉、唐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254429_comment'></div>朝廷用人，抑又拘于格法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254429_comment'></div>虽纪纲大治，承平过于百年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254429_comment'></div>而风俗寖偷，祸患生于一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254429_comment'></div>重以权臣之荆棘，了无国士之弓旌，恩必已归，爵惟私市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254429_comment'></div>幸圣人之更化，仰明哲之佐朝，苟一善之荐闻，皆趣召而赐对，布在列位，使无遗材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254429_comment'></div>自非猖狂疾病之流，孰不奔走竭蹶而至？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254429_comment'></div>不特引君于道，又将观国之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254429_comment'></div>夫何戆愚，亦在齿录！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254429_comment'></div>伏念某少知学问，长迫饥寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254429_comment'></div>一经之传，既不足以自奋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254429_comment'></div>五斗之养，特未免于为贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254429_comment'></div>窃尝妄意于古人，故亦希纵于诸彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254429_comment'></div>三从吏选，仅为祖逖之先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254429_comment'></div>五试词场，迄拜孟明之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254429_comment'></div>朅繇县宰，始见公车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254429_comment'></div>询事考言，曾乏过人之虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254429_comment'></div>料敌制胜，妄陈决策之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254429_comment'></div>方惧触于严诛，乃遽叨于美仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254429_comment'></div>宦于九扈，职预百司，祗怀受粟之羞，讵识献芹之陋！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254429_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官道存经世，业懋享天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254429_comment'></div>藻鉴士流，欲贤愚之并用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254429_comment'></div>权衡帝载，思邪正之汇分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254429_comment'></div>旧蒙一盼之私，曲示兼容之度，致兹幼贱，猥荷甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254429_comment'></div>某敢不力探师友之渊源，恪守高曾之规矩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254429_comment'></div>惟农夫之有畔，岂敢越思？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254429_comment'></div>若射者之反求，粗知正己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254429_comment'></div>庶靡隳于职业，以无忘于恩怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254429_comment'></div>过此以还，未知攸措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1254429_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年9月</a>　上书枢府，乞朝廷早下诏书，明示敌人败盟，使军民预知国事，同心协力，共济事机。作品：《上枢府札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上枢府劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254396")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254396'>某窃见朝廷自夏秋以来，以敌人意欲败盟，戒严边备，选任将帅，简练军实，为计甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254396_comment'></div>惟是旬日传闻，声势颇炽，道路汹汹，皆以未知所向为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254396_comment'></div>虽庙谋深秘，非中外所可得闻，然人心不安，缓急何以应敌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254396_comment'></div>质之舆论，谓宜即有诏书，明示远近，俾军民士大夫晓然预知国事，然后同心协虑，共济事机，所系甚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254396_comment'></div>而或者以为朝廷不欲先露失和之旨，若便降诏，遂有形迹，但当隐忍持重，厉兵秣马，以俟其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254396_comment'></div>此固善也，奈人心不安何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254396_comment'></div>然前日既遣使讫，固欲和尔，彼乃不受吾使，再定期日，指索大臣，继而止要泛使，吾皆拒而不遣，是形迹已成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254396_comment'></div>况又受其流亡之民，纳其降附之地，不可以为无迹，而独于诏书惜之何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254396_comment'></div>若必待侵犯吾圉，然后降诏，是时事属仓猝，淮甸之人必至奔扰，江浙之众当亦动摇，而四方万里之远，安能一日而谕及？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254396_comment'></div>今为之始可以安人心而作士气也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254396_comment'></div>语有之：「明其为贼，敌乃可服」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254396_comment'></div>今日诏书，但当极言屈己和戎，所以惠安海内，而彼既败盟，则有不得已而后应之意，万一不至用兵，夫复何害？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254396_comment'></div>异时六飞果遂顺动，始别为誓师一诏，以决大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254396_comment'></div>作两节施行，似不相妨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254396_comment'></div>若或迁延，致其传檄境上，事出倒置，浮言胥动，虽鞭之长不及马腹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254396_comment'></div>某人微位下，仰恃门下一日之眷，用私布于左右，如蒙采取，愿止以钧意白而行之，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1254396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　其妻卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月</a>　再上札子，建议采取防范措施，以防金人渡江。作品：《十月末乞备御白札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十月末乞备御白劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254359")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254359'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254359'>一、敌已深入淮甸，今日所当防江，未闻朝廷火急措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254359_comment'></div>如镇江、建康、采石、池口诸处，人兵各有多少，如何分布，宜遣使不住宣谕，激励将士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254359_comment'></div>仍乞指挥沿江守臣，速行团结民兵于无官兵处，声势相望，各守江岸，以护乡井为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254359_comment'></div>但得人心齐一，只能奋击炮石，踏弩放箭，便可守御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254359_comment'></div>盖敌人恃众渡江，不比华人须择岸口，定是多缚排筏，一时散渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254359_comment'></div>若止控守渡口，致其别处登岸，不在官兵地方，便至失事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1254359'>一、敌若未敢渡江，只据淮甸，得州守州，得县守县，则江左岂能得奠枕？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254359_comment'></div>今不知扬州、和州尚有大军多少，并戍马军直来甚处会合，枢密行府如何措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254359_comment'></div>传闻敌已乏粮，煮马而食，宜密降处分诸将，此事更须精加察探，恐其排筏木未备，声此误我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254359_comment'></div>若果曾断其粮道，渐至饥乏，乞上手书戒敕诸将，皆以国事为念，同心勠力，出奇奋击，但痛败得一二阵，使彼遁去，然后可保无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254359_comment'></div>只便退军保江，敌已宿兵运粮，则山寨、水寨之人何所归附，将来淮甸如何攻取？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254359_comment'></div>扬州不保，通泰遂失，海道直与常熟、江阴相对矣，沿江纲运如何运行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254359_comment'></div>岂得但以保江为言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254359_comment'></div>此事切须奏知，审问诸将方略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1254359'>一、自淮上交锋，今已一月，敌人迫江，又已旬馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254359_comment'></div>阴雨冱寒，前有大敌，将士劳苦，而朝廷未住常程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254359_comment'></div>虽欲外示閒暇，然不急之务，皆未省去，无以鼓动军心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254359_comment'></div>傥车驾未顺动，宜遣王人遍行抚问，如特支犒设之类，有不可缓者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254359_comment'></div>并岁帑之费，亦宜且降指挥，依数桩管，欲专充激赏使用，以慰累年积忿冒矢之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1254359'>一、敌已垂军深入，不顾其后，但乞敕诸将之未渡江者，若果已断其粮道，彼众饥乏，则可会合一战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254359_comment'></div>此贵捷速，盖虑其济师运粮，则我军却当腹背受敌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254359_comment'></div>如其不然，彼众我寡，但能坚壁清野，时出奇兵，略其粮道，扰其营垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254359_comment'></div>彼若不归，延日持久，彼国当自有变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254359_comment'></div>盖中原人心已离，所签军士涉数千里之远，岂不思归，特畏其法令严酷而我之胜形未见，故未敢动尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254359_comment'></div>其沿江诸将并监司、帅臣、总领等，合令日下具平安状申，以察事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1254359'>一、昨来降诏亲征，正欲激励将士，今敌已渡淮，即亦宜径临江上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254359_comment'></div>然沿路排办，祗备多日，恐难但已，却致将士及四方疑惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254359_comment'></div>谓宜暂驻平江，以相事势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254359_comment'></div>今幸刘帅大捷，宜令诸将之已渡江者，疾速济师，以为犄角，直须驱逐过淮，方得今冬无虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254359_comment'></div>其刘帅军合先犒赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1254359'>一、广德军一路，自溧水直抵馀杭，敌人往年尝由此入，合有兵马控御，乞选将星夜沿路择要害措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254359_comment'></div>亦集民兵团结，仍多置斥堠，如夹冈路、吴江长桥，亦宜密加屯守，以备不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254359_comment'></div>此下策也，不得不虑，而平江沿海对淮，亦宜复置一官，抽集水军以为警逻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1254359'>一、自亲征诏下，有进发日子，及敌已逼真州，行朝居民，类多迁徙，四方士大夫之待选者，往往亦归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254359_comment'></div>窃恐传播有过其实，乞令进奏院日下报状，并入斥堠，庶使四方排日皆知朝廷动静，以消境内之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254359_comment'></div>如荆襄、四川报状，尤要疾速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254359_comment'></div>此事虽小，所系甚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254359_comment'></div>其斥堠铺，宜添差使臣，不住往来驱催，如有警急，许巡铺使臣径具飞申，务要知远近事宜，而朝廷机速房，更乞严加约束，无至泄漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254359_comment'></div>近日刘帅有密奏，人能诵之，前者诏檄未颁，已传于外，岂不决体伤事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1254359'>一、比见枢密行府已招效用，则行在亦宜招集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254359_comment'></div>盖辇毂之下，无赖游手至多，富家大姓，一旦迁移，不肯放债借钱，此辈无所得食，便至失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254359_comment'></div>昨来京师盖尝鼓倡横议，或于斜街暗巷，恣行剽夺，致居民不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254359_comment'></div>岂若朝廷损少钱米聚而养之，俾一二将校团结收管，虽未必皆中用，且得不至生事，候平定日却行放散，所费显属不多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1254359'>一、将来车驾进发，亦乞三两日一降指挥，存问临安居民，如放房钱、支赈济米之类，俾人日知巡幸所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254359_comment'></div>如有捷报，依次关留司出榜，仍乞临安府分差使臣，责以军法，认定地方，夜巡觉察贼盗，并奸细放火惊动之扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1254359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1254359'>一、近因人家迁徙，传闻严州界上并长河堰下，已曾劫了舟船，陆路亦有剽夺恶少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1254359_comment'></div>乞降指挥，侧近州县督责巡尉，不住躬亲于道路巡警，若有此类，并行军法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1254359_comment'></div>其巡尉失觉察，亦以军法从事，庶得警肃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1254359_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年12月</a>　十二月（己亥朔）壬寅，以汤思退荐，兼临安行宫留守司干办公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年12月</a>　十二月甲辰，司农少卿杜莘老（起莘）出知遂宁府，有诗送行。作品：《送杜少卿起莘知遂宁府以“高名千古重如山”为韵七首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送杜少卿起萃知遂宁府以高名千古重如山为韵七首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_3_243492'>尚友千载馀，斯心岂徒劳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243492'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243492_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243491?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243491'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243491'>十年天壤间，久矣闻公名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243490_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243489?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_2_243489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243489'>公行幸迟迟，去国犹去鲁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243494'>节谊知不足，文章焉取馀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　张元干（仲宗）卒，有挽词。作品：《挽张元干国录词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243337' class='_poem'><div class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243337")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243337_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243337'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243337'>左学驰声旧，中朝得录初。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243337'>宏材知底用，壮志亦成虚。<div target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243336'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243336'>一第固已晚，九迁人共期。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243336'>功名虽有命，寿考独无时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243336'>门士韬圭璧，诸郎袭礼诗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243336'>他年振儒学，犹慰九原悲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243336'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243336_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　年初，代汤思退撰问高宗起居札子。作品：《代留守司起居札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254369' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254369' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254369?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代留守司起居劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254369")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254369_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254369'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254369'>臣伏审车驾进发巡幸，已抵建康者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254369_comment'></div>窃以强敌渝盟，自贻陨命，天师戡难，所向奏功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254369_comment'></div>尚勤銮辂之时巡，甫居陪都而肆觐，凡在观听，孰不欢呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254369_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下，体胜残去杀之仁，修安民和众之武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254369_comment'></div>事之皮币，初岂吝而不为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254369_comment'></div>锻乃戈矛，非得已而后用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254369_comment'></div>天之所助，鬼得而诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254369_comment'></div>旌旃方动于江淮，号令已宣于河洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254369_comment'></div>惟时机会，系国安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254369_comment'></div>冀观馀孽之豆分，少徯中原之响应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254369_comment'></div>庶出万全之策，以恢亿世之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254369_comment'></div>既疆圉之肃清，将舆图之尽复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254369_comment'></div>臣久叨眷遇，粗有朴忠，属暂司管钥之留，不能执羁靮而从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254369_comment'></div>跂望行阙，臣无任拳拳激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1254369_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　立春日，作感怀诗。作品：《立春感怀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243166' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243166' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243166?labeling=true' target='_blank'>立春感怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243166")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243166_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243166'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243166'>南北驱驰老病身，不堪节物更催人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243166'>梅梢白白犹藏腊，蔬甲青青便作春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243166'>铁马渐欣边塞静，土牛还祝岁时新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243166'>圣朝文物从兹始，元日郊丘得上辛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243166'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243166_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年2月</a>　汤思退（进之）出知绍兴府，有诗送行。作品：《送汤丞相帅会稽》三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送汤丞相帅会稽<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span "poem_title_243306")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243306'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243306_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243306'>䌽绶不妨龙衮贵，锦衣真与故乡同。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243306_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
