target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243307_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243307'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243307'>翰墨英名多士先，经纶长策万方传。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243307'>久知燕许文章大，要自皋夔事业贤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243307'>曲水兰亭脩竹外，都门祖帐百花前。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243307'>去天尺五调元旧，肯使邦人借一年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243307'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243307_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243485?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243485'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243485'>畴昔追风幸执鞭，词场好在笔如椽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243485'>十年睎骥犹瞠若，晚岁登龙未偶然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243485'>下客阳春惊白雪，何人绿水近红莲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243485'>尚应九里蒙河润，他日一天今二天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243485'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　得其友庞谦孺（祐甫）寄来上年所作《水调歌头》词，和之。作品：《水调歌头·和庞祐父见寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>和庞祐甫见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243565")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243565'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243565'>落日澹芳草，烟际一鸥浮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243565'>西湖好处，君去千里为谁留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243565'>坐想敬亭山下，竹映一溪寒水，飞盖共追游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243565'>况有樽前客，相对两诗流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243565_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243565'>笑谈间，风满座，气横秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243565'>平生壮志，长啸起舞看吴钩。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243565'>红白山花开谢，半醉半醒时节，春去子规愁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243565'>梦绕水西寺，回首谢公楼。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_243565_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　三、四月间，送尹穑（少稷）归玉山。作品：《送尹少稷序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254468' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254468' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254468?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送尹少稷序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254468")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254468_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254468'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254468'>予尝观战国之时重士，士之见其君至有立谈而为卿相，不则厚币加礼，而不敢屈焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254468_comment'></div>盖楚不用则之晋，齐不用则之燕，皆以士为贫富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254468_comment'></div>而士亦自恃其才力、辨说，以为举世之大，将不可一日而无我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254468_comment'></div>及夫天下既一，士之获见于君，率以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254468_comment'></div>设科置目，虽有长材异行，非自贾者盖有不得选焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254468_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254468_comment'></div>贵贱之势殊，而取舍之时异也，士固轻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254468_comment'></div>必有人焉，自好而特立，返其重者于己，移其轻者与人，俾在上者不得以其名利爵禄而要之，此视其道之何如尔！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254468_comment'></div>今年秋，友人尹少稷召而至于京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254468_comment'></div>方少稷之未来也，公卿交荐之，部使者显言之，以为宜在本朝者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254468_comment'></div>及其来也，侍从之贤则就见之，百执事之良争识之，退而咸曰少稷之论信可听，其才信可庸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254468_comment'></div>御史闻之，扬于廷曰，尹某之直谅也，其可储之以备台谏之选矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254468_comment'></div>翰林西掖诸公，又有诵其诗于众者，曰少稷之文盖如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254468_comment'></div>已而陛献其言，天子以语大臣：是盖东州佳士，何以处之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254468_comment'></div>无几何，少稷得用为枢密院编修官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254468_comment'></div>少稷既拜命，退而言归，语其所厚者曰：吾不选于吏者三十年矣，吾才无取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254468_comment'></div>有田在怀玉之下，可耕而食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254468_comment'></div>与其诎吾志而徇时，孰若安于命以全我也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254468_comment'></div>少稷既去，不知者色然异之，曰：编摩，士之高选，盖有欲而不得者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254468_comment'></div>且其次仅旬日，少稷不屑，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254468_comment'></div>其知者亦怅然望之，曰：甚矣，吾道之难行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254468_comment'></div>得一人于此焉可喜，失一人于此焉可惋，少稷不少忍，吾党之士孤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254468_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254468_comment'></div>以少稷之贤，公卿挽于前，部使者推于后，从官、御史、词臣、百执事之良左右而掖之，天子动色称善，自一命之微有列于右府，士之得此，足以为其身荣，而少稷如逃负避喧，蹀躞焉行而不止，真明于去就者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254468_comment'></div>然予闻之，自金主之死，大河南北之民望旌旗而思宋，汉中之兵虽张，而两淮之备未饬，以战则无功，以和则受辱，此君相之谋蚤夜而不释者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254468_comment'></div>朝廷不用士则已，如用也，果无以还吾少稷哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254468_comment'></div>少稷异时肯而复来，尚足以慰夫吾党之士也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1254468_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年7月</a>　上札子建议妥为安置归正人。作品：《论归正忠义人钱米田札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论归正忠义人钱米田劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254357")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254357'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254357'>窃见沿淮诸处，近缘边境旱蝗，归正忠义之人动数千计，若不优加存恤，无以昭示国家德泽，若欲家给人足，实恐州县不能应付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254357_comment'></div>而目今诸处所申，多是便欲依诸军例尽行支破请受，或欲借请粮之类，并不分别人数，开具名色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254357_comment'></div>有司执法，例皆不敢批放，而归正之人待报日久，别无衣食，必至悔怨，理宜措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254357_comment'></div>欲望朝廷行下逐处，遇归正忠义人到，且依常平法，大人小儿支破钱米如赈济之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254357_comment'></div>却行取责数内情愿充军应得等仗之人，即与支破军人请受，拨隶诸军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254357_comment'></div>或武艺高强，情愿充效用之人，即与支破效用请受，拨隶效用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254357_comment'></div>其不愿充军及不迭等仗、别无武艺之人，且与接续赈济钱米，于淮南两路取拨閒田或官庄田土，支借牛具种子，各令服业，候至来年收麦时候，始行罢给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254357_comment'></div>庶得上不虚费大农之储，下有以固结归顺向化之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1254357_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　上书同知枢密院事张焘，劝其“勿谓本等之位有常职”，应以“朝夕纳诲”为己任。作品：《上张同知书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷13。）</span><div id='poem_1254406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上张同知书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254406")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254406'>某闻之，君子出而应世，用其规模，取舍必有素定于胸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254406_comment'></div>而人君之信贤，莫大于进用之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254406_comment'></div>盖规模取舍，不有素定，则动为世之所移；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254406_comment'></div>进用之始，不竭底蕴，以告于上，则后日不为人君之所尊信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254406_comment'></div>孟子之见梁王，守仁义之说而不易也，虽不用，其道益尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254406_comment'></div>商鞅之见孝公，每下其说以取合焉，宜其有不终之祸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254406_comment'></div>士生于世，其以孟子为法而鞅为戒哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254406_comment'></div>此在贤者，所以欲观其进用之始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254406_comment'></div>洪惟圣天子践阼，举朝之臣不足以膺注想之重，而必以徵阁下为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254406_comment'></div>手札而召，亲降色词而问，阁下所言，其尽之也，士复何憾！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254406_comment'></div>万有一为思虑之所不及，则天下之望何自而释哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254406_comment'></div>自权臣之死，太上皇帝更美万化，既七八年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254406_comment'></div>主上绍隆大统，忧勤匪懈，又数月矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254406_comment'></div>救天下之弊，孰不曰人材？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254406_comment'></div>闻一善则举之，见一贤则招之，百执事之位至无虚焉，而天下之弊终以不去，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254406_comment'></div>有人材之名，无实用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254406_comment'></div>孟子有言：不信仁贤，则国空虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254406_comment'></div>夫国之空虚，非无仁贤也，有而不能信，是亦空虚尔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254406_comment'></div>今之人材，有不得其言者矣，有不得其职者矣，有不得其地者矣，徒欲人人聚之本朝，以为观美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254406_comment'></div>譬之作室者，闻天下之有良材，不惜千金而市，然犹露宿于野；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254406_comment'></div>疾病者，闻四方之有良药，不惮千里而求，然犹伏枕而卧，曾不知所以用之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254406_comment'></div>故大匠之用材，不踰丈引而足以支大厦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254406_comment'></div>良医之用药，不越铢两而足以已奇疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254406_comment'></div>自古人材非天降地出，特在用不用之间，不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254406_comment'></div>夫一人之智不若众人之智，一人之力不若众人之力也，今诿事于人，以一人为不足，岂若合众智以图之，合众力以举之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254406_comment'></div>合众人者，非一人往，使一人窥之，又使一人待之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254406_comment'></div>合众多之论定其当，而使一人行焉，则无不济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254406_comment'></div>日者阁下劝主上以诹访天下之事，固求治之要也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254406_comment'></div>然天下之事有先后，患在门庭则先治门庭，患在腹心则先治腹心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254406_comment'></div>今日之患，外患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254406_comment'></div>外患既急，要先治之于门庭，而阁下特欲付之将帅而不问，此某之所未谕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254406_comment'></div>盖某尝指靖康而论矣，当时更革号令，无非朝廷美事，惟御敌之策，未能称是，不过大臣将兵以救河东，坚守京城以待四方勤王之师而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254406_comment'></div>向使大臣果能用兵如周瑜、陆逊，四方勤王之师果可倚重如李、郭，盖未害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254406_comment'></div>徒有其名而不知其不可用，岂不上误社稷而下误生灵哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254406_comment'></div>今固未至此，然去岁敌使兴慢侮之言，议者皆曰可战矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254406_comment'></div>非天相我，则几至阽危，而战卒不胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254406_comment'></div>金主既殒，两淮凋瘵已甚，迩来先我致好，议者皆曰可和矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254406_comment'></div>使者一往而被辱，再行而不受，而和卒不成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254406_comment'></div>自和战之未遂也，议者则曰可守矣，若又如和战之谬，岂不大可虑耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254406_comment'></div>夫战则当有其备，和则当有其谋，守则当有其地，非可伥然妄动，以侥倖于万一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254406_comment'></div>战既无备而和既无谋矣，则所守果何地哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254406_comment'></div>以骄将御惰兵，而一二书生角无用之谈者，半岁往来而不决，两淮之间未见其有控扼者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254406_comment'></div>夫敌之强弱存亡盖不必问，苟有以自固吾圉，要当汰择将帅，简练兵马，度要害之地，高城深池而必守焉，见利勿动，见疑勿惊，而彼能越吾地为盗者，人不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254406_comment'></div>日夜以图之，假以数年，吾之事力既振，何往而不利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254406_comment'></div>然县官所少，又不过曰财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1254406_comment'></div>夫财非所虑也，朝廷能一战而复中原，虽仕者罢俸，耕者辍食，其谁敢怨！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1254406_comment'></div>惟其有无用之蠹，但见其不足也，今每事不欲撙节，而止务财赋之增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1254406_comment'></div>儒士龌龊，任用不快，必使豪健之吏，驰骋四出，以网罗利源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1254406_comment'></div>就令得人如王鉷、杨慎矜、裴延龄数辈，当时非不号能，自今观之，有益唐室哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1254406_comment'></div>近者已用一二小臣措置酒坊于外，不识主上何自而知其人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1254406_comment'></div>此弊一开，异时百官有司皆可自他涂出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1254406_comment'></div>上之宰相、执政，次则侍从之臣，台谏一有论列，无不罢斥，内侍之微，武臣之贱，阅月踰时，章四五上而仅免焉，不识谁为主上谋之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1254406_comment'></div>庙堂之贤，安可谦逊退托而不任此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1254406_comment'></div>方主上富于春秋，践阼未淹月，举措一不得宜，无正之者则习熟而行，后将有难正者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1254406_comment'></div>阁下勿谓本等之位有常职而不可言也，天下之士望阁下者，以彼不以此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1254406_comment'></div>主上之待阁下，亦异于他人矣，阁下而不言，谁当言者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1254406_comment'></div>朝夕纳诲，以辅台德，正阁下之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1254406_comment'></div>闻之故老，建中靖国初，起范忠宣公于颍，忠宣已自病，不能视物，慨然欲行，其亲戚子弟固邀止之，至肩舆伪游于园以为在道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1254406_comment'></div>忠宣悟而叹曰：「宰相吾为之矣，夫复何求！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1254406_comment'></div>尔辈知其一，未知其二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1254406_comment'></div>主上新即位，欲访治道，以吾老臣，言可信也，使吾得见主上而一言，胜于他人之百言矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1254406_comment'></div>忠宣之论，正阁下今日比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1254406_comment'></div>《诗》不云乎：「德輶如毛，民鲜克举之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1254406_comment'></div>我仪图之，惟仲山甫举之，爱莫助之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1254406_comment'></div>衮职有阙，惟仲山甫补之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1254406_comment'></div>盖山甫之补衮，在于能举其德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1254406_comment'></div>而人之爱山甫，在于图德而莫助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1254406_comment'></div>阁下今山甫也，凡某之言，阁下或以为然，则固某之幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1254406_comment'></div>以为不然，其委而置之，无俾某有好名之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1254406_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1254406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　上御史中丞辛次膺（起李）书，论“天下可忧者一，可虑者二”作品：《上辛中丞书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254398?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上辛中丞书<span class='inlineComment2'>（次膺）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254398")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254398_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254398'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254398'>某之得见于门下三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254398_comment'></div>始则阁下之在春官，某以妄应科目，贽其业而见焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254398_comment'></div>中则阁下帅闽而归，某为县于建安，以属部之吏而见焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254398_comment'></div>今也阁下召还于朝，居中执法之任，某亦滥预于百执事之列而复见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254398_comment'></div>踽踽而趋，寒暄而词，意阁下曾未省其面目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254398_comment'></div>阁下之名满天之下，某之愚仰慕盛德，固将卜其遇否，七年之间乃三见而不得致其言焉，亦异于古人一面而谈当世之事者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254398_comment'></div>今当世之事，非某所得谈也，虽然，不敢废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254398_comment'></div>盖天下可忧者一，可虑者二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254398_comment'></div>夫天下有所谓大计，有所谓先务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254398_comment'></div>先务审矣，馀则可以序而推之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254398_comment'></div>今国家不议其大计与其先务，而乃姑试为之，战则姑试而战也，和则姑试而和也，守则姑试而守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254398_comment'></div>朝夕自治者，徒欲百废具举，一旦缓急，计将若何，岂非可忧者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254398_comment'></div>主上之求治亦云切矣，然前日在藩邸，一二小臣使令于前，故得与议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254398_comment'></div>今有天下之大，则天下之才皆我用也，外廷之士曾未尽获进见，而左右近习日有闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254398_comment'></div>宰执侍从之贵，台谏一议则逐之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254398_comment'></div>内侍而典戎器，武臣而治榷酤，章四五上而几不可逐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254398_comment'></div>后有甚者，台谏之言何自入哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254398_comment'></div>此可虑之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254398_comment'></div>诸葛孔明有言：「亲贤臣，远小人，先汉所以兴隆也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254398_comment'></div>亲小人，远贤臣，后汉所以倾颓也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254398_comment'></div>人君之患，莫大于以近习为腹心而朝士为外人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254398_comment'></div>汉元帝有萧望之、刘向，不与之共政而乃任恭、显；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254398_comment'></div>唐文宗有裴度、李德裕，不与之谋事而乃委训、注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254398_comment'></div>后世观之，则固颠倒错谬，当时为之，未之觉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254398_comment'></div>盖小人得用之始，莫不言财利，其终则足以盗威权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254398_comment'></div>不言财利则人君无以谓其能，不盗威权则无以引奸邪而自助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254398_comment'></div>今主上励精庶政，每事欲亲而未得其要，涉于丛脞，则其间易入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254398_comment'></div>以酒坊一事言之，小人骎骎其倡财利之端矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254398_comment'></div>既已荐用人材，士大夫间岂得无刘、柳辈，傥复寖盛，安能保其不从哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254398_comment'></div>此可虑之二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254398_comment'></div>夫事固未至此，要将有以折其萌而削其根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254398_comment'></div>且以德寿宫官属观之，不选大臣从官为使，而独任宦者提举，宜其无所裨益，致私酤之谤闻于天下，而土木花石之运未已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254398_comment'></div>向使儒士参于其间，当必有规正者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254398_comment'></div>故某窃愿主上亦求儒士，以与谋事于宫中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254398_comment'></div>然士风不振已久，以为不肖而无过之可指，以为贤而无善之可议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254398_comment'></div>要之其才为无所用，徒欲偷懦苟容以侥倖于富贵者甚众，不大有以区别之，亦无补于国家之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254398_comment'></div>夫天下大计不定，人君之侧犹有小人间之，而士大夫风俗如此，阁下宜所深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254398_comment'></div>孟子曰：「惟大人为能格君心之非」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254398_comment'></div>夫格之者，渐之以言而后可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254398_comment'></div>以阁下操履之正，名节之伟，主上不即登之政路，而尚以屈耳目之寄，是盖欲朝夕闻阁下之言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254398_comment'></div>他人徒能言之，而阁下之言则能信于主上，安有不格者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254398_comment'></div>皇祐中，仁宗患台谏之任轻，王安简公以前执政命为中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254398_comment'></div>安简受而不辞，乃慨然论事，至留班以争张尧佐四使之除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254398_comment'></div>又言河朔根本之地，将帅之非其人者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254398_comment'></div>又言唐质肃之贬为过，而致言路不通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1254398_comment'></div>狄武襄不当任枢筦之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1254398_comment'></div>意气凛凛，廷臣为之耸动，仁宗谓其得风宪体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1254398_comment'></div>盖风宪之地，非老成重臣，无以振举大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1254398_comment'></div>而搏击琐细之论，世不乏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1254398_comment'></div>主上之待阁下，有符于仁祖矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1254398_comment'></div>阁下之自任，其无愧于安简！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1254398_comment'></div>意者造膝之言，有不得闻于外也，而某也北方之鄙人，守家世之训，不忍自同于流俗，犹复哓哓于阁下之门，多见其不知量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1254398_comment'></div>然就有道而正焉，斯学者之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1254398_comment'></div>故不敢自以为是，并以前者所上封事之副为献，惟阁下不鄙其愚而教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1254398_comment'></div>或谓其可取，因其言而陈之，则某之幸也，非敢望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1254398_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1254398_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　知抚州张孝祥（安国）葺鲁公堂，与闻，有诗达之。作品：《鲁公堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鲁公堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243544")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243544'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243544'>鲁公之节非一死，其谁碑之子曾子。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243544'>鲁公之德人未知，其谁堂之张紫微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243544'>继公作郡五百载，登堂思公宛如在。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243544'>江南遗墨处处传，鲁公去作麻姑仙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243544'>一杯相与借风月，但见云碧开池莲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243544'>紫微声名今第一，归上鸾台应不日。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243544'>笑谈千里无兵戎，临川草木生春风。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243544'>他年道傍儿女说，不思鲁公思张公。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243544'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_243544_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　徐度（敦立）奉祠，元吉代作谢表。作品：《代徐侍郎谢宫祠表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254328' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254328' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254328?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代徐侍郎谢宫祠表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254328")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254328_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254328'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254328'>典铨法从，久怀窃位之羞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254328_comment'></div>赋禄真祠，更遂养疴之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254328_comment'></div>恩辉逾厚，感涕何言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254328_comment'></div>伏念臣性本阔疏，才仍浅陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254328_comment'></div>早缘执戟，不为当路之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254328_comment'></div>晚预赐环，最取众人之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254328_comment'></div>使北庭于将变，持汉节以仅还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254328_comment'></div>擢副民曹，顾已亡于善状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254328_comment'></div>易司吏选，曾不畏于多言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254328_comment'></div>徒知肝胆之欲输，岂谓筋骸之难强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254328_comment'></div>衰颓弥甚，疢发动者两三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254328_comment'></div>灾患相仍，意不如者七八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254328_comment'></div>虽际飞龙之运，自甘退鹢之踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254328_comment'></div>尚轸皇慈，曲从私志，既假珍台之佚，复联书殿之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254328_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下德合无私，功存善贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254328_comment'></div>扩大明于日月，获望清光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254328_comment'></div>拯微命于风波，少安散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254328_comment'></div>示盖帷之罔弃，俾栈豆以知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254328_comment'></div>臣敢不益佩弦韦，自亲药石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254328_comment'></div>老马或知于道路，固绝望于驰驱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254328_comment'></div>犁牛无用于山川，第服勤于耒耨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254328_comment'></div>誓坚晚节，靡坠素风。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1254328_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='244ffe2b771a45478a2064153d01bf1c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("244ffe2b771a45478a2064153d01bf1c");'><span id='244ffe2b771a45478a2064153d01bf1c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1164')">1163-1164年</a>，46-47岁</div><div id='244ffe2b771a45478a2064153d01bf1c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年1月</a>　年初，进为司农寺丞。作品：《谢司农寺丞启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254432?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢司农寺丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254432")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254432_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254432'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254432'>入联簿正，已参列寺之华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254432_comment'></div>进贰司均，更冒部丞之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254432_comment'></div>知怜逾厚，愧负有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254432_comment'></div>伏念某才匪适时，学惟为己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254432_comment'></div>猿投林而竞啸，穷已弗任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254432_comment'></div>骥伏枥以长鸣，志徒未改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254432_comment'></div>轗轲技能之莫售，栖迟禄位以常淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254432_comment'></div>顷辞负弩之劳，亦预招弓之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254432_comment'></div>献言文陛，初何补于明时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254432_comment'></div>窃食太仓，乃滥叨于满岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254432_comment'></div>诘曲常思于避阱，聱龄岂惮于挥车！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254432_comment'></div>得路弹冠，嗟簿书之已暇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254432_comment'></div>闭门挟筴，较州县以过优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254432_comment'></div>方怀乞外以便亲，敢谓叙迁而易命！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254432_comment'></div>介之推未尝言禄，夫岂遐遗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254432_comment'></div>烛之武少不如人，孰云可用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254432_comment'></div>祗荷无私之化，曲推不施之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254432_comment'></div>激昂懦衷，奋励盛际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254432_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇仆射相公功存社稷，道洽生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254432_comment'></div>举天下一于仁，侔伊尹之重任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254432_comment'></div>拨乱世反之正，倚周公之迓衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254432_comment'></div>未忘特达之私，益示兼容之度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254432_comment'></div>某敢不誓全家法，恪奉官常？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254432_comment'></div>俾司万石之储，讵知报国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254432_comment'></div>倘守一经之旧，犹足事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254432_comment'></div>过此以还，未知攸措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254432_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1254432_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　送许尹知宣州。作品：《送许侍郎知宣州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243487' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243487' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243487?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送许侍郎知宣州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243487")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243487_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243487'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243487'>我公名满东西川，一持使节几十年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243487'>桥经万里坂九折，儿童学语知公贤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243487'>上皇诏下嗟见晚，归来荷橐趋甘泉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243487'>平生所学欲尽试，新语仅奏囊中篇<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：公献所著书，太上皇称善。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243487'>两淮破碎赖整理，百工蛊敝资镵镌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243487'>念公虽老猷自壮，何谓宜去请益坚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243487'>玉音三谕不可挽，一麾且复临江壖。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243487'>宣城景物今更妍，木瓜如瓠栗如拳。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243487'>敬亭山下蹑游屐，叠嶂楼中呼酒船。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243487'>谢公已往诗句在，公有妙语真齐肩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243487'>却招李白吊杜牧，收揽风月酬云烟。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243487'>中原未复敌未灭，政成请公须著鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243487'>吾君有意询黄发，庙堂之谋当万全。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243487'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_243487_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年4月</a>　上书张浚，主张“以和为疑之之策，以守为自强之计，以战为后日之图”作品：《谢张魏公书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢张魏公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254400")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254400'>某愚贱无似，比承少傅相公入觐，幸获趋拜屦舄之光，不量固陋，妄以狂瞽之言干渎严听，岂谓未赐诛责，特枉书教，慰藉甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254400_comment'></div>仰纫撝抑，下情岂胜悚惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254400_comment'></div>重惟国家安危之寄，元勋旧德，无出相公之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254400_comment'></div>主上躬不世之姿，志清中原，一时身任大事，为中外所仰，四夷所畏，亦孰踰相公者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254400_comment'></div>士挟区区一斑之见，岂真足以助经纶之素哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254400_comment'></div>惟其相公功成名遂之切，是以各务进其所有，以为门下献而忘其恧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254400_comment'></div>而相公又不自居其宏远高大而纳之，则天下之善，将举为相公用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254400_comment'></div>何往而不济！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254400_comment'></div>昔杨修、丁敬礼作文，好使他人润饰改定，曰：「文之佳丽，吾自得之，后世谁知定吾文者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254400_comment'></div>此言虽小，可以喻大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254400_comment'></div>恭惟相公功业之就，将自有之矣，后世谁知助相公以言者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254400_comment'></div>而不弃微贱，无拒之之意，盛德伟度，是以出此，故某抚衷自幸，而姑述以谢万分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1254400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　陆游（务观）出为镇江府通判，还绍兴，有诗赠行。作品：《送陆务观得倅镇江还越》二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243316' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243316' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243316?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送陆务观得倅镇江还越<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243316")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243316_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243316'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243316'>高文不试紫云楼，犹得声名动九州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243316_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243316'>金马渐登难避世，蓬莱已近却回舟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243316_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243316'>烧城赤口知何事，许国丹心惜未酬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243316_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243316'>归卧镜湖聊洗眼，雨馀万壑正争流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243316_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243316'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243316_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243315?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243315'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243315'>前年边马饮江水，烽火瓜州一水间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243315'>正使楼船多战士，要须京岘作重关。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243315'>平戎得路可横槊，佐郡经时应赐环。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243315'>把酒赋诗甘露寺，眼中那更有金山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243315'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　友人李鼐（仲镇）作室名“懒窠”，有诗赠之。作品：《李仲镇懒窠》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李仲镇懒窠<span class='inlineComment2'>（癸未年作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243442")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243442'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243442'>我性天下懒，自谓世莫双。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243442'>朅来官中都，懒极济以憃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243442'>有如千黑鱼，东西转桥矼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243442'>又如橐驼卧，厌逐群吠尨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243442'>鼻洟任纵横，胞转徒膀肛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243442'>纷纷夸夺儿，见我语辄哤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243442'>平生李公子，老大同乡邦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243442'>奈何夺我有，收敛付一窗。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243442'>作窠寓以名，异音乃同腔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243442'>金马可避世，何殊鹿门庞。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243442'>君看富贵涂，机危甚缘橦。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243442'>争荣仅锱铢，力欲九鼎扛。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243442'>金朱拥丹毂，视之亦蝼蛖。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243442'>爱君阳羡居，有田种兰茳。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243442'>溪山带城郭，松竹环旌幢。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243442'>连娟几脩眉，清歌艳明釭。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243442'>客至即尽醉，不待金石撞。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243442'>尚馀诗语工，词源倒三江。<div id='poem_sentence_17_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_243442'>好懒得真懒，使我心益降。<div id='poem_sentence_18_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_243442'>何时半作分，临流听琤淙。<div id='poem_sentence_19_243442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_243442'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_243442_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　有词寄知平江府张孝祥（安国）作品：《临江仙·寄张安国》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>寄张安国</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243588")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243588'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243588'>自古文章贤太守，江南只数苏州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243588'>而今太守更风流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243588'>熏香开画阁，迎月上西楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243588_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243588'>见说宫妆高髻拥，司空却是遨头。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243588'>五湖莫便具扁舟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243588'>玉堂红蕊在，还胜百花洲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_243588_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　八月底或九月初，其兄元龙（子云）出守池州，有诗送行。作品：《清旷亭送子云得有字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243527' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243527' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243527?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清旷亭送子云得有字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243527")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243527_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243527'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243527'>欢期苦难逢，离别乃易久。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243527'>天涯老兄弟，况复亲白首。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243527'>田园固不足，功名亦何有。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243527'>今年送兄行，正尔作太守。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243527'>池阳古名郡，地控大江口。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243527'>舟来武昌鱼，车载桑落酒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243527'>登临得齐山，端不负重九。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243527'>公馀亦堪乐，尚有此客否。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243527'>天威动江淮，狂寇行授首。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243527'>努力幸驰驱，腰看印如斗。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243527'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_243527_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年10月</a>　朱熹（元晦）入对，除武学博士，待次，还闽，有诗送行。作品：《送朱元晦》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243484?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送朱元晦</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243484")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243484_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243484'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243484'>前年恨君不肯来，今年惜君不肯住。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243484'>朝廷多事四十年，愚智由来各千虑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243484'>君来正值求言日，三策直前真谏疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243484'>诋诃百事推圣学，请复国雠施一怒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243484'>天高听远语不酬，袖手翩然寻故步。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243484'>我知君是谏诤才，主上聪明得无误。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243484'>一纸底用教鹖冠，百战应当启戎辂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243484'>江山千里正风雪，岁月峥嵘倏将暮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243484'>有田可耕屋盖头，君计未疏吾亦去。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243484'>君归为谢武夷君，白马摇鞭定何处。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243484'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_243484_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　上侍御史周操（元持）札子，乞奏朝廷蠲除福建诸州“钞盐钱”及“上供银”等弊害。作品：《上周侍御札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254397' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254397' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254397?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上周侍御劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254397")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254397_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254397'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254397'>某伏睹正月二十五日圣旨，以福建六州地震，令本路帅臣监司条具民间利病，措置宽恤事件，疾速闻奏，有以见主上勤恤民隐，祗畏天戒，欲海峤之民安于田里，德至渥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254397_comment'></div>如闻本路仅以琐尾数事应诏，曾未副圣主焦劳之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254397_comment'></div>某尝仕于闽，见其民之贫者莫甚于上四州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254397_comment'></div>其为害者莫若二事，一曰钞盐钱，二曰上供银。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254397_comment'></div>是二者无岁不有诉讼，省部阴知其说，监司明睹其患，以经费所在为不可去，曾不知其弊亦有可去者焉，请试陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254397_comment'></div>所谓钞盐钱者，景祐元年才十万贯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254397_comment'></div>元丰二年始增六万贯，然三分之二则容人入纳于榷货务而兴贩者也，一分则漕司般卖以充上四州岁计者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254397_comment'></div>自绍兴三年住罢客钞，漕司认钱十五万贯，欲专其利，则州县向来一分岁计，自合从本司抱认，不可暗增一分于钞盐之内而使州县别添岁计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254397_comment'></div>既不逐纲取拨，又不论奏豁除，乃接续增添至三十万贯，州县大困输纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254397_comment'></div>后因提刑吴逵申请，仅减八万贯，今犹二十二万贯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254397_comment'></div>四州之地，从横千里，运盐之数无穷而食盐之家有限，上司期会，急于星火，州县不得已，往往随产钱科于平民，下户科于耆保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254397_comment'></div>议者徒知卖盐违法，不知势当如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254397_comment'></div>所谓上供银者，祖宗以来福建有岁额钱二十万贯，熙宁二年始令买银。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254397_comment'></div>时价低小，一贯止得一两，故为银二十万两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254397_comment'></div>其后银价虽增而银额不减，蔡京修崇宁上供格，遂定为福建路上供银。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254397_comment'></div>建炎初，宣谕朱廙尝指言之，州县犹有馀钱，陪贴收买，以及二十万两之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254397_comment'></div>近年科名日增，银价日倍，州县不复有馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254397_comment'></div>故下四州之银取于僧寺，上四州之银取于民户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254397_comment'></div>其取于僧寺者不过削其徒之食，犹未甚害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254397_comment'></div>取于民户者，则以盐折之，而仅偿其半价，拘催督迫，铢两毕输，器物钗珥，杂然并陈，受纳之际，恻然可哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254397_comment'></div>议者徒知买银违法，不知势亦当如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254397_comment'></div>绍兴三十年，转运副使王时升始见钞盐之弊，乃献本司钱三十万缗，以补州县三十五年以后积欠钞盐钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254397_comment'></div>近者转运判官王瀹、陈弥作等，始见上供银之弊，又献本司钱二十七万馀缗，以代上四州今岁上供银，使不得科敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254397_comment'></div>为监司者，用心亦可嘉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254397_comment'></div>然止是暂宽州县目前之急，不能为一路永远之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254397_comment'></div>今欲为一路永远之利者，莫若以钞盐钱俾漕司，岁认其半，其馀责之州县，则于朝廷经费初无所损，而州县实受其赐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254397_comment'></div>或谓若使漕司岁认，恐不能办，曾不知福建漕司自罢钞盐，而运纲所得增盐之利甚多，又有米麦他色科名之入，前者兴造不绝，妄用百出，众所共知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254397_comment'></div>时升辈自三十年十一月至今年二月，实及三年，所献通计五十七万馀缗，是每岁可馀十九万缗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254397_comment'></div>钞盐三之一不过七万三千缗，上供银之半不过十二万缗，正可了办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254397_comment'></div>如漕司果不肯认，则乞委之他司或专命一官，俾稽考覈实本路财赋出入之数，不务收其羡馀，惟在必行，去此二弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254397_comment'></div>然后稍减州县盐纲，命逐纲取拨钞盐钱，以时出卖，不得科卖于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254397_comment'></div>今州县上供银，以常年所给之半，并今年漕司所认之半，足可尽还其价，而不得科买于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254397_comment'></div>宿弊顿除，财用亦足，易咨怨为欢谣，革厚敛为宽政，和气洋溢，岂不消变异于远方哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254397_comment'></div>恭以侍御尝持节于彼，则一路之费所宜动心，可以言而无疑，而某言之则似有嫌，是以不若告诸左右，伏惟幸察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1254397_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　二三月间，除度支郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年4月</a>　兼淮西宣谕司参议官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　上书汤思退言淮甸事。作品：《论淮甸札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254358?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论淮甸劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254358")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254358'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254358'>某窃见朝廷博询筹策，欲以经理淮甸为守御之计，此最自治之先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254358_comment'></div>似闻诸将之议，有欲移庐州于舒州、和州于西关、光、濠、安丰于横涧，而列城栅于淮上者，有谓移并州郡，未蒙永远之利，先受目前之扰，姑以山寨扼险、屯兵聚粮以备缓急者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254358_comment'></div>虽侍从台谏方议其事，下位小官不当妄预，然苟有所见，幸今公道既开，安可辄避刍荛之贱，隐默不告？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254358_comment'></div>惟钧慈略其进越之罪而试详焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254358_comment'></div>某以为前之说既不可行，而后之说为未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254358_comment'></div>盖前之说徒知以地为险者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254358_comment'></div>庐州地虽平坦，昔刘仁赡盖尝守寿州矣，王师有不能下，即今庐之寿州县是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254358_comment'></div>庐州不移于寿春县而移于舒州，是退避之谋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254358_comment'></div>和州之有东西关，此控扼之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254358_comment'></div>至于横涧等处，虽有险阻，皆非可为州郡之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254358_comment'></div>又况敌方遣使议和，两淮流亡次第归业，一旦骤移数州于内地，人心岂不动摇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254358_comment'></div>且诸将尚以京东、河北招讨为名，而吾之措置若此，何以慰中原之望哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254358_comment'></div>此所谓不可行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254358_comment'></div>中原未得，则淮甸吾之藩篱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254358_comment'></div>淮甸不固，大江岂可备御？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254358_comment'></div>今若寂然无所经画，听州郡之自为，特恃山寨、水寨以为退保之策，且虽列栅置戍，不过二百人，骑不过三十匹，而无大兵以为重镇，缓急有警，则糜溃奔骇犹前日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254358_comment'></div>然则今日之策，当议重兵于淮上，而列栅置戍，以为营田，州郡略其名而务其实，则犹可哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254358_comment'></div>何谓重兵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254358_comment'></div>绍兴之初，一军驻楚州，一军驻和州，一军驻庐州，角立相应，北人亦莫之敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254358_comment'></div>自和好之兴，不许驻兵淮上，故移江左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254358_comment'></div>今诸将豢于宴安者二十年，惟知江左屯驻之便，未有肯过江而戍者，朝廷安可不为之计哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254358_comment'></div>若徒以一二千人分屯淮上，而大军止驻建康、镇江，则淮甸未见其可保也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254358_comment'></div>何谓置戍以为营田？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254358_comment'></div>夫营田之不可为者，诸将不欲耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254358_comment'></div>若使诸将于营田，每择人遣之，如耕其私田，则营田之效久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254358_comment'></div>军兴以来，一二大将置庄于淮甸，动至数万石，所耕皆荒田，所用皆军人也，而国家独不可哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254358_comment'></div>今若募人杂军士以为营田，而择军中所汰使臣可委者领之，即其地以为堡栅，籍其丁以为弓箭手，命所掌使臣以为知城寨官，则淮南之地不日可尽耕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254358_comment'></div>何谓州郡略其名？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254358_comment'></div>盖淮南州郡有不若江左一县者多矣，人民未集，财赋未充，命一太守则必有供给之奉，公帑之须，招兵置吏之冗，所费多矣，且又难得资序相当之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254358_comment'></div>岂若姑以倚郭知县兼军使而守之，而并省其外县，择京官选人可用者不次而用，则名废而实举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254358_comment'></div>凡此三说，某所臆断，恐无以裨庙谟之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254358_comment'></div>恭惟钧造择而行之，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1254358_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年6月23日</a>　为淮西宣谕使王之望以“向为宣谕司参议官，招权妄作”劾罢。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='971ade6e86ac4e5baff29d520d729b36_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("971ade6e86ac4e5baff29d520d729b36");'><span id='971ade6e86ac4e5baff29d520d729b36_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>，48岁</div><div id='971ade6e86ac4e5baff29d520d729b36' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年2月</a>　陆游将二人唱和之作结集，名《京口唱和集》并作序。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6ae007f97ce2467a83890e3016ef8858_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6ae007f97ce2467a83890e3016ef8858");'><span id='6ae007f97ce2467a83890e3016ef8858_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1166')">1165-1166年</a>，48-49岁</div><div id='6ae007f97ce2467a83890e3016ef8858' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　有诗寄其兄元龙。作品：《寄别子云》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243365?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄别子云</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243365")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243365'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243365'>江干风雪敝貂裘，兄弟相看已白头。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243365'>两月追随无十日，一春离别甚三秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243365'>清时官职难频窃，异县田园合早求。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243365'>并戏母前端有日，省郎虽美不如州。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243365'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243365_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　陈康伯（长卿）卒，有挽词。作品：《故赠太师丞相文恭陈公挽词三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243281?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故赠太师丞相文恭陈公挽词三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243281")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243281'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243281'>拱揖消狂寇，从容奉两宫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243281'>临危几谢傅，忍事实娄公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243281'>陶冶无偏党，经纶尽朴忠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243281'>再来金鼎地，高卧亦成功。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243281'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243281_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243280' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243280?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243280_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243280'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243280'>扶疾祗严诏，邦基整屡危。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243280'>紫宸朝奏事，黄阁暮兴悲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243280'>德望仪千载，恩荣冠一时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243280'>石龟山下路，谁为记丰碑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243280'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243280_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243279' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243279' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243279?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243279_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243279'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243279'>凛凛循良吏，休休一介臣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243279'>投艰推宇量，御侮赖精神。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243279'>给侍恩虽渥，怀归志莫伸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243279'>平泉开甲第，花木未经春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243279'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243279_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　时诸军冒滥功赏，奸弊百端，元吉上札子建议限期许之自营，免罪改正。作品：《论诸军冒赏札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论诸军冒赏劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254356")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254356'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254356'>伏见朝廷比修军政，汰拣冗籍，更易将帅，威令复振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254356_comment'></div>惟是功赏一事，如出战、暴露、从卫、守把之类，项目颇多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254356_comment'></div>昨缘将帅非人，保明奏请之间不无伪冒，或增减功效，或添入姓名，受赂不公，任情轻重，奸弊百端，时有陈告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254356_comment'></div>近据殿前司白旗子队谭进告论鲁真等、前军使臣张仪告论洪盛等、马军司左军蔡仲告论田俊等，蒙朝廷送大理寺究治，委是告论得实，虽已将冒赏人追夺元官资，并保明不实将佐并降官行遣外，窃虑诸军尚有似此冒滥之人，若不措置许之自首，深恐日后告论稍多，有失行伍上下之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254356_comment'></div>欲望朝廷备坐行下三衙并驻劄诸军，大字出榜，晓谕逐军寨门，如有似此功赏不实，已转官资，或申奏未下之人并元保明不实将佐，并候指挥到限一月日，许经逐军或所在官司尽行陈告，并与免罪改正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254356_comment'></div>如出限不首，却致因事发露，定将犯人并保明将佐取旨重作施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254356_comment'></div>庶得不致引惹告讦，而军无滥赏，有以激劝实立功效之人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1254356_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　陆游（务观）改任隆兴府通判，元吉有序达其任所。作品：《送陆务观序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送陆务观序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254469")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254469'>凡世俗所慕于爵禄富贵者，必有贤人君子所尝居之官，相与诵叹，以为美谈而不释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254469_comment'></div>言郡守指黄霸，言县令指卓茂，言别驾指庞统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254469_comment'></div>夫霸与茂之云者，以其为丞相、为太傅，于向之所为爵禄富贵，诚有之也，而统则疑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254469_comment'></div>且统自以兴风俗、长道业、论帝王之策为己任，其视诸葛孔明实伯仲间人，而当时遂谓一别驾可展其骥足，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254469_comment'></div>夫蜀岩国也，其壤地褊蹙，无以容天下之士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254469_comment'></div>其官列弗备，无以尽天下之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254469_comment'></div>彼治中、别驾，几盛世六卿矣，后徒以其人而慕焉，殆亦可悲也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254469_comment'></div>国家之制，自卿相至一命几级，自台阁至州县几阶，自王畿至于穷荒绝徼几万里也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254469_comment'></div>朝与一官，夕畀一职，曾未足伤朝廷之大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254469_comment'></div>旦而引之东隅，暮而寘诸西陲，亦无害幅员之广也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254469_comment'></div>吾友陆务观之移倅豫章也，则又有疑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254469_comment'></div>然豫章大府也，为连帅之贰，以兼制兵民之重，此固周瑜、鲁肃所望，于统而不可得者，而吾务观得之，抑又何疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254469_comment'></div>盖务观之于丹扬则既为贰矣，迩而迁之远，辅郡而易之藩方，其官称小大无改于旧，则又使之冒六月之暑，抗风涛之险，病妻弱子，左饘右药，不异于醝荈之商，揭囊而贾赢，造物其安取此也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254469_comment'></div>夫以务观之才，与其文章议论，颉颃于论思侍从之选，必有知其先后者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254469_comment'></div>既未获逞，下得一郡而施，亦庶几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254469_comment'></div>岂士之进退必有时哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254469_comment'></div>圣天子在上，二三贤隽在列，不谓之时不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254469_comment'></div>然务观舟败几溺，而书来诧曰，平生未行江也，葭苇之苍茫，凫雁之出没，风月之清绝，山水之夷旷，畴昔尝寓于诗而未尽其髣髴者，今幸遭之，必毋为我戚戚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254469_comment'></div>盖其志尚不凡如此，吾犹为之戚戚而言，亦不知务观者耶？</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1254469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　是年，与晁公武（子止）交往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　进左司员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　上札子极论和糴之弊。作品：《论和糴札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254354' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254354' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254354?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论和籴劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254354")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254354_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254354'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254354'>窃见近缘江西湖南旱伤，上供米斛恐至不足，朝廷支降钱银会子，就浙西、江东、淮南丰熟去处收籴，以充大农之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254354_comment'></div>其银并会子，并依街市现行价数纽计，仍以足㪷算为省㪷，非不详尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254354_comment'></div>而州郡不能措置，漕司失于拘催，或户部所拨钱间有未到，仍不画时申请，例成科敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254354_comment'></div>似闻平江府诸县，每石止支钱六百文，其馀州郡，有既支价钱，继行追减数百文，以符合漕司纳定之价者，每石有加耗三㪷者，有依苗米例收取漕司出剩者，有尅钱四百文充水脚靡费者，此浙西之弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254354_comment'></div>江东一石始支四贯省，近却止作二贯省，已支者亦皆追取，而建康人户来诉，犹是一贯省科籴一石，又闻每贯更尅头脚等钱，此江东之弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254354_comment'></div>舒州之民，不惮千里，经省投状，乞免和籴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254354_comment'></div>滁、和、无为等州，亦甚困扰，闻每石只支一贯五百省，此淮南之弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254354_comment'></div>而皆妄称系有指挥，嫁怨于公上，岂朝廷和籴之意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254354_comment'></div>欲望敷奏，特赐处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254354_comment'></div>其浙西诸郡，须管尽数支还价钱，已支者不得追减，并不得加量耗米及尅留水脚靡费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254354_comment'></div>若江东则已减二十万石，所支钱银，可令通融收籴三十万石之数，亦不得辄收头脚等钱，委朝士之在江淮者覈实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254354_comment'></div>淮南米价，依数支给，尤须加意，盖淮甸边面，二税犹不尽起，岂宜横有科歛如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254354_comment'></div>然亦恐三路价钱，或有未敷起纲之费，颇不能办，即乞降圣旨，更捐十万缗以补之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254354_comment'></div>傥有违戾，令御史台察举，其守令、监司，悉行罢黜，以为不恤民力、不知体国者之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254354_comment'></div>夫江西、湖南既已均被赈廪之恩，而浙右、江淮谷贱伤农，却蒙均籴之惠，则和气四达，今岁之丰，可不卜而知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254354_comment'></div>天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1254354_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　李远（器之）赠诗卷，有诗答之。作品：《李器之惠诗卷》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李编修器之惠诗卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243443")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243443'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243443'>尘埃仆仆日走趋，胸中倒悬一字无。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243443'>迫人簿领推不去，眼明忽见千骊珠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243443'>矍然惊呼此诗欤，如醒乍解病获苏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243443'>归来明灯喜无寐，手不忍释自卷舒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243443'>语新格健意有馀，风骨峭硬中含腴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243443'>猛如横阵舞刀槊，清若雅宴调笙竽。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243443'>我穷已极君益迂，学此似费千金屠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243443'>前有太白后长吉，君家诗名宜复初。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243443'>明明天子开石渠，叹我短后追长裾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243443'>时平合第从臣颂，请君早上承明庐。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243443'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_243443_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　陆游（务观）以言者论其“力说张浚用兵”罢归，有诗寄来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年6月</a>　除直秘阁，出为江南东路转运判官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='078f852150db4b068e892bb59fe502f9_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年7月</a>　七月中下旬，改除大理少卿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　其兄元龙（子云）有诗见寄，答之。作品：《次韵子云送儿女至昭亭见寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243426' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243426' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243426?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵子云送儿女至昭亭见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243426")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243426_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243426'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243426'>岩岩昭亭山，度岁一再行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243426'>吾亲在其下，有路如砥平。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243426'>风物岁时佳，岂问楚与荆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243426'>胡为不得往，使我涕泗横。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243426'>出身备王官，敢自颓家声。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243426'>圣皇察庶狱，小大必以情。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243426'>哀矜且勿喜，死当使之生。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243426'>念昔栖闽陬，孤童共营营。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243426'>菽水曾几何，青紫望一经。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243426'>弟兄亦云幸，假节仍专城。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243426'>别离乃频有，仆奴费邀迎。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243426'>安仁赋閒居，要自贤西征。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243426'>板舆日欢侍，儿女森在庭。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243426'>岂比隔山岳，空书问安宁。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243426'>薄田可负郭，不归定谁令。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243426'>壮士志中原，边尘暗幽并。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243426'>拟蹑冒顿居，端谋渭南耕。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243426'>书生复何事，三入老承明。<div id='poem_sentence_17_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_243426'>应知当馈叹，廊庙资扶倾。<div id='poem_sentence_18_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_243426'>忍作寒蝉喑，愿为威凤鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_19_243426_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_243426'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_243426_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年8月16日</a>　奏大理狱空，有诏奖谕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年10月</a>　族祖韩球（美成）妻李夫人于信州建家庙崇福庵，十月，元吉为记。作品：《崇福庵记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>崇福庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254552")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254552'>古者葬而不封，盖远之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254552_comment'></div>中古而降，则既封矣，然墓而弗祭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254552_comment'></div>成周之礼则祭矣，故冢人祭墓为尸，然未有守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254552_comment'></div>其曰守墓禁与墓大夫之职，皆典其禁令而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254552_comment'></div>两汉而下，守墓之家始有闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254552_comment'></div>夫葬而封，封而祭，祭而守，岂后世之俗寖不逮于古欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254552_comment'></div>亦曰礼之变而无悖者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254552_comment'></div>谨其兆域之原，护其松槚之植，易其庐而屋焉，假人而掌之，子孙岁时必至而不敢忘，圣人复起，宜有取乎此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254552_comment'></div>自浮图氏之说兴，士大夫之家欲守其坟墓者，率致其徒，国家著令，从而许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254552_comment'></div>其爵算有不得命为寺，则亦自筑精舍，选择一二而处焉，以为较之丁壮而无妻孥之累，洁齐寂净，庶以严乎鬼享也，天下之俗几何幸哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254552_comment'></div>秘阁修撰韩公之为都大提点坑冶铸钱也，当绍兴之十五年，请于朝曰，所领凡九路，不可以谋尺寸之产，惟母太硕人郑之丧未葬，将卜地于信州上饶县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254552_comment'></div>诏俞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254552_comment'></div>于是兆于明远乡禅寂院之东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254552_comment'></div>无几何，公使于蜀，又帅于夔，而不幸捐馆舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254552_comment'></div>绍兴之二十年，其继室李夫人奉公之柩祔窆焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254552_comment'></div>越五年，于墓左始为屋数十楹，以处浮图氏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254552_comment'></div>又十有三年，益大葺之，范金为钟，楼居其上，门闼室宇，以备以严，视佛庙之规，虽微而体具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254552_comment'></div>始山未有泉，庀工之日，斸土而泉涌，已而有露降于墓木而甘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254552_comment'></div>夫人嘅叹，谓其有物阴相之也，因名曰崇福庵，买牒而度为僧者三人，买田以赡夫僧者踰六十亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254552_comment'></div>盖韩氏家许昌，渡江而南，坟墓既不可族矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254552_comment'></div>修撰公蚤以才谞自奋，历尚书郎，宣力四方，隐然为时吏师，而不得世其贵，以尽发其蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254552_comment'></div>平生未尝营产业，仅克有地以葬其亲，而身没数千里外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254552_comment'></div>取二犹子子之，繇夫人而后家道立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254552_comment'></div>夫人间关东归，既教其子以诗书，而躬布衣粝食，翛然自得，以从浮图氏之学，凡舍宅之外，悉捐其赀，以为是庵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254552_comment'></div>尝曰吾夫之力所不及者，吾以一妇人之力，阅二十寒暑而卒成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254552_comment'></div>修撰公讳球，字美成，于某为祖父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254552_comment'></div>某寓于信，亲见夫人遇事有法，可以为难，故为道礼之变，且述夫人之志以示后之子孙，俾知孝云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254552_comment'></div>乾道四年十月，右朝散郎、守大理少卿韩某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1254552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　送张子颜（几仲）知泰州。作品：《送张几仲知泰州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张几仲知泰州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243308")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243308'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年11月28日</a>　有诏与修《绍兴新法》<br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　服除，至临安复官。任左司郎中提领榷务都茶场。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　清明后一日，与范成大等人游西湖。作品：《清明后一日同诸友湖上值雨》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清明后一日同诸友湖上值雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_243377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243377'>弱柳自随烟际绿，幽花还傍雨边明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
