id='poem_sentence_3_243377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243377'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243377_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年5月</a>　女螺夭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年8月</a>　兼权中书舍人。作品：《辞权中书舍人札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年8月</a>　八月下旬，应诏荐举王师愈（与正）、周炯、崔敦诗（大雅）作品：《应诏举所知状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254349' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254349' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254349?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应诏举所知状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254349")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254349_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254349'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254349'>具位某准尚书省劄子节文，诏台谏侍从各举所知一二人，疏其事实，可以充是何职任，八月二十三日，三省同奉圣旨依奏者，今具如后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254349_comment'></div>一、左奉议郎、前权发遣信州军州事王师愈，曾任潭州长沙知县，委有政绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254349_comment'></div>诸司列荐，继为严、信两郡，戢吏爱民，不扰而办治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254349_comment'></div>持论疏通，耻为无用之学，堪充郎官以上职任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254349_comment'></div>一、右宣教郎、新差通判随州军州事周炯，曾任信州弋阳知县，摧抑豪强，不避怨谤，继移祁门、休宁两县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254349_comment'></div>持身廉介，遇事严明，吏畏而民爱，催科并依省限先足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254349_comment'></div>堪充郡守监司职任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254349_comment'></div>一、左文林郎、两浙路转运司干办公事崔敦诗，服勤州县，不废古文，所撰《国朝铙歌鼓吹曲》，笔力雄健，有唐柳宗元风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254349_comment'></div>又尝为《资治通鉴要览》七十卷，贯穿该洽，议论醇正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254349_comment'></div>堪充馆阁职任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254349_comment'></div>右，臣所举，并是诣实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254349_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1254349_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　跋尹焞《论语解》作品：《书尹和靖论语后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书尹和靖论语后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254500")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254500'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254500'>和靖先生《论语解》，词极简严，将俾学者深味其旨而有所自得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254500_comment'></div>乾道庚寅岁，某忧居上饶，过先生门人王德修，问此书亡恙，且曰：「子异时官守，不刊行之耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254500_comment'></div>某于是愧其言，会明年复将官中都，度未可辑也，乃以旧年兄弟手所抄本往累故人赵德庄于建安，庶可成焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254500_comment'></div>昔和靖尝云少从伊川先生学《易》，时伊川出《易传》七十馀家，和靖茫然未知所从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254500_comment'></div>伊川曰：「日观一爻可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254500_comment'></div>继有所质问，伊川色庄而气严，未尝语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254500_comment'></div>或曰：「未也，姑求之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254500_comment'></div>已而意有所会，伊川始忻然为之剖析诸传，而伸以己说，盖终身不忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254500_comment'></div>故其诲人，亦欲如此，此书所以简严者欤？</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1254500_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年1月17日</a>　奏请完善并严格执行《牙人法》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年2月4日</a>　有旨依旧兼权中书舍人，元吉以非科举出身再辞。作品：《二月再辞札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254363?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又二月再辞权中书舍人劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年2月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254363")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254363'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254363'>某伏准尚书省劄子，今月四日，三省同奉圣旨，某依旧兼权中书舍人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254363_comment'></div>重念某昨蒙指挥，缘林机差充接送伴，时暂兼权上件职事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254363_comment'></div>今来系正有窠阙，而某以无出身人，尚兹摄承，恐贻众议，欲望朝廷特赐敷奏，别行选差，以安愚分，不胜厚幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1254363_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年2月25日</a>　除权吏部侍郎。作品：《辞除权吏部侍郎奏状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span>《再辞奏状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254341?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞除权吏部侍郎奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年2月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254341")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254341_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254341'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254341'>右，臣伏准尚书省劄子，二月二十五日，三省同奉圣旨，韩某可除权吏部侍郎，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254341_comment'></div>臣闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254341_comment'></div>伏念臣禀资愚戆，赋分奇穷，五叨宰掾之华，九阅岁躔之换。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254341_comment'></div>比更忧患，尤觉病衰，逮兹隶职之期年，不胜旷官而愒日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254341_comment'></div>方欲自祈于远外，敢期忽被于褒迁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254341_comment'></div>揆之私谊则非宜，质之公论则未称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254341_comment'></div>况准铨部，尤号剧曹，倘微通鍊之才，曷任甄平之寄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254341_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下，曲垂渊鉴，俯亮危诚，别求当代之俊髦，以副一时之器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254341_comment'></div>吁天之切，请命惟期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254341_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254341_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1254341_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1254342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再辞奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年2月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254342")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254342'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254342'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，以臣辞免除权吏部侍郎恩命，奉圣旨不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254342_comment'></div>臣以疏远迂陋之质，家世荷国厚恩，今蒙陛下拔擢，俾列贰卿，在臣么么，可谓荣遇，不当固有辞避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254342_comment'></div>重念臣才力不能逾人，学问无以异众，自还宰士之列，复承词掖之虚，狂言屡发而每被矜容，孤踪久滞而尤加轸恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254342_comment'></div>然群彦方疑于去就，而微臣独冒于迁除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254342_comment'></div>虽夙恃于圣知，恐难免于众议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254342_comment'></div>况班列之中，多有在臣上者，遽兹超躐，尤不遑安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254342_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下廓天地之量，回日月之明，察臣粗守朴忠，怜臣素祈静退，收还成命，改畀真材，使之宣力于四方，尚能仰答于鸿造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254342_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254342_comment'></div>所有恩命，未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254342_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1254342_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　举苏峤（季真）自代。作品：《举苏峤自代状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254348' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254348?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举苏峤自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254348")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254348'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254348'>具位某准令，诸侍从授讫，三日内举官一员充自代者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254348_comment'></div>右，臣伏睹右朝奉郎、尚书吏部员外郎苏峤，议论坚明，操履纯正，名臣之裔，绰有典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254348_comment'></div>臣实不如，举以自代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254348_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1254348_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　是春，送叶衡（梦锡）赴任荆南。作品：《送叶梦锡赴荆南》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243303' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243303' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243303?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送叶梦锡赴荆南</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243303")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243303_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243303'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243303'>南郡开边古上流，君王侧席用嘉谋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243303_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243303'>壮怀何止入云梦，雄略行看半九州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243303_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243303'>风劲鼓声连岸动，雪晴江影与天浮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243303_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243303'>一樽莫作新亭语，勋业归庸尚黑头。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243303_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243303'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243303_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年4月2日</a>　以位列从班，援例祀及五世，作文祭告祖先。作品：《作主告庙文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>作主告庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年4月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254643")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254643'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254643'>粤乾道八年，岁次壬辰，四月己亥朔，初二日庚子，孙男具位云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254643_comment'></div>某祗荷先训，兹冒从班，稽摭礼经，祀及五世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254643_comment'></div>爰以孟夏初吉，作主于庙，涓日告迁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1254643_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年4月</a>　四月庚申，应和州守胡元功之请，为张孝祥诗集作序。作品：《张安国诗集序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254476?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张安国诗集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254476")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254476'>诗之作，得于志之所寓，而形于言者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254476_comment'></div>周《诗》既亡，屈平始为《离骚》，荀卿、宋玉又为之赋，其实诗之馀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254476_comment'></div>至其托物引喻，愤惋激烈，有风雅所未备，比兴所未及，而皆出于楚人之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254476_comment'></div>后之学者，执笔跂慕，而终身不能道其一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254476_comment'></div>或曰楚之地富于东南，其山川之清淑，草木之英秀，文人才士遇而有感，足以发其情致而动其精思，故言语辄妙，可以歌咏而流行，岂特楚人之风哉，亦山川之气或使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254476_comment'></div>自唐以来，诗人寖盛，有得于天才之自然者，有资于学问而成之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254476_comment'></div>然才之不足，不能卓越宏大，则失之浅近而无法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254476_comment'></div>学之不至，不能研深雅奥，则失之蹈袭而无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254476_comment'></div>舍李、杜而降，咸有可议者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254476_comment'></div>呜呼，若吾安国之诗，其几于天才之自然者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254476_comment'></div>安国少举进士，出语已惊人，未尝习为诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254476_comment'></div>既而取高第，遂自西掖兼直北门，迫于应用之文，其诗虽间出，犹未大肆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254476_comment'></div>逮夫少憩金陵，徜徉湖阴，浮湘江，上漓水，历衡山，而望九疑，泛洞庭，泊荆渚，其欢愉感慨，莫不什于诗，好事者称叹，以为殆不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254476_comment'></div>盖周游几千里，岂吾所谓发其情致而动其精思，真楚人之遗意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254476_comment'></div>虽然，安国之诗清婉而俊逸，其机杼错综如茧之方丝，其步骤蹀躞如骥之始驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254476_comment'></div>若天假之年，施藻火而御和鸾，其谁曰不宜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254476_comment'></div>惜其不幸蚤世，予尝欲为之哀词，悼其平生，未果也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254476_comment'></div>历阳胡使君元功，集安国诗，得若干篇，将刻而传之，以慰其乡闾之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254476_comment'></div>又掇其歌词，以附于后，属予序引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254476_comment'></div>予于是收涕而怀，有不忍述者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254476_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254476_comment'></div>士大夫或未识安国，咏其诗而歌其词，襟韵洒落，宛其如在，亦足以悲其志之所寓，而知其为一世之隽杰人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254476_comment'></div>乾道八年四月庚申，颍川韩某序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1254476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年4月</a>　是月，诏令疏决罪犯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年5月</a>　五月己丑，跋邓润甫（温伯、圣求）除拜帖。作品：《跋邓圣求除拜帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋邓圣求除拜帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254481")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254481'>邓安惠公制册深厚宏雅，自成一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254481_comment'></div>东坡先生相与酬唱，尝并直玉堂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254481_comment'></div>逮其拜辖，乃假手贺之，岂应用之文，特礼不可废者，或欲试其门人笔语能道己意否耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254481_comment'></div>乾道壬辰五月己丑，颍川韩某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1254481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年5月</a>　时孝宗宠信近习张说，任其为签书枢密院事，朝臣因反对而被逐者甚众，是年五月，元吉进故事以讽谏。作品：《壬辰五月进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷11。）</span><div id='poem_1254511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬辰五月进故事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254511")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254511'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254511'>《国史·薛居正传》，太祖尝谓居正曰：「自古为君者鲜克正己，为臣者多无远识，盖君臣之道，不得其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254511_comment'></div>吾爱唐太宗受人谏疏，直抵其非而不耻，以朕所见，不若自不为之，使人无异词也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254511_comment'></div>又《吕蒙正传》，太宗谓蒙正曰：「古所谓君臣道合者，情无间尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254511_comment'></div>故事必无隐，而言皆从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254511_comment'></div>今既列于位，得以献可替否，虽言未必中度，朕亦当共议而更之，俾协于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254511_comment'></div>朕固不以居尊自恃，使人不敢言也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254511_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1254511'>臣闻人君之德，莫大于纳谏，而后世称纳谏之盛者，无如唐文皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254511_comment'></div>其臣王圭、魏徵之徒，号善谏诤，至于无言不从，无事不听，可谓至美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254511_comment'></div>惟太祖皇帝圣见高远，不以文皇纳谏为难，而以自不为之，使人无可谏为善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254511_comment'></div>大哉言乎，前世帝王所不逮也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254511_comment'></div>昔《书》成汤犹曰「改过不吝」，是不能无过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254511_comment'></div>若吾太祖，将无事之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254511_comment'></div>《本纪》又载太祖一日罢朝，不乐内侍，有问者，上曰：「尔谓帝王可容易行事耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254511_comment'></div>早来前殿乘快处分一事有失，史臣必书，所以不乐也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254511_comment'></div>盖太祖皇帝常以乘快处分为悔为戒，兢兢业业，罔敢怠忽，宜其周旋却顾，当时无可谏之事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254511_comment'></div>臣又闻之，事君之义，有犯无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254511_comment'></div>所谓犯者，不过触危严，冒忌讳，其用心则忠至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254511_comment'></div>夫有隐则见利而不陈，遇害而不指，挟奸导谀，务为身谋，人臣之罪莫越是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254511_comment'></div>惟太宗皇帝圣见高远，于二三大臣，既欲其情之无间，且欲其事之无隐，犹曰「不以居尊自恃，而使人不敢言也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254511_comment'></div>大哉言乎，亦前世帝王所不逮也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254511_comment'></div>《书》所谓「启乃心，沃朕心」，「尔无面从，退有后言」，实是道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254511_comment'></div>故太宗又谓宋琪曰：「朕周旋欸曲，商确时事，盖欲通上下之情，无有壅蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254511_comment'></div>卿等但直道而行，绝其私请，无得有所顾避也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254511_comment'></div>盖太宗皇帝每虑群臣不由直道而交通私请，戒之使无所顾避，固当靡不尽其情矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254511_comment'></div>仰惟皇帝陛下至仁大度，同符太祖，谋猷施设，罔不诹于故实而宪于谟训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254511_comment'></div>臣愿陛下兼听广览，以太祖之训，益隆圣德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254511_comment'></div>好问察言，以太宗之训，深励群臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254511_comment'></div>夫使会朝清明，而常无可谏之事，人臣皆知直道事君，而举无不尽之情，则治效何患不成，中原何患不复哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254511_comment'></div>此臣区区日夜以冀也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1254511_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年7月28日</a>　嫁幼女五十六娘于南康县主簿孟植（元立）作品：《纳婿祝文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254647?labeling=true' "poem_title_1254647")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254647'><div id='poem_sentence_1_1254647_comment'></div>男女及时，成兹嘉礼，恭见于庙，是宜佑之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1254647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_title_243325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243325'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243325'>功名相望十年前，白首官曹仅接联。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243325'>良玉要须更九火，明珠那得閟重泉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243325'>清风遂作双溪咏，老手悬知剧郡便。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243325'>奏课不妨聊第一，归来更著祖生鞭。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年9月</a>　再进故事，以李绛对唐宪宗为例，言人君不能以“谏官朋党”为言，拒纳讽谏，“自古纳谏昌，拒谏亡”作品：《九月再进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷11。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年12月5日</a>　跋李遵勖（公武）帖。作品：《跋李和文帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋李和文帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年12月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254480")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254480'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254480'>国朝文雅，至章圣时乃盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254480_comment'></div>杨、刘二公，制作彬彬，为天下表仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254480_comment'></div>而和文公以勋阀尚帝女，笔力颉颃，号相师友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254480_comment'></div>此帖盖与中山论禅，可概见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254480_comment'></div>晚尝援韦嗣立故事，祈衲禄以老山林，其胸次所蕴，视富贵真何物耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254480_comment'></div>乾道八年十二月五日，颍川韩某盥手以观。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1254480_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>，56岁</div><div id='8dd5ac69964f437a8134d5384ac6fe42' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年4月23日</a>　四月，返临安覆命，转一官。作品：《辞免奉使回转官状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免奉使回转官状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年4月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254338")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254338'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254338'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，以臣奉使回程，四月二十三日，三省同奉圣旨转一官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254338_comment'></div>臣仰惟圣神在御，务广至仁，聘问之交，是为常礼，如臣不肖，叨预从班，曾何补于事功，实坐縻于岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254338_comment'></div>暂将明命，臣之职也，初无专对之劳，可冒信赏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254338_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下，曲回天造，特寝误恩，察臣粗守朴忠，怜臣素无矫伪，姑以旧典，推以官属，俾臣且仍故秩，以效尺寸，庶稍安于愚分，期不负于圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254338_comment'></div>所有恩命，臣未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254338_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254338_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1254338_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年5月12日</a>　除吏部侍郎。作品：《辞免除吏部侍郎状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除吏部侍郎状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年5月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254343")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254343'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254343'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，五月十二日，三省同奉圣旨，韩某可除吏部侍郎，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254343_comment'></div>有命自天，措躬无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254343_comment'></div>伏念臣赋才甚下，造学不优，一辞州县之劳，四冒台省之入，孰云末路，误简圣知！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254343_comment'></div>叙流品于三铨，粗叨满岁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254343_comment'></div>畅威灵于万里，谨止踰时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254343_comment'></div>尺寸靡长，毫分何补？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254343_comment'></div>徒怀中愤之激，妄意事功之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254343_comment'></div>丹陛献言，但为昨日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254343_comment'></div>黄扉受宠，乃不崇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254343_comment'></div>虽大君欲砺于庶工，然微臣敢尸于异数？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254343_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下，推此施以待天下豪杰之士，扩此意以收海内智谋之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254343_comment'></div>将力置于中兴，宜坐屈于群策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254343_comment'></div>若愚虑获伸于一得，则荣名何在于九迁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254343_comment'></div>曲轸危衷，姑仍旧列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254343_comment'></div>惟有忱辞之自竭，尚祈渊听之可回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254343_comment'></div>庶俾厚恩，不为虚受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254343_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254343_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1254343_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年5月</a>　举朱熹自代。作品：《举朱熹自代状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举朱熹自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254351")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254351'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254351'>具位某准格，诸侍从授讫，三日内举官一员充自代者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254351_comment'></div>右，臣伏睹左迪功郎、前差充枢密院编修官朱熹，气质端方，议论通亮，安贫守道，力学能文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254351_comment'></div>虽累有召命，而熹以禄不及亲，未肯出仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254351_comment'></div>方今奔竞成俗，熹之廉退，所宜奖擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254351_comment'></div>臣实不如，举以自代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254351_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1254351_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年5月</a>　进故事，以刘邦待郦食其为例，强调人君好儒应重视“善调一天下之儒”，而“尚文词，穷训传”，“第欲谈经，而不肯任事”，则非人君好儒之实。作品：《癸巳五月进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸巳五月进故事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254514")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254514'>《汉书·郦食其传》，沛公略地陈留郊，麾下骑士适食其里中子，沛公时时问邑中贤豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254514_comment'></div>骑士归，食其见谓曰：「吾闻沛公<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1254514", 1254514, "Clauses/6/Comments/1")'>嫚易</span>人，有大略，此真吾所愿从」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254514_comment'></div>骑士曰：「沛公不喜儒，未可以儒生说也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254514_comment'></div>骑士从容言食其所戒者，食其至，入谒，长揖不拜，曰：「足下欲助秦攻诸侯乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254514_comment'></div>欲率诸侯破秦乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254514_comment'></div>沛公骂曰：「腐儒！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254514_comment'></div>夫天下同苦秦久矣，故诸侯相率攻秦，何谓助秦」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254514_comment'></div>食其因言六国从衡时，沛公喜，赐食其食，问计安出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254514_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1254514'>臣闻世之论汉高者，类以不喜儒为言，及观食其之事，岂诚不喜哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254514_comment'></div>盖高祖所不喜者，恶夫盗其名而无所适用云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254514_comment'></div>食其一言六国成败，遂推之食而问之计，既下陈留而封之为广野君，是一时有用之才，帝未尝不喜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254514_comment'></div>自周衰道学不传，士之号为儒者，徒能诵说陈言而不达当世之务，故听其语若可行，责其实则罔效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254514_comment'></div>且复自处于优閒畏懦之地，以苟倖世之富贵，所以动见厌弃，儒者之名殆为此辈污之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254514_comment'></div>汉兴三人，若食其特辩士之雄，而亦以儒自命，叔孙通仅能定朝会之仪，陆贾时时说诗书而著《新语》，大抵所抱负类不醇正，猎取儒之近似者，而帝已喜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254514_comment'></div>惟张子房玩意黄老，雍容近道，未始以儒自名，帝亦不悟其为儒而独见尊礼，况夫荀卿所谓善调一天下之儒，使帝遇之，安得而不喜哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254514_comment'></div>以是言之，尚文词，穷训传，非人君好儒之实，而后之儒者，第欲谈经而不肯任事，皆高祖之所不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254514_comment'></div>臣窃以为今中国之所以未操胜算者，正在人材太弱，士大夫虚名有馀而实用不足，其弊皆由儒者无以自振，惟圣天子作成砥砺而易其俗尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254514_comment'></div>且人材犹金玉也，镕范久然后其剂良，琢磨工然后其质美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254514_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「追琢其章，金玉其相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254514_comment'></div>勉勉我王，纲纪四方」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254514_comment'></div>言文王之能官人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254514_comment'></div>陛下知此久矣，臣固未可以立谈尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254514_comment'></div>然人材众多，要皆有用，而养其资力，俾无妄进之心，责其实效，俾无避事之意，庶几虚名之患消，将有真儒为时而出，汉高之风，何足仪也！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1254514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年5月28日</a>　诏令疏决罪犯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年8月</a>　进故事，以太祖评郭从义击球技艺精绝，然“此非将相所为”之言，论人君“器使诸将，留神万机之暇，不深取其技，而责其谋”作品：《八月进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷11。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年8月</a>　丁丑，方滋卒于平江，有挽词。作品：《方务德侍郞挽词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243152' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　荐郭见义、蔡迨（肩吾）于朝，未果。作品：《荐郭见义、蔡迨札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荐郭见义蔡迨劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254364")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254364'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254364'>臣仰惟陛下躬文明之治，旁求儒雅，以阐帝王之制，尤以轸念故家人物为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254364_comment'></div>如臣愚钝不肖，叨蒙睿眷，每加殊奖，窃思报国，但有荐贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254364_comment'></div>臣伏见朝奉郎、权发遣光化军郭见义，故宣徽使郭逵之后，力学能文，才藻宏掞，虽以进士登科，而恬退不务进取，甘心远官，时无知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254364_comment'></div>又伏见从政郎蔡迨，名臣文忠蔡齐之后，学有家法，笔力雅健，得制作之体，久困州县，无因自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254364_comment'></div>二人者皆中原旧族，忠信修饬，绰有典型，恐可副圣神蒐延之意，资承明著述之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254364_comment'></div>不如所举，臣甘被罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254364_comment'></div>惟是进越，冒渎天听，臣无任恐惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254364_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1254364_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　怀友人陆游，有词寄之。作品：《水调歌头·寄陆务观》（明月照多景）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>寄陆务观</a><span id='poem_sentence_1_243566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243566'>豪气如今谁在。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
