href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月3日</a>　除敷文阁待制，出知婺州。作品：《辞待制与郡状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span>《谢除待制表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞待制与郡状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254339")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254339'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254339'>臣恭闻恩命，跼蹐靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254339_comment'></div>伏念臣以寒远之踪，荷圣神之眷，擢寘从班，俯仰再岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254339_comment'></div>技能短拙，曲赐并容，议论迂疏，每蒙奖与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254339_comment'></div>惟自叨逾过甚，筋力弗任，已具丐閒之章，方欲朝夕上列，敢期天造，尚使治民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254339_comment'></div>碎骨縻躯，未知报塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254339_comment'></div>惟是西清次对之职，礼秩优厚，守符重寄，惧弗克堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254339_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下推天地从欲之仁，扩日月必照之施，怜臣粗守朴忠，素无矫伪，收还职名之命，改授一在外宫观差遣，庶几愚分稍安，免致清议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254339_comment'></div>臣无任陨越之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1254339_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1254317' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254317' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254317?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除待制表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254317")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254317_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254317'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254317'>分符出守，已叨便近之藩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254317_comment'></div>锡命宠行，尚缀禁严之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254317_comment'></div>恳辞莫遂，跽受弥兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254317_comment'></div>伏念臣久以庸愚，误蒙简拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254317_comment'></div>周游省户，参掾属者九年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254317_comment'></div>密勿从班，备铨衡于两选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254317_comment'></div>积有丘山之厚戾，了无尘雾之微劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254317_comment'></div>外并名州，实踰分愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254317_comment'></div>中联美职，滋冒恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254317_comment'></div>恍然未定之惊魂，甚矣横流之感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254317_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下仁如天大，德与日升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254317_comment'></div>器使群材，菅蒯尽归于采掇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254317_comment'></div>生成庶汇，虫鱼感遂于飞潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254317_comment'></div>曲示眷私，用光临遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254317_comment'></div>臣迹虽违于丹陛，名犹滥于清厢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254317_comment'></div>惟近臣献纳之私，未殚于补报；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254317_comment'></div>若刺史中和之布，敢负于使令？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254317_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1254317_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月8日</a>　其兄元龙（子云）为中书门下省检正诸房文字。十二月八日，除直宝文阁权江东路计度转运副使。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='db3d6066c1db4b898e577195cb0ce2fc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("db3d6066c1db4b898e577195cb0ce2fc");'><span id='db3d6066c1db4b898e577195cb0ce2fc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1178')">1176-1178年</a>，59-61岁</div><div id='db3d6066c1db4b898e577195cb0ce2fc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年5月22日</a>　五月，至临安。二十二日，除权吏部尚书。作品：《辞除权吏部尚书状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞除权吏部尚书状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年5月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254344")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254344'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254344'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，五月二十二日，三省同奉圣旨，除臣权吏部尚书，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254344_comment'></div>臣闻命自天，措躬无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254344_comment'></div>伏念臣去国虽更于再岁，承流尚玷于两州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254344_comment'></div>课其治状则无以逾人，省其廉隅则第知守己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254344_comment'></div>夙被圣神之眷，躐跻侍从之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254344_comment'></div>岂其记怜于九重之中，遂蒙收召于千里之外！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254344_comment'></div>内朝赐觐，粗陈狂瞽之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254344_comment'></div>天听不违，曲赐褒嘉之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254344_comment'></div>窃怀尺寸区区献忠之意，敢有丝毫汲汲幸进之心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254344_comment'></div>乃奉殊恩，宠班常伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254344_comment'></div>矧是三铨之长，实司群吏之成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254344_comment'></div>虽往岁暂冒于摄承，而一旦遽膺于迁陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254344_comment'></div>顾贤能之在列，且隽杰之尚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254344_comment'></div>揣其分义则非宜，稽之公议为可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254344_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下，俯全旧物，特轸鸿慈，还渥涣于误颁，柬真才而擢任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254344_comment'></div>有如愚陋，俾以退閒，庶几微臣志尽自知之明，仰副圣朝官无虚受之义，臣不胜愿幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254344_comment'></div>所有恩命，臣未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254344_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1254344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年5月</a>　五月底，进故事，以唐太宗“引诸卫将卒习射显德殿庭”事，论人主“志不可一日忘敌”作品：《丙申五月进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷11。）</span><div id='poem_1254516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙申五月进故事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254516")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254516_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254516'>《唐书》，太宗引诸卫将卒习射于显德殿庭，谕之曰：「四裔侵盗，自古有之，患在边境小安，则人主逸游忘战，是以寇来莫之能御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254516_comment'></div>今朕不使尔曹穿池筑苑，专习弓矢，居閒无事则为尔师，突厥入寇则为尔将，庶几中国之民可以少安乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254516_comment'></div>数年之间，悉为精锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254516_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1254516'>臣闻太宗可谓不忘突厥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254516_comment'></div>当时群臣不察，以为兵刃至御在所，而后世诸儒亦议太宗阅武殿庭，以人主之尊而行将帅之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254516_comment'></div>臣知太宗之志在突厥者，以其非得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254516_comment'></div>盖唐初外裔之患莫甚于突厥，自隋即以公主妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254516_comment'></div>高祖得天下，群盗角之，惧其为助，故卑词厚币，约以连和，其礼有为之屈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254516_comment'></div>及连岁内侮益甚，至欲迁都避之，不胜其愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254516_comment'></div>武德八年，命有司削其敌国之礼，更以书为诏若敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254516_comment'></div>其酋颉利，因自将其众袭武功而瞰渭桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254516_comment'></div>时太宗方即位，以六骑直出，与颉利隔水语，仅成白马之盟，引兵退舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254516_comment'></div>由是言之，高祖之愤几贻大悔，未若太宗之能忍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254516_comment'></div>然帝虽能忍而其志不可一日忘敌，故敌退未踰月，即殿庭以教战士，校其射艺，诱以厚赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254516_comment'></div>此特其一端尔，他所以备敌者，从可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254516_comment'></div>贞观之治，用贤纳谏之方，选将练兵之法，皆足以自致于安强，然后坚坐不瞬，以待其隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254516_comment'></div>及颉利势衰，羊马多死，又与突利相攻击，诸部皆畔，逮贞观四年，始命李靖以六总管之师才十万人，破之阴山，擒颉利以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254516_comment'></div>观帝之告群臣，有曰：「国家初定，太上皇以百姓之故，奉突厥诡而臣之，朕常痛心疾首，思一刷耻于天下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254516_comment'></div>其劝高祖不必移都，则曰：「愿假数年，系颉利之颈致之阙下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254516_comment'></div>至是果酬其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254516_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254516_comment'></div>有志者，事竟成，必有忍其乃有济，太宗之谓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254516_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254516_comment'></div>待外国之礼或可屈，而志不可屈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254516_comment'></div>惟礼或可屈，故权时之宜有所不校，若太王事獯鬻、文王事昆夷，于传有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254516_comment'></div>惟志不可屈，故勾践之报吴、太宗之擒颉利，皆是道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254516_comment'></div>臣窃仰国家今与敌和，岂异是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254516_comment'></div>日者奉使之臣，辱命而还，陛下既以备正典刑矣，敌之骄慢吾使而礼有未得伸者，固不能不动心，然亦何足与校是非曲直乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254516_comment'></div>臣所愿陛下沈几先物，扩帝王之度以容之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254516_comment'></div>坚忍不顾，厉太宗之志以图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254516_comment'></div>如闻敌境旱蝗已久，民心离贰，诸雏各擅兵柄，互相窥伺，天道如闻，岂无颉利之变！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254516_comment'></div>陛下圣德英武，远迈于太宗，假以岁月，则渭上之耻，未必不启吾定襄之功也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254516_comment'></div>臣是以因贞观之事以證之云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1254516_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年6月1日</a>　与蔡洗等上集议安南国奏状。作品：《蔡洗等集议安南国奏状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蔡洗等集议安南国奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年6月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254335")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254335'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254335'>臣等具位准尚书省劄子，安南国李天祚追赠及其子李龙𣉙合袭封事，五月十四日，三省、枢密院同奉圣旨，令侍从台谏两省官同共议定闻奏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254335_comment'></div>右，臣等窃惟国朝故事，待蕃夷之礼最为详备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254335_comment'></div>若高丽嗣子，则待其请命，然后封以为高丽国王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254335_comment'></div>若占城、三佛齐、阇婆诸国，则待其入贡而遂以为本国王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254335_comment'></div>惟是奉命安南，甚有次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254335_comment'></div>其始嗣立，则封交趾郡王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254335_comment'></div>中间数年以后，则封南平王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254335_comment'></div>及其身后，则追赠南越王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254335_comment'></div>自太祖、太宗至于累朝，必加三命，未之或改者，盖以安南本交州内地，实吾藩镇，因仍世袭，使护安南一道，非他外邦自有土地人民不尽臣之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254335_comment'></div>所以渐次封爵，时示恩荣，其羁縻制御之道不得不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254335_comment'></div>今来李天祚既薨，其子龙𣉙嗣袭，自合遵用祖宗旧章，以行封爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254335_comment'></div>恭惟圣慈渊虑，乃使臣等定议，岂以淳熙元年曾以天祚为安南国王，已有国名，疑其礼亦异数故耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254335_comment'></div>臣等闻朝廷昨以安南国王命天祚者，初非其国抗章有请，特以贡献驯象方物，守藩岁久，锡之此名，以宠天祚而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254335_comment'></div>安南本都护之称，非可名国，而南越之封甚大，自汉以来用之，则天祚既没，宜用典故追赠南越王可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254335_comment'></div>其子龙𣉙，虽云嗣袭，然未有功勋，亦宜只遵典故，所加节钺官称，初封交趾郡王，庶为允当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254335_comment'></div>若朝廷谓已曾锡之安南国名，不可虚设，则宜去其安南都护，稍加以为知安南国事足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254335_comment'></div>盖高丽嗣子，每次亦称权知高丽国事上表，此其据也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254335_comment'></div>彼或祈乞，但令广西吊祭监司明谕此意，候他时职贡不阙，续当赐安南国王真命，不复更封南平王矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254335_comment'></div>如此则昨所赐安南国名，姑以易南平王之号，犹须身后始得封为南越，上不失祖宗渐进之意，下足以尽羁縻制御之道，而于我之事体无所亏损，彼之名称无所镌改，似为可行不易之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254335_comment'></div>若便欲使其子嗣袭封王位，而褒赠天祚别以师傅之官，且加美谥，则是朝廷自变其礼，而不以藩镇小夷待之，骤与外国诸蕃一同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254335_comment'></div>不知既袭王爵数年之后，却加以是何恩数？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254335_comment'></div>其将遂以南越王与之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254335_comment'></div>此不可不过为之虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254335_comment'></div>臣等所议如前，惟圣主择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254335_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254335_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1254335'>准三省帖子，今月初一日，赴都堂集议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254335_comment'></div>右，某等近奉圣旨集议安南国追赠袭封事，已连书具奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254335_comment'></div>缘某等所议并是考据典故，委曲详备，别无未尽事理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254335_comment'></div>所有国名，系已带知安南国事，即非遽有夺其王爵，欲俟他日职贡不阙，然后加封，庶使外夷明知祖宗以来封爵次第，不至别有觊望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254335_comment'></div>所议如前，谨具申三省、枢密院，伏乞照会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254335_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1254335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年6月</a>　是月，除朱熹为秘书郎，熹辞不赴召。元吉两次致书，质以“平日所学何事”作品：《答朱元晦书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷13。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年7月18日</a>　风雨中观潮，有诗，周必大（子充）以内直不赴，次韵其诗，约以秋半再往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年7月</a>　是月，进故事，以三国时吴张温利用“好为清议”的暨艳，解决“郎省混浊淆杂”之事为例，论清议之弊。作品：《七月进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷11。）</span><div id='poem_1254517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>七月进故事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254517")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254517'>《吴志·张温传》，温引致暨艳，以为选曹郎，至尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254517_comment'></div>艳性狷厉，好为清议，见时郎省混浊淆杂，多非其人，欲臧否区别，贤愚异贯，弹劾百寮，率皆贬高就下，降损数等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254517_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1254517'>臣闻清议之始，犹公议也，所以论人材之贤不肖，以助国之赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254517_comment'></div>然议者当出于上，不当见于下，当施于公，不当徇于私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254517_comment'></div>故《周礼》有八议之辟，而汉以议郎设官，是法令之行，政事之大，朝野之臣皆得议之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254517_comment'></div>然周之弊，郑人聚于乡校，以议执政之善否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254517_comment'></div>流而至于战国，以成处士横议之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254517_comment'></div>汉之弊，太学诸儒嘘枯吹生，而甘陵有南北部，公卿以下畏其贬议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254517_comment'></div>自是而降，清议遂为无实之言，故山简以为郭泰、许劭之论，明清议于草野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254517_comment'></div>夫议非出于草野者也，故曰天下有道，则庶人不议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254517_comment'></div>以三公之际，暨艳辈乃欲施清议于选曹，虽当时居位贪鄙、志节污卑者，皆降为军吏，置在营府，然意其嫉恶太甚，清浊太分，谪罚太骤，而不能无私喜怒于其间，故终至于怨愤之声积，浸润之谮行，而艳与徐彪亦不保其身矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254517_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254517_comment'></div>自公议不行而变为清议，清议不已而肆为清谈，皆无益于天下国家，而适足以致搢绅之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254517_comment'></div>今日士夫以为清流之议者，尤非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254517_comment'></div>至于妄尊大而好为虚名，昧世务而不切实用，宜神圣之所深念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254517_comment'></div>臣是以因得辨之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1254517_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年9月</a>　九月，进故事。以西汉魏相辅宣帝以达中兴之效为例，论治国必须“深达时变”作品：《九月进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷11。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　建议严祠禄之给。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年11月</a>　十一月庚午，跋司马光《倚几帖》作品：《跋司马公倚几帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254484?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋司马公倚几铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254484")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254484_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254484'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254484'>温文正公《倚几铭》，今《传家集》所未见者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254484_comment'></div>铭文甚简，而注义特详，其告君之善，惟恐不尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254484_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1254484", 1254484, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>勾注</span>涂改甚多，而无一字行草，其敬谨之至，未尝斯须忘，可不法哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254484_comment'></div>淳熙三年十一月庚午，颍川韩某观。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1254484_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年11月2日</a>　进为吏部尚书。作品：《辞吏部尚书状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254345' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254345' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254345?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞吏部尚书状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年11月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254345")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254345_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254345'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254345'>右，某准尚书省劄子，十一月二日，三省同奉圣旨，韩某可除吏部尚书，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254345_comment'></div>臣闻命震惊，罔知攸措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254345_comment'></div>伏念臣禀资驽下，赋性拙疏，技能不异于众人，问学无闻于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254345_comment'></div>自簉周行之列，亲逢上主之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254345_comment'></div>摄词命于西垣，荐承睿奖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254345_comment'></div>滥铨衡于文部，益荷圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254345_comment'></div>承流两郡而初无抚字之功，锡命九关而复被招徕之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254345_comment'></div>逮膺常伯，曾未踰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254345_comment'></div>徒以世受国恩，幼循家训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254345_comment'></div>服其职业之间者，罔敢避怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254345_comment'></div>献于聪明之下者，每务尽忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254345_comment'></div>虽乾坤之大，无所不容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254345_comment'></div>然蝼蚁之微，退辄自惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254345_comment'></div>岂期冀幸，乃冒为真！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254345_comment'></div>惟念臣早岁驱驰，固有功名之愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254345_comment'></div>中年遭遇，实无爵禄之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254345_comment'></div>傥臣言得用于明时，则臣志已摅于平日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254345_comment'></div>至于假臣之过分，适以重臣之不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254345_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下，曲轸至仁，特收成涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254345_comment'></div>俾臣姑仍旧职，亦足副于使令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254345_comment'></div>容臣少效微劳，庶以逃于谤戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254345_comment'></div>所有恩命，臣不敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254345_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254345_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1254345_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年1月</a>　正月，进故事，以邓禹对汉光武例，论天下之兴衰，在德之薄厚，不在得地之大小。作品：《丁酉正月进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷11。）</span><div id='poem_1254519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁酉正月进故事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254519")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254519'>《后汉书·邓禹传》，光武自蓟至信都，使禹发亡命，得数千人，令自将之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254519_comment'></div>别攻拔乐阳，徙至广阿，光武舍城楼上，披舆地指示禹曰：「天下郡国如是，今始乃得其一，子前言『以吾虑天下不足定』，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254519_comment'></div>禹曰：「方今海内淆乱，人思明君，犹赤子之慕慈母，故兴者在德薄厚，不在大小」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254519_comment'></div>光武悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254519_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1254519'>臣观光武，可谓知难者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254519_comment'></div>语有之：「君以为难，易将至焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254519_comment'></div>方其用兵河朔，仅得一郡，观天下郡国之众，怛然自畏，虑己之不能取也，以问于禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254519_comment'></div>为禹者，以他人论之，当时更始据关西，赤眉、青犊之属，动以万数，三辅假号，往往群聚，必劝其君以厉兵秣马，壮其威力，以角一旦之胜，而禹乃曰「在德薄厚，不在大小」，是料光武必足以定天下，欲广其德以收天下之心尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254519_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254519_comment'></div>此三代王者之佐之言，伊尹、吕望所以思济斯民者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254519_comment'></div>故光武至邯郸，分遣官属，徇行郡县，理冤结，布惠泽，录囚徒，存鳏寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254519_comment'></div>其敕冯异，有曰「今之征伐，非必略地屠城，要在平定安集之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254519_comment'></div>皆禹有以发之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254519_comment'></div>后世乃以禹不能径攻长安为疑，然禹以谓赤眉新拔长安，财富充实，锋未可当，盗贼群居，无终日计，财谷虽多，变故万端，盖姑欲假以岁月，待其自毙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254519_comment'></div>禹之谋固不尽用，而师行有纪，降者日以千数，停车住节，劳来父老，以慰其讴吟思汉之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254519_comment'></div>光武以功赏之，非其谋识所先后者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254519_comment'></div>今以天下之半而谋恢复，则舆地固已远过汉光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254519_comment'></div>而强敌纵横几踰五十年，其势将亦自毙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254519_comment'></div>圣主盛德日新，施者厚矣，群臣宜亦有禹之谋，而不计近功以图之，则中兴为日月可冀也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1254519_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年2月</a>　针对选举改官之弊，上札子乞严申铨试帘试之法。作品：《论铨试帘试札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254353' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254353?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论铨试帘试劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254353")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254353_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254353'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254353'>检准淳熙三年三月二十七日敕，臣僚劄子节文：「铨试之弊，甚者身不至场屋，赂他人冒名入试，无以辨其真伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254353_comment'></div>而又门禁不密，有自外传藁本而入者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254353_comment'></div>欲望明诏有司，程文以经义诗赋时议为去留，刑法以律义为去留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254353_comment'></div>其合格者，参选日召保识官二员，批书印纸，令吏部覆试，依太学帘试诸生法」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254353_comment'></div>三省同奉圣旨依奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254353_comment'></div>缘当年铨试在上件指挥之前，未曾举行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254353_comment'></div>今来铨试在近，合行申明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254353_comment'></div>本部照对铨试出官人，已有节次申严指挥，每二人取一人，不许用恩例免试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254353_comment'></div>其考校去留，门禁不密，合系类试所施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254353_comment'></div>参选日，召保识官二员，已有现在条法外，覆试一节，缘本部系铨选注拟之地，日逐官员参铨选量引验，事体不一，即与太学专一教养士子官舍不同，难以帘试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254353_comment'></div>欲移就别所引试，则参选人数先后不齐，便同再试，致施行未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254353_comment'></div>窃详臣僚所请，止为冒名入试之弊，其冒名就试、代笔、传义，自依贡举条制，并许人告，同保并保官及官司书铺知情者，各与同罪，同保人永不得应举，及乾道四年申明指挥，不得射保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254353_comment'></div>引试日，试官于帘前引问，代笔人并令人代者，同保人降两月名次定罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254353_comment'></div>本部今措置欲增立罪赏，即不须更用帘试虚文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254353_comment'></div>乞自今年铨试为始，应就试先召保识官二员，委保正身不是代名，别无违碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254353_comment'></div>至参选日，就用保官，更不再召引保，并入试日并责书铺识认状，及同保互相保委系是正身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254353_comment'></div>特立赏格，许人告首，如有冒名入试之人，根勘得实，犯人与保官、同保人一例收坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254353_comment'></div>其同保人仍依贡举法，铨试不中人与展两次铨试，内试中人降一年名次，书铺重行断罪，馀依现行条法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254353_comment'></div>庶得不致冒犯，可以杜绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254353_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷特降指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1254353_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年3月8日</a>　奏李塾等人应贤良方正能直言极谏科词业为次优。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　是春，曾与吕祖谦（伯恭）游雨中西湖。作品：《雨中同伯恭至湖上》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雨中同伯恭至湖上</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243469")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243469'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243469'>莫嫌鞭马踏春泥，茶鼎诗囊偶共携。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243469'>山色雨深看更好，湖光烟接望还迷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243469'>连天花絮飞将尽，夹道蒲荷长欲齐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243469'>官事得閒须洗眼，蓬壶只在帝城西。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243469'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　陈良祐（天与）起知徽州，有诗、词送行。作品：《送陈天与知徽州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span>《贺圣朝·送天与》（斜阳只向花梢驻）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243317' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243317' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243317?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送陈天与知徽州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243317")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243317_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243317'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243317'>台阁英名二十年，卜居那得便林泉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243317'>履声旧振星辰上，谏墨犹存雨露边。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243317'>欲考治功三府近，且施惠政一州先。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243317'>黄山看尽须黄阁，六月天池更著鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243317'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243317_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺圣朝 送天与</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243597")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243597'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243597'>斜阳只向花梢驻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243597'>似愁君西去。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243597'>清歌也便做阳关，更朝来风雨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243597_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243597'>佳人莫道，一杯须近，总眉峰偷聚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243597'>明年归诏上鸾台，记别离难处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年7月</a>　进故事，以唐太宗与王珪论“君臣同德，则海内安”为例，论“君臣相须”之道。作品：《丁酉七月进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷11。）</span><div id='poem_1254520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁酉七月进故事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254520")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254520'>《唐书·王圭传》，太宗召为谏议大夫，帝尝曰：「正主御邪臣，不可以致治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254520_comment'></div>正臣事邪主，亦不可以致治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254520_comment'></div>惟君臣同德，则海内安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254520_comment'></div>朕虽不明，幸诸公数谏正，庶致天下于平」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254520_comment'></div>圭进曰：「古者天子有争臣七人，谏不用则相继以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254520_comment'></div>今陛下开圣听，采刍言，臣愿竭狂瞽，佐万分一」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254520_comment'></div>帝以圭推诚纳言，每存规益，帝益任之，迁侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254520_comment'></div>帝使太常少卿祖孝孙以乐律授宫中音家，技不进，数被谯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254520_comment'></div>圭与温彦博同进曰：「孝孙循谨士，陛下使教女乐，又责谯之，天下其以士为轻乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254520_comment'></div>帝怒曰：「卿皆我腹心，乃罔上为人游说耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254520_comment'></div>彦博谢罪，圭不谢，帝默然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254520_comment'></div>明日，语房玄龄曰：「帝王纳谏固难矣，朕夙夜庶几于前圣，昨责圭等，痛自悔，公等勿惩是不进谏也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254520_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1254520'>臣闻君臣相须，如手足之卫头目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254520_comment'></div>有是君也而其臣不足以辅之，有是臣也而其君不足以使之，则失其所以相须者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254520_comment'></div>故君在审择其臣，而臣在忠事其君，未有君臣之志不同，其德不合，而能成天下之治者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254520_comment'></div>太宗之说，可谓知者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254520_comment'></div>然君之患常在于不能纳谏，臣之患常在于不能尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254520_comment'></div>以太宗之明圣，是其于兵机将略、戡定祸乱，足以追迹汤、武，其于躬行仁义、力致太平，足以庶几成、康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254520_comment'></div>其大者既以安定天下，自馀行事，固亦无甚过举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254520_comment'></div>汲汲然导房玄龄使谏，如此则朝廷之上，一日万几之间，何虑其阙失哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254520_comment'></div>夫谯责孝孙以教宫中音技之不进，岂亦太常协律之职，实人君过举之细，管仲所谓未能害霸者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254520_comment'></div>而圭与彦博过虑而言，便有轻士之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254520_comment'></div>太宗始亦怒之，终则悔之，又诏玄龄辈勿惩是而不谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254520_comment'></div>当时责成大臣纳诲以辅台德，可谓无隐情矣，其致贞观之治也宜哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254520_comment'></div>臣以是知君臣皆正之明验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254520_comment'></div>且太宗之说固正矣，使其臣不正，其肯为太宗尽言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254520_comment'></div>一事之不谏，则天下之事将有不闻者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254520_comment'></div>故臣下之邪正，在于言与不言之间，明君不可以不察也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1254520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年7月</a>　李塾曾以文卷上元吉。七月间，元吉答书勉之。作品：《答李塾书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷13。）</span><div id='poem_1254412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答李塾书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254412")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254412'>七月日，某顿首复书贤良李君足下：某昨与令外舅游，闻足下隽才甚著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254412_comment'></div>日者复幸尊公同制而升，得奉周旋，每以未见足下为恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254412_comment'></div>中都坌冗，日力不暇给，虽欲从多闻之士以讲明道艺之蕴，如无绳而絷马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254412_comment'></div>敢意高谊不遗，跫然足音乃临于蔀室，宠以书教，述古今言行之要，取士之略，知唐制不逮于汉而本朝独近于古者，粲然其文之华也，铿然其韵之美也，渊然其中之宏而渥然其外之泽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254412_comment'></div>夫制举之缺，自元祐以迄今，圣天子蒐罗于四方，而足下昆弟褎然为首，以振眉山之旧，礼乐法度之源，兵农刑政之本，足下讲之熟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254412_comment'></div>六经之说无不习，百家之言无不通，此犹未足道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254412_comment'></div>窃尝念之，中原困于兵革者逾五十年，衣冠沦于涂炭，天子盖不忍为之屈，思得非常之材，以摅天下之愤，而复致周道之兴，故乡举里选为未足，而前史以为制举者，所以待非常之材也，上心慕焉，足下宜有以副此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254412_comment'></div>某之老懦，徒将拭目于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254412_comment'></div>虽然，不敢忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254412_comment'></div>既勤厚意之辱，故辄上以为谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254412_comment'></div>异时功名之来，足下徐举武而收之，始可以为今日贺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254412_comment'></div>不宣，某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1254412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　七、八月间，两上与同僚集议状，乞革除出官改官中繁冗虚伪之弊。作品：《集议繁冗虚伪弊事状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年8月</a>　进故事，以汉武帝策问董仲舒为言，论“大道”之要。作品：《八月进故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷11。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　钱端礼（处仁）卒，有挽词。作品：《故宫使参政钱公挽词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243269' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243269' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243269?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故宫使参政观文钱公挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243269")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243269_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243269'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243269'>忠孝全家法，清修极道腴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243269'>雍容调庶政，谈笑靖边隅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243269'>许国心犹壮，安时貌不枯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243269'>脩龄才七十，谁为隔黄垆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243269'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243269_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243268' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243268' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243268?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243268_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243268'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243268'>甲第依香火，栖心不离禅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243268'>颐神虽绿野，纪绩自凌烟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243268'>荣观丹丘外，真游弱水边。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243268'>佳城近刘阮，觉路有飞仙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243268'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243268_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年9月</a>　为兴国陶去泰（茂安）园亭作记。作品：《东皋记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254554' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254554' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254554?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东皋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254554")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254554_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254554'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254554'>东皋者，陶氏之园也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254554_comment'></div>陶氏之先，自晋始显，而渊明令彭泽，高风峻节，足以蹈厉一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254554_comment'></div>其诗语文章所及，后之君子喜道之，况其族姓家江南，本其苗裔者，则典型馀烈，故应概见而不妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254554_comment'></div>茂安实陶氏诸孙，始予见其试于学宫，声名籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254554_comment'></div>既而佐大农，从幕府于淮西，犹慷慨有功名之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254554_comment'></div>逮为尚书郎，则已华发萧然，不复问功名富贵事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254554_comment'></div>而间为予言其所居之胜，在兴国，与郡治共一湖水，将归老焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254554_comment'></div>后数年，茂安果自湖湘之使事，挂其衣冠以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254554_comment'></div>又数年，则以书来言曰：杭湖而东，得地数十亩，以为东皋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254554_comment'></div>东皋中为一堂，曰「舒啸」，南望而行，花木蔽芾，以极于湖之涯，作亭曰「驻屐」，西则又为「莲荡」小阁，挹湖光而面之，馀可以为亭为榭者尚众，而力有未及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254554_comment'></div>力之及者，名葩异卉，间以奇石，而松竹之植，稍稍茂密矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254554_comment'></div>至于山光之秀列，湖波之演迤，风日发挥，四时之景万态，则亦不待吾力者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254554_comment'></div>吾虽老矣，得以朝夕自逸，而时与宾客游于其间，往往爱之不忍去，独憾子之未见也，可以为我记之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254554_comment'></div>予曰：夫世之所慕于渊明者，非特其去就可尚也，惟其志意超然旷达，适于物而不累于物，有所得者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254554_comment'></div>庄子曰：「山林欤，皋壤欤，使我欣欣然而乐欤」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254554_comment'></div>且山林皋壤，非世俗悦于耳目者也，所遇之乐，不自知而发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254554_comment'></div>故虽樵夫渔父，负薪鼓枻，歌声若出金石，而况于贤士大夫得之者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254554_comment'></div>今茂安世之贤士大夫也，脱迹于名利之场，休心于寂寞之境，是宜得其乐，而自附于乃祖，以荣其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254554_comment'></div>而予方奔走于朝市，闻茂安之风，盖已堪愧，而茂安乃欲予文以道其意，亦俾予知归之有不可缓者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254554_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254554_comment'></div>予固未有茂安居之胜也，异日倘遂其归而耕于灵山之下，千里命驾，以访茂安于东皋，相与植杖而耘，咏歌归来之辞，举酒道旧，以谢湖山之美，庶不为渊明之羞矣夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254554_comment'></div>淳熙四年九月，颍川韩元吉记<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254554_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1254554'>韩：原脱，据聚珍本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1254554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1254554'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1254554_0'>⑴ 《南涧甲乙稿》卷一五。又见《南宋文范》卷四三。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1254554_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年9月24日</a>　论“捕盗之赏非特选人改官一事”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年11月</a>　其子淲纳庐州通判晁子阖女为妇。作品：《淲纳妇祝文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淲纳妇祝文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254645")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254645'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254645'>淳熙四年，十一月丙申朔，二十七日壬戌，具位云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254645_comment'></div>某之男淲，娶妇晁氏，朝奉郎、新通判庐州子阖之女，盖以道舍人之孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254645_comment'></div>爰以嘉日，归见于庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254645_comment'></div>契谊既厚，子孙其宜之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1254645_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年2月</a>　二月，上札子，请申严武臣关升程试。作品：《措置武臣关升札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254360' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254360' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254360?labeling=true' target='_blank'>措置武臣关升劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254360")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254360_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254360'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254360'>臣窃以文武两迁，皆有关升之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254360_comment'></div>文臣则皆用考第举主，自初官而升令录，自知县而升通判，自通判而升知州，其法甚严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254360_comment'></div>武臣则惟有关升亲民一节，其法颇异，故武举军班武艺特奏名出身人止用两任四年，馀人皆用两任六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254360_comment'></div>虽有考第之差，而无举主之限，惟进纳人用七考，有监司、知州、通判三员奏举，始得亲民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254360_comment'></div>绍兴以来，从军大小使臣，许理在军年月以为资任，宗室全用宫观岳庙，归正归朝人止用不釐务任数，皆得关升，固异于祖宗之法矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254360_comment'></div>臣闻祖宗朝最重武臣亲民资序，必历亲民，始得擢用，与文臣改官亲民事体略等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254360_comment'></div>况今圣神临御，外则用为提刑、郡守，内则增置閤门舍人，同于观阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254360_comment'></div>小则通注知县、县尉，俾历民事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254360_comment'></div>则武臣关升之法，亦宜稍同文臣，以明陛下文武并用之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254360_comment'></div>淳熙初，臣僚有请武臣亦用举主四人，内监司一人，方许关升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254360_comment'></div>又有亲民关升正副将，而正副将关升小郡州钤辖、路分副都监之目，其格太繁，故不可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254360_comment'></div>臣前岁十月亦尝论此，是时特蒙陛下开纳，后来未见别有施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254360_comment'></div>臣愚以谓政贵简严而易举，法贵轻重之适宜，夫欲使武臣尽如文臣，必用奏举，逐任关改，则举主诚不易得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254360_comment'></div>莫若止循旧法而附益之，使武举军班武艺特奏名出身人用两任四考而不用举主，自馀皆须六考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254360_comment'></div>内有州县职事，或诸司官属，一任二考<span class='inlineComment2'>（职事并官属合立定色目。）</span>，举主二人，内监司一人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，方许关升亲民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254360_comment'></div>内有战功者，免用举主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254360_comment'></div>虽如宗室已有釐务窠阙，归正归朝之人亦有釐务期限，一等行之，似亦未害，惟进纳之官则仍旧法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254360_comment'></div>盖武臣转至武翼郎以上，入仕三十年，两遇大礼，既关升者便许奏荐，恩例匪薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254360_comment'></div>而举主所以保任其终身，监司所以廉察其能否，若州县诸司官属差遣，皆有职掌，可试以事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254360_comment'></div>异时人材更练，必有副陛下之用，益可观矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254360_comment'></div>事若甚微，法意有在，惟圣旨念焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254360_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1254360_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1254360'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1254360_0'>⑴ 文臣关升通判亦用举主二人，内监司一人。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1254360_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年2月</a>　上札子，请申严武臣关升程试。作品：《措置武臣关升状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span><div id='poem_1254382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>措置武臣关升状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254382")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254382'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254382'>今月二十三日，准尚书省劄子，大小使臣关升，从军理任，必以战功为别，其从军者必以实历为先，稍用荐举，以异于战功之士等事，缘有未尽，送某限三日措置申尚书省，今具措置下项，须至申闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254382_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1254382'>一、在法，使臣两任监当，实及六年满替，年三十以上者，到部方与关升亲民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254382_comment'></div>昨因绍兴九年四川宣抚使申请，随军大小使臣理为资任，自给到吏部理任差帖印结日实及六年，许免到部，就任关升亲民，依旧从军使唤，无朝省付身，以二日当一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254382_comment'></div>缘有功人与无功未有旌别，欲乞从军理任后曾立军功转官实及六年，依旧许行关升外，其不曾转官人亦合依无付身例，以二日当一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254382_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1254382'>一、从军使臣若在军未成关升考任，因离军任州县诸司差遣，自依外任通理关升外，其偶缘老病，不堪披带，拣汰差充不一务窠阙，合行优假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254382_comment'></div>欲乞免行关升，止与通理考任，依格升注差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254382_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1254382'>一、非从军在外使臣，旧法系合实历六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254382_comment'></div>乾道七年申请，并于历过考任内，须要实历州县职事，或诸司官属一任二考，方许通理前后任关升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254382_comment'></div>窃虑一能更历事任，欲乞并要实历州县职事或诸司官属两任四考，通理六考，方行关升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254382_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1254382'>一、宗室许历外任，正欲更练职事，近来多注岳庙差遣，习为废弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254382_comment'></div>缘乾道元年已有复置宗室监当釐务窠阙，欲乞亦要实历州县职事或诸司官属一任二考，通理四考，方行关升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254382_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1254382'>一、武臣荐举状，止有升陟任使一等，自来仅当功分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254382_comment'></div>自淳熙元年于荐举武臣升陟状内立一两纸，添作举充亲民任使，稍为优异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254382_comment'></div>欲乞除从军人外，应武臣六考内，并要升陟举状二纸，内举充亲民一纸，欲使关升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254382_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1254382'>一、归正归朝使臣者不系从军，并釐务差遣，既无职掌，合与优假，依拣汰人例免行关升，止令吏部通理所历考任，依格升注差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254382_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1254382'>一、所有军班吏职出身及进纳人等关升，已有专法指挥者，并令依旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254382_comment'></div>右谨具申尚书省，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1254382_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年2月25日</a>　乞严州县官吏铨量之法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年2月</a>　是月，乞出知州郡，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　清明日，与兄元龙（子云）、族兄元象（中父、中甫）游雨中西湖。作品：《清明日雨中同中甫、子云二兄集湖上》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清明日雨中同中甫子云二兄集湖上</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243376")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243376'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243376'>莫辞冲雨湿春衣，要看湖山滴翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243376'>絮重欲飞堤柳暗，花寒无赖海棠稀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243376'>官忙未觉追游少，酝美犹堪尽醉归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243376'>屈指薰风来几日，绿荷簪水已依依。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243376'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年5月</a>　建康瓦棺寺重建戒坛，是年五月，应僧慈济之请，为作记。作品：《崇胜戒坛记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254555' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254555?labeling=true' target='_blank'>崇胜戒坛记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254555")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254555'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254555'>佛刹之在江左，莫先于金陵之瓦棺寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254555_comment'></div>盖自东晋兴宁二年，移陶官秦淮之北，而以其南旧陶地施僧慧力，以为之寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254555_comment'></div>或曰瓦官谓陶官也，后讹以为棺尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254555_comment'></div>又曰昔有僧诵《法华经》者，以有虞氏之制葬于城隅，而莲华生其上，故寺以瓦棺得名，然莫可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254555_comment'></div>考之寺记，晋武帝宁康三年，始建戒坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254555_comment'></div>唐贞观二年，造阁三成，高二十五丈，挟以东西二阁，通十有九楹，为一方雄杰之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254555_comment'></div>其后阁坏于南唐，又新之，号吴兴阁，而寺名升元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254555_comment'></div>宋有天下，易升元为崇喜阁，亦烬于火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254555_comment'></div>太平兴国五年，更锡崇胜院额，戒坛在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254555_comment'></div>建炎渡江，兵寇杂扰，寺宇无一存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254555_comment'></div>绍兴之十九年也，有寓僧福涛，慨然欲复之，而寺基废为军营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254555_comment'></div>会慈济大师初政，以慈恩教法自北方之汉，曰吾教江南未有传也，闻智者大师尝讲正观，造疏钞于此，则此地宜为讲席久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254555_comment'></div>相与庐其侧，以告于有司，请于朝，得其地才什一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254555_comment'></div>施者渐集，而涛遽化，政主之馀二十载，悉力营焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254555_comment'></div>凡殿宇像设与夫讲授之堂、栖息之室、庖湢库廪，无不备具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254555_comment'></div>乃致院事，以付其徒，甲乙传之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254555_comment'></div>书来请曰：初政幸未死，得以了此寺缘也，愿有以记其始末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254555_comment'></div>顷予将漕江东，见其营缮之劳、工筑之力而志之不怠也，以为佛之徒能坚忍不拔，期于事之必集如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254555_comment'></div>然予闻佛之说以空为宗，以寂灭为乐，以身为伪，以诸相为妄，故虽垢衣乞食，坐卧不过桑下，而能神通变化，一光明中，台殿宝阁，弹指悉现，以起人敬畏之心，示其庄严佛土而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254555_comment'></div>后之读书者，不解佛所说义，乃欲竭人之力，穷土木之工，以崇饰塔庙，效其髣髴，然神通示现者无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254555_comment'></div>方人之土木者有限，故言治者诋以为生民之蠹，而事佛之实，固不在是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254555_comment'></div>今慈济师则不然，惟以讲演妙义，动化一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254555_comment'></div>随其志之所遇与施者所可及，而使荆榛瓦砾之墟，复为道场清净之域，规制仅足，不侈不陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254555_comment'></div>亦建大阁，崇且百尺，造为千佛，以五时教法，寘机轮之藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254555_comment'></div>远近从学，持钵而食者，动溢千指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254555_comment'></div>其视正观升元寺宇之旧，若三千大千世界纳一毛孔，而四方上下，随处各异，又如四大海水入一蹄涔，而鱼龙虾蛭，游戏自在，不知是大是小，是同是别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254555_comment'></div>师闻之曰：是中安有大小同别耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254555_comment'></div>曩者仁宗皇帝赐一宝珠，径大四寸，镇在戒坛，前日劫火洞然，此珠不坏，照耀虚空，如揭日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254555_comment'></div>又顾长康曾于寺室手画金粟如来之像，号为神妙，吾得旧本刊置壁间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254555_comment'></div>有人如此，入吾寺门，受其足戒，能于宝珠恭敬作礼谛观，审见此寺八百年间无成坏相，隐然常住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254555_comment'></div>况于经营建立，比量大小，作去来今，何有是处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254555_comment'></div>欲解斯义，往问金粟，或说半偈，当能了之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254555_comment'></div>予笑曰诺，因为之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254555_comment'></div>淳熙五年五月，具位韩某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1254555_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年6月4日</a>　建议整顿滥设修法书局。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年8月</a>　七月间，陆游自蜀还朝，除提举福建常平茶事，元吉与之相见甚欢，八月赴任，有诗送行。作品：《送陆务观福建提仓》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送陆务观福建提仓<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作洪适诗）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243497")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243497'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243497'>觥<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>船相对百分空，京口追随一梦中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243497'>落纸云烟君似旧，盈巾霜雪我成翁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243497'>春来茗叶还争白，腊近梅梢尽破红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243497'>领略溪山须妙语，少迂使节上凌风<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：仆为建安宰，作凌风亭。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243497'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_243497'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_243497_0'>⑴ 《永乐大典》卷七五一八作航</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_243497_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年8月4日</a>　请予增改父母年甲而冒封的进士以处罚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年8月12日</a>　八月，请外任，十一日赐诏不允，再辞，十二日除龙图阁学士知婺州。作品：《辞龙图阁学士状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷9。）</span>《除龙图阁学士谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞龙图阁学士状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年8月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254340")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254340'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254340'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，八月十二日，三省同奉圣旨，除臣龙图阁学士与郡者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254340_comment'></div>臣闻命过优，震惧无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254340_comment'></div>伏念臣猥以凡庸，久玷从列，蒙圣知为甚异，荷恩渥为至隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254340_comment'></div>玩岁愒日，尸位素餐，自知既明，冒昧有请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254340_comment'></div>陛下天地父母之仁，未忍捐弃，倘欲徇其私志，畀以承流宣化之任，在臣愚分，已为叨逾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254340_comment'></div>惟龙图秘职，首冠西清，稽之故事，则非贤达而罔居，质之近制，则须功勤而乃授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254340_comment'></div>岂臣猥琐，所可克承！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254340_comment'></div>至于郡寄，臣欲自效，则不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254340_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下洪覆无私，大明旁烛，收还宸涣，以穆师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254340_comment'></div>或乞依昨降指挥，检会臣前来除臣日职名，依旧带行，庶几不至过有侥倖，以明圣朝选授之公，以全下臣知止之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254340_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254340_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1254340_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1254318' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254318' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254318?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除龙图阁直学士谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年8月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254318")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254318_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254318'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254318'>冒三铨之久，长玷近班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254318_comment'></div>首六阁之联，遽叨美职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254318_comment'></div>恩踰意表，愧溢颜间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254318_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚惧、顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254318_comment'></div>窃以入从出藩，本侍臣之常礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254318_comment'></div>循名责实，斯主上之至权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254318_comment'></div>逮夫宠数之骤加，必有劳能之可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254318_comment'></div>仰河图于东序，是惟冠百世之弥文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254318_comment'></div>通禁橐之西清，必以待一时之旧老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254318_comment'></div>如臣者少而孤陋，晚益颛冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254318_comment'></div>符节屡颁，久载驰于周道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254318_comment'></div>玦环递赐，怅几入于修门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254318_comment'></div>未酬神圣之知，窃有满盈之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254318_comment'></div>兹由常伯，自诡便藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254318_comment'></div>纶命高华，岂谓疏荣之特异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254318_comment'></div>奎传炳耀，殊非避宠之能安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254318_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下汤圣日跻，尧仁天覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254318_comment'></div>察臣持循法令，粗知课力之方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254318_comment'></div>俾臣宣布诏条，曲示临民之渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254318_comment'></div>顾此鸴鸠之质，曷窥龙马之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254318_comment'></div>臣敢不祓饬懦衷，答扬隆施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254318_comment'></div>官虽外服，尚司宝禁之储；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254318_comment'></div>名在诸儒，敢忘论思之报？</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1254318_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　以元吉恩，追赠其父为通议大夫，焚黄遥祭。作品：《焚黄祭先考通议文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>焚黄告祭先考通议文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254662")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254662'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254662'>某比自天官，得请补郡，蒙恩列职学士，遂以彝典上延祢庙，赠阶从班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254662_comment'></div>追念坟垄，陷为异域，辄因讳日祭奠，用申焚黄之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254662_comment'></div>神灵不隔，庶其鉴之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1254662_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年9月9日</a>　与兄元龙（子云）、族兄元象（中父）登龙山饮酒话别。作品：《重九日中甫、子云二兄会别龙山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span>《醉落魄·戊戌重阳龙山会别》（菊花又折）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243509?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243509'>秋风作霜枫叶丹，扁舟未发龙山湾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243509'>山头窣堵半天出，十年笑我几往还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243509'>今年结束值重九，爱此山水照高寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243509'>亲朋话别情总厚，兄弟白首仍苍颜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243509'>相留一笑不易得，争挈美酒罗盘餐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243509'>登高正尔在高许，下视扰扰真尘寰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243509'>追思姑孰有故事，雅宴亦复同此山。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243509'>虽云小异得佳客，主人须猬怀胸奸。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243509'>沧波至今洗遗恨，岂若我辈同清欢。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243509'>是时郊原新雨足，历历烟树明江干。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243509'>放怀自知人境异，极目顿觉天宇宽。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243509'>惜无五弦寄妙手，已有征雁横云端。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243509'>南飞休论九万里，东游更渡五百滩。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243509'>明宵酒醒会相忆，梦绕百级凭飞栏。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243509'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_243509_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>醉落魄/一斛珠<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>戊戌重阳龙山会别</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_243626'>菊花又折。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243626'>今年真是龙山客。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243626'>杯行潋滟新醅白。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243626'>一醉相欢，莫便话离恻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243626_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243626'>从教破帽频欹侧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243626'>楼头霜树明秋色。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243626'>凭高待把疏星摘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243626'>天近风清，不怕暮云隔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_243626_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

余杭

德清

id='poem_sentence_0_243356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243356'>境静故应閒可乐，形臞犹有病相随。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243353'>敢将名利期当世，直欲文章似古人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1149')">1148-1149年</a>，31-32岁</div><div id='d529fd7922234a2b8a3157225899cb5d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>　与范端臣（元卿）游苕溪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年8月</a>　叶梦得（少蕴）卒，有祭文。作品：《祭叶少保文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭叶少保文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254648")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254648'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254648'>呜呼天乎，而酹公乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254648_comment'></div>典型其不可见，而后生者卒无师乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254648_comment'></div>天之生材，弗畀其全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254648_comment'></div>有能全之，其用则愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254648_comment'></div>或几于用，而啬其年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254648_comment'></div>兹世大患，从古以然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254648_comment'></div>惟公之材，可谓全矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254648_comment'></div>虽有智者，莫得而器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254648_comment'></div>贯穿六经，驰骋百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254648_comment'></div>笑谈千言，落笔万字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254648_comment'></div>时取其馀，施于政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254648_comment'></div>妙龄秀发，独步当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254648_comment'></div>遂以文鸣，入裁帝制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254648_comment'></div>群凶在朝，公不诡随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254648_comment'></div>晚逢中兴，丞辖是司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254648_comment'></div>历殿大邦，有仁有威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254648_comment'></div>隐然江淮，声誉四驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254648_comment'></div>闽盗俶扰，尺箠笞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254648_comment'></div>公曾不留，山林是思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254648_comment'></div>归奉祠宫，年既七十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254648_comment'></div>挂冠之请，靡俟终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254648_comment'></div>上心嘉公，赐以旌节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254648_comment'></div>子孙满前，丘壑自佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254648_comment'></div>优游福寿，数指可屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254648_comment'></div>凡世所患，公无其一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254648_comment'></div>今盖棺其何憾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254648_comment'></div>而天下犹且痛惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254648_comment'></div>岂公之材虽用而不久于庙堂，公之年虽高而不及于百岁，徒令多士诵其文章，四夷想其风采！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254648_comment'></div>时无老成，邦国殄瘁，则孰不闻风而咨嗟，过车而堕泪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254648_comment'></div>某早以大父之契，登公之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254648_comment'></div>无尺寸之长，而猥蒙国士之待；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254648_comment'></div>有通家之旧，而不翅子弟之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254648_comment'></div>训诱之谊，敢或不遵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254648_comment'></div>曾数月之不见，遂俯仰于千春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254648_comment'></div>此其所以呼天自悼，而一哀有倍于众人也！</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1254648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年8月</a>　叶梦得（少蕴）卒，有挽诗。作品：《叶少保挽词六首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243162' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243162' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243162?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243158'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243158'>翰墨通家旧，吁嗟大父时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243158'>追随千里驾，酬唱百篇诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243158'>小器惭非远，孤童误见奇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243158'>慇勤授简意，敢负昔年期<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243158'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_243158'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_243158_0'>⑴ 自注：公在闽中作万象亭，某为之赋。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_243158_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_243157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243157?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243157'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243157'>忆罢仪曹试，登门语更亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243157'>故怀如昨日，一醉赏馀春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243157'>佳句犹沾墨，遗编竟掩尘<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：公欲序高祖文集。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243157'>烟云变朝暮，感慨独伤神。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243157'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243157_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>　冬，苦寒，寺僧以炭为赠。作品：《明老惠炭戏以二小诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_243051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明老惠炭戏以二小诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243051")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243051'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243051'>雪里难逢送炭人，地炉炙手便生春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243051'>酸寒东野真堪笑，解道曲身成直身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243051'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243051_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243052?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243052'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243052'>道人作喜每逢场，一束乌薪发电光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243052'>便使樽前化红袖，不妨笑杀许旌阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243052'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243052_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　送邹橒（德章）之庐州教授任。作品：《送邹德章序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送邹德章序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254462")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254462'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254462'>仕将为道耶，学焉而行之，固为道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254462_comment'></div>亦为利耶，不耕绩焉，而资于上，非利而何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254462_comment'></div>故虽孔子其历聘诸侯者，思以行其道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254462_comment'></div>有公养之就焉，亦以食其利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254462_comment'></div>而《记》亦曰「大言入则受大利，小言入则受小利」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254462_comment'></div>夫利与道不啻水火，而圣人之所不废者，盖亦权其轻重而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254462_comment'></div>一于道焉，则是贫者必择禄而后养也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254462_comment'></div>一于利焉，则是蹠之粟有不必辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254462_comment'></div>是故居上位而道不行，万钟弗顾也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254462_comment'></div>居下位而道无诎，虽升釜弗耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254462_comment'></div>今之仕者何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254462_comment'></div>挟策而咏诗书，执笔而习文词，既已利之矣，幸而得焉，汲汲然惟惧其不富且贵，则其于利岂有已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254462_comment'></div>且上以是求旃，吾以是应旃，苟舍是而由他术，则愈下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254462_comment'></div>向之利之者，诚不得已也，而今之利之者，其亦不得已哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254462_comment'></div>然则古之所谓仕者常概诸道，今之所谓仕者常怵于利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254462_comment'></div>嗟乎，今之人其无意于古乎，几何不指此以为迂且阔也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254462_comment'></div>晋陵邹德章有意于古者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254462_comment'></div>始予见德章于吴中，则从有司之试也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254462_comment'></div>后再见焉，则德章已有列于仕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254462_comment'></div>予与德章复皆寓于龟溪，五日不问寒温，则仆从以请，十日不相往来，则两家婢子有嗟异之色，盖未尝不相从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254462_comment'></div>既再岁，德章之仕有期，而具舟将行矣，而予之羁栖益甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254462_comment'></div>德章不以夸于予，而以责于予曰：子无以语我乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254462_comment'></div>虽然，德章自少力学，年逾四十而始齿一命，亦可谓勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254462_comment'></div>同年之交游，甫从事于州县，而德章暂得尉，朝廷易之以主庐府之学，则亦不可谓不有合也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254462_comment'></div>今天下之吏，参倍于其缺，贫者数米而待，不下三四年，而德章故秋拜官，今秋就道，抑又一快意事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254462_comment'></div>是三者皆无足为德章道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254462_comment'></div>予尝闻其乡人言，德章，道乡先生之犹子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254462_comment'></div>自道乡起家，邹氏之子弟不登进士科者六十馀年矣，而得吾德章，容貌昂然，长身鬒须眉，皆有似于道乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254462_comment'></div>又道乡之始仕也，实掌教于淮南，今德章之于庐，亦淮南之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254462_comment'></div>故其风烈，庶几继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254462_comment'></div>然道乡之名满天下，正谏而不顾其身，窜逐而不忘其君，彼真以道自任者，德章其复他求哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254462_comment'></div>职之所当为，义之所可行，毋徇于世俗，而俾吾之道有立焉，则亦足以继之矣，非必践于其位，法于其言，然后以为继也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254462_comment'></div>若夫异日之富且贵，此今之仕者所宜动心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254462_comment'></div>如志于古也，其患无之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254462_comment'></div>德章遂以予言为然，信以契其乡人之望也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1254462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　选为龙泉主簿，将之任，作《归耕堂》诗辞友人。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>归耕堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243416")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243416'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243416'>退之手板愧丞相，渊明束带羞督邮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243416'>纷纷雀鼠待一饱，岂若植杖耘西畴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243416'>刘郎大耳最叵信，刚道田园不可求。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243416'>摩挲髀肉事鞍马，坚卧百尺营高楼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243416'>安知南阳扶耒手，谈笑为君分九州。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243416'>我来龟溪二三载，此策未办诚淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243416'>他年釜甑得长满，区区肯顾监河侯。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243416'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_243508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243508'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243508_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　三月下旬或四月初，施钜知徽州赴任，有诗送行。作品：《送施徽州二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243319' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243319' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243319?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送施徽州二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", id='poem_sentence_0_243319'>御史英名世罕俦，峨冠聊复渐承流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243319_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243319'>治功要自先冯翊，大惠何妨始歙州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243319_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243319'>野媪定知还去虎，山民从此罢赍牛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div
