href='/Writing/243318?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243318_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243318'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243318'>江出新安见底清，黄山高势碧峥嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243318_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243318'>裤襦会遣民皆有，枹鼓悬应夜不鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243318_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243318'>蜡屐未须怀别墅，虎符今喜得名城。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243318_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243318'>他时一榻容徐稚，端共舆人乐政成。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243318_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243318'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243318_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2bebf7928044420fb7c16c7e3a557bd8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2bebf7928044420fb7c16c7e3a557bd8");'><span id='2bebf7928044420fb7c16c7e3a557bd8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1153')">1152-1153年</a>，35-36岁</div><div id='2bebf7928044420fb7c16c7e3a557bd8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年7月</a>　刘一止（行简）上疏请老，复秘阁修撰致仕，元吉代作谢表。作品：《代刘给事谢复秘阁修撰致仕表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254327' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254327' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254327?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代刘给事谢复秘阁修撰致仕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254327")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254327'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254327'>窃食真祠，久逼桑榆之暮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254327_comment'></div>拜恩内阁，遂荣田里之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254327_comment'></div>揣己踰涯，荷天从欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254327_comment'></div>伏念臣奋身寒远，赋分奇穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254327_comment'></div>从六艺以决科，仅而得仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254327_comment'></div>接诸儒而奏技，晚特逢时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254327_comment'></div>顷游宪府之联，获冒书林之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254327_comment'></div>螭蚴载笔，尝预记于王言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254327_comment'></div>凤阁判花，复滥司于帝制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254327_comment'></div>进膺琐闼，数侍清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254327_comment'></div>乃遽速于颠济，迄自投于閒散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254327_comment'></div>乡闾作佚，既阅十年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254327_comment'></div>香火无功，殆逾数任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254327_comment'></div>惟是衰残之质，寖登耄耋之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254327_comment'></div>力已弗胜，无复为驹之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254327_comment'></div>老将奚逭，徒怀化鹤之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254327_comment'></div>祗有布其腹心，庶自乞其骸骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254327_comment'></div>岂期睿眷，特贲殊私，稍还论述之名，俾识退休之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254327_comment'></div>义兼念旧，恩出再生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254327_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下簪履兴慈，盖帷示轸，欲曲全于小物，肆纡照于容光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254327_comment'></div>谓臣麋鹿之姿，岂轩裳之是适；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254327_comment'></div>怜臣犬马之齿，曾钟漏之几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254327_comment'></div>许以传家，尚为报国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254327_comment'></div>臣敢不效忠自勖，守道勿渝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254327_comment'></div>击壤而歌唐虞，预识丰年之瑞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254327_comment'></div>闭门而咏周孔，益知化日之长。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1254327_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　春在德清。怀友人梁士衡，以诗寄之。作品：《寄梁士衡》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243368' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243368' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243368?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄梁士衡<span class='inlineComment2'>（癸酉年作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243368")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243368_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243368'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243368'>江上潮声日夜来，相望踪迹共尘埃。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243368'>乱花洗雨红成阵，叠嶂连天翠作堆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243368'>山市放歌知屡醉，沙津独步想千回。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243368'>松林月出溪桥夜，犹忆当年对野梅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243368'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243368_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
龙泉
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1b47935c3654443784ddd3b649dd43ef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1b47935c3654443784ddd3b649dd43ef");'><span id='1b47935c3654443784ddd3b649dd43ef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>，32岁</div><div id='1b47935c3654443784ddd3b649dd43ef' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　秋后，赴龙泉任。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='47b42df983da40628e012ba408d43f4d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("47b42df983da40628e012ba408d43f4d");'><span id='47b42df983da40628e012ba408d43f4d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1151')">1150-1151年</a>，33-34岁</div><div id='47b42df983da40628e012ba408d43f4d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　由丽水返龙泉。五、六月间，于主簿厅之南作双莲堂，有文记之。作品：《双莲堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254573?labeling=true' target='_blank'>双莲堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254573")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254573'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254573'>听事之南，有地数亩，平池面其前，古木荫其上，东南诸峰，罗列四出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254573_comment'></div>或曰是故为堂者，前主簿撤之，以为今听事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254573_comment'></div>予始至而爱之，思复其旧，会予假职事于郡，力不果为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254573_comment'></div>明年自郡还，舟行次南山下，见大木数十若栋楹者，弃于岸次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254573_comment'></div>或曰前郡有命治邮亭西津外，材且具水则暴至，而郡亦命止焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254573_comment'></div>予笑曰，是其以相我哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254573_comment'></div>归而谒诸县，尽得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254573_comment'></div>前所谓堂者，横植四楹，不卑不陋，始于五月之乙亥而迄于六月之壬子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254573_comment'></div>僝工之五日，有双莲生于舍之背，遂以名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254573_comment'></div>夫自古以来，仁人君子抱其器而不得施于时，守其道而老死于世者，盖非特世之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254573_comment'></div>世方求材而君子不逢其求，故在上者叹于无材，而材者伤于不用，此岂特人为然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254573_comment'></div>方予之为是堂也，废为瓦砾之场，鞠为荆榛之墟，过之太息而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254573_comment'></div>而轮囷合抱之材，适皆弃于山荒水涯，几为樵苏薪槱之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254573_comment'></div>一旦瓦砾荆榛者，变而为几席樽俎之胜，而轮囷合抱者，引而致于云霄之上，施斤斧，被丹雘，以逃寒暑而避风雨焉，彼岂取必于人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254573_comment'></div>是二者适相值以应吾之须而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254573_comment'></div>而君子不安其命，以俟后之须者，亦惑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254573_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254573_comment'></div>今龙泉为邑，二浙之穷处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254573_comment'></div>经营名利者不出其涂，出入富贵者不由其境，水行败舟，陆则折轴，四望而行，绵历巇险，不数百里不得郡邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254573_comment'></div>而吾与数君子仕焉，当其尘埃倥偬之暇，徜徉于兹，商天下之治乱，道古今之人物，已则酣歌起舞，劝酬交错，把酒赋诗，以极一时相从之乐，彼奔走势利者，盖亦愿此而不可得，于吾之道不既有所处乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254573_comment'></div>然堂之景物日益佳，后来之从事者日益众，为堂之计且无穷，故一草木之异何足以动吾心，姑志其实，使知自吾得之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254573_comment'></div>于是闻者以予为知言，请书以为堂之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1254573_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　送县尉连必达之新任。作品：《送连必达序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送连必达序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254465")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254465'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254465'>论州县之职下主簿尉一等，则无士之颉颃而尚气者，或不屑为之，然公卿之贵，间亦由此而渐进，譬之升阶焉，躐其级而跻其颠，必至于堂奥而后止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254465_comment'></div>官虽卑，其与民甚迩，故尉之职日逻于乡，月周于境，邑犬一吠，则援枹而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254465_comment'></div>凡里闾铢两之奸，影捕足蹑，志于必获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254465_comment'></div>死者在道路，则为反覆验视，惟恐民之无告也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254465_comment'></div>主簿之职，总邑之冗籍，凡民赋之上于官者，虽钱以釐计，米以撮计，必躬印其券，执朱墨以与小吏校，惟恐民之蒙扰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254465_comment'></div>簿之职稍安而尉之职稍劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254465_comment'></div>然簿虽安閒，奉檄以走他郡，官冷仆隶呵叱不前，所至公宇萧然如传舍，盖天下则同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254465_comment'></div>而尉之将送警护，法不出百里之内，设部曲，张旗帜，声金鼓，以怖远近，行色有光焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254465_comment'></div>一旦馘寇有加，则受赏而迁，更爵而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254465_comment'></div>故吏之好閒而无能者，往往幸为簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254465_comment'></div>喜功而望进者，往往幸为尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254465_comment'></div>二职均贱，而犹有美恶焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254465_comment'></div>予世之无能者也，贫不能养，方为簿于剑川，而延平连君必达适为之尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254465_comment'></div>君之言曰：吾岂恶閒者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254465_comment'></div>是特偶然尔，进退吾有命，功名不可以妄求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254465_comment'></div>由是必达之在尉，安静而不挠，间获盗当赏，则推而与其下，曰吾躬不能捕也，安可诳人而冒法？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254465_comment'></div>且杀彼以荣，我亦不忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254465_comment'></div>问邑之士大夫，必曰必达盖贤也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254465_comment'></div>问邑之民，必曰尉君于我有惠爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254465_comment'></div>故予虽不获久与君游，而悉其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254465_comment'></div>虽然，必达通经力学，自少有闻于乡，从天子得科第，试吏于此而称于民、称于士大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254465_comment'></div>其于当世之富贵，宜乎将由此而遂进矣，信乎其若阶而升者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254465_comment'></div>而予何足以自见，因其行也，姑道其所以然者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1254465_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年7月</a>　送其友李秀实之余杭主簿任。作品：《送李秀实序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李秀实序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254460")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254460'>绍兴之二十一年秋七月，吾友李秀实将主簿于馀杭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254460_comment'></div>秀实所居之邑，贤士大夫相与言曰：馀杭，小邑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254460_comment'></div>士之通经力学问而能成名以自立其家者，近推吾秀实之昆弟焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254460_comment'></div>故吾之徒岁时相与嬉游，閒暇相与往来，诗章文字，相与唱咏而酬和，杯酒谈笑，相与欢呼而谐谑，亦惟吾秀实昆弟之间为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254460_comment'></div>今其皆仕矣，行有日矣，吾之徒岁时孰与嬉游？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254460_comment'></div>閒暇孰与往来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254460_comment'></div>诗章文字，孰与唱咏而酬和？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254460_comment'></div>杯酒谈笑，孰与欢呼而谐谑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254460_comment'></div>以吾之私，固愿其留也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254460_comment'></div>然而人之爱其人，亦将使其功名彰于时而才业见于用欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254460_comment'></div>抑幸其终老里闾而未尝相舍也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254460_comment'></div>秀实之仕也，其将有遇焉者矣，则又言曰：主簿，卑官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254460_comment'></div>以秀实之所有，与今瀛州、藏室之选角逐于时，未知其孰为后先，而乃使之仆仆于令丞之末，与小吏课朱墨，书升尺，敛板庑下，以望上官之颜色，资廪粟以养其亲，则功名其果有期，其才业果不至于掩抑欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254460_comment'></div>某遂言曰：夫金、玉，天下之至贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254460_comment'></div>金之孕于山也，块然无以异于土也，治之则见焉，治之屡者则其质愈精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254460_comment'></div>使世不用金则已，如用焉，饰美泽之车，模甲父之鼎，吾知必于是乎取之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254460_comment'></div>玉之孕于山也，块然无以异于石也，攻之则见焉，攻之至者，则其文益著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254460_comment'></div>使世不用玉则已，如用焉，会期之圭璧，宗庙之罍斝，吾知必于是乎取之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254460_comment'></div>惟君子之于道也亦然，退然无以异于众人也，试诸事则辨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254460_comment'></div>其所试者多，则其道益广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254460_comment'></div>使世不用君子则已，如用焉，宰天下、运四海，皆君子之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254460_comment'></div>然君子之在下位，虽治一官，与宰天下不殊，举一职与运四海不殊，贱其官而弗为，易其职而无所事，非君子然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254460_comment'></div>自天子驻跸于吴，视其郡如京，视其附邑如畿，馀杭盖畿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254460_comment'></div>畿之郊，其刺举之任，非能不居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254460_comment'></div>畿之内，其尹之任，非通官大人不处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254460_comment'></div>而况朝廷耳目之近而接焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254460_comment'></div>以秀实之贤，犹惧其或不遇，则下焉者其何望哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254460_comment'></div>虽然，秀实无以其官之微而贱之，无以其职之下而易之，循吾道而俟焉，其将有遇焉者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254460_comment'></div>予久与秀实游，固知其不乐于为彼而乐于为此也，念无以纾别者之意，因摭是以为赠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1254460_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
丽水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1c19b77ed4a14831aa0c52a8e53ba131_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1c19b77ed4a14831aa0c52a8e53ba131");'><span id='1c19b77ed4a14831aa0c52a8e53ba131_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>，32岁</div><div id='1c19b77ed4a14831aa0c52a8e53ba131' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　未几，至丽水，假职事于郡，上书处州守臣施钜。作品：《上处守施察院书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上处守施察院书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254402")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254402'>某闻之，艺莫贵乎士，而馀民不能及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254402_comment'></div>然馀民之业莫不得售，而士之业反有不得售者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254402_comment'></div>今夫农朝而耕，暮而耘，以播殖五谷，一旦负五谷以适市，则市贾争趋焉，而世之人且曰此天下之良农也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254402_comment'></div>今夫工执技巧以事上，贾列其货于肆，而人见其器用之精，珠珍之富，则亦曰此天下之良工也、良贾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254402_comment'></div>其术益夸而人益贵，天下莫不以其名归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254402_comment'></div>惟士则不然，六艺之文无不习也，百家之说无不讲也，天地万物之理无不穷也，古今治乱之原无不通也，藏之惟恐其不深，养之惟恐其不固，苟暴于外，曰我能工是道也，我能明是说也，天下之人非特笑之，又从而贱之，且以为终无有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254402_comment'></div>夫以农商百工而得良名，以士而得贱名，故为士者或老死而不遇，则亦号于世曰，人不我知则贵矣，人不知亦嚣嚣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254402_comment'></div>农商百工守其业，士守其道，固自有轻重，后世之士不知守道之为务，反自贱而轻用之，此所以益见薄于世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254402_comment'></div>虽然，古之君子岂不欲用于世哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254402_comment'></div>孔子、孟子历聘诸侯，辙环天下，至于不得逞而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254402_comment'></div>盖士之于道，其用也从而见诸言事，非可豫定也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254402_comment'></div>而发于言者，有所不可隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254402_comment'></div>当其可与言而不言，君子以为固；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254402_comment'></div>不可与言而与之言，君子以为狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254402_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254402_comment'></div>以颜氏之如愚，非仲尼莫能识；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254402_comment'></div>至鬷明之不言，虽叔向几亦失之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254402_comment'></div>某北方之鄙人，少习于书，顾其不才，方为县之小吏，以从事于簿书米盐之间，而幸阁下来守是邦，其于分际之相远，名实之未加，固不可轻进其说以贻贱士之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254402_comment'></div>而石林叶公辱道其姓名于阁下，意阁下亦欲闻其言而察其为人，然不敢以请，姑道其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254402_comment'></div>恭惟阁下以通亮特达之资，济博厚高明之学，尝为天子耳目以观听四方之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254402_comment'></div>地方千里而为之侯伯，可以禁奸暴而安百姓，退不肖而举贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254402_comment'></div>而某者猥先众人，以卜于阁下，于是不可以不言，阁下其亮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254402_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1254402_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
缙云
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='33afdbad176c4041bf2aa310a388de37_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("33afdbad176c4041bf2aa310a388de37");'><span id='33afdbad176c4041bf2aa310a388de37_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>，34岁</div><div id='33afdbad176c4041bf2aa310a388de37' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　秋冬之际，离任龙泉，返临安候调，过缙云，游仙都山。作品：《夜宿玉虚宫……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_243075' -----title
上饶
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f247f47ad59140bd96ef40c908ceb6ae_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f247f47ad59140bd96ef40c908ceb6ae");'><span id='f247f47ad59140bd96ef40c908ceb6ae_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，应知信州黄任荣（择之）之辟，至上饶，赴信州幕府任，有诗寄其兄元龙（子云）等。作品：《赴信幕寄子云、叔左日右奂及同寺》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴信幕寄子云叔■<span class='inlineComment2'>（日奂）</span>及同寺<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243482")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243482'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243482'>回首寺桥同社客，想因明月话离愁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243482'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243482_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_243292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243292'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243292'>谢三船上醉同归，黄四花边手屡携。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243292'>巷里何曾异南北，屋头还复记东西。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243524'>颇讶地轴涌，未觉天柱亏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243524'>不让昆崙高，遂使泰华移。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243524'>诸峰七十二，磊砢略可推。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243524'>骈观拥佛髻，远睇凝蛾眉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_243170' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243170' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243170?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伏日诸君小集沈明远以小疾不预作诗戏之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", id='poem_sentence_21_243409'>裘穿心易怯，履败足微跫。<div id='poem_sentence_21_243409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_243409'>荷笠閒垂钓，回船稳系桩。<div id='poem_sentence_22_243409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_243409'>清狂时仄帽，泥饮屡空缸。<div id='poem_sentence_23_243409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_243409'>酬唱才皆敌，歌嘲语或哤。<div id='poem_sentence_24_243409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_243409'>闭门嗟懒惰，授简愧愚憃。<div id='poem_sentence_25_243409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_243409'>戈戟森磨厉，韶钧富击摐。<div id='poem_sentence_26_243409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_243409'>絮盐翻雅况，兰竹变新腔。<div id='poem_sentence_27_243409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_243409'>取醉华灯烂，催归戍鼓𪔔。<div id='poem_sentence_28_243409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_243409'>晴檐成夜雨，更听陇头泷<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《南涧甲乙稿》卷五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_29_243409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_243409'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_243409_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243017?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵沈明远春尽书事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243017")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243017'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243017'>街槐园柳绿初连，花尽春归思黯然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243017'>密叶鸣琴清梦断，白云双眼暮山前。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243017'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243017_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年，再得一女，尹穑以诗慰之，元吉次韵答谢。作品：《平生八见女而存者五人比又得女少稷作诗见宽次韵谢之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>平生八见女而存者五人比又得女少稷作诗见宽次韵谢之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243414")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243414'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243414'>渐老思似续，抚怀良惘然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243414'>空馀岁寒心，凛凛松柏坚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243414'>平生孔明妇，贫贱房且专。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243414'>生女不生男，造物宁我偏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243414'>娈彼五娇儿，弄瓦相随肩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243414'>人言可御盗，无乃缪以千。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243414'>囊金不办嫁，择婿那敢全。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243414'>今年又增一，比比安求旃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243414'>觉贫与觉富，可笑还可怜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243414'>向来两童乌，泡幻随变迁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243414'>应门固未计，畴复与我玄。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243414'>我家岂无人，文章绍编笺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243414'>经心不能释，欲语气已填。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243414'>筮言晚当见，默祷资明蠲。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243414'>行年且四十，那得慰眼前。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243414'>陶公谓胜无，此论吾师焉。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243414'>舒宣傥可待，弓裘犹足传<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243414'>今者事方殷，烦君费诗篇。<div id='poem_sentence_17_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_243414'>君诗妙难敌，巨刃迎小鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_18_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_243414'>炯炯明月珠，一一照眼圆。<div id='poem_sentence_19_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_243414'>吁嗟人生事，岁月如奔川。<div id='poem_sentence_20_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_243414'>岂不舒我忧，熊罴梦丰年。<div id='poem_sentence_21_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_243414'>蓬门亦何祥，但见巾帨悬。<div id='poem_sentence_22_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_243414'>会当亦添丁，荷锄赋归田。<div id='poem_sentence_23_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_243414'>老妻鼓掌笑，子意将谁愆。<div id='poem_sentence_24_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_243414'>须知百男恶，未若一女贤。<div id='poem_sentence_25_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_243414'>矧子四壁空，盖头无尺椽。<div id='poem_sentence_26_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_243414'>儿女分所定，底用相镵镌。<div id='poem_sentence_27_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_243414'>尚应具扁舟，江湖穷溯沿。<div id='poem_sentence_28_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_243414'>为君聘络秀，椎牛事烹煎。<div id='poem_sentence_29_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_243414'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_243414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_243414'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_243414_0'>⑴ 自注：退之称其子云：固宜常有人，文章绍编笺。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_243414_0'>⑵ 自注：渊明诗云：弱女虽非男，慰情良胜无。则五子亦后出也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_243414_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='26a0ecd417164e3ab57586a068991036_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1156')">1154-1156年</a>，37-39岁</div><div id='26a0ecd417164e3ab57586a068991036' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年11月</a>　有启贺施钜自吏部侍郎进为参知政事。作品：《贺施参政启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺施参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254440")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254440'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254440'>伏惟擢从铨部，荣贰钧衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254440_comment'></div>老成延登，未觉典型之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254440_comment'></div>有德并进，益知朝廷之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254440_comment'></div>成命甫传，舆情大慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254440_comment'></div>窃以士君子之行道，所贵逢时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254440_comment'></div>卿大夫之致身，必将辅国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254440_comment'></div>中兴在御，不次用人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254440_comment'></div>苟非一代之豪英，曷副四方之公望！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254440_comment'></div>恭惟某官器端厚而不挠，学粹纯而有源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254440_comment'></div>月旦之评，至行存乎孝悌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254440_comment'></div>蕃宣之效，成绩懋乎循良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254440_comment'></div>久寓迹于林泉，几功名志大而不偶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254440_comment'></div>逮赐环于台省，真富贵时至而自来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254440_comment'></div>然丞疑之任，虽协赞于上公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254440_comment'></div>而政事之联，亦调娱于万务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254440_comment'></div>历观近岁之比，殊乏大臣之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254440_comment'></div>自非从容中道而咸适其宜，则曷以进退有度而不失其正？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254440_comment'></div>真贤得位，多士向风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254440_comment'></div>伫观彝鼎之书，遂正衮衣之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254440_comment'></div>某受知特厚，趋庆莫遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254440_comment'></div>骧首辕间，敢有弹冠之志？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254440_comment'></div>庇身宇下，徒怀望履之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254440_comment'></div>抃蹈之情，实倍伦等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254440_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1254440_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年7月</a>　施钜知静江府，元吉代作到任谢表。作品：《代施资政谢静江府到任表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254325' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254325' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254325?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代施资政谢静江府到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254325")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254325'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254325'>擢从祠馆，就领帅符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254325_comment'></div>恩许自新，顾驰驱而敢后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254325_comment'></div>荣踰始望，徒跼蹐以自遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254325_comment'></div>已见吏民，具宣诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254325_comment'></div>伏念臣性资凡陋，术业空疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254325_comment'></div>比叨预于政机，迄无裨于国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254325_comment'></div>老将耄及，宁逃负乘之讥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254325_comment'></div>福过灾生，积有素餐之戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254325_comment'></div>曲荷乾坤之造，尚宽鈇钺之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254325_comment'></div>窃食投閒，慨惊魂之未定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254325_comment'></div>衔恩起废，恍神观以俱还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254325_comment'></div>惟兹八桂之封，外控百蛮之壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254325_comment'></div>奉琛面内，庙谟方事于绥怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254325_comment'></div>剖竹临边，阃寄益资于镇抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254325_comment'></div>岂翳衰钝，可副使令！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254325_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下大度兼容，至明洞照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254325_comment'></div>任贤而福天下，迈成汤选众之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254325_comment'></div>进德以尊朝廷，迪虞舜知人之哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254325_comment'></div>洪启同寅之治，聿求共理之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254325_comment'></div>臣敢不仰体眷慈，誓殚绵力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254325_comment'></div>虽听风观化，未能追循吏之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254325_comment'></div>而省事清心，亦足示远人之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254325_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1254325_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　春，闻朝廷平反冤狱，惩告讦之人，有诗感怀。作品：《圣政更新诏书正告讦之罪因得小诗十首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_242988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>圣政更新诏书正告讦之罪因得小诗十首<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_242988")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242988_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_242988_0'>① 原按：《通鉴续编》：绍兴二十五年十月，秦桧死，黜桧姻党。十一月，释赵汾及李孟坚、王之奇等自便。十二月，复张浚、胡寅、张九成等二十九人官；徙李光、胡铨于近州。二十六年正月，追复赵鼎、郑刚中等官。此诗所谓十年言路皆支党，雷州司户却生回，卫公精爽故依然，皆记其事。谨附识。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242988'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242988'>恶复凶终事久知，岂知圣断不踰时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242988'>小儒未叹周南滞，但喜逢人敢说诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242988'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242988_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242987?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242987'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242987'>桓温将死谢安起，霍氏初除魏相来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242987'>谁与圣君安大业，巍巍廊庙可无材。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242987'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242987_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242986?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242986_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242986'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242986'>圣朝遂失诛元载，公议犹能去霍山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242986'>落胆徒闻温御史，不知睿意在群奸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242986'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242986_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242985?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242985'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242985'>元祐诸公秉国均，诏条先请惠吾民。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242985'>孤雏腐鼠何劳逐，准拟朝廷政事新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242985'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242985_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242984?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242984'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242984'>金貂七叶谁能必，石椁三年计自愚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242984'>得鹿覆蕉真一梦，求鱼缘木信狂图。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242984'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242984_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242983?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242983'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242983'>献可争先诋荆国，莹中居首论莆阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242983'>十年言路皆支党，前无一语讥安昌<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：支党，用诏语。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242983'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242983_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242982?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242982_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242982'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242982'>近闻羔雁已成群，藻鉴渠能泾渭分。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242982'>急士且须侯雍齿，得贤端可吏朱云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242982'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242982_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242981?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242981'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242981'>刺字几漫冠欲尘，向来浮薄自纷纷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242981'>尔曹胸次多周孔，忍作铜山破贼文。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242981'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242981_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242980' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242980' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242980?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242980_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242980'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242980'>荆棘谁令满路栽，雷州司户却生回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242980'>独怜阳陆真天命，不见承平公道开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242980'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242980_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242979' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242979' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242979?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242979_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242979'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242979'>潮阳初谪八千里，中令俄成十九年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242979'>地下修文应泚笔，卫公精爽故依然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242979'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242979_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6521f0a220214e38bfe557183251ec2a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6521f0a220214e38bfe557183251ec2a");'><span id='6521f0a220214e38bfe557183251ec2a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>，39岁</div><div id='6521f0a220214e38bfe557183251ec2a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>三、四月间，上书周葵（立义）作品：《上信守周侍郎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254404?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上信守周侍郎书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254404")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254404'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254404'>君子之学，必其内有所主，然后外有所不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254404_comment'></div>然世之君子，每切切然以得位为足以行其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254404_comment'></div>及其未也，则歉然以为道将不行，而不知不行者不害其为道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254404_comment'></div>古之圣贤，其未得位也，则养其所谓道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254404_comment'></div>其既得位也，则行其所谓道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254404_comment'></div>苟位不可居也，则亦全其所谓道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254404_comment'></div>是故投之富贵而不惊，屈于贫贱而不耻，凡吾之所以出处进退者，无非以道为准的焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254404_comment'></div>以一身而论之，则有穷达之殊，以道而观之，盖未始有二，吾知为道而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254404_comment'></div>至此而不能惑者，惟其学之内有所主也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254404_comment'></div>昔者伯夷之清，伊尹之任，柳下惠之和，孟子皆以为圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254404_comment'></div>其清与任，世固以为不可跂及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254404_comment'></div>至于所谓和者，遂以为将无所往而不合，盖世俗之所谓和也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254404_comment'></div>及观士师之三黜，与孟子之所言，然后知圣人之和与世俗异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254404_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254404_comment'></div>进不隐贤，必以其道，遗佚而不怨，阨穷而不悯，此圣人之所谓和也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254404_comment'></div>夫圣人之所谓和者，进必以其道也，使不以其道，是安能不怨而不悯哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254404_comment'></div>故曰「直道而事人，焉往而不三黜」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254404_comment'></div>又曰「不以三公易其介」，则和之中又有直焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254404_comment'></div>而天下之论，遽以为无所往而不合者，则亦昧于圣人之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254404_comment'></div>则有以悻为直者，及其困也，于道不能无枉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254404_comment'></div>有以矫为直者，及其过也，于道不能无悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254404_comment'></div>惟圣人寓其直于和之中，故虽纵横万变，必至于道而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254404_comment'></div>虽有鈇钺之怒不能威，虽有轩裳之利不能诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254404_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254404_comment'></div>内有所主故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254404_comment'></div>某不佞，学于圣人之门，有志于此久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254404_comment'></div>少之时，闻阁下之名，常有愿见之心，不意今者获在幕府，是以敢冒昧而自进其所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254404_comment'></div>然窃观阁下之在朝廷，自中秘而为御史，自御史而司言动，真以道事君者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254404_comment'></div>退自吴门，优游里社，若无意于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254404_comment'></div>属者天子感悟，驿召旧人，阁下始以连帅之重留为春官，以总成均之政，意阁下之道，将自此而得行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254404_comment'></div>然而坐席未煖，出守于外，质诸道路，阁下议论之际，又有所不容者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254404_comment'></div>士之闻阁下之风，意其特立独行，以傲睨天下之士，言不可得而交，貌不可得而接也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254404_comment'></div>今也获拜于庭，以望见盛德之容，宽然其不矜，退然其不吝，凡小吏之所以事大官者，至忘其所畏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254404_comment'></div>然后知阁下其和而直者也，内有所主者也，深得圣人之道者也，故某愿三沐而受教焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1254404_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>送沈作喆（明远）之江西转运司任。作品：《送沈明远序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送沈明远序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254459")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254459'>部使者之职，所以廉察一道，翕张其财赋，疏理其狱讼，而举刺其官吏，厥任甚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254459_comment'></div>朝廷为之设属焉，将以佐其长，治其部，俾悉应夫使者之职而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254459_comment'></div>十数年来，使者之属，漫不之选，非出恩家则倖门，文书总总，懵不悉为何许事，间以豢乳臭子，则轻脱自肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254459_comment'></div>甚者假使者之权以把握州县，斗怒其长，开阖其黜陟，黩货而济其私，故贤士大夫率诋而议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254459_comment'></div>天子方新政事，当位者不敢蹈其故常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254459_comment'></div>今年春，吾明远始用为江西转运之属，贤士大夫则又曰，以明远之学且甚文与其才之可用也，岂特一部使者之属哉，乃自师儒而迁，岂丞相以犹子之嫌，故推而远之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254459_comment'></div>虽然，使明远不以丞相之故，少寘于承明著作之地，其谁曰不宜，然而特以是屈焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254459_comment'></div>吾是以贺使者之属得人，将自兹始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254459_comment'></div>大官厚禄，固非君子之慕也，非君子亦不能有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254459_comment'></div>自麓而跻于巅，自涯而涉其流，其必有渐乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254459_comment'></div>若是则明远之所蓄与士之所期，信不可以迟速计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254459_comment'></div>既相与言，因为之序以送之，且歌以系之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254459_comment'></div>歌曰：鼓桂󶏺兮汛兰舟，乘春风兮放中流，雨漫漫兮云油油。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254459_comment'></div>江之南兮千里，山有庐阜兮津有彭蠡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254459_comment'></div>其蓛笋蒲兮其鲙鲂鲤，其荼孔甘兮其酎则旨，奉亲之寿兮可以至喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254459_comment'></div>玉策兮金绳，漆书埃墁兮斯文未登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254459_comment'></div>桂宫兮宣室，干云委路兮工师未即。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254459_comment'></div>嗟摇落兮春菲，彼功名兮各自有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254459_comment'></div>时倏往兮易失，期子于高墉兮庶以永日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1254459_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>送同幕杨安止赴调。作品：《送杨安止罢信幕赴调》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送杨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>安止罢信幕赴调</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243495")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243495_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_243495_0'>① 原作汤，据聚珍本改</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243495'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243495'>后生仰前辈，今世思古人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243495'>岂重岁月久，所怀风俗淳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243495'>昔我家闽中，龟山实其邻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243495'>出门尚群盗，欲往志不伸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243495'>相从朋旧间，得语尽可珍。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243495'>俯仰今几何，遗编半埃尘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243495'>白头入幕府，始与夫子亲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243495'>夫子龟山裔，麇麚见祥麟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243495'>晚同柱后史，无心问平津。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243495'>典刑在眉睫，温然异群伦。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243495'>向来簿领中，挟书听谆谆。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243495'>岂不开我塞，异闻此其真。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243495'>亦或举樽酒，笑谈忘贱贫。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243495'>同僚各分散，世事日以新。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243495'>遥怜郑公乡，俎豆犹莘莘。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243495'>弹冠定不苟，家庭有书绅。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243495'>道学固未泯，吾谋复谁陈。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243495'>尚想金马门，西湖醉馀春。<div id='poem_sentence_17_243495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_243495'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_243495_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>始与张孝祥（安国）游。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>罢信州幕职。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>长女复嫁吕祖谦（伯恭）<br /></div><div class='label1' id='812297081a2c4281a4258f2f30251f2b_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1170')">1169-1170年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='812297081a2c4281a4258f2f30251f2b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　春尽还上饶忧居，杜门读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年6月</a>　其友张孝祥（安国）卒，讣闻，作文悼之。作品：《祭张舍人文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭张舍人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254657")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254657'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254657'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254657_comment'></div>安国之才，一旦千里，信朝燕而暮越，历万险而不踬，非方皋与造父，孰得撙其衔辔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254657_comment'></div>发嘉誉于儿童，首英名于多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254657_comment'></div>脱蛟鲸之垂涎，排鸳鸑而接𦐠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254657_comment'></div>奋长缨于册府，见诸老之戢袂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254657_comment'></div>出拥六州之麾，入裁两院之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254657_comment'></div>烂珠璧于文词，捷风雨乎政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254657_comment'></div>洒妙墨之琳琅，倾高谈于意气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254657_comment'></div>边陲望其威声，黎民歌其遗惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254657_comment'></div>驰骋十有五年，畴不谓之已试！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254657_comment'></div>亦足以方驾群豪，轶步当世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254657_comment'></div>嗟人生之多艰，固靡限乎富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254657_comment'></div>眷昔贤之有言，无八九之如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254657_comment'></div>况屈吾安国之指，十不满其一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254657_comment'></div>上则谐于父母，下则拊于兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254657_comment'></div>委涧藻之莫收，乏阶兰之或莳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254657_comment'></div>触炎高而遽疾，卧空舟而倏逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254657_comment'></div>委盖棺于朋友，付弱女于诸婢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254657_comment'></div>功名鼎来，赍志没地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254657_comment'></div>他人不能一日，行路为之陨涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254657_comment'></div>尚何三事之可欷，百龄之足计哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254657_comment'></div>我方衔忧，公讣奄至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254657_comment'></div>死生契阔，俯仰则异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254657_comment'></div>仅馀丰碑，绝笔千字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254657_comment'></div>惟恸哭之云阻，寓斗酒而往酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254657_comment'></div>望孤坟于钟山，尤仿像于一醉也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1254657_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　秋，覆朱熹书，以“圣人妙处在合”，“释氏之弊在分”作品：《答朱元晦书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷13。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　为朱熹清湍亭题诗。作品：《朱元晦清湍亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243424' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243424' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243424?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朱元晦清湍亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243424")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243424_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243424'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243424'>青山足佳游，远睇欲无路。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243424'>稍寻绝涧入，始辨云间树。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243424'>泉声若招客，倚杖得夷步。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243424'>惊湍泻乱石，激激有清趣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243424'>风微鸟哢幽，日彻鱼影聚。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243424'>居然鱼鸟乐，正欠幽人住。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243424'>野僧岂忘机，作亭以兹故。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243424'>因君赋新诗，我亦梦其处。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243424'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_243424_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　忧居上饶。是年似有兰溪之行，与范端臣（元卿）、吕祖谦（伯恭）、曾正中游栖真寺灵洞。<br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年2月</a>　跋两贤堂石刻吕本中（居仁）、韩驹（子苍）、曾几（吉甫）诗帖。作品：《跋吕居仁韩子苍曾吉甫诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《四库辑本别集拾遗》页139。）</span><div id='poem_1254507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋吕居仁韩子苍曾吉甫诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙七年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254507")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254507'>广教仁老，既为吕、曾二公立两贤堂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254507_comment'></div>又得公所书数诗及韩子苍舍人酬唱，刻石置堂上，可与好事者言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254507_comment'></div>前辈文采风流，零落殆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254507_comment'></div>其交友情谊，尚因其诗笔往来见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254507_comment'></div>淳熙七年二月丁酉，颍川韩某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1254507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　是秋，得祠禄，提举太平兴国宫，有谢表。作品：《谢提举太平兴国宫表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254312' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254312' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254312?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢提举太平兴国宫表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254312")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254312_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254312'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254312'>窃辅郡之符，自贻谤戾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254312_comment'></div>赋真庭之禄，俾逭饥寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254312_comment'></div>滋佩恩怜，徒深感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254312_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐、顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254312_comment'></div>伏念臣学知为己，仕切慕君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254312_comment'></div>荷圣神识拔于众人之中，遭逢特异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254312_comment'></div>躐侍从周旋于六官之表，忌嫉已多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254312_comment'></div>惟思朴直以尽忠，讵敢窥觎而倖进！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254312_comment'></div>朅因请外，复玷承流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254312_comment'></div>谓抑强禁暴者，刺史之常规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254312_comment'></div>若避事怀私者，古人之深耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254312_comment'></div>岂虑中伤之铢积，遂能摇动于风闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254312_comment'></div>含沙几类于短狐，射市乃遭于强弩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254312_comment'></div>诬其怨望，固已坠臣于深渊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254312_comment'></div>蔑以贪污，直欲锢臣于圣世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254312_comment'></div>赖至仁之在上，知群下之隐情，洞见肺肝，保全躯命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254312_comment'></div>然臣恐惧阅三时之久，羁穷怀十口之忧，未容放迹于山林，但有投诚于君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254312_comment'></div>函蒙鸿造，肆轸馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254312_comment'></div>縻廪稍于安閒，贷驰驱于衰病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254312_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下曲成万物，怀保小民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254312_comment'></div>力辨忠邪，益恢张于治具；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254312_comment'></div>大明黜陟，庸丕变于士风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254312_comment'></div>将寻尺之有施，示盖帏之罔弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254312_comment'></div>察其既往，许以自新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254312_comment'></div>臣敢不砥砺素衷，激昂晚节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254312_comment'></div>无功而禄，第为糊口之羞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254312_comment'></div>有命不渝，尚切粉身之报。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1254312_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　徙居上饶南涧新宅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　又作列岫亭。作品：《列岫亭用范伯升韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>列岫亭用范伯升韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243420")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243420'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243420'>自我来南溪，池塘几春草。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243420_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243420'>结茅依云端，爱此山回抱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243420_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243420'>奇峰七十二，罗列景逾好。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　陆游（务观）寄著色山水屏，有诗答之。作品：《陆务观寄著色山水屏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243456?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陆务观寄著色山水屏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243456")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243456_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243456'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243456'>我居面山俯潺湲，凭轩卧牖皆见山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243456'>山光水影入怀袖，秀色爽气非人寰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243456'>故人怜我新结屋，犹恐看山未能足。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243456'>丹青写作何许图，不碍闭门聊纵目。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243456'>千峰缭绕生白云，小舟荡漾横江滨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243456'>楼台高下出兰若，杳渺似有钟磬闻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243456'>坐惊岩壑环四壁，寥落高秋变春色。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243456'>方壶瀛洲远不隔，武陵桃花定谁识。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243456'>君不见韦侯绝笔画古松，黑雨白日摧虬龙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243456'>杜陵老翁三叹息，况有山木洪涛风。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243456'>又不见玉堂真仙草诏罢，静爱春山郭熙画。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243456'>文章信美身不閒，青<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>嶂白波眼中借。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243456'>我今乘间身未衰，杖藜独步哦新诗。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243456'>出门见山入见画，佳兴自喜来无时。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243456'>卧龙山腰镜湖尾，知有高斋照清泚。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243456'>功名逼子未得休，归坐玉堂应记此。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243456'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_243456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_243456'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_243456_0'>⑴ 原作清，据聚珍本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_243456_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　作可止斋，书请袁说友（起岩）题诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　与徐釐（应祺）唱和，并为其兼净亭作铭。作品：《次韵徐应祺小楼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span>《兼净亭铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_243211' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243211' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243211?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵徐应祺小楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243211")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243211_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243211'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243211'>潋潋清波泊路衢，垂垂高柳对扶疏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243211'>已知百尺楼堪卧，况有三重茅可居。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243211'>我老讵能赓鲍谢，君才端合绍严徐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243211'>直须座上千钟酒，浇起胸中万卷书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243211'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243211_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1254597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兼净亭铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254597")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254597'>徐应祺种竹溪上，结茅竹间，曰为挟筴之地，其宗人行仲取东坡诗语，名以「兼净亭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254597_comment'></div>应祺曰：此非特水竹然也，亦聊以寓吾心尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254597_comment'></div>予过而爱之，应祺请铭以述其意，为作数语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254597_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1254597'>古士爱竹，朝暮竹间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254597_comment'></div>竹不并水，犹如住山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254597_comment'></div>有乐水者，日临清流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254597_comment'></div>无竹与依，汎然具舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254597_comment'></div>嗟哉徐子，结亭自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254597_comment'></div>惟水与竹，乃二者俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254597_comment'></div>水清十寻，竹密千挺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254597_comment'></div>澄波修干，接影交映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254597_comment'></div>好事来观，目以「兼净」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254597_comment'></div>是中有象，非色非想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254597_comment'></div>挟筴徜徉，契我心赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254597_comment'></div>曾不取舍，鱼与熊掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254597_comment'></div>问之何得，得于《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254597_comment'></div>《春秋》之本，上下可求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254597_comment'></div>惟虚惟一，以息以游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254597_comment'></div>吾闻圣贤，道以治世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254597_comment'></div>匪若野人，罔舍内外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254597_comment'></div>子曷逮止，时行则行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254597_comment'></div>既明子心，亦成子名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1254597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年12月</a>　十二月丙午，跋苏轼六帖。作品：《跋东坡帖六纸》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋东坡帖六纸</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254488")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254488'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254488'>东坡前四帖，以倅杭及黄冈时书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254488_comment'></div>后帖言屡乞解职，则在朝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254488_comment'></div>淳熙七年十二月丙午，韩某观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254488_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1254488_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　应邵武友人黄永存（坚叟）之请，为其所筑囿台命名曰 “云风”，并作记。作品：《云风台记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>云风台记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254559")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254559'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254559'>凡人之情，郁则思舒，局则思放，低滞则思高明夷旷之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254559_comment'></div>古之人作囿以游，筑台以观，否则之山林而托焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254559_comment'></div>虽仲尼之圣，犹登泰山而临吕梁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254559_comment'></div>岂不若是将无以寓其情耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254559_comment'></div>然君子务以适其情，而未始纵其情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254559_comment'></div>务以适其情者，不过避喧以习静，升高以望远，俾山林皋壤接乎吾前，而尘垢秕糠不溷吾中而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254559_comment'></div>永嘉黄使君坚叟乡昭武也，其居一榻之外，无所游览，久之得舍北地数亩，规以为囿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254559_comment'></div>面山者为堂，面竹者为亭，作室于花间，置槛于溪涘，则既有名佳之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254559_comment'></div>而昭武之南山，最为奇秀，联属如屏障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254559_comment'></div>其西则君山，远在百里之外，耸直倚天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254559_comment'></div>城之中有山号登高，熊踞而虎卧，林木苍然，大溪络其下，东北诸峰，合遝四出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254559_comment'></div>坚叟筑台而望之，其崇仅寻丈也，凡一郡之山无逃焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254559_comment'></div>书来请予名，予少尝寓昭武，与坚叟游其山川，胜槩历历可想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254559_comment'></div>则以告之曰：韩文公诗，有云「东堂坐见山，云风相吹嘘」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254559_comment'></div>子之为是台也，以山故耶，山之状不可以名，盍试以「云风」命之，何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254559_comment'></div>坚叟喜曰：云之与风，即山之自出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254559_comment'></div>今吾老矣，仕于四方，得郡而将行，顾未能终耕里闾，而惟徜徉花竹之阴，因台之成，披襟矫首，以睨夫云风之去来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254559_comment'></div>当其滃然之奇，漻然之清，以荡吾目而触吾怀，吾之乐则无尽，而君亦何自知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254559_comment'></div>予曰：予固不得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254559_comment'></div>盖尝思之，以坚叟之才，遇事有立，自为州县官，官声卓然，宜其蚤获用于世，而婆娑晚境，犹为天子守千里之地于海隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254559_comment'></div>其所设施虽未为不遇，然而尝闻之，古之贤者每以致身功名之会，则为依乘风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254559_comment'></div>今圣明在上，罗天下之士，以清中原而复太平之业，则夫云集而应龙翔，风薄而万窍怒，子之功名得无其时，又何蹙缩于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254559_comment'></div>坚叟谢曰：吾岂为是也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254559_comment'></div>君既名之，则亦书之，将以示吾乡之人，以无忘君之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254559_comment'></div>于是书之台上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254559_comment'></div>淳熙七年十二月，颍川韩某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1254559_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　张子顔（几仲）由隆兴府移知绍兴府，除夕前一日，会饮于上饶传舍。元吉与会，题张子颜所藏醉道士图。始自号南涧翁。作品：《题张几仲所藏醉道士图》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_243135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243135?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题张几仲所藏醉道士图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", id='poem_sentence_0_243135'>何须坐客总能文，呼酒相逢日暮云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243135'>醉倒尽如狂道士，夜归谁问故将军<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243135'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243135_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_note_243135_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年1月</a>　跋《北齐校书图》作品：《跋北齐校书图》<span id='poem_sentence_0_243536'>高齐校雠谁作图，一时䌷书亦名儒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243536'>网罗卷轴三千馀，俗儒非真类迂愚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243536'>雌黄是正定不无，虚文末学徒区区。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243536'>丹书写此犹不渝，高鬟侍女曳红裾。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243536'>两骓帕鞍立奚奴，罢琴涉笔倾酒壶。<div id='poem_title_1254666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭四十四抚干叔文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年5月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254666")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254666'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254666'>淳熙八年，岁次辛丑，五月二十五日庚子，族侄易、族孙元吉、元修等谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于叔公四十四抚干韩公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254666_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254666_comment'></div>古先圣人，谓葬曰归，死或未葬，魂犹如羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254666_comment'></div>惟公之丧，远来自夔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254666_comment'></div>旅泊万里，踰三十期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254666_comment'></div>匪有仕者，归曷可期！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254666_comment'></div>既续公后，人皆涕洟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254666_comment'></div>某等咸寓是邦，逢车载驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254666_comment'></div>禅寂之山，母弟所栖，公其往焉，庶安于斯。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1254666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　赵蕃（昌父）赴辰州司理参军任，索赠言，元吉以诗送行，蕃次韵答之。作品：《送赵蕃辰州司理》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243320' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_4_1254598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_243614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243614'>绝景画图中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
