id='poem_sentence_3_243614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243614'>不惜归鞍照月，直教破帽吹风。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243614_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　韩淲自贵池归，携蜀人史千（伯强）来书及诗卷，元吉奇其才，答书及诗，劝其出仕。作品：《答史千书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷13。）</span>《史千伯强浮沉市廛……赠以绝句二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_1254415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答史千书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254415")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254415'>某顿首复书伯强隐君贤弟足下：曩闻从者尝经上饶，不获一见之幸，每以怅怅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254415_comment'></div>小儿来自秋浦，窃知从长者游，乃辱书縢之贶，辞义粲然，三复不能去手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254415_comment'></div>既已至慰，苍莨小亭又蒙惠然题咏，增光林壑，以重老朽之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254415_comment'></div>且拜近诗一轴，因叹足下才气议论卓伟如此，《汤谏》序文尽之矣，犹踸踔尘埃间，理有未喻，造物者抑将大其蕴而后发耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254415_comment'></div>来书所谓人才不可偏废者，确乎至当，安得用材者人人言此言哉，则天下事信无不举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254415_comment'></div>何由面布，凭纸耿耿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254415_comment'></div>蜀道辽邈，西归岂易，所寓尚可留否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254415_comment'></div>更希与时消息，以树远业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254415_comment'></div>区区不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1254415_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242978' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242978' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242978?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史十伯强浮沈市廛自号道人而笔力议论不可掩抑岂隐者耶观其诗卷赠以绝句二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_242978")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242978_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242978'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242978'>未容君识得君诗，添我幽栖一段奇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242978_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242978'>会有吹嘘天上去，沈香亭北要新词。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242978_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242978'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242978_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_242977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_242977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/242977?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_242977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242977'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242977'>头上尘冠岂易弹，匣中长剑箧中丹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242977'>放怀风月真馀事，好向朝廷策治安。<div id='poem_sentence_1_242977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_242977'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_242977_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　知信州林枅（子方）重建牙门，元吉为记。作品：《信州新建牙门记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254558?labeling=true' target='_blank'>信州新建牙门记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254558")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254558'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254558'>信之地势，来自灵山，中道石起如龙，鳞鬣隐现，至郡而伏，以赴于渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254558_comment'></div>前山品立如覆钟釜，水渟若留怀玉，高峰出艮隅，森植犹束笋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254558_comment'></div>故老相传得阴阳之胜，虽宣和青溪之盗，建炎寇攘云扰，皆莫能犯其地，而郡治岿然独在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254558_comment'></div>然南有牙门而不为观台，仅成一楼，与县之庋敕书者比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254558_comment'></div>阅岁既久，瓦腐甓圮，楹桷摧朽，殆将压焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254558_comment'></div>淳熙之七年也，莆阳林侯枅由中秘书来莅兹郡，既再岁矣，侯之政一以儒雅缘饰，简易而不烦，士民安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254558_comment'></div>岁适屡登，因以馀力大治其城壁与其四达之门，犹于牙门蛊敝未之议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254558_comment'></div>民相与言曰，吾侯宜为此矣，然距其舍我之日不数月，则奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254558_comment'></div>侯闻之叹曰，古之君子，所寓之舍犹必葺于一日也，况公宇乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254558_comment'></div>吾虽不敏，尚能为尔成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254558_comment'></div>好事者则又曰，州远于山而附于水，乏土，不可斸也，前人未能为之观台者，不以是耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254558_comment'></div>并庾有堆阜，侯呼庾吏问曰：平之无伤乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254558_comment'></div>曰：庸何伤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254558_comment'></div>侯笑曰：土于是焉取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254558_comment'></div>众欢然大服，乃以七月壬子，遂兴其役，增卑以为高，撤故以为新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254558_comment'></div>凡畚锸斤斧之工，悉厚其直，盖无一歛于民者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254558_comment'></div>踰两月告成，台崇十有六尺，楼其上，又二十尺，左右为两夹楼而阁道翼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254558_comment'></div>不侈不陋，适其地形之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254558_comment'></div>士民德侯之深，伟侯之绩，而惜其将解印绶也，愿有以识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254558_comment'></div>夫门阙之制尚矣，自天子至诸侯，所以出政令，时启阖，肃宾师一也，下观而化，于是乎在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254558_comment'></div>故雉门两观之作，书于《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254558_comment'></div>而汉儒记礼，乃以为库门、天子皋门，雉门、天子应门，惟鲁以周公之故用焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254558_comment'></div>然考之《大雅》，则皋、应二门之筑，亦周为诸侯之时，其因于商者可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254558_comment'></div>故其《诗》曰「乃立皋门，皋门有伉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254558_comment'></div>乃立应门，应门将将」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254558_comment'></div>且伉之为言，高也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254558_comment'></div>将将为言，严正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254558_comment'></div>岂诸侯之门必高且严正，然后应于礼欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254558_comment'></div>国朝著令，门厦藻栱之施，莫不有制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254558_comment'></div>惟郡之正牙门得用重屋立台，而设鸱覆㼧，其制特异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254558_comment'></div>盖揭镇名、建旌牙其上，鸣笳伐鼓以令昏旦者，视门以为表，非其舍宅比耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254558_comment'></div>信之为州，四百二十有三年矣，其地控闽粤、邻江淮、引二浙，隐然实冲要之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254558_comment'></div>山川秀发，人物繁夥，异时多士之隽屡冠天下，而宰辅之出，间亦蜚声名、立事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254558_comment'></div>其风俗兴起，固未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254558_comment'></div>今林侯举久坠之典，克合于古，斧藻面势，有光辉焉，非若汎然楼观登临之美，以为执事者游览之资而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254558_comment'></div>虽然，侯之车既攻而马既驾矣，不懈以思，不惑以移，断然图之而不日成之，以徇其民之愿欲，则侯之中所存与其所操执者，天下之事何往而不可为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254558_comment'></div>某方卜居郡郊，见其民之喜，而嘉其事之能立也，因为之书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1254558_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　应诸道坑冶铸钱使李大正（正之）之请，撰铅山《膽泉铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《铅山县志》卷26。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　春，作《拙蚕赋》，慨“不能务悦于人”者，能“自全其天”<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_1254273' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254273' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254273?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拙蚕赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254273")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254273'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254273'>韩子晨起，视窗中有物延缘，投隙抵穿，口如飞蛛，足若蛰蚿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254273_comment'></div>呼妪辈问之，妪笑曰，是拙蚕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254273_comment'></div>丝疏而弗绩，食饱而嗜眠，亡所用旃，戏置此焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254273_comment'></div>韩子感而赋之曰：翳樗栎之不材兮，信能保其天年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254273_comment'></div>岂有用之则贵兮，抑不用之或偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254273_comment'></div>吁造化者奚私兮，盍亦赋之自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254273_comment'></div>惟桑虫之何知兮，生蠢蠢而比肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254273_comment'></div>资采摘而不自养兮，甘鼎镬之烹煎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254273_comment'></div>大则施于纨绮兮，细则丽为纯绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254273_comment'></div>虽曰衣被四海兮，犹为蟪蛄之所怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254273_comment'></div>方众巧之竞骛兮，万族仰哺而争先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254273_comment'></div>何茧栗之弗为兮，耻营躯而自缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254273_comment'></div>匪畏死而遁逃兮，将羽化而飞翾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254273_comment'></div>宜妇姑指以为拙兮，蹇冥心于弃捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254273_comment'></div>彼庄生取喻于牺牛兮，支离攘臂于兵间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254273_comment'></div>不能务悦于人兮，殆亦自全其天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254273_comment'></div>圣有抱璞而深藏兮，时有不争于尚贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254273_comment'></div>粤抚槛而三叹兮，吾亦乐乎《太玄》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1254273_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年5月</a>　上年底，辛弃疾（稼轩）罢湖南安抚使，寓居于上饶之带湖，元吉与之过从甚密。是年五月，辛弃疾为赋祝寿词。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　辛弃疾（稼轩）带湖新居成，赋《蝶恋花》求韩元吉为记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年6月</a>　为金华潘景宪（叔度）可庵作记，论“人道即天道”作品：《潘叔度可庵记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潘叔度可庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254561")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254561'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254561'>物莫不有生，而人莫甚于畏其死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254561_comment'></div>世以养生为言者，求其气之所自来而保其神之所可至，呼噏运动，以规天地之造化，曰委形蜕骨，可无死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254561_comment'></div>而为西方之学者，从而诮之，以为人之生皆妄也，惟舍其生，然后见其不妄者存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254561_comment'></div>是谓发真归元，而得以出于死生之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254561_comment'></div>二说既立，未有不奇而信之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254561_comment'></div>虽然，彼固有激而云斯可也，犹以死生为累者耶，是亦遗人道而慕天道，孰知人道即天道也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254561_comment'></div>生虽不舍，岂不足以闻道，而死何足以累道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254561_comment'></div>在人犹在天也，苟不有见，徒自分尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254561_comment'></div>故曰「朝闻道，夕死可矣」，然则道何自而闻乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254561_comment'></div>又曰「未知生，焉知死」，然则生何自而知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254561_comment'></div>《易》之《系》乃曰「原始反终，故知死生之说」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254561_comment'></div>且死生既有其说矣，始之与终殆亦相似，而圣人不以其说示人者，欲人之自知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254561_comment'></div>由不能自知，故切切然惟他人之说是信，目瞪口呿，则亦无惑乎异端之言有以入之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254561_comment'></div>自汉以还，世之儒者仅能谈治道而不能知率性之道，于是治天下与性命之原，判然为两涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254561_comment'></div>千有馀年，以道为何物，则又特以为不过于君臣父子之间，礼乐刑政之际，所以治天下则然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254561_comment'></div>而论者轻之曰，尔之治天下，吾绪馀土苴也，而道常在于虚无恍惚之中，清净寂灭之域，外夫死生，弃夫人事，然后足以为道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254561_comment'></div>而儒者盖亦歛衽避之而不敢问，不则摭其近似而求合焉，是天下有二道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254561_comment'></div>盍亦观夫太极之生，阴阳之运，万物之作，在天成象而在地成形，动静隐显，莫适而非道，则其在我何独于死生而疑之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254561_comment'></div>圣人相授，惟精惟一，而仲尼所谓一以贯之者，曾未之见欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254561_comment'></div>予尝病世之学者不复知此久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254561_comment'></div>顷岁閒居，尝与吕伯恭论之，今伯恭不幸已往，而金华潘景宪叔度，从伯恭游最久而密者也，笃信好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254561_comment'></div>既连丧其室人，买地于金华之别麓，号「叶山」，以营其二内之藏，而虚其中央，以为他日自归之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254561_comment'></div>筑室于傍，因以游息，而语其乡人曰：吾非以厚死，吾之生亦在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254561_comment'></div>与予之说似合，而伯恭之友朱元晦，以闻道之意名之曰「可庵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254561_comment'></div>而叔度自名其前之堂曰「退老」，取伯恭之言以名其后之室曰「共学」，左则曰「庶斋」，右则曰「省斋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254561_comment'></div>二斋储书且万卷，以待朋友之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254561_comment'></div>市良田百亩，以为讲习聚食之资，而积其馀以赡并舍之百家，岁称贷而给之，目其仓曰「友助」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254561_comment'></div>省斋之南有堂曰「明极」，以伯恭旧以名其先人之精舍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254561_comment'></div>亡虑为屋五十楹，规地可千尺，用意勤勤若是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254561_comment'></div>予两窃为婺之守，值叔度庵未成，不获一至其处，而叔度乃欲予文为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254561_comment'></div>盖潘氏旧居松阳，以儒名家，逮移金华，而叔度又世其科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254561_comment'></div>自谓体弱不任趋走，曾未试于仕，气貌臞然而道艺日进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254561_comment'></div>距城十里，始为是庵，足以晨出而暮返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254561_comment'></div>其山水之环密，景物之閒旷，同志者至亦忘其归，而叔度每翛然自得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254561_comment'></div>夫士大夫耽生而恶死，厌常而喜异，一为茔宇，不曰旷达齐物，则必觊倖幽冥无穷之福，于吾圣人之学率未之究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254561_comment'></div>故予追思曩与伯恭所谈，为及死生大略，皆叔度之欲闻，亦以告其乡之士友，俾知叔度之意在此而不在彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254561_comment'></div>淳熙九年六月，颍川韩元吉记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1254561_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年6月</a>　六月丁巳，周必大进知枢密院事，有贺词启。作品：《贺周知院启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺周知院启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254442")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254442'>伏审显膺制命，升冠枢庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254442_comment'></div>庙堂裁万化之原，久资共政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254442_comment'></div>帷幄决千里之胜，兹赖本兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254442_comment'></div>眷意式隆，舆情胥忭，伏维庆慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254442_comment'></div>恭以枢密知院相公，器博而量远，学富而识宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254442_comment'></div>黼黻之文，濯江汉而并丽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254442_comment'></div>金石之操，亘寒暑而不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254442_comment'></div>蚤繇异科，遍仪华贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254442_comment'></div>出处系天下之重，议论发众人之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254442_comment'></div>裁诏北门，明白适帝王之体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254442_comment'></div>典铨南省，澄清无流品之淆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254442_comment'></div>逮入辅于政几，果重承于帝赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254442_comment'></div>是畴伟望，独总事枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254442_comment'></div>太尉而掌北军，几资妙算；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254442_comment'></div>冢宰之均四海，伫见延登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254442_comment'></div>某夙荷深知，欣聆渥涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254442_comment'></div>少年场屋，敢论逸步之先？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254442_comment'></div>晚景丘园，尚费鸿钧之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254442_comment'></div>其为欣蹈，实倍等伦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1254442_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年9月9日</a>　重九，与辛弃疾游云洞，有唱和。作品：《云洞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span>《水调歌头·水洞》（今日我重九）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>云洞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243407")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243407_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_243407_0'>① 在信州西（原按：此诗据《广信府志》补入。）</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243407'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243407'>挥策度绝壑，撑空见楼台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243407'>丹崖几千仞，中有佛寺开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243407'>老僧如远公，应门走蒿莱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243407'>下马问所适，褰衣指崔嵬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243407'>飞阑倚石磴，旷荡无纤埃。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243407'>坐久意颇惬，爽气生樽罍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243407'>仙棺是何人，蜕骨藏莓苔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243407'>举酒一酌之，慨然兴我怀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243407'>丹砂固未就，白鹤何时来。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243407'>不如生前乐，长啸且衔杯<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《南涧甲乙稿》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243407_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243407'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_243407_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>水洞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243567")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243567'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243567'>今日我重九，莫负菊花开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243567'>试寻高处，携手蹑屐上崔嵬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243567'>放目苍岩千仞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243567'>云护晓霜成阵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243567'>知我与君来。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243567'>古寺倚修竹，飞槛绝纤埃。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243567_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243567'>笑谈间，风满座，酒盈杯。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243567'>仙人跨海，休问随处是蓬莱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243567'>落日平原西望。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243567'>鼓角秋深悲壮。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243567'>戏马但荒台。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243567'>细把茱萸看，一醉且徘徊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_243567_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年9月</a>　朱熹来访，约徐安国同游南岩，辛弃疾闻讯后至。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　是秋，淮西安抚使延玺于郡城合肥建新楼，请命名为记，元吉取“风声鹤唳，以为王师”故事，名为“风鹤楼”。寄北图中原之望，并为记。作品：《风鹤楼记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>风鹤楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254560")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254560'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254560'>楼在合淝淮之南，故秦九江郡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254560_comment'></div>至汉孝文析其郡，又为庐江，实今西路也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254560_comment'></div>自春秋季年，吴尝会于橐皋，而汉封淮王，皆社于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254560_comment'></div>及孙、曹纷争，则以合淝寓扬州之治，筑为新城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254560_comment'></div>晋人扼淝水以败秦师，周世宗厉兵正阳，攻战于紫金山下，遗迹具在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254560_comment'></div>故今庐州形胜，腹巢湖，控涡颍，膺濡须，枕灊皖，隐然为用武之郊，置连帅以总兵民，厥任重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254560_comment'></div>乾道初，诏遣大将暨建康留钥之臣，同视庐城，浚其沟隍，增其甓埴，益固以坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254560_comment'></div>乃营田以寓兵，列戍以卫民，由是帅守之寄，尤遴其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254560_comment'></div>淳熙八年，武节大夫延侯玺来镇是邦，属岁旱荒，流徙塞涂，公私睊睊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254560_comment'></div>侯内抚饥羸，外弭寇攘，整财治军，准绳有度，官吏协和，民庶安辑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254560_comment'></div>其明年秋，政成事简，益求所未至葺而更之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254560_comment'></div>会大雨，水暴注，两市桥坏，伐木于山，以济病涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254560_comment'></div>又访州之贤哲故象，庙而享之，以兴起其俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254560_comment'></div>于是民服侯之化知所后先，惠而不扰，忠而能力也，相与言曰：吾侯劳于我矣，宜有以佚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254560_comment'></div>先是州廨之背有台，号「熙熙」，为岁时登临燕乐之所，久废不治，蓬生而土圮，愿复其旧，以纪吾成，以侈后观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254560_comment'></div>侯则谢曰：台固美矣，其可为乐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254560_comment'></div>然民之幸相与也，其取桥之馀材，台之旧址，因农之隙、卒伍之暇，为一楼以望四郊，虽不敢效前贤筹边之作，而骧首纵目，慨然俯仰，以无忘圣君顾忧，庶思效吾职者，则犹可哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254560_comment'></div>其冬楼既成，因其郡佐来请记之而问所以名者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254560_comment'></div>予尝行燕、赵、魏之野，有感于战国之事，盖城堞相望二三百里，坦坦而近，非有高山巨川之阻，而迭为长雄，势莫相下，世则以谓兵为险也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254560_comment'></div>然兵固自若，亡虑常数十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254560_comment'></div>以乐毅、廉颇用之则强，以庞涓、赵括用之则败，是岂在于兵，特以人为重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254560_comment'></div>及观谢幼度之战，正今合淝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254560_comment'></div>是时晋之渡江馀五十年，西北劲兵枭骑宁有在者，而能用吴楚之人以破其百万之众，至闻风声鹤唳，以为王师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254560_comment'></div>岂天之助者耶，亦人力尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254560_comment'></div>今朝廷视淮西几河朔比也，以为长城，以为北门，匪文武之英，智略之士，畴克任此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254560_comment'></div>而折冲厌难，俾数千里之地既庶而教，习于技击而隐于耕锄，蓄愤养威，不胜从军之乐而务为安强，如侯之用心，岂易云者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254560_comment'></div>夫幼度远矣，方万窍之号，九皋之鸣，闻于天外，功名之士，盖有起舞而叹者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254560_comment'></div>今遂以「风鹤」命之，亦纪其故实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254560_comment'></div>予虽不获奉侯之樽俎，从容楼上，以临淝水、望洛涧，八公之山，草木依然，英风壮气，可想而见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254560_comment'></div>后之登临者，识侯之用心，其忍忘哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1254560_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　九、十月间，邵阳教授沈千里之任，便道来访，请为其父母作墓志铭。临别，有诗送行，沈至玉山，有诗寄来，元吉次其韵。作品：《送沈千里教授邵阳》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span>《次韵沈千里玉山道中见寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243313' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243313' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243313?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送沈千里教授邵阳</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243313")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243313_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243313'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243313'>縠纹江畔得君诗，俊逸清新字字奇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243313'>一笑偶成归妹约，几年还见外孙辞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243313'>横经绛帐地虽远，给劄金门天未迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243313'>痛饮离骚吾事尔，湘山风物与春期。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243313'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243313_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵沈千里玉山道中见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243201")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243201'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243201'>霜晴怀玉自生烟，寒色凄凄过雁边。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243201'>路转湘南知几日，山连楚尾又穷年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243201'>相期鸡黍情欢甚，惜别尘埃意黯然。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243201'>马上哦诗冲暮雪，清风怀我北窗眠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243201'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243201_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　李泳（子永）赴临安改秩，元吉、辛弃疾与宴，有诗词送行。作品：《送李子永赴调改秩》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243311?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李子永赴调改秩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243311")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243311'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243311'>逸骥骞腾十二闲，追风那复驻辕间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243311'>向来官况诚留滞，此去诗情记往还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243311'>会课未妨更美秩，趣班聊喜近天颜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243311'>割鸡莫费千牛刃，奏赋金门入道山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243311'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243311_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年12月</a>　淮西安抚使延玺重建包拯（希仁）、马亮（叔明）祠，十二月，元吉为作记。作品：《庐州重建包马二公祠堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐州重建包马二公祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254562")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254562'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254562'>贤者之在天下，其生也有以惠于人，则死也亦有以怀其心，故虽闾巷匹夫思慕而不能忘，敬畏而不敢慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254562_comment'></div>此岂或使之然哉，惟其名久而行愈彰，身亡而道益著，百世而下如一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254562_comment'></div>故古之为治者，于一乡之贤，一国之望，必尊礼而敬事之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254562_comment'></div>或不可见，则亦谨视其墓域，严共其庙貌，几若奉其先者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254562_comment'></div>非觊其威灵祸福也，所以兴起其俗而动化其民，使知贤者之不泯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254562_comment'></div>宋有直臣曰包孝肃公，庐之合淝人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254562_comment'></div>其在庙堂不能一岁而薨，而其乡人至今祠公于节妇台下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254562_comment'></div>盖公少以孝行闻于里闾，擢第得官，不忍去其亲之左右，丧则庐于墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254562_comment'></div>及移之事君，当仁祖朝，天下可谓承平，而切切论谏，有古诤臣之风，海内称其姓位而不名，至外夷之族愿赐氏以同其宗，况其桑梓之地，可得而忘之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254562_comment'></div>然节妇者，亦公之子妇崔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254562_comment'></div>始公之子诞通判潭州而卒，崔守志以事舅姑，公哀伤之甚，以为无子，崔则告曰：公有幼子，尚可弃乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254562_comment'></div>公骇而问所以，崔曰：公曩所黜媵妾，生子于父母家，貌甚类公，能诵诗书，今七岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254562_comment'></div>公喜，顾其夫人取之以归，拊之曰，汝非崔氏不得为吾子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254562_comment'></div>及公没，他日崔氏一子亦死，其母自荆州来，欲夺而嫁之，誓而弗许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254562_comment'></div>乃身送母至家而后归，且曰若强我留，当殡于尺组之下，幸以尸还包氏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254562_comment'></div>既乡人上其事，朝廷既赐封邑，旌表其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254562_comment'></div>故公之旧宅燬于兵火，而表台岿然独在，号为节妇台云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254562_comment'></div>因相与塑公像以为祠，凡雨旸疾疫必祷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254562_comment'></div>栋宇卑陋，非所以为一郡之观先贤之礼者，士民欲新之久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254562_comment'></div>淳熙八年，武节大夫延侯玺安抚淮西，既再岁，民和而政成，始徇其欲而为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254562_comment'></div>寓公之像于中，而肖其张夫人与子及妇于后堂，位貌显设，俨如家庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254562_comment'></div>侯则又曰，忠肃马公亦是邦之杰也，与公皆家合淝，皆尝典其乡郡，凛有惠爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254562_comment'></div>今俱绘于学宫，博士、诸生，以时奠其墓矣，顾其祠久废，是宜并祀而无疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254562_comment'></div>于是即其旁规地，以建忠肃之祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254562_comment'></div>二役既兴，远近嘉叹，栋楹榱桷，不日以具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254562_comment'></div>既告成，崇扉邃宇，规制甚备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254562_comment'></div>侯躬率僚吏，奉而安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254562_comment'></div>老稚骈观，罗拜歛衽，如复见二公端委正色于黄堂之上，亦可谓不言之教矣乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254562_comment'></div>惟孝肃讳拯，字希仁，自中丞、三司，嘉祐末仅为枢密副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254562_comment'></div>忠肃公讳亮，字叔明，由太平兴国起家，历事三朝，出入侍从，判尚书都省，以太子少保致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254562_comment'></div>其位朝本末与崔氏之事，有传在史，固不待述，而侯乃以庐人之意，请为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254562_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254562_comment'></div>世之论孝肃第以刚正敢言、辨忠邪、诋权倖、犯天子颜色以议国本、罢内降为难，而某独叹其初为监察御史时，首言国家取士用人未得其实，岁赂缯币非御戎之策，宜选将练兵以为边备，此诚知天下大计，为万世虑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254562_comment'></div>忠肃公智略明敏，虽不至枋用，然识诸名公于未达，自吕文靖、田宣简、宋元宪、陈恭公而下，期以辅相，流知人之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254562_comment'></div>其裁剸繁剧，纵释逋负，破械脱缚，全活诖误，前后千有馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254562_comment'></div>领麾符者凡十有七，善政固多，而某独叹其在长沙日，亡命卒剽掠为患，有捕而杀之者，吏坐以死，公特贷之，曰是为民除害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254562_comment'></div>逮移江宁，行次九江，属岁旱民饥，湖湘漕米适至，公移文守将，发以赈民饥，不问其可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254562_comment'></div>真识权知变而喜任事者，非世俗拘挛之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254562_comment'></div>今延侯膺一道之寄，来治于庐，乃追美二公，志之大者，书而揭诸祠下，庶几士大夫知而慕之，不徒纪其岁月而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254562_comment'></div>淳熙九年十二月，具位韩某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1254562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　是年，自编词集，谓“有未免于俗者，取而焚之”，存之者，名《焦尾集》，并为序。作品：《〈焦尾集〉序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254471' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254471' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254471?labeling=true' target='_blank'>焦尾集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254471")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254471_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254471'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254471'>《礼》曰：「士无故不彻琴瑟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254471_comment'></div>古之为琴瑟也，将以和其心也，乐之不以为教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254471_comment'></div>士之习于琴者既罕，而瑟且不复识矣，其所恃以为声而心赖以和者，不在歌词乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254471_comment'></div>然汉、魏以来，乐府之变，玉台诸诗已极纤艳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254471_comment'></div>近代歌词，杂以鄙俚，间出于市廛俗子，而士大夫有不可道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254471_comment'></div>惟国朝名辈数公所作，类出雅正，殆可以和心而近古，是犹古之琴瑟乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254471_comment'></div>或曰歌词之作，多本于情，其不及于男女之怨者少矣，以为近古何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254471_comment'></div>夫诗之作盖发乎情者，圣人取之以其止于礼义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254471_comment'></div>《硕人》之诗，其言妇人形体态度，摹写略尽，使无孔子而经后世诸儒之手，则去之必矣，是未可与不达者议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254471_comment'></div>予时所作歌词，间亦为人传道，有未免于俗者，取而焚之，然犹不能尽弃焉，目为《焦尾集》，以其焚之馀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254471_comment'></div>淳熙壬寅岁，居于南涧，因为之序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1254471_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年12月</a>　施师点为签书枢密院事，有贺词。作品：《贺施枢密启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254438?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺施枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254438")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254438'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254438'>伏审光膺制命，擢贰枢庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254438_comment'></div>琐闼论思，允著弼谐之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254438_comment'></div>岩廊注意，并资寅亮之谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254438_comment'></div>睿眷有加，舆情胥慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254438_comment'></div>恭以枢密参政量宏而德粹，学富而行高，文华搴两汉之英，议论躐众贤之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254438_comment'></div>出临藩翰，为一时抚字之良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254438_comment'></div>入步禁涂，极当世儒先之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254438_comment'></div>璧水道山之布武，螭坳凤掖之并游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254438_comment'></div>况羽翼于春官，继仪型于夕省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254438_comment'></div>中立不倚，知无不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254438_comment'></div>果聆筹幄之登，仍预政机之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254438_comment'></div>同寅以司宥密之化，伫见殊勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254438_comment'></div>夹辅以立太平之基，尚观显拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254438_comment'></div>某蚤瞻德宇，久阔光尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254438_comment'></div>托迹乡枌，窃有依凭之幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254438_comment'></div>庇身祠馆，尚繄陶冶之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254438_comment'></div>抃蹈之私，实倍夷等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1254438_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年1月</a>　邵武朱钦则建堂于其父墓所，元吉名之曰“滋德”，并为作记。作品：《滋德堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>滋德堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254565")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254565'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254565'>君子行事，未尝必其报也，而天之所以报于人，初不可期以久近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254565_comment'></div>盖尝以世俗论之，近者在其身，久者在其子孙，皆所以为报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254565_comment'></div>故郭令公之贵第其考者垂三十年，而汉之杨氏为三公者数世，其理则一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254565_comment'></div>而人人遂以百年之报为远，曾不知于天地之大，亦朝暮尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254565_comment'></div>然古有言曰，活千人者子孙有封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254565_comment'></div>夫活千人犹有其事也，不幸而无所事，何用见其德哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254565_comment'></div>圣人之事天，则曰作善降之百祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254565_comment'></div>孟子曰：「鸡鸣而起，孳孳为善，舜之徒也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254565_comment'></div>则善者，果何事也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254565_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254565_comment'></div>今世之所谓善，鸡鸣而起，匍匐鬼神者有焉，口诵佛老之书者有焉，然薰茹蔬，戒夫杀食者亦有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254565_comment'></div>是固未为不善，质其行事，则或不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254565_comment'></div>吾意古之为善，有不在是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254565_comment'></div>及观孟子之说，曰「存其心，养其性，所以事天也」，然后知古之事天即为善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254565_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254565_comment'></div>夫天者，善之元也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254565_comment'></div>善者，道之继也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254565_comment'></div>天既以性而命我，而我以道之继者事之，则其心与性之存者，顾何假于外为！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254565_comment'></div>至于能活千人，则亦充其无欲害人之心而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254565_comment'></div>予少寓昭武，买田在郡之东，有朱姓萃居一乡，号多贤士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254565_comment'></div>时朱君令图为里之豪，而善不见外，循循教其子弟甚力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254565_comment'></div>后十有馀年，令图之子钦则登进士第，未几始仕，而又以赏更其秩，乡闾始叹异曰：「令图之门何以致是耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254565_comment'></div>予闻而告之曰：「是盖为善之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254565_comment'></div>其所以为善，非今世俗之谓尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254565_comment'></div>及钦则将为县于巴陵，泣而言曰：「钦则齿之一命而官于建安，吾父幸见之矣，今遂宰邑以临于民，吾父不及见也，悲莫甚焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254565_comment'></div>岁时得以拜而事之者，墓所有堂，其为我名之而有以记之，以昭吾父之善，俾子孙视而不敢忘也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254565_comment'></div>予曰：「子之先君子所植厚矣，乡闾犹莫得而名，而吾何足以知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254565_comment'></div>虽然，惟其不可知，此固遗子者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254565_comment'></div>吾闻之，植德务滋，譬之水与木焉，其流日以深，其枝叶日以盛大，故愿以『滋德』名子之堂，而以德之说表其上，不特俾君之子孙视而不敢忘，庶几一乡之贤亦敬慕而不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254565_comment'></div>《诗》有之，『德輶如毛，民鲜克举之，我仪图之』，可不务乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254565_comment'></div>淳熙十年正月，颍川韩元吉记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1254565_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年1月</a>　序自著《系辞解》作品：《〈系辞解〉序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254470' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254470' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254470?labeling=true' target='_blank'>系辞解序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254470")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254470_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254470'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254470'>《易》之作何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254470_comment'></div>圣人将以传天下之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254470_comment'></div>或曰道其可以言传乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254470_comment'></div>曰言不可传，则焉用圣人，故曰「书不尽言，言不尽意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254470_comment'></div>然则圣人之意，其不可见乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254470_comment'></div>圣人立象以尽意，设卦以尽情伪，系辞焉以尽其言，变而通之以尽利，鼓之舞之以尽神，此之谓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254470_comment'></div>夫传圣人之意者，言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254470_comment'></div>因圣人之言以求者，道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254470_comment'></div>故辞既言尔，凡陈于卦而附于爻、皆辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254470_comment'></div>而后世又以不陈于卦、不附于爻、泛然论《易》之指归者，别谓为《系辞》，或曰《大传》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254470_comment'></div>有议其非孔子之作，吾意其为赞《易》道以黜八索者，非孔子莫能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254470_comment'></div>不然，其必有自而传欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254470_comment'></div>古人传《易》者多矣，或指其象，或定其数，或究其理，而于《系辞》独取其大意而略焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254470_comment'></div>间又讲之而不备，泥之而不通，则所谓象之与数，数之与理，固无自而合也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254470_comment'></div>三者无自而合，其于圣人之道，能尽而知者鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254470_comment'></div>学者欲探圣人之道，当自《易》始，欲明圣人之意，当自《系辞》始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254470_comment'></div>于是而得焉，知天之所以为天，人之所以为人，施之天下，何务之不成，何功业之不见哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254470_comment'></div>况夫异端之说，皆不攻而自破矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254470_comment'></div>予生尝有誓，年至六十乃敢著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254470_comment'></div>淳熙戊戌岁，既六十有一，始志其自得者，作《系辞解》，阅再岁而仅成，因序而藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254470_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254470_comment'></div>后之君子有所自得，然后于吾言为可信，千载而下，使圣人之道复传，是则圣人之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254470_comment'></div>淳熙十年正月，颍川韩某序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1254470_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　春，汤邦彥（朝美）得自便还金坛，有诗送行。作品：《送汤朝美还金坛》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送汤朝美还金坛</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243486")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243486'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243486'>腾驹轻卧驼，野蔓欺落木。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243486'>举头便干霄，春至亦重绿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243486'>人生百年内，万事纷过目。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243486'>得为蠖步伸，失作蠵颈缩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243486'>古来旷达士，一视等蛮触。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243486'>功名本时命，用舍岂荣辱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243486'>汤公涉南荒，岁月犹转毂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243486'>几年卧新州，宁肯事鸡卜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243486'>身安一瓢饮，志大五车读。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243486'>朅来灵山隈，跫然慰虚谷。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243486'>濯足山下泉，爱我泉上竹。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243486'>相从一长笑，忍效阮生哭。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243486'>胸中经济略，欲语动惊俗。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243486'>谁知天意回，归棹如许速。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243486'>春风正浩荡，江水清可掬。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243486'>海涛拍千峰，挂席下浮玉。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243486'>遥欣倚门念，三径欢僮仆。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243486'>送君得无恨，我步嗟局促。<div id='poem_sentence_17_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_243486'>要看万里途，更试参云足。<div id='poem_sentence_18_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_243486'>家山幸毋留，吾皇思陈牍。<div id='poem_sentence_19_243486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_243486'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_243486_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　辛弃疾招饮，即席赋词。作品：《好事近·辛幼安席上》（华屋翠云深）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243574' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243574' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243574?labeling=true' target='_blank'>好事近<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>辛幼安席上</a><span "poem_title_243574")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243574_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243574'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243574_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243574'>老来沈醉为花狂，霜鬓未须镊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243574_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年5月</a>　叶衡（梦锡）卒，有挽词。作品：《叶梦锡丞相挽词二首》<span id='poem_content_243164'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243164'>制邑腾嘉誉，升平遂一州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243164'>雍容持从橐，慷慨动宸旒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243164'>相业看调鼎，兵机久运筹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243164'>勋庸元未究，湖海泪空流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243164'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243164_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243163?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年5月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243163_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243163'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243163'>味道苏仙井，言归鬓尚青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243163'>仅周新甲子，还仰旧仪刑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243163'>秘殿欣疏宠，华钟待勒铭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243163'>追随樽酒地，愁绝最高亭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243163'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243163_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　致书周必大（子充），荐宗室赵成忠，必大有覆书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　姜特立（邦杰）寄诗稿来，有诗答之。作品：《姜特立寄近诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>姜特立寄近诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243478")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243478'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243478'>双溪岩曲芦江岸，每见君诗句益奇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243478'>渐喜青云今得路，岂妨白雪尚摛词。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243478'>断蛟入海功何壮，披腹排云世共知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243478'>斫却月中丹桂手，朝阳应占凤凰枝<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：姜五中乡荐，今为春坊。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243478'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　应僧怀璧之请，撰《建宁府开元禅寺戒坛记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254564?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建宁府开元禅寺戒坛记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254564")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254564'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254564'>佛学之徒，以寂静能忍为心，而以勤苦不退转制事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254564_comment'></div>故有断其肢体以求师授法，死而至于更生，犹未忘其所营造者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254564_comment'></div>用是以崇其塔庙，故虽穷山绝壑，必得其地而居之，而率有成焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254564_comment'></div>岂类于吾儒所为执德之不回而正固之干事者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254564_comment'></div>盖特用之于其一法尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254564_comment'></div>始予守建宁，而城南有大寺曰开元，负山面溪，形势雄峙，世传以为吴大将吕蒙旧居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254564_comment'></div>建炎初火于巨盗，蕝而未辑，长老僧怀璧住而慨然曰，当以试吾愿力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254564_comment'></div>不数年，则新其大门，更其两庑，辟殿庭，兴寝室，轮奂规画，严且整矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254564_comment'></div>去岁之冬，又以书来曰：寺有授戒之坛，吾学之所甚重，盖其誓夫新为僧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254564_comment'></div>自绍兴三十有二年移置于寺，而犹寓于方丈之地，非天子诞弥之节莫得宣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254564_comment'></div>府县之官，拜祝其下，而坛宇到今弗备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254564_comment'></div>乃先捐其平生衣资，然后募诸施者，且取寺之赡众之馀，合为之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254564_comment'></div>鸠工庀材，甓石三成，琢镂锼巧，极其精制，衡馀百尺，从六十尺有二，崇过四十尺，丹髹其楹，绘采其壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254564_comment'></div>而左翼军将刘琮者，思子明之功，施作佛像其中，四大神介胄其隅，以为之卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254564_comment'></div>起五月辛未，至十二月而毕，亡虑三千缗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254564_comment'></div>而窃欲予文以记，三返而益勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254564_comment'></div>夫闽之八州，以一水分上下，其下四郡，良田大山，多在佛寺，故俗以奉佛为美，而佛之庐几甲于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254564_comment'></div>若上州则虽有僧舍，类皆空乏不给，况残毁之馀，能从事于土木哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254564_comment'></div>璧旧为衢、信二刹，人所钦向，而用心精勤，汲汲靡懈，故至则成就若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254564_comment'></div>予是以知天下之事，不患于人之不能为，而患在人之不肯为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254564_comment'></div>使士大夫遇事能有坚忍不拔之志，则亦何功之不可成，何业之不可广也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254564_comment'></div>故其有请，不复究浮屠之说、毗尼之教以衒诩其徒，而以有于吾心者举而示之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254564_comment'></div>然璧亦老矣，闻其筑室于山，盖将休焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254564_comment'></div>因为此书，俾建溪之人岁时嬉游梅山陆泉之下，以观开元绀宇之盛，知其兴复自璧始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254564_comment'></div>淳熙十年五月，具位韩某记并书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1254564_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d6d9abd15f194598883e364d5c528546_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d6d9abd15f194598883e364d5c528546");'><span id='d6d9abd15f194598883e364d5c528546_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1246')">1183-1246年</a>，66-129岁</div><div id='d6d9abd15f194598883e364d5c528546' class='detail'><a href="javascript: id='poem_title_243363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243363'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243363'>使君谈笑两桥成，人向晴虹镜里行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243363'>更辟轩窗待游览，要看山水倍澄明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243363_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　秋，题诗苍筤亭。作品：《题苍筤亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243548?labeling=true' "poem_title_243548")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243548'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243548'>手种苍筤数百竿，筑亭相与枕书看。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243548'>故知落落非春事，直有青青共岁寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243548'>一壑自欣幽意足，三年独得此君欢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243548'>萧然风露千寻影，搔首哦诗独凭栏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243548'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年8月</a>　傅自得（安道）卒，有挽词。作品：《挽傅安道郎中词二首》<span target='_blank'>挽傅安道郎中词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243343")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243343'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243343'>节槩存先烈，文才蔼俊声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243343'>弟兄联膴仕，父子擅英名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243343'>密勿栖郎省，光华拥使旌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243343'>甘泉虚从橐，曾未席恩荣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243343'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243343_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243342?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243342'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243342'>蚤负凌云气，长怀流水音。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243342'>词场俱白首，世路只丹心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243342'>妙语空成诵，欢盟讵可寻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243342'>泉山几千里，涕泪俱沾襟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243342'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243342_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年8月</a>　朱熹作武夷精舍，元吉为记。作品：《武夷精舍记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《方舆胜览》卷11。）</span><div id='poem_1254584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254584?labeling=true' target='_blank'>武夷精舍记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254584")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254584'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254584'>武夷山在闽粤直北，其山势雄深盘礴，自汉以来，见于祀事，闽之诸山皆后出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254584_comment'></div>其峰之最大者，丰上而敛下，岿然若巨人之戴弁，缘隙磴道，可望而不可登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254584_comment'></div>世传避秦而仙者，蜕骨在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254584_comment'></div>溪出其下，绝壁高峻，皆数十丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254584_comment'></div>崖侧巨石林立，磊落奇秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254584_comment'></div>好事者一日不能尽，则卧小舟，杭溪而上，号为九曲，以左右顾视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254584_comment'></div>至其地或平衍，景物环会，必为之停舟曳杖，徙倚而不忍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254584_comment'></div>山故多王孙，鸟则白鹇、鹧鸪，闻人声或磔磔集崖上，散漫飞走而无惊惧之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254584_comment'></div>水流有声，其深处可泳，草木四时敷华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254584_comment'></div>道士即溪之穷，仅为一庐，以待游者之食息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254584_comment'></div>往往酌酒未半，已迫曛暮而不可留矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254584_comment'></div>山距驿道才一二里许，逆旅遥望，不惮仆夫马足之劳，幸而至老氏之宫宿焉，明日始能裹饭命舟，而溪之长复倍于驿道之远，促促而来，遽遽而归，前后踵相属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254584_comment'></div>余旧家闽中，为宦于建安，盖亦遽归之一耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254584_comment'></div>吾友朱元晦居于五夫山，在武夷一舍而近，若其外圃，暇则游焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254584_comment'></div>与其门生弟子挟书而诵，取古《诗》三百篇及楚人之词哦而歌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254584_comment'></div>得酒啸咏，留必数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254584_comment'></div>盖山中之乐，悉为元晦之私也，余每愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254584_comment'></div>淳熙之十年，元晦既辞使节于江东，遂赋祠官之禄，则又曰吾今营其地，果尽有山中之乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254584_comment'></div>盖其游益数，而于其溪五折负大石屏，规之以为精舍，取道士之庐犹半也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254584_comment'></div>诛锄草茅，仅得数亩，面势清幽，奇木佳石，拱揖映带，若阴相而遗我者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254584_comment'></div>使弟子具畚锸，集瓦竹，相率成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254584_comment'></div>元晦躬画其处，中以为堂，旁以为斋，高以为亭，密以为室，讲书肄业，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1254584", 1254584, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>琴歌酒赋</span>莫不在是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254584_comment'></div>余闻之，恍然，如寐而醒，醒而后隐，隐犹记其地之美也，且曰其为我记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254584_comment'></div>夫元晦儒者也，方以学行其乡，善其徒，非若畸人隐士，遁藏山谷，服气茹芝，以慕夫道家者流也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254584_comment'></div>然秦汉以来，道之不明久矣，吾夫子所谓志于道亦何事哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254584_comment'></div>夫子圣人也，其步与趋，莫不有则，至于登泰山之颠而诵言于舞雩之下，未尝不游，胸中盖自有地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254584_comment'></div>而一时弟子鼓瑟铿然，春服既成之咏，乃独为圣人所予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254584_comment'></div>古之君子息焉者，岂以是拘拘乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254584_comment'></div>元晦既有以识之，试以告夫来者，相与酬酢于精舍之下，俾或自得，其视幔亭之风，抑又何如也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254584_comment'></div>是岁八月，颍川韩元吉记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1254584_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年11月</a>　李椿（寿翁）卒，有挽词。作品：《李寿翁侍郎挽词》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243235' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243235' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243235?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李寿翁侍郎挽词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243235")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243235_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243235'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243235'>同解铨衡并把麾，五年相望楚江湄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243235'>邻墙会面尝谈易，吏选偷閒更说诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243235'>北客遭逢人共叹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，南州流转事难知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243235'>投簪自有江湖志，云白天青泪满颐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243235'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_243235'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_243235_0'>⑴ 自注：公陛辞日，上有北人难得之谕。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_243235_0'>⑵ 自注：公临终作诗，有白云青天之句。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_243235_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年11月</a>　贵溪县尉郑肇之（子仁）治小轩于尉舍，元吉榜之曰“绝尘”并为记。作品：《绝尘轩记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绝尘轩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254568")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254568'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254568'>贵溪尉舍，旧有黄梅出于垣间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254568_comment'></div>元符己卯岁，廖明略举宋广平之事，题曰「能赋堂」，以况尉君曾敬之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254568_comment'></div>明略既为之记，而晁无咎题其后，谓其于敬之远矣，无咎又和其试茶、看花二诗，有「两绝尘」之句，则敬之为人固可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254568_comment'></div>后八十有二年，福唐郑肇之子仁实为尉于此，乃葺堂之坏而更新之，访梅蘖而增培之，亦治其东偏为小轩，寘笔研书帙其间，以朝夕坐卧而休焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254568_comment'></div>会秩满将更，而予因榜之曰「绝尘」，盖取于无咎之诗语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254568_comment'></div>夫三君子远矣，廖、晁以馆阁英名，留落是邦，曾君以相家子，文采风流，号有典型，一时酬酢往来，歆艳后辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254568_comment'></div>其于广平之赋，殆有感而发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254568_comment'></div>若夫绝尘之喻，则颜子之望于夫子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254568_comment'></div>虽诗人比兴无所不用其意，然予亦岂独为梅花而发哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254568_comment'></div>子仁通于学而邃于文，学业过人远甚，方从事词章之科，其奔逸青云，皆自此始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254568_comment'></div>故予复感而书焉，庶几异时为尉舍之美谈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254568_comment'></div>淳熙癸卯十一月，颍川韩某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1254568_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年1月10日</a>　观郑望之（显道）所藏钦宗、高宗手书，题跋。作品：《题郑侍郎所得钦宗御书后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span>《题郑侍郎所得太上皇帝御书后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题郑侍郎所得钦宗御书后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年1月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254501")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254501'>靖康改元，敌骑薄京师，朝廷备守布河灌之兵于城下，宰执与二三侍从议遣使军前，皆未肯往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254501_comment'></div>郑公时为驾部，独入都堂问状，遂假以工部侍郎，少宰张邦昌脱所衣紫袍，兵部尚书路允迪解腰下金带并鞍勒狨坐借公，登时启行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254501_comment'></div>公平日慷慨有志气，谈笑无所惮，中使押至安上门，缒而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254501_comment'></div>敌帅知公至，亦遣吴孝迪等来，夜会于河灌帐中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254501_comment'></div>且曰皇子郎君赵州见新天子即位赦，以手加额，曰今无所争矣，而议割河朔、犒军金帛二事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254501_comment'></div>公与其使还至都亭驿，则已四鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254501_comment'></div>钦宗皇帝御批若此，公有记录甚详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254501_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254501_comment'></div>事变仓猝，噬脐何追，尚忍言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254501_comment'></div>淳熙十一年正月十日，具位韩某敬书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1254501_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1254502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题郑侍郎所得太上皇帝御书后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年1月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254502")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254502'>郑公再以珠玉使金营，时太上皇帝既至军前矣，而金人方因姚平仲劫寨事，送公于都统寨，将害之也，太上皇帝为之泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254502_comment'></div>盖君臣同患难，故公在侍从，独示以三书，谓之熟敌情伪，可料之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254502_comment'></div>公虽不至柄用，优游林下，年几九十，其福寿之蕴，敌人何所容其刃耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254502_comment'></div>淳熙十一年正月十日，具位韩某恭览御笔，敬题其后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1254502_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年1月</a>　为其友章甫（冠之）所居易足堂为记。作品：《易足堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>易足堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254566")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254566'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254566'>楚有士好游躐衡庐之巅，泛洞庭，下彭蠡，凡林薮之幽，川泽之奥，无不足也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254566_comment'></div>意未云足，闻有三神山在东海之中，其上多奇禽异卉，人之寿而仙者居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254566_comment'></div>意乃甚慕，庶几可一至也，殚其产以治舟，竭其力以聚粮，没岁穷年，莫能见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254566_comment'></div>恐惧于波涛之渊，既惫而归，里之父老从而笑之，曰曩子之志甚锐也，吾未可以言焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254566_comment'></div>今其倦矣，吾语子游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254566_comment'></div>子独不见夫吾之居乎，依于数仞之丘，而辟为寻丈之室，隐几而卧，屦未始蹑乎阈也，瞑目而游于胸中，而四方万里之远，子所未至者也，吾皆至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254566_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254566_comment'></div>子之游者事乎外，而吾之游者事乎内也，顾安用仆仆然东西行为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254566_comment'></div>昔者秦、汉之侈也，贵为天子，富有四海，力固已并诸侯，威固已服四夷，而惟以其身之未能升天也，旦旦而求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254566_comment'></div>有方士者，尝为之幻，导之而升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254566_comment'></div>其所见宫室之美、嫔嫱服御之盛，若有以异于人世间也，恨莫能留，涉笔而志其墉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254566_comment'></div>明日视之，则尽己之宫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254566_comment'></div>是何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254566_comment'></div>由其心之未舒，则纵其耳目之欲者未制，故希于外者无已焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254566_comment'></div>由是而言，祸莫大于不知足，而富常在于知足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254566_comment'></div>况子以匹夫之贱，规规以好游名天下，亦安往而后足哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254566_comment'></div>友人章冠之闻而叹曰，吾非好游者也，借是以推天下之事，其不类于游者几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254566_comment'></div>彼富与贵，是人之所欲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254566_comment'></div>今吾有数亩之田可耕，数椽之屋可庇矣，虽万钱之厨、千间之厦，不是过也，岂不为甚富矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254566_comment'></div>邑之士以吾为可亲，贤卿大夫以吾为可与游，开卷执筴而咏焉，古今事物之情举无所遁，俯仰于天地间，盖亦无愧，岂不为甚贵矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254566_comment'></div>故吾尝自以为足，而人常恨吾之不足，特未知世之所谓既富且贵者，其心果能如吾之足哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254566_comment'></div>今吾仅营一堂矣，将以「易足」名焉，则何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254566_comment'></div>夫冠之诗人也，与予兄弟交最厚且久，其清苦贫窭，予亦常恨其不足者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254566_comment'></div>而闻其说若此，犁然有当于予心，遂书以为堂之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254566_comment'></div>其山川之胜，风景之佳，冠之必能自见于诗尔，予尚何所言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254566_comment'></div>淳熙十一年正月，颍川韩元吉记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1254566_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　社日，与赵善扛（文鼎）游鹅石，有唱和。作品：《次韵赵文鼎同游鹅石五首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span>《次韵赵文鼎雨中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243031' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243031' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243031?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵赵文鼎同游鹅石五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243031")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243031_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243031'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243031'>缭绕云山溪水南，溪光溶漾滴晴岚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243031'>不知日暖花争艳，但觉风和酒易酣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243031'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243031_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_242996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_242996'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_242996'>宛宛溪流九曲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>湾，山猿时下鸟关关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_242996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_242996'>钓矶茶灶山中乐，大隐苍屏<span
