id='poem_note_242996_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年5月11日</a>　辛弃疾生日，元吉赴寿筵，即席赋词，辛和之。作品：《水龙吟·寿辛侍郎》（南风五月江波）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《彊村丛书·南涧诗馀》）</span><div id='poem_243563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水龙吟 寿辛侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年5月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243563")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243563'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243563'>南风五月江波，使君莫袖平戎手。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243563'>燕然未勒，渡泸声在，宸衷怀旧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243563'>卧占湖山，楼横百尺，诗成千首。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243563'>正菖蒲叶老，芙蕖香嫩，高门瑞、人知否。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243563_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243563'>凉夜光躔牛斗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243563'>梦初回、长庚如昼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243563'>明年看取，锋旗南下，六骡西走。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243563'>功画凌烟，万钉宝带，百壶清酒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243563'>便留公剩馥，蟠桃分我，作归来寿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_243563_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年5月12日</a>　元吉生日，辛弃疾以元吉前韵赋词为寿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年5月12日</a>　李商叟有诗为寿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　应绩溪县令虞俦之请，为该县所建苏文定公（辙）祠作碑文。作品：《苏文定公祠碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷19。）</span><div id='poem_1254603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏文定公祠碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254603")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254603'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254603'>歙之绩溪县西隅，有亭曰「翠眉」，不知其何人作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254603_comment'></div>前则二小山对出，自亭而望，妩然如眉，地势平衍，林木茂蔚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254603_comment'></div>元丰末，苏文定公为县，爱其幽清，时往游焉，赋诗其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254603_comment'></div>公去而邑人思之，即亭为祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254603_comment'></div>中更党籍禁锢之馀，书毁迹灭，重为寇攘之厄，井邑荡然，公之遗翰，了无在者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254603_comment'></div>绍兴中，好事者饰县廨一堂，名以「景苏」，后令曹训刻公在绩溪所为诗三十六篇于石，而摩公之像于亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254603_comment'></div>岁月寖久，栋宇弗支，淳熙十年，公之曾孙秘阁修撰谔，为江南东路转运副使，按行邑中，来拜祠下，出俸钱付县吏，曰修之，勿以烦民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254603_comment'></div>时奉议郎宣城虞俦方祗县事，愧而谢曰：「此令之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254603_comment'></div>昨为令者，以频岁救荒，故未能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254603_comment'></div>俦至甫几月尔，固将及之，其敢用公之私钱」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254603_comment'></div>某适以行役过县，俦道其所以，且愿得文以为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254603_comment'></div>其明年来曰，祠成久矣，辟亭为四楹，得家庙本，别绘公像于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254603_comment'></div>前为轩槛，以面两山，后为便舍，以待游者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254603_comment'></div>以公之爱其处，规制仍旧，不敢侈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254603_comment'></div>夫公之名满天下，而文章诵于四夷，功烈论议且载信史，岂须记而后传？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254603_comment'></div>盖绩溪在江左，岩邑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254603_comment'></div>公之为令，仅以半载，而邑人至今乃不忘，则其道德所加，必有未施信而民信之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254603_comment'></div>虽然，公之对制策，当仁祖朝已负敢言之气，而几见黜于有司，驱驰州县，不得用于台阁者踰二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254603_comment'></div>逮东坡先生以诗得罪，公亦坐贬于筠，起废而来绩溪，则既五十矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254603_comment'></div>自是始还，曾不数年，任言责、司翰墨，以翊政路，而登门下省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254603_comment'></div>则向之忌嫉于公，而蹭蹬不偶者，未足为公叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254603_comment'></div>昔公自蜀入京师，纵观山河之雄，宫阙之壮，上书韩太尉，实自比司马迁，欲求天下之奇闻壮观以激发其志气，顾以一县之微，一亭之小，耳目所寓，未厌而乐之，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254603_comment'></div>公尝有言曰：「天下之乐无穷，而以适意为悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254603_comment'></div>方其得意，万物无以易之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254603_comment'></div>其斯之谓欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254603_comment'></div>今虞君之政，惓惓慕公，而徇民之思，以志于公所游之地，则绩溪者，殆公之桐乡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254603_comment'></div>故某摭民之谣，以为祀神之章，俾岁时酹公而歌焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254603_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1254603'>公之居兮岷峨西，怀栾坡兮家具茨，翠眉之山兮何足以嬉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254603_comment'></div>公之来兮昆崙丘，大江注兮九河流，翠眉之水兮何足以游？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254603_comment'></div>嗟公视于天壤兮等于浮沤，扰扰万类兮是惟蜉蝣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254603_comment'></div>抚兹百里兮曾何异于九州，剖折狱讼兮亦吾庙谋，不为此弃兮讵为彼留！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254603_comment'></div>金闺兮玉堂，调神鼎兮辅岩廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254603_comment'></div>朝临汝水兮暮栖海康，荣枯贵贱兮公以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254603_comment'></div>藐祠庭兮山之左，杉千章兮竹万个。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254603_comment'></div>公之去来兮世莫可期，惨云车兮斯人是思。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1254603_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　前知广州连南夫（鹏举）因不附和议，为秦桧所斥，卒后四十馀年无碑铭。是年，其子#（上半为“雝”下半为“玉”）请于元吉，元吉“因考订其行事，叙而碑之”作品：《连公墓碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷19。）</span><div id='poem_1254605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>连公墓碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254605")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254605'>宣和五年，故宝文阁学士连公讳南夫以秘书省校书郎假太常少卿贺女真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254605_comment'></div>来年正月，会金使李靖来告太祖之丧，朝廷遂除公接送伴，改命为祭奠吊慰使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254605_comment'></div>公前以面对更京秩，天子记其才气可用，而蔡攸方领枢密，阴忌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254605_comment'></div>大臣亦谓敌有丧，可以虚声动者，欲稍变契丹旧仪，合祭吊两使为一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254605_comment'></div>且诏公吾所奉赏设金缯与借粮米，皆已副金人之需，而西京应蔚、奉圣、归化、儒妫等州，逮令未交，宜开谕交取以来，公不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254605_comment'></div>至敌果以祭吊并聘为言，公从容对曰：「告哀使仅留三日尔，朝廷亟欲报命，故因某送伴而遣，殆有司失照例，非有意也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254605_comment'></div>所议漫不答，反以纳张觉与燕山之民有所诮诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254605_comment'></div>公慷慨复曰：「本朝兵将盖多，何至须一张觉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254605_comment'></div>燕民之来稍众，未尽见尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254605_comment'></div>论辩不屈，遂成礼而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254605_comment'></div>归即为上言：「敌好不可保也，朝廷所仰大将则郭药师，兵则常胜军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254605_comment'></div>比年军政不修，新边无河山之阻，而粮食未均，蓟州卒有羸饿，河朔马群尽空，无留良焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254605_comment'></div>愿选中国将帅以制药师，练中国士卒以制常胜军」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254605_comment'></div>因面奏刘延庆败十万众，皆童贯赏罚不明，至其遁走，且厚币以易云中而以捷奏，乞斩贯、延庆以谢天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254605_comment'></div>然城池不坚，器械不利，敌有轻视中国心，不一二年将不遗馀力而来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254605_comment'></div>徽宗皇帝闻公言大骇，尽以所论付枢密院、宣抚司，而攸、贯之徒皆切齿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254605_comment'></div>始公道迁秘书郎，既还迁起居舍人，七年三月，遂拜中书舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254605_comment'></div>言者观望大臣，诋公为不职，除右文殿修撰知庆源府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254605_comment'></div>公曰庆源在河北，正宣抚所隶，何可居，挝登闻鼓论其事，愿易他所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254605_comment'></div>即改濠州，淮南小郡也，而言者志未逞，复谓公谢表有讥讪，降一秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254605_comment'></div>是岁十二月，敌果率众逼京师，钦宗皇帝讲和敕下，即论敌情十患，愿因诸道之兵未遣亟击之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254605_comment'></div>靖康二年，除待制徽猷阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254605_comment'></div>公曰吾惟备一州矣，缮治濠城，凿巨石五百步，运甓塞淮流之贯城者，增城为三丈，立楼橹，并城开稻田十里以为泞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254605_comment'></div>二圣北狩，或言伪楚赦且至，公密伺于境上，曰有赍赦者当斩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254605_comment'></div>已而宗室数十，丐纳官职以去，公持之恸哭，曰：「南夫宋臣，且侍从也，义当保兹垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254605_comment'></div>况元帅康王在外，必应天命，诸君幸毋恐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254605_comment'></div>即遣人驰蜡书劝进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254605_comment'></div>建炎登极，诏公再任，公又论讲和致祸之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254605_comment'></div>闻集议驻跸，即上疏祈幸关中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254605_comment'></div>且谓敌势甚炽，秋高马肥，必为渡河绝淮之计，画捍御策为四十条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254605_comment'></div>复移书李纲、郭三益，宜用汉高捐关东以与黥布、韩、彭之策，以燕云致其地豪杰，以辽东致高丽，以契丹故地致契丹遗族，其论甚壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254605_comment'></div>继有召命，而敌已至扬州，濠民惧无与守也，挽公不得行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254605_comment'></div>明年，除显谟阁直学士知江宁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254605_comment'></div>未踰月，大驾驻江宁，即府治为行宫，公竭力营缮，无一弗备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254605_comment'></div>又乞江北置三大都督，分总陕西、两河、淮南诸路，而自荐一二大臣为可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254605_comment'></div>语出惊众，即丐外祠，命知桂州，又改饶州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254605_comment'></div>金人已自江浙破豫章、临川，游骑至饶境，公科丁壮为固守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254605_comment'></div>敌虽不犯，而群盗蜂起，有侯进万馀来攻，公大辟城扉以疑之，贼惶惧未知计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254605_comment'></div>公夜炽火，声鼓震天，进遂惊溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254605_comment'></div>而刘文舜大艑数十，由南康而下，公躬部民兵，昼夜乘城，矢石几尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254605_comment'></div>时御营统制王德号王夜叉，驻兵庐陵，公飞书邀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254605_comment'></div>众畏其不来，德得书泣曰：「我尝系建康狱，连公为守，待我厚，当死报之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254605_comment'></div>以舟师不三日至，文舜惧，请降，诛其渠魁五人而散其众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254605_comment'></div>有王念经者，以左道聚愚民至十馀万，公劝德追击，至贵溪，斩首数万级，复为民者几倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254605_comment'></div>绍兴改元，张琪既破新安，直抵城外，公遣将败之，伏尸四十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1254605_comment'></div>于是饶以块然小垒，而能却金兵、捍群盗，独立于江左，饶人至今祠公不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1254605_comment'></div>而公以疾得请临安府洞霄宫，未几起知信州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1254605_comment'></div>始诏守臣具民间利病或边防五事，公应诏论十一事，且指赦令倚阁二税为非，曰：「安有占田而不输税者，军旅调度顾可阙乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1254605_comment'></div>移泉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1254605_comment'></div>朝廷下福建造舟以备海道，遣使督促。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1254605_comment'></div>公曰舟用新木，难遽办，且湿恶易坏，若以度牒钱买商船二百艘，则省缗钱二十万矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1254605_comment'></div>从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1254605_comment'></div>时诏亲征伪齐，公慨然献议，引汉卜式愿尽死节、马伏波以马革裹尸之意，乞扈从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1254605_comment'></div>不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1254605_comment'></div>在泉二年，提举江州太平观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1254605_comment'></div>岭南水陆盗贼充斥，刘宣自章贡扰揭阳，郑广、周聪抄海道，而曾衮据釜甑山者七年，其馀妄称大王、太尉、铁柱、火星、飞刀、打天之号凡十八火，动数千人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1254605_comment'></div>即起公经略安抚广东，进宝文阁学士，兼措置虔、闽盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1254605_comment'></div>公入境，召大将韩京激厉使之，且按诛惠州孔目吏与曾衮表里者，合诸郡兵，以次年平定，降者遣诣密院，或分置军中，擒获者戮于市，胁从者还其业，岭峤遂清，诏书奖谕，迁官一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1254605_comment'></div>而公裁决明审，滞讼悉空，番禺之人立祠作碑以纪其绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1254605_comment'></div>徽宗与宁德后凶问至，公上疏曰：「事已如斯，追救何及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1254605_comment'></div>惟用兵可以雪耻，宜乘军民痛忿，竭作北向也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1254605_comment'></div>郦琼既叛，公又言豫贼得琼，正在疑贰，愿以刘光世为前驱讨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1254605_comment'></div>逮河南故地暂得，公亦进封事，以为殆天授我，机不可失也，正不可以得地小恩而忘二圣播迁大耻，当乘其未备击之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1254605_comment'></div>复提举太平观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1254605_comment'></div>盖公自靖康深以和议为非，至谓不知讲和为何策，国家之难皆和议有以致，执论不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1254605_comment'></div>及故地虽失，慈宁还归，宰相以成功自居，指公为异论之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1254605_comment'></div>言事者奉其意，以公在广日用讲和霈恩放杜充之子自便为非，由是落宝文阁学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1254605_comment'></div>绍兴十三年正月二十六日，终于福州寓舍，春秋五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1254605_comment'></div>呜呼，公盖应处士之曾孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1254605_comment'></div>处士德安人，讳舜宾，欧阳文忠公表其墓，所谓孝友温仁以教其乡者，赠至金紫光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1254605_comment'></div>其第三子讳庸，公之祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1254605_comment'></div>考则讳仲涉，赠至通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1254605_comment'></div>妣杨氏、高氏，赠淑人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1254605_comment'></div>公字鹏举，年二十四进士上舍释褐，授颍州司理参军，移鼎州教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1254605_comment'></div>省罢，调澧阳尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1254605_comment'></div>丁内艰，调襄邑主簿、虔州教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1254605_comment'></div>未赴，除辟廱正、礼制局检讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1254605_comment'></div>补校御前文籍，遂为校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1254605_comment'></div>徽宗一见奇之，仅踰年，擢之侍从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1254605_comment'></div>气正而言直，艰难变故，志在经纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1254605_comment'></div>其言曰：「《易》穷则变，变则通，今之祸变，真变也，而通之道寓焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1254605_comment'></div>故始献议幸关中，继则议迁江陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1254605_comment'></div>且谓天子当留神武事，以激昂将士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1254605_comment'></div>乞仿讲筵之制，置侍射侍驭之官以待诸将；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1254605_comment'></div>选三等豪户仿六郡良家子以充禁卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1254605_comment'></div>乞先图李成则盗贼可无患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1254605_comment'></div>然朝廷既诛六贼，凡除授有讨论之目，公则曰：「何示天下以不广也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1254605_comment'></div>惟当共筹，所以报金人而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1254605_comment'></div>又谓可以用人死命无过爵赏，而朝廷吝惜太甚，请优立告变赏格，而增重帅守之权，皆不顾众异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1254605_comment'></div>州县各阙官而悉罢权摄，公则曰：「议者不过为朝廷惜请给之费，宜听其权而监司察其私，严其缪举同罪之罚，则无废事矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1254605_comment'></div>及举行赃吏杖脊朝堂之令，公自信州条具言曰：「选人七阶之俸，不越十千也，军兴物价倍百，当先养其廉，稍增其俸，使足赡十口之家，然后复行赃吏旧制」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1254605_comment'></div>朝廷是之，增选人茶汤之给，天下称诵，以为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1254605_comment'></div>在濠遇渊圣受禅，首乞下罢天宁节宴设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1254605_comment'></div>及建康初对行宫，即劝天子以汉高、唐太宗之英武而行孝悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1254605_comment'></div>又曰：「宫阙少安矣，当思二圣在沙漠而未安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1254605_comment'></div>于此朝群臣则问以迎二圣之策，于此见将士则问以回二圣之谋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1254605_comment'></div>太上皇帝为之感动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1254605_comment'></div>盖公于论思靡不尽，而不为拘挛龌龊之论，才略从横，仅见于诛锄寇盗，绥靖一方，曾未得究其所施，诚可哀者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1254605_comment'></div>其帅岭南，惧涉瘴疠，自誓不受俸给，以祈全家生还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1254605_comment'></div>及被赏进官，力辞不肯受，朝廷不从，竟以回授其兄哲夫，而以俸给推与其兄妹及侄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1254605_comment'></div>自广而归，扶携仕族之不能归者数家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1254605_comment'></div>平生奏补，先其孤幼，轻财好施，家无馀赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1254605_comment'></div>绍兴十五年十一月十五日，葬于怀安县稷下里崇福山之原，而未克有铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1254605_comment'></div>淳熙之十一年，其子𤫔来告，因考订其行事，叙而碑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1254605_comment'></div>公官至中大夫，赠左正奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1254605_comment'></div>娶王氏，邻臣之女，赠淑人，先公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1254605_comment'></div>男三人：𤫔，朝奉郎、权发遣邵州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1254605_comment'></div>瑴，承奉郎、监秀州华亭县袁步盐场；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1254605_comment'></div>莹，承奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1254605_comment'></div>女二人，长以疾废，次适将仕郎刘蘧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1254605_comment'></div>瑴、莹与次女皆前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1254605_comment'></div>孙男二，孙女九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1254605_comment'></div>有奏议三十篇，文集二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1254605_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_113_1254605'>文武之分，肇岂自古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1254605_comment'></div>治功则文，戡定斯武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1254605_comment'></div>嗟世诵说，乃以为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1254605_comment'></div>侮至患生，孰济我民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1254605_comment'></div>伟矣连公，处士之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1254605_comment'></div>以文决科，勇且有仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1254605_comment'></div>公初奉使，请诛边臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1254605_comment'></div>不惧不惊，天子圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1254605_comment'></div>祸乱方兴，刻意武事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1254605_comment'></div>矢谋于朝，用则不既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1254605_comment'></div>御戎鄱津，殄寇海滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1254605_comment'></div>笑谈之间，有劳有勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1254605_comment'></div>政令恩威，英明恺悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1254605_comment'></div>烝尝于民，才则我忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1254605_comment'></div>以和为功，吾其可同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1254605_comment'></div>成败奚言，第输我忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1254605_comment'></div>惟公之忠，匪顾其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1254605_comment'></div>孰能昭之，赍志没地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1254605_comment'></div>怀安之原，稷下之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1254605_comment'></div>罔愧于先，后其有传。</div><div id='poem_sentence_132_1254605_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　知台州熊克（子复）以诗来，作长句谢之。作品：《熊子复惠十诗作长句谢之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>熊子复惠十诗作长句谢之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243547")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243547_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243547'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243547'>白首相期翰墨中，衰龄况是甲庚同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243547'>久怀妙论传犀麈，尚喜清诗附驿筒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243547'>柳长五株知讼少，麦呈两穗报年丰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243547'>去天一握归来近，密令畴庸可拜公。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243547'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243547_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年2月10日</a>　跋永丰周日章兄弟所藏曾几书帖。作品：《跋曾吉甫帖后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋曾吉甫帖后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年2月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254479")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254479'>永丰周日章、日新兄弟，少力于学，尝以师谒曾吉甫于茶山，此其报字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254479_comment'></div>公之去茶山踰二十年矣，周氏兄弟华发萧然，犹连蹇场屋也，览之叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254479_comment'></div>淳熙十二年二月十日，南涧翁韩某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1254479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年3月</a>　为赵彥秬（周锡）作《竹友斋记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>竹友斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254567")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254567'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254567'>赵彦秬周锡寓于东阳佛舍，种竹百馀，以朝夕其下，名曰「竹隐」，而告于予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254567_comment'></div>予曰：竹则佳矣美矣，然隐非吾子事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254567_comment'></div>吾闻古之所谓隐者，谓其时命之大谬而不可以出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254567_comment'></div>今子以帝族之贤而圣明在上，一试而得官，再试而暂踬，然子之论议卓然益高，文辞蔚然益华，校今多士之选曾何后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254567_comment'></div>齿壮而发鬒，特时有未至而已，何遽以隐为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254567_comment'></div>吾将更以为「竹友」，则何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254567_comment'></div>周锡曰：君之语我厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254567_comment'></div>夫友者，同志之称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254567_comment'></div>竹之志谓何，而人何得以友之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254567_comment'></div>予曰：古之所谓友者，岂惟同志之谓，盖亦友其德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254567_comment'></div>竹之志不得而通，抑其德有似于君子欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254567_comment'></div>今夫春而华，夏而茂，秋而成且实，冬而复其根，则固草木之常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254567_comment'></div>惟竹为不然，以拱把之姿而怀金石不渝之操，以寻丈之材而蕴松柏后凋之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254567_comment'></div>虽葩卉艳发，澹然不为之迁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254567_comment'></div>雪霜冱严，挺然不为之槁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254567_comment'></div>依乎山巅，放乎水涯，气凌云霄之上，舞佳月而啸清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254567_comment'></div>若不复为世用也，逮其用焉，穴而吹之，足以为威凤之鸣，协律吕之和，挺而箦之，足以障洪河而庇广厦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254567_comment'></div>荐之清庙而为笾莒，纳之金匮而为简筴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254567_comment'></div>帷堂以为帘，设几以为簟，总竿以为箾，傅羽以为箭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254567_comment'></div>旅于菁茅而不为侈，杂于木屑而不为贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254567_comment'></div>则竹之用无施而不可焉，是其虚心以近道耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254567_comment'></div>今子之未至者，时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254567_comment'></div>使圣人而能为时，则冬起雷而夏造冰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254567_comment'></div>惟时至然后应，则亦何事于隐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254567_comment'></div>且君子坐卧于竹阴，而吟咏于一室，于中怀之得，固亦无异于隐者，俟有用而发焉，宜无以隐名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254567_comment'></div>惟竹之德有似于君子，故愿吾子友之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254567_comment'></div>淳熙十二年三月，颍川韩某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1254567_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　信守郑汝谐（舜举）邀游所居蔗庵，赋诗纪之。作品：《题郑舜举蔗庵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243551' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243551' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243551?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题郑舜举蔗庵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243551")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243551_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243551'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243551'>吾州富佳山，脩竹连峻岭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243551'>居然缚尘埃，一见辄心醒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243551'>岂知刺史宅，跬步閟清景。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243551'>古木盘城隅，石径幽且迥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243551'>当年徐常侍，坐爱云水冷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243551'>溪南群峰秀，矗矗锥出颖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243551'>郑公闭阁暇，独步毗庐顶。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243551'>曰此气象殊，逍遥步方永。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243551'>唤客倒清樽，燃薰煮奇茗。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243551'>庭空无一事，宾吏绝干请。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243551'>佳处由渐入，斯语烦记省。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243551'>渊明尝有语，结庐向人境。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243551'>恍如白莲社，挥麈对宗炳。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243551'>谁云忙里閒，要识动中静。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243551'>我来款妙论，散策步林影。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243551'>心田豁丛茅，气马罢征骋。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243551'>他时记棠阴，老意亦深肯。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243551'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_243551_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年5月12日</a>　是年辛、韩生日，复以上年《水龙吟》韵唱和，相互为寿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年11月</a>　遇郊祀，加食邑，有谢表。并请荫补其兄元龙之孙榘。作品：《郊赦加食邑谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254321' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254321' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254321?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郊赦加食邑谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254321")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254321_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254321'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254321'>礼行效报，初莫预于骏奔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254321_comment'></div>恩衍户租，乃重沾于惠术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254321_comment'></div>叨荣逾厚，揣分知惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254321_comment'></div>伏念臣久去班联，尚尸祠禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254321_comment'></div>材能素谫，了无横草之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254321_comment'></div>齿发寖彫，第有守株之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254321_comment'></div>莫致庆成之善颂，遂膺进律之殊褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254321_comment'></div>骈邑既增，取禾兴愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254321_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下化参天地，道通神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254321_comment'></div>方万岁以成纯，躬致严禋之祀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254321_comment'></div>靡一夫之不被，益均臣庶之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254321_comment'></div>申贲丝纶，用彰典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254321_comment'></div>臣敢不誓图报称，钦佩眷慈？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254321_comment'></div>纵观渭上之朝，讵忘异日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254321_comment'></div>独抱周南之病，自信馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254321_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1254321_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　是冬，大雪，与郑汝谐唱和。作品：《次韵郑守舜举喜雪四首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span>《郑守用前韵见示因亦和答四首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_243021' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243021' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243021?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵郑守舜举喜雪四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243021")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243021_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243021'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243021'>好雪相仍岁又除，丰年瑞事总堪书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243021_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243021'>未嫌款段追千骑，化作张仙跨白驴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243021_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243021'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243020_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243019?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243019'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243019'>银似豪家没奈何，玉成高垒更巍峨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243018'>月下更期看国艳，凌波那更舞江妃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243018'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243018_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243059?labeling=true' ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243059")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243059'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243059'>腊里三看雪满衢，使君当奉十行书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243059'>先生履敝人应笑，泥滑东家许借驴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243059'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243059_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243058?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243058'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243058'>九陌歌呼属后游，一蓑风景付渔舟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243058'>相逢且向南溪看，玉作灵山万石楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243058'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243058_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243057' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243057' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243057?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243057_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243057'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243057'>振廪縻金气自和，政声谁为勒嵯峨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243057'>牛羊垄上饥民绝，鹅鸭池边勇士多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243057'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243057_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243056' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243056' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243056?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243056_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243056'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243056'>天巧由来不露机，冰澌剪出万花飞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243056'>琼珰似识汉川女，瑶瑟更逢湘浦妃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243056'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243056_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　应泰州守万钟之请，作《泰州水门鼓角楼记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254571?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泰州水门鼓角楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254571")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254571'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254571'>淮甸之郊，介江而濒海，曰海陵郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254571_comment'></div>其地富鱼盐，骈商贾，河流贯城中，舟行若夷路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254571_comment'></div>其门跨水者三，岁久而敝，浮桁以制冲，棂扉以置钥，曾无以示禁而严闉阇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254571_comment'></div>钱唐万侯以儒雅饰吏事，守郡之明年，政成而令修，乃重理所谓三水门者，且楼其上，以临望四郊之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254571_comment'></div>民俗喜曰，吾公可谓知所务矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254571_comment'></div>无几何，郡之鼓角楼垫而壤，民又叹曰，吾公其可忘此哉，请亦新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254571_comment'></div>侯则谢曰：钟被天子命守是邦，无能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254571_comment'></div>始至之日，库之缗钱仅数百，庾之斛粟才数十也，旱暵既作，祷而幸应，麦菽旋登，粳稌云委，因得尽心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254571_comment'></div>兵吏之赋既充，岁时之用粗给，故方隅无犬吠之惊，以鼓舞尧舜之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254571_comment'></div>然城扉之防奸，征税之自入，有不可缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254571_comment'></div>今民之居尚茨于茅苇，而守之舍则亦寖备，夏屋渠然，以朝夕安处，虽一楼未葺，庸何伤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254571_comment'></div>而父老相与沓言之，宾客士大夫怂恿之，曰楼之于郡府，皋门之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254571_comment'></div>笳鼛之攸在，无不设者，如目之有眉，面之有颡，虽若不系于用，而天下不可阙焉，著自古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254571_comment'></div>考其近之岁月，作于绍兴之丁巳，盖四十有八年矣，由公而遂废，其忍乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254571_comment'></div>于是又以其馀力，始为之楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254571_comment'></div>既成，翼以二垛楼于外，遂为一郡杰特之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254571_comment'></div>夫古之君子为政而美者，无非以善于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254571_comment'></div>民之所欲而拒之，所弗欲而强之，皆非所以善于民者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254571_comment'></div>况夫土木之功，缮修营造之役，虽圣人亦所甚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254571_comment'></div>惟刺史二千石，心一不在乎民，则沽整办之誉以衒其风力者有之，增耳目之奇以自娱自奉者亦有之，下则伤于财而蠹于民，适资匠胥之盗窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254571_comment'></div>《春秋》于门观之作、台囿之筑，无不谨者，抑以是夫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254571_comment'></div>今万侯之政则既善矣，澹然不志于功利而蛊敝是去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254571_comment'></div>逮及举事之际，不自以为足，踌躇四顾，殆有所不得已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254571_comment'></div>至因其民之所愿欲，然后为之轮奂翚飞，不侈于前，不夸于后，无一取诸民，无一劳其民者，用能谈笑以底于成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254571_comment'></div>推是以往，举而措诸天下可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254571_comment'></div>海陵儒学之乡，吾意其士子必有歌而颂之者，将转而上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254571_comment'></div>故其规制之略、费用之目，皆无足以书，特书其善于民者，以彰侯之用心，俾后人其知焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1254571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年12月</a>　跋吕本中与魏矼（邦达）昆仲诗帖。作品：《跋吕居仁与魏邦达昆仲诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《四库辑本别集拾遗》页138。）</span><div id='poem_1254510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254510?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋吕居仁与魏邦达昆仲诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254510")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254510'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254510'>吕舍人久寓上饶，后葬于德源山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254510_comment'></div>故其晚年诗章，多见于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254510_comment'></div>今辰州魏使君所藏五篇，盖与其尊公侍郎及其季父邦杰、叔祖父元章者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254510_comment'></div>龙图则张殿中彦素尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254510_comment'></div>一时文士相从之适，气韵风流，为可概见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254510_comment'></div>虽无老成人，尚有典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254510_comment'></div>长啸宇宙间，高才日陵替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254510_comment'></div>古之诗人类有叹耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254510_comment'></div>淳熙乙巳岁十二月，颍川韩某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1254510_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年1月</a>　正月初，以高宗年八十庆典，进封颍川郡公，加食邑。作品：《谢进封颍川郡公加食邑实封表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254322' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254322' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254322?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢进封颍川郡王加食邑实封表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254322")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254322_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254322'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254322'>慈皇介寿，霈及敷天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254322_comment'></div>微臣何功，例叨进律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254322_comment'></div>仰止王言之贲，遽跻公社之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254322_comment'></div>伏念臣材不逮中，愚无所用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254322_comment'></div>蚤蒙异擢，讵忘补报之阶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254322_comment'></div>自取谤伤，尚窃安閒之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254322_comment'></div>方舜治格无为之盛，乃尧龄臻难老之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254322_comment'></div>千岁有逢，万邦胥庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254322_comment'></div>锡爵遂超于五等，疏封且冒于多田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254322_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下老老以兴民，君君而赋政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254322_comment'></div>盛礼备乐，成仪焕于两宫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254322_comment'></div>宥罪薄征，欢声溢于四表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254322_comment'></div>慨兹朽质，曷副深仁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254322_comment'></div>臣敢不誓罄丹诚，思酬洪造？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254322_comment'></div>老当益壮，况怀伏枥之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254322_comment'></div>用之则为，益励守株之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254322_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1254322_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　应安仁县丞韩暦请，为作《饶州安仁县丞厅记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饶州安仁县丞厅记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254570")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254570'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254570'>凡天下官府，虽曰临民，而栋宇之设，类不能逮夫浮屠老氏之舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254570_comment'></div>盖浮屠、老氏，其徒务为夸大，既营其居而不会其费，苟费不具则有弗为，规制未备则亦弗已，故磨于岁月，次第相付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254570_comment'></div>州县之力有不可冀者，而士之居官，望迁而幸去，远不过三年，近止一二岁，视之若传舍然，绵蕝草创，殆无必葺之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254570_comment'></div>始锐而终怠，作于前或弛于后，非有慨然持不回之志，未易举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254570_comment'></div>国家肇造，乾德中始诏官廨增葺创造，对书于新旧官历，其不葺者殿一选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254570_comment'></div>至景德三年，又定为印纸之目，廨宇间数既书其亏损，至添盖则又曰配民与不配民，皆所以防制官吏，欲其不茍而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254570_comment'></div>自印纸之改式也，后生不能旧制，而官吏之茍日滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254570_comment'></div>数十年来，加之以兵火，因之以匮乏，官廨不整尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254570_comment'></div>饶为望州，安仁为剧县，丞为上佐，其廨在县治之西，面覆盆之山，俯玉石之津，山水秀异，阴阳家以谓得庐山之一趾，然其宇蛊坏，久不可居，至寓于他所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254570_comment'></div>淳熙十年，从政郎韩君历为丞，始锐意新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254570_comment'></div>惧其费无所取也，先是君之来邑，例有迓夫之直，君储之不肯用，而用以市一山之木，梁楹乃具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254570_comment'></div>而民之输役庸者，亦例有公廨之入，君复不肯用，而亦不肯尽废，铢两积之，以陶瓦伐石，且为工匠之募。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254570_comment'></div>邑以剩粟助之，阅再岁而仅集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254570_comment'></div>其厅事堂庑，庖湢厩车，粗备而不陋，足以称其官而民无一词以为扰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254570_comment'></div>吾是以知天下之事，有志者竟成，而顾望退缩，以为不可为者，特系其能否尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254570_comment'></div>祖宗之制，于是可稽，而君之廉勤能力，于是可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254570_comment'></div>君颍人也，于吾族犹诸父行，绩学守官箴，盖有家法，故不敢溢美以书，而书其实以识于宇下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254570_comment'></div>淳熙十三年正月，具位韩某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1254570_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年2月</a>　作《铅山周氏义居记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254572' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254572' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254572?labeling=true' target='_blank'>铅山周氏义居记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254572")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254572_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254572'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254572'>东南之俗，土狭而赋俭，民啬于财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254572_comment'></div>故父祖在，多俾子孙自营其业，或未老而标析其产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254572_comment'></div>近岁因为之立法，虽曰欲绝异时争讼之弊，而纷纭斗阋，殊无睦姻忠厚之气，贤士大夫每以为病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254572_comment'></div>信安之地，犬牙于闽，铅山又在南，孕金青，殖宝货，壤厚而泉沃，类多大家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254572_comment'></div>周氏世为舒灊人，继迁金陵，避五季之乱，来家鹅峰之下，盖三百年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254572_comment'></div>有祠号将军者，最其始祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254572_comment'></div>系虽莫可谱，其曰承志、曰谊者，皆累祖业儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254572_comment'></div>至处士钦若，字彦恭，有声三舍间，晚不事举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254572_comment'></div>慕其舅祖里儒刘煇之义，尝曰刘公举进士，天下第一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254572_comment'></div>作《起俗记》，以诋讥不义之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254572_comment'></div>其祖妣之丧，有二季父，而公自以嫡孙而为之重服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254572_comment'></div>买田聚书，教养其族之贫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254572_comment'></div>邑令名其社曰「义荣」，是可法尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254572_comment'></div>处士始欲与其伯仲同居而不异籍，自以身在季不得专，切切为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254572_comment'></div>逮其病亟，当绍兴二十二年六月也，索纸书字二百馀，以戒其四子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254572_comment'></div>有曰：「吾平生教汝读书，固不专于利禄，欲汝等知义，以兴美薄俗尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254572_comment'></div>我病必不瘳，汝等尽孝以事母，当以义协居，勿有异志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254572_comment'></div>居舍虽小不足耻，田园虽寡不足虑也，不能遵吾训，是谓不孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254572_comment'></div>他日或仕，不以廉自守，是谓不忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254572_comment'></div>不孝不忠，非吾子孙也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254572_comment'></div>越六日而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254572_comment'></div>其配虞氏，贤而守义，恸哭而藏其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254572_comment'></div>淳熙四年，其子曰藻、曰芸、曰苾、曰芾稍长矣，虞乃以遗命陈于民部，祈给之凭，有司方下州县覈其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254572_comment'></div>又七年，藻等益壮以有立，继乞曰：母老矣，官未给凭，无以安母心，以明父训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254572_comment'></div>于是部符于州，州帖于县，始坐条令而予之据，以昭示其子与孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254572_comment'></div>盖国家之制，愿以财产不许子孙分割典卖者，官为给据，子孙不得追改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254572_comment'></div>而虞又自请异时子孙或违父母命，各居异业，许外人告而闻于朝省，坐以不孝之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254572_comment'></div>于是乡人莫不钦叹，而贤士大夫者相与来言，求予文以记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254572_comment'></div>予为之出涕而言曰，先王之教以孝弟为本，士之训子以义方为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254572_comment'></div>自先王之教陵迟而不振也，秦之法民不分异者倍其赋，而德色于父，谇语于母，汉兴犹或有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254572_comment'></div>故历代以来，于族居而义聚者，官必旌其门闾，复其户租，以表厉于众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254572_comment'></div>此无他，由为士者徒能诵六艺之文，以干取禄位而务殖其家，不知有以启导其子孙之善意，则亦宜乎风俗寖坏而未之或革也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254572_comment'></div>昔陶靖节，晋之高士，其称颍川、济北二贤以戒其子者，第以同居共财为首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254572_comment'></div>唐之崔郸，一门孝友，四世同爨，兄弟六人皆至三品，史以为未有也，可谓难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254572_comment'></div>逮我朝至道中，南康洪氏累叶聚舍，期功百口，建塾馆于雷塘以诲子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254572_comment'></div>太宗皇帝嘉之，赐以御书百轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254572_comment'></div>其弟文举入谢，天子又书「义居」之字以为宠，且命之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254572_comment'></div>其子待用，遂登巍科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254572_comment'></div>非积善彰明之效也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254572_comment'></div>夫处士之善，世无知者，其秉心蹈义，于是可传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254572_comment'></div>《传》有之，「制宅命子，足以观士」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254572_comment'></div>而虞氏，故殿中丞戬之孙，年九十矣，华颠素裳，既受封邑，尚惟保其夫之训以励其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254572_comment'></div>而藻等孝友孜孜，克成其父母之志馀三十年，后将弗坠，周氏其自此兴乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254572_comment'></div>洪惟圣明在上，今年方崇两宫期颐之庆，推恩宥于天下，或转而上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254572_comment'></div>至道故事，其申贲于岩邑，以风动于东南，殆无疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1254572_comment'></div>周氏岁入不能二千斛，内外几六百指，养其偏亲，时其祭祀，给其嫁婚，皆有定式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1254572_comment'></div>岁又以十万钱招延儒士，俾其幼稚学礼无缺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1254572_comment'></div>俭以足用，是可则云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1254572_comment'></div>淳熙十三年二月癸亥，具位韩某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1254572_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年3月</a>　其兄元龙卒于宣城，三月，有文祭告。作品：《告先兄墓文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>告先兄墓文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254667")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254667'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254667'>淳熙十三年，岁次丙午，三月，弟具位某，谨以清酌之奠，敢昭告于亡兄河图大卿之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254667_comment'></div>某往岁遣淲诣省，尝令具言某之侥倖奏补，当以及兄诸孙，以厚先君之世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254667_comment'></div>去冬复遇郊禋，遂获有请，以荫矩孙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254667_comment'></div>今其受命，虽曰某之志愿粗伸，俯仰之间，仅踰三年，痛兄之不及见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254667_comment'></div>遥望丘垄，有泪如洗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254667_comment'></div>敢祈鉴之，默赐保祐，俾之有立，克绍家规，庶吾兄弟之情，永永不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254667_comment'></div>寓书陈词，但切悲感。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1254667_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年5月11日</a>　辛弃疾生日，元吉以双鹤为寿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年5月12日</a>　元吉生日，辛弃疾、王德和与宴，有唱和。作品：《水调歌头·席上次韵王德和》（世事不须问）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243571?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>席上次韵王德和</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年5月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243571")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243571'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243571'>世事不须问，我老但宜仙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243571'>南溪一曲，独对苍翠与孱颜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243571'>月白风清长夏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243571'>醉里相逢林下。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243571'>欲辩已忘言。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243571'>无客问生死，有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_243571", 243571, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>竹报平安</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243571_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243571'>少年期，功名事，觅燕然。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243571'>如今憔悴，萧萧华发抱尘编。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243571'>万里蓬莱归路。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243571'>一醉瑶台风露。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243571'>因酒得天全。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243571'>笑指云阶梦，今夕是何年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_243571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年8月</a>　跋《管子》，以其书为“战国游士之述”，而非管仲之作。作品：《读〈管子〉》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254504?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读管子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254504")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254504'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254504'>《管子》之书，战国游士之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254504_comment'></div>孟子曰：齐桓公之于管仲，学焉而后臣之，故不劳而霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254504_comment'></div>则仲之与桓公，平日谋国议政者，其亦详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254504_comment'></div>然举而著之书者，则齐国之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254504_comment'></div>当是时，齐有稷下之邑，盖亦是尧舜，非桀纣，谈道德而言仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254504_comment'></div>虽仲之作内政以寓军令，在于强兵富国而霸齐，今其书则尚权术，务笼络，要以愚其民而用其力，驳杂为甚，已有战国之风，不知仲之说果若是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254504_comment'></div>故吾意其为游士之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254504_comment'></div>庄周之言曰：「道术为天下裂」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254504_comment'></div>盖六经未经圣人之手，则士之谈道者不能淳且正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254504_comment'></div>汉兴，贾谊、晁错之流，莫不推尊管氏之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254504_comment'></div>使是书而得尽用，则亦犹之乎申韩之刑名，商鞅、李斯之惨刻，岂复先王爱民养人之政哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254504_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254504_comment'></div>孔子之后，犹有孟子，其言王政，皆本于仁义，粹然一出于正，后世推之以为孔、孟，非虚语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254504_comment'></div>孟子之论管仲，止于以其君霸，而未尝议其治齐之政，夫是以疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254504_comment'></div>淳熙丙午八月，南涧翁书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1254504_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　是秋，送族弟元修归广东赴任。作品：《送元修归广东》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243301' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243301' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243301?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送元修归广东</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243301")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243301_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243301'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243301'>十年门户苦彫零，屈指天涯几弟兄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243301'>羁旅可堪怀世事，典型谁与振家声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243301'>惊心朔岸秋风急，极目南溟瘴雾横。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243301'>好过贪泉未应酌，少年游宦要冰清。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243301'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243301_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　冬，大雪，携酒访辛弃疾，同至雪楼观雪，有唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　年底，郑汝谐（舜举）赴召临安，与宴，赋词送行。作品：《菩萨蛮·郑舜举别席侑觞》（诏书昨夜先春到）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243607?labeling=true' target='_blank'>菩萨蛮<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>郑舜举别席侑觞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243607")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243607'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243607'>诏书昨夜先春到。留公一共梅花笑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243607'>青琐凤凰池。十年归已迟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243607_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243607'>灵溪霜后水。的的清无比。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243607'>比似使君清。要知清更明。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243607'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243607_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　春，王宁赴调改秩，有诗送行。作品：《送王德和赴调改秩》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243302' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243302' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243302?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王德和赴调改秩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243302")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243302_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243302'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243302'>樽酒盘蔬语夜阑，三年犹得几追欢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243302_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243302'>海棠半折春方好，杨柳都青社正寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243302_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243302'>筹画定应瞻武帐，文华端合侍金銮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243302_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243302'>割鸡底用磨天刃，迟日湖山满意看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243302_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243302'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243302_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年5月12日</a>　七十生日，辛弃疾有词为寿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　未久，即卒于上饶，陆游、赵蕃等有挽诗、祭文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　葬上饶城东。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　是年冬，入祀广信府学。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
信阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bced1053dae54584994960efbe6135db_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bced1053dae54584994960efbe6135db");'><span id='bced1053dae54584994960efbe6135db_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>，37岁</div><div id='bced1053dae54584994960efbe6135db' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　奉差至信阳，识苏峤（季真），一见相倾，为其淡斋作记。作品：《淡斋记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淡斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254547")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254547_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254547'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254547'>绍兴二十四年，予始识吾季真于信阳，爱其温然之文，挺然之姿，将有以世其家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254547_comment'></div>既而谓予曰：吾尝以「淡」名吾斋，吾自求其说不可得也，子能为吾言之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254547_comment'></div>予笑曰：子能言而不言者也，而吾可以不言言之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254547_comment'></div>夫天下之至美者，五味也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254547_comment'></div>至贵者，五色也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254547_comment'></div>嗜于口而悦于目，虽吾不异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254547_comment'></div>醴吾知其为甘，鹾吾知其为咸，醷吾知其为酸，姜桂吾知其为辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254547_comment'></div>至于泊然而无味者，非子之说乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254547_comment'></div>青黄者，吾知其为黼黻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254547_comment'></div>红紫者，吾知其为绮绣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254547_comment'></div>至于混然而无色者，非子之说乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254547_comment'></div>故泊然而无味者，水之谓也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254547_comment'></div>混然而无色者，太虚之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254547_comment'></div>今夫水流为江河，发为井泉，挹之浏然以清，激之锵然以鸣，投之五味而随所入焉，而水之质盖不可名状也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254547_comment'></div>人见其味之泊然也，遂以淡归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254547_comment'></div>今夫太虚大而寓于天地，小而限于一室，山岳窒之而不为盈，瓮盎贮之而不为幽，间以五色而随所寓焉，而太虚之质盖不可名状也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254547_comment'></div>人见其色之混然也，遂以淡归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254547_comment'></div>且彼其能受五味而纳五色者，岂不以其质之不可名状欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254547_comment'></div>使其定而不易，则酸者不可以为咸，而青者不可以为黄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254547_comment'></div>君子之于道也，内以存其心，外以应于事，虽酢酬万变而无留焉者，是亦将泊然混然而后已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254547_comment'></div>夫惟泊然混然，故随所用而无不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254547_comment'></div>然世之为是说也，茍以为无婴于名利而不湛于嗜欲，泛然与世不相町畦，则亦不足以独立于万物之表，是犹畏夫五味之泊、五色之杂者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254547_comment'></div>由是之说也，虽朝泊于五味而暮杂于五色，固未有害，彼其明于体而未达于用耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254547_comment'></div>季真曰：然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254547_comment'></div>子之说信辩矣，吾将寘于壁而徐思之，子其以是为记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1254547_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
鄂州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='94b87de670ef4c52a63d9f6699493016_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("94b87de670ef4c52a63d9f6699493016");'><span id='94b87de670ef4c52a63d9f6699493016_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>，37岁</div><div id='94b87de670ef4c52a63d9f6699493016' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　过武昌，赋诗感怀。作品：《武昌春色》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_243055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>武昌春色</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243055")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243055'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243055'>樊山宫殿已成陈，烟雨阴晴到处春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243055'>花柳不知兴废事，隔江相倚斗时新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243055'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243055_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
