-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='956a67b6d3a14429ba90ade6a9236664_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("956a67b6d3a14429ba90ade6a9236664");'><span id='956a67b6d3a14429ba90ade6a9236664_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>，39岁</div><div id='956a67b6d3a14429ba90ade6a9236664' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年3月</a>　奉差至建康，因便上书江东运判叶义问（审言）作品：《上叶运使书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254403' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254403' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254403?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上叶运使书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254403")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254403_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254403'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254403'>运使直阁郎中阁下：论世之治乱，孰不曰人材？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254403_comment'></div>论人材之所以为治乱，孰不曰贤不肖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254403_comment'></div>夫以一贤者与一不肖者在上，兹固未足以为治乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254403_comment'></div>惟其一贤者在上，而众贤者将由是以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254403_comment'></div>一不肖者在上，而众不肖者亦由是以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254403_comment'></div>贤者众则天下之事斯日以举，不肖者众则天下之事斯日以废，此其所以为治乱之极欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254403_comment'></div>虽然，天下之事所以不举者，此固不肖者之罪也，而贤者预有责焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254403_comment'></div>夫既已号为贤矣，而天下之事顾有不举者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254403_comment'></div>是有二说焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254403_comment'></div>不肖者之弊在于不能为，而贤者之弊在于不敢为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254403_comment'></div>夫不能为者，是其智不足而力不任也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254403_comment'></div>不敢为者，非其智不足而力不能，时有以禁之，势有以夺之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254403_comment'></div>天下之事，不患不肖者之不能为，而患莫大于贤者之不敢为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254403_comment'></div>昔者西汉盛时，汲长孺至以矫节而发淮南之仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254403_comment'></div>及其后也，诸葛丰以司隶而返去其节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254403_comment'></div>以二事而校之，岂不系于敢为与不敢为之时哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254403_comment'></div>国家比年以来，天下之吏大而在朝廷，小而在郡县，谄谀相师，偷懦相承，号为不肖者，盖已不胜其众，而其间所谓贤者，缩手畏避，亦近于不敢为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254403_comment'></div>今也主上举权纲而大振之，网罗天下之贤者，思尽付以天下之事，不啻如退阿进即墨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254403_comment'></div>然而不能为者，固无足以议此，而能为者，顾亦何所畏避而不为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254403_comment'></div>要须有人焉而为之倡，然后天下风俗可以少变而趋于大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254403_comment'></div>窃尝反覆而思之，其举而倡之，莫如阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254403_comment'></div>夫以过情之语而妄说于人，某亦不忍为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254403_comment'></div>盖去年冬，主上始新政事，驿而召者十人，阁下实在其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254403_comment'></div>曾未数月，自博士而为郎，自郎而赐对，遂宠以延阁之名而付以一路之事，书名御屏，赐以鞍马，礼遇之数，皆近世所无有，是主上之待阁下，将有不止此者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254403_comment'></div>以主上之待阁下将有不止此，则试于外也，岂不亦观阁下所为而将有以付与之欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254403_comment'></div>不识阁下何以为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254403_comment'></div>以他人之材，固有不能为者，阁下自少年以直亮闻于当世，而志气日以宏，声名日以大，苟从而见诸事业，是犹骛八骏于九轨之道，纵横驰骋，无不如意，信非不能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254403_comment'></div>阁下又素负敢为之名，而遇可为之时，八州数十县之众亦不为少，货财之虚赢，狱讼之缓急，奔走之吏，引其廉能而罢其贪懦，与夫国家之利病，民人之休戚，问之使者所不能为者，岂无可为者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254403_comment'></div>某尝怪世之士大夫类知以其职之为职，而不知其职之所以为职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254403_comment'></div>夫以其职之为职，是犹富人之营其家，苟以利于我者，为足以富而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254403_comment'></div>知其所以为职，是犹廉吏之营其家，得一物焉必究其所从来，不徒欲富而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254403_comment'></div>夫所谓部使者，按籍而督州县之赋，执笔以奉朝廷之命，限岁以举小大之吏，是不可谓有为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254403_comment'></div>州县之赋，敢究其所当得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254403_comment'></div>朝廷之命，敢论其可从与否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254403_comment'></div>小大之吏，岁举之外，敢有所论荐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254403_comment'></div>是犹可得而名言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254403_comment'></div>至其不可得而名言者，则又在所设施耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254403_comment'></div>以一道而推之，难至于天下可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254403_comment'></div>某北方之鄙人，仕为郡之小吏，顾其平生，颇知自守，未尝以进取为事，非有左右为之先，非有权贵为之援，特以慕下风而仰盛德，以求见于阁下，乃刺口而论天下之事，此在古人则为言深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254403_comment'></div>然主上以特达而知阁下，意阁下之待天下之士亦当以此，是以自恃而不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254403_comment'></div>恭惟阁下少霁其威严，而幸听其猖狂之论，上以副主上之所期，下以为天下士夫之倡，则某者傥受知于门下，为不忝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254403_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254403_comment'></div>某惶恐再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1254403_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='47cc5f03493f474e9d8787d5d5463bda_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("47cc5f03493f474e9d8787d5d5463bda");'><span id='47cc5f03493f474e9d8787d5d5463bda_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>，40岁</div><div id='47cc5f03493f474e9d8787d5d5463bda' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　至建康，上书知建康府兼行宫留守张焘，并以所著《三国论》进。作品：《上建康帅张尚书书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷13。）</span><div id='poem_1254405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上建康帅张尚书书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254405")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254405'>某读《诗》至于「我思古人，实获我心」，未尝不叹于古人之难遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254405_comment'></div>又读《诗》至于「虽无老成人，尚有典型」，然后知老成之亦足以为古人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254405_comment'></div>盖士方穷时，莫不有志于天下之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254405_comment'></div>惟其求之当世而无以告语，由是必思于古之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254405_comment'></div>苟或当世而有以告语也，则又何思于古之人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254405_comment'></div>然学者之弊，常在于好古而不识其实，则以为古之事不可行于今，而今之人不能尽如古，规规然守其说，以取高于世俗，是皆近于古而不切于用者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254405_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254405_comment'></div>且上此而百世，可以为古矣，下此而百世，岂不又以吾为古哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254405_comment'></div>彼其说曰：「吾有取于古之人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254405_comment'></div>古之人有尧舜焉，有桀纣焉，不独有孔子，而有盗蹠焉，则又可概取乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254405_comment'></div>惟其取于能获我心，则可谓云尔矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254405_comment'></div>某之始学也，固亦未免斯弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254405_comment'></div>得一言而信之，以谓可行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254405_comment'></div>行之而窒焉，则慨然以为无复古人之事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254405_comment'></div>及其既长也，以为古人既不可见，得见老成者斯足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254405_comment'></div>顾其饥寒憔悴，犹以上世之泽，齿一命于州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254405_comment'></div>然某之仕也，始亦未尝求人之知，而待其自知焉，然而知之者无几也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254405_comment'></div>故屡厄于铨选之法，每更一官，则一试于吏部，盖人独试于始仕，而某独三焉，世莫不笑其迂也，某之意盖有所不得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254405_comment'></div>窃尝深念，闻阁下之风，而足迹不至于门墙，姓名未通于典谒，阁下过听，千里而召之，意者将以察其貌而闻其言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254405_comment'></div>夫以一命之贱而见于天子之从臣，郡佐之卑而谒于连帅之大府，其上下有等衰，其礼貌有轻重，是固未可以倾盖而谈，更仆而语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254405_comment'></div>阁下虽欲其言，何自而闻之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254405_comment'></div>不然，某试诵其所欲言者，而阁下试听之可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254405_comment'></div>今天下之事，某不知其缓急先后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254405_comment'></div>十数年来，用事者所以藉口而谢天下，不过息兵二字而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254405_comment'></div>自息兵之外，政事日以不修，风俗日以大坏，譬犹人之病醉，昏昏扰扰，肢体与向者同而举措与向者异，固不可指言其状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254405_comment'></div>天下之人，盖疾视而不敢言，心语而不敢议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254405_comment'></div>属者主上翻然感悟，黜陟善恶，区别邪正，将以大新庶政之原，虽三尺童子盖亦开口吐气，以望天下之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254405_comment'></div>今既数月矣，圣意焦然于上，群议纷然于下，设施之事，若未有统者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254405_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254405_comment'></div>诚不知中外谁可以任此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254405_comment'></div>夫必欲以一人之言而更一事，以一事而下一令，此不亦失之太繁而议之太过！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254405_comment'></div>为之要者，莫若先变天下之风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254405_comment'></div>夫天下之风俗，皆起于士大夫，智者陈其谋，能者趋其事，而人君与大臣总其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254405_comment'></div>如此而不治者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254405_comment'></div>风俗既振，则天下之事皆可以叙而施行，欲兵而兵，欲农而农，欲富而富，欲强而强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254405_comment'></div>如人之元气既充，则外邪皆去，百骸九窍，怡然顺适而无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254405_comment'></div>今也贤士大夫，犹复相与退避畏缩，以为吾未至于其任，不当以先虑其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1254405_comment'></div>且古君子，君有问焉，其应如响，及其得位，而行无不如志，是岂不先虑而获哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1254405_comment'></div>虽孔子、孟子历聘诸侯，问政焉告之政，问仁焉告之仁，莫不尽其宜而适其当，谓其不先虑，吾不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1254405_comment'></div>恭惟阁下声名著于华夷，风采见于事业，隐然德望，向之所谓古人，今之所谓老成者也，宜起而任此久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1254405_comment'></div>意者规模素定于胸中，将亦兼收天下之人物，以资异日之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1254405_comment'></div>而某者不自知其浅陋，猥叙其平生，以冒昧于万一之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1254405_comment'></div>夫持方寸之木于大匠之门，虽固不少，此亦不可为无用，惟阁下其亮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1254405_comment'></div>所谓文虽多，不能尽献，往尝著《三国论》，颇有意见，阁下观之，以为何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1254405_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1254405_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b823e4c956594f65b16b4a5d5dfc7525_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b823e4c956594f65b16b4a5d5dfc7525");'><span id='b823e4c956594f65b16b4a5d5dfc7525_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，44岁</div><div id='b823e4c956594f65b16b4a5d5dfc7525' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　赴宣城省母，过建康，遇友人王嵎（季夷），同游蒋山，有次韵诗。作品：《次韵王季夷时同宿蒋山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3f65d1f78808416d96db5bf217b40706_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3f65d1f78808416d96db5bf217b40706");'><span id='3f65d1f78808416d96db5bf217b40706_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1168')">1166-1168年</a>，49-51岁</div><div id='3f65d1f78808416d96db5bf217b40706' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年8月1日</a>　八月初到江南东路转运判官任。作品：《江东转运判官谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江东转运判官谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年8月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254315")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254315'>窃食无功，久尸于宰掾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254315_comment'></div>便私有请，尚畀于使轺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254315_comment'></div>祗届部封，具宣诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254315_comment'></div>伏念臣零丁坠绪，历落凡材，一趋君玺之严，五阅岁躔之换。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254315_comment'></div>为郎甚宠，乃官谤之自贻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254315_comment'></div>去国稍淹，迄州符之未试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254315_comment'></div>曲荷乾坤之造，再瞻日月之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254315_comment'></div>南省西枢之联，曾微报效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254315_comment'></div>中台右辖之属，荐至摄承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254315_comment'></div>揣分输诚，拜恩从欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254315_comment'></div>策名中秘之府，锡节大江之壖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254315_comment'></div>地接行畿，实总陪都之调度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254315_comment'></div>迹违文陛，重勤睿训之丁宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254315_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下天覆尧仁，日跻汤圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254315_comment'></div>衡持内外，初无彼重而此轻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254315_comment'></div>器使贤愚，靡见寸长而尺短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254315_comment'></div>治厉精而匪倦，功复古之是图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254315_comment'></div>致此妄庸，姑从寄委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254315_comment'></div>臣敢不益坚素守，无负圣知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254315_comment'></div>虽揽辔登车，未究昔人之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254315_comment'></div>傥给军转漕，或殚异日之能。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1254315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　再至镇江，晤王嵎（季夷）、章甫（冠之），有怀陆游，作《满江红》词，步其原韵。作品：《满江红·再至丹阳……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243616' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243616' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243616?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>再至丹阳，每怀务观，有歌其所制者，因用其韵示王季夷、章冠之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243616")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243616_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243616'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243616'>江绕层城，重楼迥、依然山色。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243616'>□□有、佳人犹记，旧家离别。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243616'>把酒只如当日醉，挥毫剩欠尊前客。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243616'>算平林、有恨寄伤心，烟如织。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243616_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243616'>湖平树，花连陌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243616'>风景是，光阴易。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243616'>叹新声浑在，断云难觅。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243616'>暮雨不成巫峡梦，数峰还认湘波瑟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243616'>但与君、同看小槽红，真珠滴。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243616'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_243616_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年8月</a>　视察永丰圩。作品：《永丰行》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永丰行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243418")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243418'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243418'>丹阳湖中好风色，晴日波光漾南北。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243418'>湖岸人家榆柳行，风飐低昂似迎客。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243418'>系船并岸聊一呼，老农指是<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>官田圩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243418'>长衫紫领数百辈，见我罗拜长嗟吁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243418'>政和回头五十载，官长筑圩宛然在。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243418'>东西相望五百圩，有利由来得无害。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243418'>官圩民圩奚所拘，此地无田但有湖。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243418'>围湖作田事应尔，底用彻地还龟鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243418'>民圩不坚自招水，水潦何常镇如此。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243418'>官圩六十里如城，削平为湖定何理<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作里，据《景定建康志》改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243418'>请看今来禾上场，七百顷地云堆黄。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243418'>县官籴米三万斛，度僧给牒能商量。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243418'>我闻此语汗生面，千闻岂如目一见。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243418'>吾君神圣坐九重，轻易献言谁复辨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243418'>却忆吴中初夏时，畚锸去决湖田<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>围。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243418'>鸡惊上篱犬上屋，水至不得携妻儿。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243418'>无田赴水均一死，善政养民那得尔。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243418'>寄言父老且深耕，为汝驰书报天子。<div id='poem_sentence_17_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_243418'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_243418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_243418'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_243418_0'>⑴ 《景定建康志》卷三七作似</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_243418_0'>⑵ 原作田湖，据《景定建康志》乙</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_243418_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　是秋，朝廷下令江东、淮西共起夫役，开掘和州千秋涧，以为防秋之计。元吉上札子建议“就委本州，和雇人夫”，以免“两路人夫，张皇事势”作品：《上执政论千秋涧起夫札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254394' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254394' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254394?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上执政论千秋涧起夫劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254394")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254394_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254394'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254394'>某照对今月二十九日准三省、枢密院劄子，备奉圣旨，以和州开千秋涧，依白劄子内事理，江东转运司于建康府太平州火急应副人夫，开掘河道闸坝等用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254394_comment'></div>元约系二十万工，江东与淮西转运司分认各十万工，每日差夫二千人，每路各合日差千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254394_comment'></div>又奉圣旨，令逐旋兴工措置，不得张皇，除已下建康府、太平州并会问和州兴工次第外，访闻千秋涧有古沟遂，开修若成，足以保聚粮食，外固大江，实为要地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254394_comment'></div>惟是有逐旋兴工、不得张皇一节，恐负使令，不敢隐默，更合取自指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254394_comment'></div>窃详白劄子所献利便，正为自沣湖水际开挑千秋涧，至石塘下接黄水荡，仍更断岁丰桥，即有重水为阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254394_comment'></div>又云乘此湖塘无水，兴工入役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254394_comment'></div>即是现今秋冬之际，湖塘已自无水，就便火急兴工，以为防秋之计，开掘得成，无水为阻，未必可恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254394_comment'></div>况收刈是时，遽起夫役，每州日五百人，十日一替，亦得一百日，方得凑成十万工数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254394_comment'></div>每番差官沿路部押，地头董役，往来宿食，沿江便应骚动，深虑无缘不至张皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254394_comment'></div>欲望钧慈，更赐详酌敷奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254394_comment'></div>若止欲逐旋兴工，谓宜就委本州和雇人夫，日役千人，减省工料，渐次开掘，依旧总领所应副钱米，不至更起两路人夫，张皇事势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254394_comment'></div>如蒙灼见，所陈湖塘已是水涸，开掘得成，其利亦在来年春夏始可潴水捍御，即乞更待冬深收成之后，农夫少隙，次第兴工，公私为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254394_comment'></div>伏见太宗朝何承矩在沧州建议开塘泊，系以水田为名，而命承矩为沿边屯田使，故塘成而敌始觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254394_comment'></div>今若避张皇之患，即望朝廷将上件事理密付守臣监司知悉，而委官逐一相度措置，别降指挥，只以开通漕运为名，庶得稳当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254394_comment'></div>某人微位下，特以职事所及，僭越申禀，或刍荛之议，万一可采，岂胜厚幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254394_comment'></div>干冒威严，某下情惶惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1254394_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年10月</a>　再上札子，由千秋涧论及江北防务。作品：《与执政论千秋涧事宜札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span><div id='poem_1254395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与执政论千秋涧事宜劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254395")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254395'>某窃以初冬戒序，恭想某官光辅圣神，天人攸相，钧候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254395_comment'></div>某比者被命与抚谕同司淮西水利，愚懵不肖，猥荷使令，敢不罄竭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254395_comment'></div>虽诸司定议，事已具闻，而其间琐细有不能尽者，无由面禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254395_comment'></div>窃计钧慈亦欲详见，故列之别纸，以俟采择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254395_comment'></div>此区区刍荛之志，而况于叨奉旨意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254395_comment'></div>某数日走和州境内，究观淮西地利，得其大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254395_comment'></div>盖昭关以北，大路骈来，所谓关者，有其名尔，关傍之路实自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254395_comment'></div>稍依丘陵，聚重兵为营寨，以与敌拒，使彼不敢越而南，策之上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254395_comment'></div>此地不能遏，直抵千秋涧，则吾之气亦夺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254395_comment'></div>而千秋涧者，岂不可攻之地哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254395_comment'></div>特愈于无尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254395_comment'></div>若以都统制刘源之说，欲姑以千秋涧内为家计寨而力战于前，则庶几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254395_comment'></div>其地接沣湖者犹险，下数里则无险矣，但当以水为阻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254395_comment'></div>水至穷冬，未知深浅如何，又所险者非闽蜀高山峻岭之比，坡陀冈阜，淮南之险不过如此尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254395_comment'></div>而城筑之崇，仅能如往岁瓜洲之垒，须厚为兵屯，然后可固也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254395_comment'></div>然和州现兴者三役，未兴者一役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254395_comment'></div>千秋涧一也，姥下河二也，韦游沟三也，日役数千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254395_comment'></div>惟千秋涧成，粗可控扼，姥下河所开沙夹，欲使居民保聚其上，彼已破州城而至江岸，岂限一河而不能寨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254395_comment'></div>然舟行可以不由采石山下，此前日太平守纷纷谓其恐夺采石之说者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254395_comment'></div>或谓江流北岸可急，而南岸迂缓，亦在商贾自择之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254395_comment'></div>韦游沟者，可灌溉以为民田，非可以保江也，此外未兴之役号清溪涧，其工浩大，不宜遽举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254395_comment'></div>就使得成，我万有一失，彼得自巢湖口引舟而来，麻、沣二湖水寨便破，径傅城下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254395_comment'></div>虽有千秋戍，何所用之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254395_comment'></div>此事皆以告胡昉，当亦自止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254395_comment'></div>然昉之意，实有可嘉，士大夫选愞而不肯任事已久，而昉能慨然奋励，又其赋役均平，年丰谷米狼戾，民户虽劳，莫不服从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254395_comment'></div>间有过节，在朝廷酌而任之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254395_comment'></div>某仰恃爱眷，敢私布之，幸赐容察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254395_comment'></div>向寒，更乞上体注倚，珍护寝饔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254395_comment'></div>倚俟端拜，下情不胜驰颂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1254395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年10月</a>　十月底，千秋、姥下、石跋三河告成，元吉与龙大渊、刘源、梁竑等出席庆典，张孝祥（安国）为作记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年11月</a>　叶衡（梦锡）为总领淮西江东军马钱粮兼提领措置营田。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年12月</a>　其兄元龙（子云）罢淮东总领，由镇江奉母来建康就养，友人庞谦孺（祐甫）来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年12月</a>　其友赵彥端（德庄）召为枢密院检正诸房文字，迁右司员外郎，请归葬其亲。有诗寄之。作品：《寄赵德庄二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄赵德庄二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243371")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243371'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243371'>报陟西枢掾，遥怜势未行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243371'>葬亲尝有请，去国岂无名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243371'>松菊关心在，江山到眼青。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243371'>琵琶洲畔宅，归计几时成。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243371'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243371_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243370' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243370' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243370?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243370_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243370'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243370'>早辱交情厚，年来事辄同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243370'>自知荣宦拙，甘为好诗穷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243370'>凫雁且依水，马牛还信风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243370'>故应怀李白，但欲老江东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243370'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243370_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年1月</a>　其兄元龙（子云）降一官，停现任宫观。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　年初，其友章甫（冠之）自仪真来，与其兄弟及庞谦孺（祐甫）相聚甚欢，并称“四老”，名其所馆为四老堂，元吉作《四老堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》拾遗。）</span><div id='poem_1254581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四老堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道三年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254581")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254581'>乾道二年秋，予自公府掾得请补外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254581_comment'></div>上不忍其穷，而犹以为可用也，俾漕于江东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254581_comment'></div>予平生喜交游，其在中朝所与游多天下知名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254581_comment'></div>遇退食之隙，及日之休暇，则亦持酒赋诗，䌷绎文史，讲论古今以为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254581_comment'></div>既骤膺使者之寄矣，宾客之至者，动以礼法相拘絷，猝猝不得款，虽强之亦往往不肯尽兴辄去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254581_comment'></div>而漕之治颇有轩亭之敞，花竹之茂，职事稍閒，可以周游闲放，而无前日交游之盛与共此者，予方以为恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254581_comment'></div>岁十二月，予兄子云自京口罢官，始得奉太夫人以就养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254581_comment'></div>弟兄晤语，颇已自适，而友人庞祐父乃自吴中来过，得之益欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254581_comment'></div>明年春，鄱阳章冠冠之复从仪真来，馆于一室，四人者昼夜语不休，閒以讽论难，而谈辩锋起，笑呼之声闻于外，向来索居之叹若醉而醒病而逾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254581_comment'></div>盖留累月，其为欢且甚矣，于是尽取所谓轩亭之名相与易之，不易更书之，而二友之所舍，因名之曰四老堂，吾四人者，实以自况也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254581_comment'></div>夫古之君子，少而学，壮而仕，老而传，皆礼之常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254581_comment'></div>年未七十，不可谓之老；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254581_comment'></div>又老者，非人子所宜称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254581_comment'></div>今吾兄弟之有亲也，而与祐父年仅五十，冠之复少于予十馀岁，皆不得谓之老，而遽以老自名者，盖皆生于羁旅，而长于贫贱，容貌苶然以衰，鬓发苍然以华，虽未老而老态已具，故辞其名而不可得尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254581_comment'></div>又四人者志尚之侔，而臭味之相似，不特相从于此，盖将相老期于山林之下，此堂之所以识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254581_comment'></div>然祐父牵于文章，仕而未达；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254581_comment'></div>冠之以诗自鸣，不肯用以求仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254581_comment'></div>而予与子云乃侥倖为郎，以蒙上之任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254581_comment'></div>子云既投劾以归，予之庸且懦，每惧其不获免也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254581_comment'></div>使吾四人者幸而至于老，既老而果得自逸于山林，回视今日所以名吾堂而为之先者，岂不信而无所愧哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254581_comment'></div>则斯堂虽陋，或以吾党之故而传，后之来者，固贤于予，亦足以知老之可慕，而人生会合之可乐也夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254581_comment'></div>二月己卯，颍川韩元吉记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1254581_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年2月</a>　二月甲戌，跋安化郡王赵士太墨迹。作品：《跋赵郡王墨迹》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋赵郡王墨迹</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254478")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254478'>少师安化郡王以宗藩之英，及见中原太平之盛，艰难渡江，享有富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254478_comment'></div>而手书此文，推原道德仁义，诋讥前代，欲使人君用为龟镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254478_comment'></div>是以知其所感者深，所蕴者厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254478_comment'></div>乾道丁亥岁二月甲戌，颍川韩某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1254478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年2月</a>　二月辛巳，虞允文知枢密院事，有贺启。作品：《贺虞枢密启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺虞枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254437")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254437'>伏审光膺制册，升冠枢庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254437_comment'></div>二府荐居，久已注安危之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254437_comment'></div>四夷耸动，益将闻道德之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254437_comment'></div>矧在知怜，尤深抃舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254437_comment'></div>恭惟枢密知院相公，负时雅望，为世真贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254437_comment'></div>隽路彯缨，轹诸儒于步武；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254437_comment'></div>军门秉羽，摧勍敌于笑谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254437_comment'></div>未酬淝水之勋，犹命东山之驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254437_comment'></div>朅从政地，自佚真祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254437_comment'></div>曾何破斧之伤，已见赐环之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254437_comment'></div>上心有在，英公宁计于去来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254437_comment'></div>舆论益归，令尹讵怀于喜愠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254437_comment'></div>惟兹宥密，足副经纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254437_comment'></div>明君可与忠言，既有资于启沃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254437_comment'></div>上策莫如自治，当遂底于安强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254437_comment'></div>伫聆彝鼎之书，进陟魁衡之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254437_comment'></div>某受知惟旧，去德未遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254437_comment'></div>断木委于沟中，固惭刻画；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254437_comment'></div>病驹伏于辕下，敢惮驰驱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254437_comment'></div>尚欣难遇之时，以观可大之业。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1254437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　庞谦孺（祐甫）辞行，有词赠之。作品：《满江红·丁亥示庞祐甫》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243617' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243617' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243617?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>丁亥示庞祐甫</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243617")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243617_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243617'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243617'>梅欲开时，君欲去、花谁同折。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243617'>应怅望、江津千树，晚烟明雪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243617'>花似故人相见好，人如塞雁多离别。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243617'>待留君、重看水边花，花边月。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243617_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243617'>台城路，山如阙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243617'>追往事，伤时节。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243617'>但春风春雨，古人愁绝。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243617'>多少扬州诗兴在，直须清梦翻胡蝶。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243617'>问他年、谁记饮中仙，花应说。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243617'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_243617_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年闰7月</a>　整理、刊刻二程语录《师说》，闰七月作跋。作品：《书师说后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书师说后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年闰7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254494")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254494'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254494'>二程先生讲论答问之言，门弟子记之，旧曰《师说》，厥后见于世，其号《河南雅言》而分大小程子者，程氏诸孙所修也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254494_comment'></div>其号《伊川杂说》，自通言明大本而下，名以为十三篇者，胡明仲兄弟所辑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254494_comment'></div>《雅言》则润色以文，间遗其意，复以章奏书记交寘其中，杨、谢诸公之语缀于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254494_comment'></div>而《杂说》者，亦广记而未择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254494_comment'></div>下此悉号《语录》，未知其谁定，尤混乱不可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254494_comment'></div>明道先生蚤没，伊川先生复坐党籍之谪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254494_comment'></div>逮还伊阙，闻诸故老，蔡京至遣人伺察之，俾无敢著书，则当时私淑其徒所记亦略矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254494_comment'></div>靖康初，公道始开，杨龟山首辟王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254494_comment'></div>建炎龙兴，先生门弟子相继有闻，《易》、《春秋》、《语》、《孟》之学，始行于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254494_comment'></div>而赵丞相尝官于洛，素知推敬其书，一时士君子靡然向之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254494_comment'></div>及秦益公当国，诸贤零落殆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254494_comment'></div>秦亦旧从洛学者也，晚乃谓人为其所惑盖三十年，且诋其说为提先手，由是虽进士之文亦不复道之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254494_comment'></div>夫圣学之有本与儒术之有传授，曾何计于时好，然天下之士惑于异端者深，溺于文辞者众，不议而非之，亦指而笑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254494_comment'></div>予家有《师说》，其编各有名氏，或者相劝传之，以谓非且笑者顾何足恤，使传而习焉，虽数十百年，千万而得一人，亦斯文之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254494_comment'></div>用釐为十卷，刊置江东漕斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254494_comment'></div>间有异同，不敢悉去，而首以尹和靖之编者，得所先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254494_comment'></div>二先生之说，不复异录者，不能尽知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254494_comment'></div>顷和靖为张子韶言，伊川暮年为《易传》，未肯出也，其学于是乎在，后生宜尽心焉，因并以记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254494_comment'></div>乾道三年后七月，颍川韩某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1254494_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年8月10日</a>　与其兄元龙、族兄元象等人游钟山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　秋游雨花台，有词记怀。作品：《水调歌头·雨花台》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>雨花台</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243569")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243569'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243569'>泽国又秋晚，天际有飞鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243569'>中原何在，极目千里暮云重。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243569'>今古长干桥下，遗恨都随流水，西去几时东。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243569'>斜日动歌管，萸菊舞西风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243569_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243569'>江南岸，淮南渡，草连空。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243569'>石城潮落，寂寞烟树锁离宫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243569'>且斗樽前酒美，莫问楼头佳丽，往事有无中。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243569'>却笑东山老，拥鼻与谁同。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_243569_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　登赏心亭，感怀赋诗。作品：《赏心亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243388' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243388' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243388?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赏心亭<span class='inlineComment2'>（亭后世传张丽华墓）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243388")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243388'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243388'>北风吹雨冷如秋，更上江干百尺楼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243388'>琼树佳人闭黄壤，石城华屋变沧洲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243388'>三峰已觉蓬莱近，二水真成汗漫游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243246' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243246' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243246?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夜坐有感寄子云<span class='inlineComment2'>（金陵作漕）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243246")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243246_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243246'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243246'>风景新亭旧往还，谁能举目较河山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243246'>宦情老去秋多感，官事忙时夜始閒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243246'>窗外槁梧风瑟缩，竹间乱石雨淙潺。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243246'>青灯已作江湖梦，同约归期早晚间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243246'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243246_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年9月</a>　九月庚午，周必大（子充、洪道）来访。癸酉，与叶衡（梦锡）、张荣宴周于雨花台。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年9月</a>　作《江东转运使题名记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》拾遗。）</span><div id='poem_1254582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江东转运使题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254582")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254582'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254582'>转运之置，虽昉于唐，然第掌水陆之输，其黜陟按察犹别命使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254582_comment'></div>至国朝始得刺举一道，吏之能否，民之戚休，狱讼钱谷，无所不当问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254582_comment'></div>庆历中，欧阳文忠公为河北都转运使，则又请与闻边事，以调军储，察将帅，仁宗因是从之，然则重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254582_comment'></div>今江东亦边也，地总九郡而治建业，天子南巡狩建业，新立行幸之宫，宿重师以控江淮，馈饷繁而道里舒，故所谓转运者，视它路为剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254582_comment'></div>元吉之滥官于此，既踰年矣，欲求前人名氏以识其居职久近，而碑志坏灭，莫可踪迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254582_comment'></div>盖问诸故府，开宝八年，江南舆地始上于职方，以杨克让知升州，寔兼转运事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254582_comment'></div>太平兴国初，遂以使樊若水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254582_comment'></div>六年，张齐贤去华相继为副，旋又充使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254582_comment'></div>时踵唐开元旧制，分江南为东西路，未几复合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254582_comment'></div>天禧四年，始定为东西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254582_comment'></div>兴国之三年也，诸路置转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254582_comment'></div>未几，复省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254582_comment'></div>嘉祐五年，又置之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254582_comment'></div>其间名卿贤大夫不能尽见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254582_comment'></div>建炎以来所尽见者，则亦有其名氏而亡其官称，或存其官称而逸其到罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254582_comment'></div>惧益远而不可考，故自建炎次第录之，得四十有八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254582_comment'></div>夫以朝廷置使之重，一道将输廉按之剧，寖失其传，由吾不肖者而复焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254582_comment'></div>则贤者之来，其忍遽废而不举也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254582_comment'></div>乾道三年九月戊子，颍川韩元吉记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1254582_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　史正志（致道）来守建康。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　与韩廷玉游宝林院，有唱和。作品：《宝林院次韩廷玉韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243250' class='_poem'><div class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243250")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243250_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243250'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243250'>山绕孤城水拍空，惜无残月照疏桐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243250'>江干云断夜来雨，木末凉生秋到风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243250'>六代兴亡知寺古，老禅神异载碑丰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243250'>诗成极目苍茫里，惜别情怀醉梦中。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　《建业书事》诗似亦是时之作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243462' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243462")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243462'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243462'>千载西州路，何人不此行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243462'>山横桃叶渡，江动石头城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243462'>天阙云端耸，秦淮雨后清。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243462'>敢论风景异，举目笑平生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月</a>　赵彥端（德庄）为江南东路计度转运副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年1月</a>　正月，雪中以诗约客登赏心亭。作品：《春雪得小诗五首且约客登赏心亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷。）</span><div id='poem_243025' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243025' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243025?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春雪得小诗五首且约客登赏心亭<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243025")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243025_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243025'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243025'>东窗坐爱枝间雪，大似酴醾压架花。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243025_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243025'>天气更晴宜有月，夜深来看玉交加。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243025_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243025'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243025_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243023' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243023' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243023?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243023_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243023'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243023'>淮南山色一千里，落水层城江更湍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243023_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243023'>何地江山有如许，与君聊趁雪中看。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243023_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243023'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243023_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243022' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243022' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243022?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243022_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243022'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243022'>腊前未见梅如雪，春到还惊雪似梅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243022'>可是天公有情思，便令花树一时开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243022'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243022_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243026?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243026_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243026'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243026'>江南绝景赏心亭，卧雪难寻旧画屏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243026'>白鹭洲前夜来雪，故应此画胜丹青。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243026'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243026_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243024?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243024_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243024'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243024'>竹炉听雪坐蒲团，长笑诗人不耐寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243024_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243024'>未办貂裘走南陌，肯来高处一凭栏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243024_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243024'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243024_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年2月</a>　金坛陈从古（晞颜）作斋名“敦复”，二月，元吉为作记。作品：《敦复斋记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敦复斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254550")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254550_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254550'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254550'>人之居，凡既往而归谓之复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254550_comment'></div>其于物，凡既失而得亦谓之复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254550_comment'></div>是复之义，皆返其故而还其初者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254550_comment'></div>人之所以为人，天地之所以为天地，其必有自矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254550_comment'></div>在人者求诸心，在天地之大，岂其无心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254550_comment'></div>日运而星飞，渊旋而岳峙，四时变化，莫有穷尽，天地之心，固未可识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254550_comment'></div>以吾心所存焉者而求诸天地，则亦不外是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254550_comment'></div>《易》于坤之震曰「见天地之心」，而其卦曰「复」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254550_comment'></div>以象而言，则阳剥而反下也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254550_comment'></div>以时而言，则阴尽而阳生也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254550_comment'></div>以数而言，则千百未形而一见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254550_comment'></div>是卦也，既不可以为阳，又不可以为阴，非复无以命之，岂一阴一阳之谓者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254550_comment'></div>固哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254550_comment'></div>先儒之说，曰天地以本为心，寂然至无者，其本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254550_comment'></div>夫天地之心，固寂然而至无，则天地亦几于息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254550_comment'></div>故无之说兴，释氏乃以空擅其宗，学士大夫未有不从而惑者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254550_comment'></div>自大而媲于细，自精而流于粗，自明而赜于幽，自常而极于变，穷天下之辨而未足以喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254550_comment'></div>昔者圣人故未尝言焉，其言者子思、孟轲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254550_comment'></div>子思、孟轲之言出于不得已，而圣人所以未尝言者，惧夫后世故以吾言为口实，将无所自得云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254550_comment'></div>《复》之六五曰「敦复无悔」，而其象曰「中以自考」，夫复至于敦厚而不薄，则真积而不已者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254550_comment'></div>其无所悔，则自质其中，而知其得者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254550_comment'></div>故曰「复以自知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254550_comment'></div>然则果何事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254550_comment'></div>就其可见者谓之仁，合而言之则谓之道，是以六二之邻于初则曰下仁，六四之应于初则曰从道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254550_comment'></div>盖仁者道之几，而道者复之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254550_comment'></div>故圣人之告颜子，以克己复礼为仁之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254550_comment'></div>夫难胜者己之私，既克者礼之复，岂吾所谓既往而归、既失而得者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254550_comment'></div>虽然，复不可过也，过则迷矣，迷则罔念而狂者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254550_comment'></div>苟不溺于无也，不陷于狂也，则圣人之门其庶几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254550_comment'></div>丹阳陈睎颜隽杰而有文，力学之士也，名其斋曰「敦复」，以志夫自考之意，而求予言以记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254550_comment'></div>顾余何足以进此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254550_comment'></div>然窃尝闻之，圣人之学，自治其一心，则推而至于治天下，本末先后，初无二致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254550_comment'></div>故复之不远，则以修身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254550_comment'></div>复之既迷，则足以败国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254550_comment'></div>自异端之肆也，亦曰治夫心者，而其说犹以一身为可外，况于所谓天下国家，孰知可离则非道也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254550_comment'></div>今睎颜亦知考于中而自见矣，其毋入于异端以务施于天下者，则睎颜真颜之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254550_comment'></div>乾道四年二月，颍川韩元吉记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1254550_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年3月</a>　三月壬申，建康留守史正志（致道）等为晋将军卞壶墓立石，元吉题额。作品：《卞壶墓识立石记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《景定建康志》卷43。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　与叶衡（梦锡）、赵彥端（德庄）游牛首山。作品：《同叶梦锡赵德庄游牛首山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243176' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243176' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243176?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同叶梦锡赵德庄游牛首山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243176")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243176_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243176'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243176'>不辞扶病触春寒，及此新晴一日閒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243176'>云外经年见双阙，马头乘兴数前山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243176'>清泉细酌巉岩上，佛窟同探紫翠间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243176'>我亦无心话禅悦，衔花百鸟自飞还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243176'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243176_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　史正志（致道）至采石，与知太平州吴芾（明可）会饮，有唱和，元吉次其韵。作品：《次韵吴明可与史致道会饮牛渚》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷5。）</span><div id='poem_243193' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243193' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243193?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵吴明可与史致道会饮牛渚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243193")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243193_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243193'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243193'>月出千山捲暮云，遥知玉节会江滨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243193'>便应击楫酬今日，不用然犀叹昔人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243193'>烟外笛声谁送晚，水边花影自迎春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243193'>风流三百年无此，况有清诗句法新。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243193'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243193_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年4月</a>　应僧道恭之请，作《隐静山新建御书毗庐二阁记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>隐静山新建御书毗卢二阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254549")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254549'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254549'>并江而南，自建业历姑熟，其山之著者曰隐静，介于句曲、九华之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254549_comment'></div>初无奇形异态，以峻拔表见于外，而涧壑逶迤，草丰木茂，五峰错立，如高人胜士超然迥出于埃壒，非世俗所得而有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254549_comment'></div>山之寺曰普惠，栋宇宏丽，佛事焕列，足以称其山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254549_comment'></div>寺之长老曰妙义大师道恭，当乾道三年，住山二十有四腊矣，禅学疏通而持律严甚，足以称其寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254549_comment'></div>恭之始来也，寺既圮于盗，因撤而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254549_comment'></div>筑大殿，植二楼，峙杰阁于南，辟丈室于背，周廊重庑，环室数百，无一榱一桷仍其旧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254549_comment'></div>恭尝自叹，以为积此岁月，其志愿之力粗已伸矣，而寺故有阁藏三朝御书百有二十轴，规制卑陋，不足妥宸章宝墨之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254549_comment'></div>客过而问之，恭则𢥠然曰：「吾敢后此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254549_comment'></div>是以庋天子之书，非有朝命、郡邑之请，惧不可为尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254549_comment'></div>可自为耶，可自为今为矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254549_comment'></div>于是鸠工庀材，夜以继日，岁十二月乙未，阁亦新焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254549_comment'></div>先是阁之建实嘉祐三年，郡人郭祥正为之记，谓其甲于寺屋也，乃以卑陋易之，则其兴造加于旧，率可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254549_comment'></div>明年三月告成，恭来言曰：以楹数之从衡为七十四楹，以尺度之高下为七十尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254549_comment'></div>中以庋御书，后为复阁，以安毗卢遮那之像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254549_comment'></div>左右飞阁，道壁涌千佛，栏楯四合，可以周旋瞻望作礼，围绕在我教中毗卢遮那广大楼阁等一切处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254549_comment'></div>使昧者于此，不劳弹指，同入如来大光明藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254549_comment'></div>而云汉昭回，炳耀大千，实我导师矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254549_comment'></div>愿并记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254549_comment'></div>盖宋室至太宗皇帝，悉平僭乱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254549_comment'></div>章圣登封降禅，以告成功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254549_comment'></div>仁宗偃武修文，跻于极治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254549_comment'></div>万几馀间，始得游意翰墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254549_comment'></div>三圣奎画，在世为多，高出唐贞观右，颁之天下，以镇夫名山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254549_comment'></div>惟隐静以梁慧严师杯渡道场，获受此赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254549_comment'></div>建炎初，贼张琪巢焉，书以仅存，是有神物阴拱而护之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254549_comment'></div>今道恭典治此山，能竭己力，美轮奂以侈上施，又崇像设，益阐其师传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254549_comment'></div>用钱凡四百万，积工凡万一千有奇，而佛像之费不在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254549_comment'></div>志勤而意广，诚可嘉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254549_comment'></div>尝读《华严》，考所谓善财童子求善知识，自妙峰极海岸国，展转南行，盖百一十许，最后始登毗卢大阁，方能了知一切庄严自在境界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1254549_comment'></div>然是童子初入胎时，七宝楼阁已现其家，乃见世尊逝多林中重阁故在，而山巅水涯，城郭市肆，人天仙鬼，诸聚集相，奔走殆遍，是遭文殊调剧不悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1254549_comment'></div>自今回观，可发大笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1254549_comment'></div>恭之不起于坐，既已庄严佛土矣，而最后因缘，犹示此阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1254549_comment'></div>善财不生，弥勒未见，将与文殊义为同异，必有能辨之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1254549_comment'></div>特以御书在焉，则甚大而光明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1254549_comment'></div>道恭笑曰：「然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1254549_comment'></div>所以求子而记者，此也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1254549_comment'></div>遂书以为记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1254549_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　上书右仆射蒋芾，认为江淮备御，筑城设关皆非计，“莫若益募州兵，以壮淮甸”作品：《与蒋丞相论淮甸筑城别纸》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷13。）</span><div id='poem_1254408' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254408' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254408?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与蒋丞相论淮甸筑城别纸</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254408")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254408_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254408'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254408'>某辄有愚见，恃相公方开公正之门，用敢贽诸左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254408_comment'></div>江东之于淮甸，盖唇齿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254408_comment'></div>某之效官既踰年矣，江淮利害亦颇讲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254408_comment'></div>士大夫孰不欲朝廷增修边备，日者诸郡往往自请筑城，诸将且为关隘之设，其说甚美，其费亦甚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254408_comment'></div>使费而有益，不问可也，然采之舆议，谓诸郡之所少者兵尔，非城也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254408_comment'></div>今兵数未之益焉，地将谁守之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254408_comment'></div>建康都统司不过五万人，所守关隘将十有馀处，每戍以三千，则仅足以分，三千果足以抗敌乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254408_comment'></div>敌众而不分，常以大势压我，而我兵不如敌众，复自分以弱其势，利害盖较然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254408_comment'></div>欲缓急资于民兵者，恐尤不足以敌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254408_comment'></div>为今之计，莫若益募州兵以壮淮甸，俾足旧额，而移筑城之费以养之，两淮得十万人则亦甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254408_comment'></div>至于关隘非至要之地，姑俟他日可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254408_comment'></div>夫千金之家，其治生财利亦有先后，茍力之未给而每事欲举焉，其自困必矣，不审钧虑以为如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254408_comment'></div>伏以相公经理万务，谅无遗策，而某怀仰知遇，不能自已，敢因修庆，布露其大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254408_comment'></div>干冒威严，愧恐无地。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1254408_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年5月12日</a>　生日，赵彥端（德庄）、丘崈（宗卿）有词为寿，元吉有和词。作品：《鹧鸪天》（雨歇云如隔座屏）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋词补辑》页26。）</span><div id='poem_243638' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243638' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243638?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹧鸪天<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年5月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243638")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243638_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243638'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243638'>雨歇云如隔座屏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243638'>薰风摇动一天青。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243638'>今年五十平头过，又喜清歌洗耳听。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243638_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243638'>浮世事，绝曾经。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243638'>此生应直斗牛星。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243638'>且倾田舍黄鸡酒，敢望君家白玉庭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_243638_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　第三女螺嫁吕祖谦（伯恭）为继室。作品：《回吕氏定婚书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷12。）</span><div id='poem_1254419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回吕氏定婚书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254419")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254419'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254419'>宋、鲁通盟，声子尝闻于继室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254419_comment'></div>郭、崔论契，伯深亦记于续婚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254419_comment'></div>顾惭旧族之馀，叠奉高门之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254419_comment'></div>伏承令侄孙宗教从政，早传世学，克自振于簪裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254419_comment'></div>而某弟运判位第三女五十一娘，未习妇功，恐粗闻于箕帚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254419_comment'></div>辱委禽之特厚，将鸣凤以重占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254419_comment'></div>盛事衣冠，既婚姻之是托；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254419_comment'></div>百年琴瑟，庶茀履以咸宜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1254419_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　任内，曾与权发遣广德军范述奏请蠲减广德军月椿钱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年5月21日</a>　除直敷文阁权知建宁府，本人以与福建安抚使王之望有嫌隙，请求别路差遣。作品：《辞免知建宁府札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《永乐大典》卷10988。）</span><div id='poem_1254388' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254388' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254388?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免知建宁府劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年5月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254388")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254388'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254388'>某伏准尚书省劄子，五月二十一日三省同奉圣旨，除某直敷文阁知建宁府，填见阙，疾速赴行在奏事讫，前去之任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254388_comment'></div>伏念某庸懦有素，昨者备数都司，蒙恩俾漕江左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254388_comment'></div>罄竭驽钝，已及替期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254388_comment'></div>方欲自露诚悃，祈就閒散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254388_comment'></div>敢期荣升内阁，易典潜藩，在于愚分，实深侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254388_comment'></div>惟是宝储秘列，职名过优，靖言罔功，非所当冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254388_comment'></div>兼某与福建安抚使王大资系有嫌隙，众所共知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254388_comment'></div>某昨任度支郎官，蒙其论罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254388_comment'></div>建宁正在统部，职事相干，法当回避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254388_comment'></div>欲望钧慈特赐敷奏，追寝进职之命，止乞陶铸别一路州军差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254388_comment'></div>某誓竭犬马之力，以明非茍免避事之意，不胜万幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254388_comment'></div>所有省劄，已寄建康府军资库，未敢祗受外，恭候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254388_comment'></div>干冒威严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254388_comment'></div>某下情无任惶惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1254388_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年6月11日</a>　改知江州。<br /></div>

-----title
天台
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年2月</a>　赴天台省母兄，渡钱塘江，中流搁浅，有诗记事。作品：《丁丑仲春将度浙江……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁丑仲春将渡浙江从者请盘沙予畏而不许既登舟乘潮以济中流胶焉捐十金募数力竟至沙上仅达西兴狼狈殊甚从者笑之感而赋诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243396")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243396'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243396'>桑田变东海，此语闻自昔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243396'>嗟我百年人，耳目讵能识。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243396'>谁言钱塘江，遂有车马迹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243396'>涨沙莽云屯，衣带仅寻尺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243396'>我初未渠信，束襜俟潮汐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243396'>是时月既望，春晴好风色。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243396'>同舟二三子，击楫意颇适。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243396'>中流类坳堂，竟作胶柱瑟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243396'>褰裳乱涛波，植杖负囊笈。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243396'>居然濯我足，长堤慰行客。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243396'>西兴忽在眼，唤渡犹顷刻。<div 台州

id='poem_title_243538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243538'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243538'>栋梁乃不取，得地且深植。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243538'>妖娆紫薇花，岁晚犹伴直。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243538'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243538_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>其兄元龙娶张孝祥妹法善为继室。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作《天台县题名记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《赤城集》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_1254586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天台县题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254586")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254586'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254586'>寓天下之治曰郡与县，其簿书期会、狱讼米盐之职，县实百于郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254586_comment'></div>盖郡则有掾有曹，各司其局，而守特视其成焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254586_comment'></div>县之官丞、主簿、尉，与令为四，号为通其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254586_comment'></div>然令无按察，丞、主簿、尉掌治各有它例，不能分总县务，其极悉萃于令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254586_comment'></div>旦起斗讼者立庭下，枚数其牒，眊焉已不胜其烦，狱之辞毕，听而后蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254586_comment'></div>暇则督民，赋课出纳，谨帐籍，官廪、士学、戍兵、役隶，月会而须给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254586_comment'></div>县或当孔道，执券而候驿者日罗络庑序，持文檄相恐动，赭皂之衣满前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254586_comment'></div>间有卒办，必取具于常赋之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254586_comment'></div>上官便文自安，不问所从来，民或诮语，则以咎令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254586_comment'></div>又为令者，秩不过七八品，势力卑甚，里居之豪，寓公之老，相与狙诖误腾谤讟，胁令以营其私，不则摇撼嘂噪，必使之去而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254586_comment'></div>令之缺榜于铨曹者率数十，阅岁踰时，皆惮不敢睨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254586_comment'></div>然国家之制，由选调而更京朝，必历令而正其资，号曰亲民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254586_comment'></div>比岁益严其格，往往不得命为他官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254586_comment'></div>由是士亦勉强自励其才，以试于县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254586_comment'></div>绍兴二十五年，吾兄子云始为令于天台，以为天台极两浙之东南，其地富山水，玉京、金庭，俱天下胜观，可以乘吏役之休，逃禅访道，从隐君子游，资禄以养亲，且应夫令之名而已，则倥偬亦不暇给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254586_comment'></div>既而叹曰：县固有剧易，事无不可为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254586_comment'></div>因为之竭日夜之力，疏剔刮磨，不事表暴，一意而持之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254586_comment'></div>未几吏民亦坦坦向化，始得从事于文墨之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254586_comment'></div>而县之前令名氏漫不可考，乃访诸塔庙之题识，推以案牍之岁月，得其可见者自郑至道而下才二十二人，将砻石刻于听事之左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254586_comment'></div>元吉方学邑于建安，从吾兄以问政，因书其事以为题名之始云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1254586_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
马鞍山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fd0f608675b549b6be9f6a438f3bf65f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fd0f608675b549b6be9f6a438f3bf65f");'><span id='fd0f608675b549b6be9f6a438f3bf65f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，44岁</div><div id='fd0f608675b549b6be9f6a438f3bf65f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　至采石，登翠螺山峨眉亭，赋词感怀。作品：《霜天晓角·蛾眉亭》（倚天绝壁）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>霜天晓角 题采石蛾眉亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243642")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243642'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243642'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_243642", 243642, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>倚天</span>绝壁，直下江千尺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243642'>天际两蛾凝黛，愁与恨，几时极！<div id='poem_sentence_1_243642_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243642'>怒潮风正急，酒醒闻塞笛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243642'>试问谪仙何处？<div id='poem_sentence_3_243642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243642'>青山外，远烟碧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_243642'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(243642)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>
