-----title
宣城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='72098b9954b9468b9835a89f3dc594ae_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("72098b9954b9468b9835a89f3dc594ae");'><span id='72098b9954b9468b9835a89f3dc594ae_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，44岁</div><div id='72098b9954b9468b9835a89f3dc594ae' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　至宣城，会晤张祁（晋彥）、张孝祥（安国）父子。作品：《次韵张晋彥书事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d851c8439a16450e9b0c6143fa0925f6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d851c8439a16450e9b0c6143fa0925f6");'><span id='d851c8439a16450e9b0c6143fa0925f6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>，51岁</div><div id='d851c8439a16450e9b0c6143fa0925f6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　其母卒，奔丧宣城。途经宁国，识知县孟泽（德润）<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1d2d0b710a7a4be9986f814078f17d0b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1d2d0b710a7a4be9986f814078f17d0b");'><span id='1d2d0b710a7a4be9986f814078f17d0b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>，54岁</div><div id='1d2d0b710a7a4be9986f814078f17d0b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　是春终丧，有宣城之行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8d959f81365b4eda9c40a857607b9b33_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8d959f81365b4eda9c40a857607b9b33");'><span id='8d959f81365b4eda9c40a857607b9b33_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>，66岁</div><div id='8d959f81365b4eda9c40a857607b9b33' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　至宣城展墓，七月返上饶，八月，应信守钱象祖（伯同）请，撰《信州新作二浮桥记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷15。）</span><div id='poem_1254563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>信州新作二浮桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254563")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254563'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254563'>淳熙十年仲夏，信溪大水，浮梁敝几垫，郡守朝奉郎钱侯象祖议新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254563_comment'></div>时岁屡歉，众惧费不能给也，侯则曰吾非取诸经赋也，矧敢敛于民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254563_comment'></div>顾吾承乏民上，愧无以及民者，惟是燕设厨传之常则加节焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254563_comment'></div>既踰年矣，公费之积或可用于此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254563_comment'></div>后两月，会予还自宣城，郡之士夫逆而诧曰：子家溪南吾州之桥成矣，前所未有也，意他郡之有亦莫及焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254563_comment'></div>且甚异者，方闵于雨，乃七月庚辰桥将系之夕，雨则大霔，四郊之禾尽兴，远近呼舞，谓将有秋，不特喜夫桥而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254563_comment'></div>子其为记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254563_comment'></div>于是相与步其上，坦如康衢，屹如崇堤，广丈五尺，危栏巨舰，材坚且良，群行不闻足音，疾驱得以并辔，信乎可诧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254563_comment'></div>又取其馀舟以杭于南港，盖两桥为舟六十艘，舟长皆四十有四尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254563_comment'></div>大桥则东西驿道所由出，南则趋闽粤焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254563_comment'></div>予睨而叹曰，古者矼石彴木而谓之桥，病其涉之厉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254563_comment'></div>后世比舟而梁焉，盖所以济不通也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254563_comment'></div>故虽盟津之险，长淮之阻，国朝为制，庀在有司，凡州县之滨于巨州者，得用为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254563_comment'></div>然或为或否，君子常以是为观政，非甚力之不足，则亦志之有怠云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254563_comment'></div>信在江东为冲，且岩邑也，力固不能甚富，而当官之怠间未免焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254563_comment'></div>异时为是桥者，必资于民，频易而屡败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254563_comment'></div>政和中，有县令郑畋始市田为之助，然不能二百亩，水旱犹半焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254563_comment'></div>淳熙改元，前吏部侍郎赵公汝愚为州，既新之矣，风雨漂摇，涛波荡激，岁才十周，舟已复坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254563_comment'></div>今钱侯之举也，当赈饥拯旱之馀，惟不惮于暂费而图其永久，可不谓难？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254563_comment'></div>未占而孚，雨以时应，人和之感，可不谓速？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254563_comment'></div>真有志而后成哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254563_comment'></div>然役兴而吏不哗，事集而下不惊，则政之无扰，于是可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254563_comment'></div>尝问其费，工亡虑五千四百有奇，钱为六千缗，糜赈民粒米之赢殆三百斛，较之前几于参倍，则其可久将亦什倍而无疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254563_comment'></div>使后之有志者率勿怠而时葺之，桥之岁月岂可计耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1254563_comment'></div>侯吴越之裔也，家世衮钺而澹如寒素，进摄郎省，来试是邦，以遵治民考功之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1254563_comment'></div>故能损二千石之得以自娱者，思及于民，移豆觞馈饷之悦于外者，以资往来无穷之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1254563_comment'></div>况其雨之喜正与桥会，在《春秋》之法，得以特书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1254563_comment'></div>故其士夫之请者，并以为喜，而士夫之喜，即其民之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1254563_comment'></div>八月戊申记并书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1254563_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
东至
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0e5e3822c5e34bec827b1269aeaf52dd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0e5e3822c5e34bec827b1269aeaf52dd");'><span id='0e5e3822c5e34bec827b1269aeaf52dd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>，45岁</div><div id='0e5e3822c5e34bec827b1269aeaf52dd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　有事至淮西，冬至日，经建德（今安徽东至），有诗感怀。作品：《至日建德道中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243436?labeling=true' target='_blank'>至日建德道中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243436")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243436'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243436'>圣皇初款帝中坛，羽檄交驰玉仗寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243436'>佳节又看当警急，劳生底用较悲欢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243436'>腐儒忧国成千虑，强敌窥人讵一端。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243436'>梦想淮南风雪里，可无消息报平安。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243436'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243436_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
镇江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='696bbd2347504c8bbd461446f236defd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("696bbd2347504c8bbd461446f236defd");'><span id='696bbd2347504c8bbd461446f236defd_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年闰11月</a>　除知饶州，至镇江省母，与陆游晤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年闰11月29日</a>　与陆游（务观）、何侑（德器）、张玉仲踏雪游焦山，观《瘞鹤铭》，并题名。作品：《隆兴甲申岁闰月游焦山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243529?labeling=true' target='_blank'>隆兴甲申岁闰月游焦山<span class='inlineComment2'>（原按：此诗据《镇江府志》补入。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年闰11月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", id='poem_sentence_6_243529'>观音岩前竹十寻，大士不死知此心。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243529'>醉归更唤殷七七，剩种好花开鹤林<span id='poem_sentence_8_243529_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　晤友人章甫（冠之）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年12月</a>　与陆游游镇江城西，遥望瓜洲，感慨系之。作品：《次韵务观城西书事二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_243010' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243010' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243010?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵务观城西书事二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243010")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243010_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243010'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243010'>腊尽雪晴春欲柔，濛濛烟柳认瓜洲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243010_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243010'>潮生潮落无穷事，江水东西不限愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243010_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243010'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243010_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243009' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243009?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_243009_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243009'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243009'>川摇百艇陆千车，多是淮南避地家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243009'>黄纸赦来戎马去，儿歌妇笑总呦哑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243009'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_243009_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年1月</a>　正月辛亥（朔日）改除考功郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年1月</a>　仍留镇江，与陆游唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年1月</a>　元夕，知镇江府方滋（务德）招饮赏梅，陆游与座，有唱和。作品：《方务德元夕不张灯留饮赏梅务观索赋古风》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>方务德元夕不张灯留饮赏梅务观索赋古风</a><span id='poem_sentence_1_243410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243410'>危亭直上花几许，水仙夹径梅纵横。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243410'>景龙灯火公尚记，耆旧出语儿童惊。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243410'>东风摇荡入烟柳，歌管错杂催离情。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 当涂
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0f96bc2762804783b994733590370c52_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0f96bc2762804783b994733590370c52");'><span id='0f96bc2762804783b994733590370c52_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>，51岁</div><div id='0f96bc2762804783b994733590370c52' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年6月</a>　解江东漕司职后，有宣城之行。至当涂，登凌歊台，有诗纪之。作品：《凌歊台》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243330' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243330' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243330?labeling=true' target='_blank'>凌歊台</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243330")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243330_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243330'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243330'>山到西江势却回，倚山楼殿更高台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243330'>天容水色望中见，帆影车尘空际来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243330'>桑柘棋分千里迥，波涛壁立两峰开。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243330'>登临拟问兴亡事，白塔亭亭锁翠苔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243330'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243330_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
芜湖
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2166dad87b3a49cb9358705a62ff5f7d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2166dad87b3a49cb9358705a62ff5f7d");'><span id='2166dad87b3a49cb9358705a62ff5f7d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>，51岁</div><div id='2166dad87b3a49cb9358705a62ff5f7d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年6月</a>　至芜湖，吊玩鞭亭，有诗。作品：《玩鞭亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷2。）</span><div id='poem_243466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243466?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玩鞭亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243466")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243466'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243466'>黄须鲜卑勇无策，自驰骏马来窥贼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243466'>贼奴但怪日绕营，起看飞尘已无迹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243466'>宝鞭不惜弃道傍，坐令老妪知兴亡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243466'>百年社稷有天意，奸锋逆焰徒鸱张。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243466'>孤城遗迹森在目，平湖无波<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>春草绿。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243466'>却对青山忆谢公，公老犹嫌人姓木。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243466'>边兵已重朝士轻，中原有路何由行。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243466'>柙中虎兕不可制，江左夷吾浪得名。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243466'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_243466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_243466'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_243466_0'>⑴ 《方舆胜览》卷一五作复</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_243466_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
青阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bd9c7439250b4a548ffaf8a5338582e3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bd9c7439250b4a548ffaf8a5338582e3");'><span id='bd9c7439250b4a548ffaf8a5338582e3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>，51岁</div><div id='bd9c7439250b4a548ffaf8a5338582e3' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游九华山。作品：《九华道中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243139' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243139' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243139?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九华道中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243139")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243139_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243139'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243139'>行人脚底不生尘，绝壁仙凡路已分。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243139'>一水奔腾崖覆雪，九峰罗立岫填云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243139'>谪仙才大三千首，国老谋深十万军。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243139'>莫对青山叹华发，丹砂未就又论文。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243139'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243139_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夜宿化城寺，得张孝祥（安国）壁间题词，和之。作品：《水龙吟·夜宿化城得张安国长短句戏用其韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水龙吟<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>夜宿化城，得张安国长短句，戏用其韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243562")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243562'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243562'>五溪深锁烟霞，定知不是人间世。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243562'>轩然九老，排云一笑，苍颜相对。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243562'>星斗垂空，月华随步，酒醒无寐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243562'>□广寒已近，嫦娥起舞，天风动、摇丹桂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243562_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243562'>极目层霄如洗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243562'>正千岩、棱棱霜气。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243562'>飞泉半落，苍崖百仞，珠翻玉碎。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243562'>金衲松成，葛洪丹就，如今千载。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243562'>叹谪仙诗在，骑驴未远，且留君醉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_243562_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

繁昌

-----title
吴江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2a55e71d1e6b42ff889024e3c41ebdb0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2a55e71d1e6b42ff889024e3c41ebdb0");'><span id='2a55e71d1e6b42ff889024e3c41ebdb0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>，51岁</div><div id='2a55e71d1e6b42ff889024e3c41ebdb0' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至垂虹亭，与范成大邂逅，时范成大赴任处州守，席间元吉赋词。作品：《水调歌头》（江路晓来雨）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>七月六日与范至能会饮垂虹。是时至能赴括苍，余以九江命造朝，至能索赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年7月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243568")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243568'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243568'>江路晓来雨，残暑夜全消。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243568'>人言天上今夕，飞鹊渐成桥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243568'>杳杳云车何处。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243568'>脉脉红蕖香度。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243568'>瓜果趁良宵。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243568'>推枕断虹卷，抚槛白鱼跳。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243568_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243568'>五湖客，临风露，倚兰苕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243568'>云涛四起，极目人世有烟霄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243568'>我送君舟西渡。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243568'>君望我帆南浦。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243568'>明日恨迢迢。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243568'>且醉吴淞月，重听浙江潮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_243568_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>别范成大、朱伯阳。作品：《松江别范至能朱伯阳》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243253?labeling=true' target='_blank'>松江别范至能朱伯阳<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年7月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243253")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243253_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243253'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243253'>弹铗功名易白头，归欤未办五湖舟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243253'>送君与我皆为守，到处逢山且纵游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243253'>薄日连云千幛晓，斜风吹雨一江秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243253'>买鱼斫鲙垂虹上，更为今年好景留。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243253'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243253_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243252?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243252'>吴歈湾月韵江船，屈指同行二十年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243252'>胜日五湖看老矣，倦游双鬓各苍然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243252'>拟寻诗酒平生社，未了尘埃薄宦缘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243252'>后夜西风相忆梦，琵琶亭下水笼烟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243252'></div><div 高邮

-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e7428f9c13834b948297a3dd1bea82c4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e7428f9c13834b948297a3dd1bea82c4");'><span id='e7428f9c13834b948297a3dd1bea82c4_link' -----title
金华
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ef8990c678a543e99f6e48b6d8c7180f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ef8990c678a543e99f6e48b6d8c7180f");'><span id='ef8990c678a543e99f6e48b6d8c7180f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>，57岁</div><div id='ef8990c678a543e99f6e48b6d8c7180f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　春，至婺州任。作品：《知婺州到任谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知婺州到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254305")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254305'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254305'>入尘法从，岁躔恍阅于再周；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254305_comment'></div>出假便蕃，道路仅更于数舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254305_comment'></div>仰体曲成之眷，敬宣宽大之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254305_comment'></div>伏念臣知力不能踰人，学术无以异众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254305_comment'></div>才疏意拙，少尝粗志于功名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254305_comment'></div>心折气摧，晚实重伤于忧患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254305_comment'></div>岂谓衰颓之朽质，寖蒙特达之圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254305_comment'></div>始寓直于掖垣，旋参华于选部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254305_comment'></div>文惟骫骳，屡承褒衮之加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254305_comment'></div>议本戆愚，悉荷威颜之假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254305_comment'></div>感洪慈之未报，揣微分而敢安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254305_comment'></div>顾此东阳，今为辅郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254305_comment'></div>财殚粟匮，适遭饥馑之馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254305_comment'></div>讼剧政繁，尤重藩宣之委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254305_comment'></div>孰云孱懦，可副选抡！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254305_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下躬慈俭以保邦，体宽仁而御下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254305_comment'></div>谓臣早更州县，或知抚字之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254305_comment'></div>怜臣久侍禁严，备识忧勤之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254305_comment'></div>贲之列职，宠以分符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254305_comment'></div>敢效昔贤，樽俎但期于赋咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254305_comment'></div>庶几汉吏，里闾稍遂于奠安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254305_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1254305_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　出郊劝农。作品：《婺州劝农文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span><div id='poem_1254389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>婺州劝农文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254389")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254389'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254389'>国家之制，守令专一劝农为职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254389_comment'></div>婺之为境至狭，民之力田者，盖有不待劝者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254389_comment'></div>然去岁一罹旱伤，阙食亦甚，朝廷课民种麦，丁宁备悉，盖虑其食不接也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254389_comment'></div>今春耕已动矣，有田者自耕之，无田者为人耕之，皆可以得食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254389_comment'></div>而乡村之间，犹有一二盗窃，或兴贩私盐，以取重罪，是志在于食而不知务本以求焉，太守甚不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254389_comment'></div>父老其道此意，以教训于子弟，麦可望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254389_comment'></div>若豆与粟，度地所宜，犹可致力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254389_comment'></div>陂塘之利，当修筑以备旱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254389_comment'></div>富豪大姓，亦惠恤闾里，鸠集而使之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254389_comment'></div>至于赈救之方，均济之策，太守其何敢辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254389_comment'></div>惟无怠于力，以服勤于田亩者，尔辈其自勉云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1254389_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年4月</a>　四月丁卯，跋仁风堂。作品：《跋仁风堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋仁风堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254482")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254482'>晋袁宏为东阳郡，谢安以扇赠之，宏曰「辄当奉扬仁风，慰彼黎庶」，盖前贤美谈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254482_comment'></div>郡有燕寝，因以「仁风」榜焉，庶修东阳故事，且俾里俗共兴于仁云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254482_comment'></div>淳熙元年四月丁卯，颍川韩某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1254482_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年6月</a>　六月戊寅，跋尹焞所书《东铭》作品：《书尹和靖所书〈东铭〉后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书尹和靖所书东铭后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254498")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254498'>和靖先生手书《东铭》，修水黄子馀所藏，寓九江时笔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254498_comment'></div>先生少喜字书，尝因书碑，同舍聚观，伊川笑谓之曰：「是固无害，第将为人役也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254498_comment'></div>自是不复书，然暮年笔力犹健如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254498_comment'></div>其教学者，必先读《东铭》，然后看《西铭》，谓从寡过而入尔，馀其知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254498_comment'></div>展玩太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254498_comment'></div>淳熙改元六月戊寅书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1254498_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年7月</a>　七月望，与陈岩肖（子象）、陈良祐（天与）、黄掞（子馀）、赵师龙（德言）秋郊观稼，并游金华洞，题名。作品：《金华洞题名》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷16。）</span><div id='poem_1254578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华洞题名</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254578")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254578'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1254578_comment'></div>寒气袭人，酌酒竹阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254578_comment'></div>支筇至中洞，饮泉乃归。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1254578_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　赵蕃（昌父）因友人徐季益有金华之行，寄诗致意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　秋试，为发解举人举行鹿鸣宴。作品：《鹿鸣宴》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷4。）</span><div id='poem_243380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243380'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243380'>金殿春风策隽贤，上林弧矢更争先。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243380'>不辞老懦聊推毂，要见飞腾总著鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243380'>勋业肇端登凤沼<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：叶公始登政地。）</span>，词章接武侍甘泉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243380'>明年贡籍还增倍，定作东州盛事传<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243380'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_243380'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_243380_0'>⑴ href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年9月9日</a>　重九，游双溪，登楼赋词。作品：《鹧鸪天·九日双溪楼》（不惜黄花插满头）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷7。）</span><div id='poem_243636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243636?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹧鸪天<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>九日双溪楼</a><span id='poem_sentence_1_243636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243636'>年年九日常拚醉，处处登高莫浪愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243636_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243636'>酬美景，驻清秋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243636'>绿橙香嫩酒初浮。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243636'>多情雨后双溪水，红满斜阳自在流。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_243636_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　毛#（平仲）赠诗文一编，以诗答之。作品：《毛平仲惠文编》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷1。）</span><div id='poem_243411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>毛文仲惠文编</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243411")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243411'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243411'>平生毛公诗，训传固已久。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243411'>纷纭齐鲁失，浪自开户牖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243411'>至哉一言蔽，可用严墨守。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243411'>渊源见云仍，梦泽吞八九。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243411'>雕章与棘句，锦绣间琼玖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243411'>嶷如犀始擢，粲若蚌初剖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_243411'>肉食乃闻韶，昼日或见斗。<div id='poem_sentence_6_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_243411'>三百篇未忘，七十子何有。<div id='poem_sentence_7_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_243411'>应如摩天刃，要是修月手。<div id='poem_sentence_8_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_243411'>时来岂无用，妙处端不朽。<div id='poem_sentence_9_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_243411'>君看夸夺儿，在后熟顾叟。<div id='poem_sentence_10_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_243411'>喧啾蛩负户，嘈囋蝉荫柳。<div id='poem_sentence_11_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_243411'>谁令口鸣悲，正使心欲呕。<div id='poem_sentence_12_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_243411'>岂无熊罴士，底问牛马走。<div id='poem_sentence_13_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_243411'>岧峣金闺门，豪杰自先后。<div id='poem_sentence_14_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_243411'>而君尚穷滞，履敝衿见肘。<div id='poem_sentence_15_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_243411'>才名三十年，肮脏惊白首。<div id='poem_sentence_16_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_243411'>我惭拜嘉赐，幼妇连齑臼。<div id='poem_sentence_17_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_243411'>相望百里远，曾未共樽酒。<div id='poem_sentence_18_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_243411'>期君颂中兴，步出次山右。<div id='poem_sentence_19_243411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_243411'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_243411_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年10月</a>　整理刊刻高祖韩维文集，有序。作品：《高祖宫师文编序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷14。）</span><div id='poem_1254472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高祖宫师文编序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254472")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254472'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254472'>高祖宫师文编仅三十卷，皆兵火后所辑，非旧本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254472_comment'></div>公自少喜为诗，然见子弟传录辄毁去，曰：「士大夫当以行义为先，是何足成名，吾以自适尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254472_comment'></div>绍圣中，党议既兴，公谪均州，归未终岁而薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254472_comment'></div>其治命则曰：「吾平生所行事自知之，他日无请谥，毋志吾墓也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254472_comment'></div>故自建中靖国以来，公虽追复元官，诸子不敢议铭事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254472_comment'></div>中兴四十年，元祐大臣往往得谥，子孙亦莫敢请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254472_comment'></div>独鲜于大受所为行状犹在，用列于篇首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254472_comment'></div>某逮事曾叔祖留司御史，时王、蔡方张，有所畏避，凡家集手自鐍之，无得观者，故公之论新法，触时禁之言，皆不传于外，而所传奏议十不四五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254472_comment'></div>南渡流离，集藁遂逸，访于四方，莫克尽获，惟诗尚多而内制特少，至其他文如与苏子美书、志程伯淳墓，士大夫虽知有之，无复见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254472_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254472_comment'></div>公固不以文自名者，其在家庭诲子弟，每以西汉为宗，故其笔力雄健，尤为南丰兄弟所推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254472_comment'></div>曾舍人既葬，必得公之文碑于道，而豫章黄太史自言因公诗得用事法，岂道德之蕴于内者深，其发于文词者皆馀事哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254472_comment'></div>小子不佞，无以绍君子之泽，独其文编负笈而藏，欲俟备而传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254472_comment'></div>惧有河清之叹，因裒而刊之东阳郡斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254472_comment'></div>夫自涯而观于澜，历阶而望于奥，亦足以知其大略矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254472_comment'></div>异日求于好事之家，继有得者，尚将附益云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254472_comment'></div>淳熙元年十月，玄孙具位某谨书<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254472_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1254472'>后：原脱，据聚珍本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1254472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1254472'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_1254472_0'>⑴ 《南涧甲乙稿》卷一四。又见《永乐大典》卷二二五三七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1254472_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　为浙东提刑按劾，上自辨札子，两乞宫观，不许，降一官，改知建宁府。作品：《自辨札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span>《谢降官表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span>《婺州乞宫观札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷10。）</span>《辞知建宁府表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254365?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自辨劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254365")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254365'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254365'>臣愚戆拙直，久荷圣知，初无尺寸之劳，仰图报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254365_comment'></div>委付一州，仅及期月，自速旷戾，祗荷宽典，不当有言，重冒宸听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254365_comment'></div>但念臣蒙提刑司所按四事，买罗专辄止以去岁退剥者多，官吏坐罪，今年欲凑足纲运，以趁省限，故令违限不纳，及所纳不中者，折纳原价，数实不多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254365_comment'></div>而坊场钱仅四千缗，及漕司贺璞兰溪酒坊所欠，境内盗贼未获，尚有限日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254365_comment'></div>至于陈桂聚众殴打税官，臣以情重法轻，故尝奏请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254365_comment'></div>惟是臣遇事率略，有失自顾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254365_comment'></div>提刑韩俣曾以劄子通与守倅，催督官钱，盖亦公移之比，而签厅官循例一面回文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254365_comment'></div>臣以卤莽，偶忘报应，今始闻韩俣谓臣有轻忽武臣之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254365_comment'></div>臣材力驽下，自蒙陛下拔擢，屡与武臣同事，被命出疆及叨馆伴、看详官制等，每务和同，何尝稍有轻忽之疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254365_comment'></div>缘俣与臣素未相识，亦臣之疏，悔愧何及？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254365_comment'></div>臣深恐职事相干，别致悔吝，故不避鈇钺，欲望圣慈许臣閒退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254365_comment'></div>而臣区区肝胆，敢具奏知，仰乞天地父母之仁，特赐睿照，臣则万幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254365_comment'></div>荐渎天威，臣无任激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1254365_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1254310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254310?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢降官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254310")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254310_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254310'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254310'>外台摭戾，难挽于深文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254310_comment'></div>中诏施仁，第从于宽典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254310_comment'></div>恩隆命薄，感极涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254310_comment'></div>伏念臣猥以庸才，叨尘辅郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254310_comment'></div>野无青草，适岁事之荐饥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254310_comment'></div>户有犀渠，复土风之善竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254310_comment'></div>慨疲驽之既竭，惭尺寸之图功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254310_comment'></div>财货未赢，阳城之政甚拙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254310_comment'></div>教条靡善，延寿之过自知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254310_comment'></div>至于报应或谬于文移，请谳务伸于法令，重贻刺举，宜在谴诃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254310_comment'></div>羸瓶之寘井湄，盖有挤而甚者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254310_comment'></div>弊车之避道左，是宜麾而去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254310_comment'></div>敢期覆帱之深，曲示保全之厚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254310_comment'></div>就移职守，特损官联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254310_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下汤网务宽，舜玑惟察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254310_comment'></div>念臣久更州县，常自信其迂愚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254310_comment'></div>怜臣昔侍禁严，每洞知其拙直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254310_comment'></div>刑于善贷，责以后来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254310_comment'></div>臣敢不仰副殊私，益坚素履？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254310_comment'></div>虽桑榆之收暮景，莫知补报之方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254310_comment'></div>若葵藿之倾太阳，尚有糜捐之所。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1254310_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1254368' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254368' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254368?labeling=true' target='_blank'>婺州乞宫观劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254368")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254368_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254368'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254368'>臣辄沥血诚，不避鈇钺，干冒渊听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254368_comment'></div>臣守藩无善，近贻监司按察，分当汰斥，圣恩宽大，第从镌等，天地父母之仁，虽臣粉骨碎身，未知图报之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254368_comment'></div>窃惟臣之事君，如子事父，犯而无隐，要在尽情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254368_comment'></div>臣之肝胆，若不披露于陛下之前，臣则有隐情之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254368_comment'></div>伏念臣迂拙，因荷陛下拔擢，寘之侍从，昨奉清光，每蒙异眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254368_comment'></div>试以辅郡，适遭旱暵之馀，公私空匮，饥民满野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254368_comment'></div>臣不敢辞难，以孤任使，罄竭驽钝，左枝右梧，幸及丰登，无所规避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254368_comment'></div>方欲祈就閒散，少息疲懦之躯，才疏政拙，遽被刺举，事之曲折，何敢自辨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254368_comment'></div>固当仰体陛下重易守臣之意，黾勉效职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254368_comment'></div>但臣多病蚤衰，心志凋耗，连年哭女，目力顿昏，自难久居烦剧之郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254368_comment'></div>况臣赋性疏直，动乏周虑，若不引避，诚恐职事之间有重悔吝，在臣孤迹，委实难安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254368_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣素无他肠，怜臣非有避事，特降睿旨，畀臣一在外宫观差遣，稍延岁月，未填沟壑，皆所以事陛下之日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254368_comment'></div>上渎宸听，臣无任陨越战惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254368_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1254368_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1254308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞知建宁府表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254308")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254308'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254308'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，十二月三日，三省同奉圣旨，差臣知建宁府，不候授告，疾速前去之任，候任满前来奏事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254308_comment'></div>臣钦闻成命，愧惧无任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254308_comment'></div>伏念臣以至愚极陋之质，荷上圣特达之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254308_comment'></div>擢寘三铨，已乏论思之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254308_comment'></div>试守一郡，迄无善最之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254308_comment'></div>徒知奉行宽大，以拊摩饥馑之馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254308_comment'></div>不虑自贻旷瘝，而招致悔尤之积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254308_comment'></div>恳祈散地，实微分之攸宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254308_comment'></div>以畀便藩，匪私心之敢望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254308_comment'></div>况建宁之钜镇，本潜跃之名区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254308_comment'></div>虽异时尝叨宰字之官，岂今日遂有镇临之幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254308_comment'></div>已试无状，启处不遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254308_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下遴选循良，布宣德意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254308_comment'></div>俾内外咸举其职，思小大务尽其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254308_comment'></div>宠以真祠，庶少安于庸懦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254308_comment'></div>假之岁月，斯曲示于保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254308_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254308_comment'></div>所有恩命，未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254308_comment'></div>臣除已交割婺州职事已与次官，一面起离前去衢信州听候指挥外，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1254308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年11月</a>　其兄元龙（子云）之江东转运副使任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　洪遵（景严）卒，有挽词。作品：《故资政殿大学士枢密洪公挽词二首》（世学推东楚）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷3。）</span><div id='poem_243266' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243266' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243266?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故资政殿大学士枢密洪公挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span "poem_title_243266")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_243266_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243266'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243266'>筹幄渊谋在，陪京惠爱多。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243266'>无因奠鸡酒，清泪洒江波。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243266'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_243266_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　其兄元龙（子云）年六十，有词为寿。作品：《鹧鸪天》（甲子今年甫一周）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋词》页1405。）</span><div id='poem_243637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹧鸪天 子云弟生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_243637")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_243637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_243637'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_243637'>甲子今年甫一周。<div id='poem_sentence_0_243637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_243637'>人间聊住八千秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_243637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_243637'>依依梅蕊看如雪，恰恰蟾华未上钩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_243637_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_243637'>分玉节，共南州。<div id='poem_sentence_3_243637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_243637'>台城辇路记重游。<div id='poem_sentence_4_243637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_243637'>相期一品归来健，兄弟华颠自献酬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_243637_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f3c018e3f48c46ba9dd6e78bf7cdfd6e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f3c018e3f48c46ba9dd6e78bf7cdfd6e");'><span id='f3c018e3f48c46ba9dd6e78bf7cdfd6e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1179')">1178-1179年</a>，61-62岁</div><div id='f3c018e3f48c46ba9dd6e78bf7cdfd6e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年9月</a>　九月下旬，至婺州任。有谢表。作品：《再知婺州到任谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷8。）</span><div id='poem_1254306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再知婺州到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254306")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254306'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254306'>冠西清之美职，已冒殊恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254306_comment'></div>分太末之名邦，仍叨旧治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254306_comment'></div>稍违行阙，即居部封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254306_comment'></div>伏念臣少尝窃慕于古人，晚始亲逢于圣主，岂谓迂疏之质，遂蒙特达之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1254306_comment'></div>造膝而贡狂愚，既屡嘉其一得；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1254306_comment'></div>披肝而导志虑，曾何补于万分！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1254306_comment'></div>罔知岁月之迁，寖荷宠灵之异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1254306_comment'></div>昨膺召节，误长从班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1254306_comment'></div>孰云铨叙之平，益愧论思之谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1254306_comment'></div>葵藿徒知向日，忍负寸心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1254306_comment'></div>犬马犹有恋轩，敢怀去意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1254306_comment'></div>第每虞于讥议，仍滋惧于满盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1254306_comment'></div>自诡为州，实难报上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1254306_comment'></div>况兹宝婺，特近太微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1254306_comment'></div>地窃重临，治行靡追于黄霸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1254306_comment'></div>时容著咏，郊居肯慕于沈侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1254306_comment'></div>祗佩眷私，若为称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1254306_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下德参天地，道冒华戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1254306_comment'></div>泰和在于唐虞，肃臣工而器使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1254306_comment'></div>仁风慰于黎庶，择守命以布宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1254306_comment'></div>施及妄庸，荐加优渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1254306_comment'></div>臣敢不恪求民瘼，寅奉藩条？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1254306_comment'></div>官联喉舌之司，顾敢忘于左右？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1254306_comment'></div>郡亦股肱之寄，誓益告于谋猷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1254306_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年10月</a>　其兄元龙（子云）由司农卿出为浙西提刑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　族弟僧祖航自镇江来省父三十三司户墓，元吉与之寻访，并为文致祭。祖航别去，有诗送之。作品：《祭三十三司户叔文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷18。）</span>《航弟自广润省坟金华二绝送之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南涧甲乙稿》卷6。）</span><div id='poem_1254665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1254665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1254665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭三十三司户叔文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34515, "南宋", "韩元吉", "poem_title_1254665")'>韩元吉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1254665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1254665'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1254665'>年月日，具位某谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于族叔父、前处州司户三十三迪功之坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1254665_comment'></div>某再叨守州，始克访叔茔厝，仅乃得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1254665_comment'></div>追念昔者叔摄事于兹，相与甚款，遂三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1254665_comment'></div>祖航为僧，四十八娘远嫁龙泉，无为叔后者，感伤之怀，如何可述？</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1254665_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_243111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_243111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/243111?labeling=true'
